package org.pronzato.fabric.api;

import org.pronzato.fabric.api.access.AccessManager;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.catalog.CatalogManager;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.connections.ConnectionManager;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.configs.ConfigManager;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.DataManagers;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.recovery.RecoveryManager;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.SecurityManager;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.schemas.SchemaManager;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.ServiceManager;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.streams.StreamManager;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.session.SessionContext;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.session.SessionImpl;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.telemetry.OtelManager;

public final class Fabric {

  private Fabric() {}

  public static SessionImpl.Builder newSession() {
    return new SessionImpl.Builder();
  }

  public interface Session extends AutoCloseable {
    
    SessionContext context();
    ServiceManager services();
    AccessManager access();
    DataManagers data();
    ConfigManager configs();
    SchemaManager schemas();
    StreamManager streams();
    RecoveryManager recovery();
    ConnectionManager connections();
    CatalogManager catalog();
    SecurityManager security();
    OtelManager telemetry();

    void start() throws Exception;

    boolean started();


    void stop();

    @Override
    void close();
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.access;

import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Optional;
import java.util.Set;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.core.services.ServiceEntitlements;

public interface AccessManager {
  enum DatasetAction {
    READ,
    WRITE
  }

  enum ServiceAction {
    START,
    INVOKE,
    READ,
    WRITE
  }

  record DatasetServiceRoute(
      String datasetId,
      String serviceId,
      String serviceDisplay,
      String serviceType,
      int candidateCount,
      boolean online) {}

  record DatasetAccess(
      String datasetId,
      String group,
      String namespace,
      String name,
      Set<DatasetAction> allowedActions,
      DatasetServiceRoute queryRoute) {}

  record ServiceAccess(
      String serviceId,
      String group,
      String name,
      String serviceType,
      boolean online,
      Map<ServiceEntitlements.Transport, Set<ServiceAction>> allowedActionsByTransport) {}

  String defaultSubject();

  List<DatasetAccess> datasets();

  List<DatasetAccess> datasets(String subject);

  List<String> queryableDatasets();

  List<String> queryableDatasets(String subject);

  boolean canQueryDataset(String datasetId);

  boolean canQueryDataset(String subject, String datasetId);

  Optional<DatasetServiceRoute> datasetQueryRoute(String datasetId);

  Optional<DatasetServiceRoute> datasetQueryRoute(String subject, String datasetId);

  List<ServiceAccess> services();

  List<ServiceAccess> services(String subject);

  List<String> callableServices();

  List<String> callableServices(String subject);

  boolean canCallService(String serviceId);

  boolean canCallService(String subject, String serviceId);

  boolean canCallService(
      String subject,
      String serviceId,
      ServiceEntitlements.Transport transport,
      ServiceAction action);

  boolean isServiceOnline(String serviceId);
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.catalog;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Optional;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionType;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.common.Semantic;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.lifecycle.DeleteBehavior;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.lifecycle.OwnershipType;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.lifecycle.PromotionBehavior;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.lifecycle.RelationshipType;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.catalog.semantics.SemanticCompletenessClass;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public interface CatalogManager {

  CatalogSearchResult search(CatalogSearchQuery query);

  CatalogSearchResult search(CatalogSearchQuery query, CatalogAccessContext accessContext);

  Optional<CatalogDetails> getAsset(String assetId);

  Optional<CatalogDetails> getAsset(String assetId, CatalogAccessContext accessContext);

  Map<RelationshipType, List<CatalogRelationshipView>> getRelatedAssets(String assetId);

  Map<RelationshipType, List<CatalogRelationshipView>> getRelatedAssets(
      String assetId, CatalogAccessContext accessContext);

  record CatalogAccessContext(
      String subject,
      String delegatedSubject,
      String lane,
      String seedAssetId) {

    public CatalogAccessContext {
      subject = Strings.trimToNull(subject);
      delegatedSubject = Strings.trimToNull(delegatedSubject);
      lane = Strings.trimToNull(lane);
      seedAssetId = Strings.trimToNull(seedAssetId);
    }

    public static CatalogAccessContext defaults(String subject, String lane) {
      return new CatalogAccessContext(subject, null, lane, null);
    }
  }

  record CatalogDetails(
      CatalogSummary summary,
      String businessMeaning,
      List<String> aliases,
      List<String> keywords,
      Semantic.Ownership ownership,
      Semantic.DataShape dataShape,
      Semantic.Freshness freshness,
      Semantic.Trust trust,
      Semantic.Usage usage,
      Semantic.ToolHints toolHints,
      SemanticCompletenessClass semanticCompletenessClass,
      int semanticCompletenessScore,
      Map<RelationshipType, List<CatalogRelationshipView>> relationshipsByType,
      Map<RelationshipType, Integer> relationshipCounts) {

    public CatalogDetails {
      aliases = aliases == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(new ArrayList<>(aliases));
      keywords = keywords == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(new ArrayList<>(keywords));
      semanticCompletenessClass =
          semanticCompletenessClass == null ? SemanticCompletenessClass.WEAK : semanticCompletenessClass;
      semanticCompletenessScore = Math.max(0, Math.min(100, semanticCompletenessScore));
      relationshipsByType = copyRelationships(relationshipsByType);
      relationshipCounts = copyCounts(relationshipCounts);
    }

    private static Map<RelationshipType, List<CatalogRelationshipView>> copyRelationships(
        Map<RelationshipType, List<CatalogRelationshipView>> value) {
      if (value == null || value.isEmpty()) {
        return Map.of();
      }
      LinkedHashMap<RelationshipType, List<CatalogRelationshipView>> copied = new LinkedHashMap<>();
      for (Map.Entry<RelationshipType, List<CatalogRelationshipView>> entry : value.entrySet()) {
        List<CatalogRelationshipView> relationships =
            entry.getValue() == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(new ArrayList<>(entry.getValue()));
        copied.put(entry.getKey(), relationships);
      }
      return Map.copyOf(copied);
    }

    private static Map<RelationshipType, Integer> copyCounts(Map<RelationshipType, Integer> value) {
      if (value == null || value.isEmpty()) {
        return Map.of();
      }
      return Map.copyOf(new LinkedHashMap<>(value));
    }
  }

  enum CatalogRelationshipDirection {
    OUTGOING,
    INCOMING
  }

  record CatalogRelationshipView(
      String fromAssetId,
      String toAssetId,
      CatalogRelationshipDirection direction,
      RelationshipType relationshipType,
      OwnershipType ownershipType,
      PromotionBehavior promotionBehavior,
      DeleteBehavior deleteBehavior,
      boolean required,
      boolean shared,
      String notes,
      String targetLocator,
      DefinitionType relatedAssetType,
      String relatedAssetGroup,
      String relatedAssetName,
      String relatedAssetNamespace) {

    public CatalogRelationshipView {
      fromAssetId = Strings.trimToEmpty(fromAssetId);
      toAssetId = Strings.trimToEmpty(toAssetId);
      direction = direction == null ? CatalogRelationshipDirection.OUTGOING : direction;
      notes = Strings.trimToEmpty(notes);
      targetLocator = Strings.trimToEmpty(targetLocator);
      relatedAssetType = relatedAssetType == null ? DefinitionType.UNKNOWN : relatedAssetType;
      relatedAssetGroup = Strings.trimToEmpty(relatedAssetGroup);
      relatedAssetName = Strings.trimToEmpty(relatedAssetName);
      relatedAssetNamespace = Strings.trimToEmpty(relatedAssetNamespace);
    }
  }

  record CatalogSearchFacet(
      Map<String, Integer> typeCounts,
      Map<String, Integer> domainCounts,
      Map<String, Integer> tagCounts,
      Map<String, Integer> ownerCounts,
      Map<String, Integer> trustCounts,
      Map<String, Integer> freshnessCounts) {

    public CatalogSearchFacet {
      typeCounts = copy(typeCounts);
      domainCounts = copy(domainCounts);
      tagCounts = copy(tagCounts);
      ownerCounts = copy(ownerCounts);
      trustCounts = copy(trustCounts);
      freshnessCounts = copy(freshnessCounts);
    }

    public static CatalogSearchFacet empty() {
      return new CatalogSearchFacet(Map.of(), Map.of(), Map.of(), Map.of(), Map.of(), Map.of());
    }

    private static Map<String, Integer> copy(Map<String, Integer> value) {
      if (value == null || value.isEmpty()) {
        return Map.of();
      }
      return Map.copyOf(new LinkedHashMap<>(value));
    }
  }

  record CatalogSearchQuery(
      String query,
      String type,
      String domain,
      List<String> tags,
      String owner,
      String trust,
      String freshness,
      Integer limit,
      String seedAssetId) {

    public static final int DEFAULT_LIMIT = 50;
    public static final int MAX_LIMIT = 500;

    public CatalogSearchQuery {
      query = Strings.trimToNull(query);
      type = Strings.trimToNull(type);
      domain = Strings.trimToNull(domain);
      tags = normalizeTags(tags);
      owner = Strings.trimToNull(owner);
      trust = Strings.trimToNull(trust);
      freshness = Strings.trimToNull(freshness);
      seedAssetId = Strings.trimToNull(seedAssetId);
      limit = normalizeLimit(limit);
    }

    public static CatalogSearchQuery defaults() {
      return new CatalogSearchQuery(null, null, null, List.of(), null, null, null, DEFAULT_LIMIT, null);
    }

    private static Integer normalizeLimit(Integer value) {
      if (value == null || value <= 0) {
        return DEFAULT_LIMIT;
      }
      return Math.min(MAX_LIMIT, value);
    }

    private static List<String> normalizeTags(List<String> values) {
      if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
        return List.of();
      }
      LinkedHashSet<String> deduped = new LinkedHashSet<>();
      for (String value : values) {
        String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
        if (normalized != null) {
          deduped.add(normalized);
        }
      }
      if (deduped.isEmpty()) {
        return List.of();
      }
      return List.copyOf(new ArrayList<>(deduped));
    }
  }

  record CatalogSearchResult(
      List<CatalogSummary> results,
      CatalogSearchFacet facets,
      int totalCount) {

    public CatalogSearchResult {
      results = results == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(new ArrayList<>(results));
      facets = facets == null ? CatalogSearchFacet.empty() : facets;
      totalCount = Math.max(0, totalCount);
    }
  }

  record CatalogSummary(
      String assetId,
      DefinitionType type,
      String group,
      String name,
      String namespace,
      String title,
      String description,
      String domain,
      String subdomain,
      List<String> tags,
      String ownerId,
      Semantic.Certification trustCertification,
      Semantic.QualityStatus trustQualityStatus,
      String freshnessCadence,
      SemanticCompletenessClass semanticCompletenessClass,
      int semanticCompletenessScore,
      int relationshipCount,
      double rankScore) {

    public CatalogSummary {
      assetId = Strings.trimToEmpty(assetId);
      type = type == null ? DefinitionType.UNKNOWN : type;
      group = Strings.trimToEmpty(group);
      name = Strings.trimToEmpty(name);
      namespace = Strings.trimToEmpty(namespace);
      title = Strings.trimToEmpty(title);
      description = Strings.trimToEmpty(description);
      domain = Strings.trimToEmpty(domain);
      subdomain = Strings.trimToEmpty(subdomain);
      tags = tags == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(new ArrayList<>(tags));
      ownerId = Strings.trimToEmpty(ownerId);
      trustCertification =
          trustCertification == null ? Semantic.Certification.NONE : trustCertification;
      trustQualityStatus =
          trustQualityStatus == null ? Semantic.QualityStatus.UNKNOWN : trustQualityStatus;
      freshnessCadence = Strings.trimToEmpty(freshnessCadence);
      semanticCompletenessClass =
          semanticCompletenessClass == null ? SemanticCompletenessClass.WEAK : semanticCompletenessClass;
      semanticCompletenessScore = Math.max(0, Math.min(100, semanticCompletenessScore));
      relationshipCount = Math.max(0, relationshipCount);
      rankScore = Math.max(0d, rankScore);
    }
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.catalog.manager;

import java.util.Locale;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.Definition;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionDataset;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionIngest;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionIngestSource;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionStream;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionType;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

final class CatalogServiceImplIds {

  private CatalogServiceImplIds() {}

  static String definitionKey(DefinitionType type, String group, String name) {
    return normalizeType(type) + "|" + Strings.trimToNull(group) + "|" + Strings.trimToNull(name);
  }

  static String normalizeType(DefinitionType type) {
    return type == null ? "UNKNOWN" : type.name();
  }

  static String defaultNamespace(Definition definition) {
    if (definition instanceof DefinitionDataset dataset) {
      return Strings.trimToNull(dataset.namespace());
    }
    if (definition instanceof DefinitionStream stream) {
      return Strings.trimToNull(stream.namespace());
    }
    if (definition instanceof DefinitionIngestSource ingestSource) {
      return Strings.trimToNull(ingestSource.namespace());
    }
    if (definition instanceof DefinitionIngest ingest) {
      String datasetId = Strings.trimToNull(ingest.datasetId());
      if (datasetId != null && datasetId.startsWith("dataset:")) {
        String[] parts = datasetId.substring("dataset:".length()).split("/");
        if (parts.length >= 3) {
          return Strings.trimToNull(parts[1]);
        }
      }
    }
    return "";
  }

  static ParsedAssetId parseAssetId(String assetId) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(assetId);
    if (normalized == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("assetId is required");
    }
    int separator = normalized.indexOf(':');
    if (separator <= 0 || separator >= normalized.length() - 1) {
      return new ParsedAssetId(DefinitionType.UNKNOWN, null, normalized, null);
    }
    String prefix = normalized.substring(0, separator).toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
    String payload = normalized.substring(separator + 1);
    String[] parts = payload.split("/");
    DefinitionType type =
        switch (prefix) {
          case "dataset" -> DefinitionType.DATASET;
          case "service" -> DefinitionType.SERVICE;
          case "stream" -> DefinitionType.STREAM;
          case "schema" -> DefinitionType.SCHEMA;
          case "config" -> DefinitionType.CONFIG_LAYER;
          case "connection" -> DefinitionType.CONNECTION;
          case "ingest" -> DefinitionType.INGEST;
          case "ingest-source" -> DefinitionType.INGEST_SOURCE;
          case "entitlement" -> DefinitionType.ENTITLEMENT;
          case "app" -> DefinitionType.APP;
          case "platform" -> DefinitionType.PLATFORM;
          default -> DefinitionType.UNKNOWN;
        };
    if (parts.length == 1) {
      return new ParsedAssetId(type, null, Strings.requireNonBlank(parts[0], "assetId.name"), null);
    }
    if (parts.length == 2) {
      return new ParsedAssetId(
          type,
          Strings.trimToNull(parts[0]),
          Strings.requireNonBlank(parts[1], "assetId.name"),
          null);
    }
    return new ParsedAssetId(
        type,
        Strings.trimToNull(parts[0]),
        Strings.requireNonBlank(parts[2], "assetId.name"),
        Strings.trimToNull(parts[1]));
  }

  static record ParsedAssetId(DefinitionType type, String group, String name, String namespace) {
    ParsedAssetId {
      type = type == null ? DefinitionType.UNKNOWN : type;
      group = Strings.trimToNull(group);
      name = Strings.requireNonBlank(name, "assetId.name");
      namespace = Strings.trimToNull(namespace);
    }
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.configs.admin;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonNode;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.node.ObjectNode;
import java.time.Instant;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.List;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionConfigLayer;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionConfigChange;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionEnvelope;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.configs.ConfigManager.ConfigAdmin;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.configs.ConfigManager.ConfigInfo;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.configs.ConfigManager;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.configs.workflow.ConfigAdminService;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class ConfigAdminImpl implements ConfigAdmin {
  private static final int DEFAULT_AUDIT_LIMIT = 20;

  private final String group;
  private final ConfigManager configManager;
  private final ConfigAdminService.Workflow workflow;

  public ConfigAdminImpl(String group, ConfigManager configManager, ConfigAdminService adminService) {
    this.group = required(group, "group");
    this.configManager = java.util.Objects.requireNonNull(configManager, "configManager");
    java.util.Objects.requireNonNull(adminService, "adminService");
    this.workflow = java.util.Objects.requireNonNull(adminService.workflow(), "workflow");
  }

  @Override
  public ConfigAdmin.UpdateResult update(ConfigAdmin.UpdateRequest request) {
    if (request == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("request is required");
    }
    String configId = required(request.configId(), "configId");
    String layerId = required(request.layerId(), "layerId");
    ObjectNode draft = requireObject(request.declaredPayload(), "declaredPayload");
    ConfigAdmin.ChangeMode requestedMode =
        request.mode() == null ? ConfigAdmin.ChangeMode.IMMEDIATE : request.mode();
    DefinitionConfigChange.ChangeMode mode = toInternalMode(requestedMode);
    Instant effectiveTimeUtc = request.effectiveTimeUtc();
    Instant expiresAtUtc = request.expiresAtUtc();
    String comment = Strings.trimToNull(request.comment());
    String subject = Strings.trimToNull(request.subject());

    DefinitionConfigChange proposed =
        workflow.propose(
            group,
            configId,
            layerId,
            draft,
            mode,
            effectiveTimeUtc,
            expiresAtUtc,
            comment,
            subject);
    if (request.approvalRequired()) {
      return new ConfigAdmin.UpdateResult(
          configId, layerId, true, "PROPOSED", toWorkflowStatus(proposed), null);
    }

    workflow.approve(group, configId, layerId, comment, subject);
    DefinitionConfigLayer published =
        workflow.publish(
            group,
            configId,
            layerId,
            null,
            null,
            null,
            comment,
            subject);
    DefinitionConfigChange current = workflow.workflow(group, configId, layerId, DEFAULT_AUDIT_LIMIT);
    return new ConfigAdmin.UpdateResult(
        configId,
        layerId,
        false,
        "PUBLISHED",
        toWorkflowStatus(current),
        toPublishedConfig(published, configId, layerId));
  }

  @Override
  public List<ConfigAdmin.WorkflowStatus> list() {
    return list(DEFAULT_AUDIT_LIMIT);
  }

  @Override
  public List<ConfigAdmin.WorkflowStatus> list(int auditLimit) {
    int boundedAudit = auditLimit <= 0 ? DEFAULT_AUDIT_LIMIT : auditLimit;
    List<DefinitionConfigChange> pending = new ArrayList<>();
    for (ConfigInfo info : configManager.listConfigs()) {
      if (info == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String configId = Strings.trimToNull(info.configId());
      if (configId == null) {
        continue;
      }
      for (String layerId : configManager.listLayers(configId)) {
        String normalizedLayerId = Strings.trimToNull(layerId);
        if (normalizedLayerId == null) {
          continue;
        }
        DefinitionConfigChange change = workflow.workflow(group, configId, normalizedLayerId, boundedAudit);
        if (isPending(change)) {
          pending.add(change);
        }
      }
    }
    pending.sort(
        Comparator.comparing(
                DefinitionConfigChange::updatedTimeUtc, Comparator.nullsLast(String::compareTo))
            .reversed()
            .thenComparing(DefinitionConfigChange::configId, Comparator.nullsLast(String::compareTo))
            .thenComparing(DefinitionConfigChange::layerId, Comparator.nullsLast(String::compareTo)));
    List<ConfigAdmin.WorkflowStatus> results = new ArrayList<>(pending.size());
    for (DefinitionConfigChange change : pending) {
      ConfigAdmin.WorkflowStatus status = toWorkflowStatus(change);
      if (status != null) {
        results.add(status);
      }
    }
    return List.copyOf(results);
  }

  @Override
  public ConfigAdmin.WorkflowStatus approveAndPublish(
      String configId, String layerId, String comment, String subject) {
    String requiredConfigId = required(configId, "configId");
    String requiredLayerId = required(layerId, "layerId");
    String normalizedComment = Strings.trimToNull(comment);
    String normalizedSubject = Strings.trimToNull(subject);
    workflow.approve(group, requiredConfigId, requiredLayerId, normalizedComment, normalizedSubject);
    workflow.publish(
        group,
        requiredConfigId,
        requiredLayerId,
        null,
        null,
        null,
        normalizedComment,
        normalizedSubject);
    return toWorkflowStatus(
        workflow.workflow(group, requiredConfigId, requiredLayerId, DEFAULT_AUDIT_LIMIT));
  }

  @Override
  public ConfigAdmin.WorkflowStatus reject(
      String configId, String layerId, String comment, String subject) {
    return toWorkflowStatus(
        workflow.reject(
            group,
            required(configId, "configId"),
            required(layerId, "layerId"),
            Strings.trimToNull(comment),
            Strings.trimToNull(subject)));
  }

  @Override
  public ConfigAdmin.WorkflowStatus cancel(
      String configId, String layerId, String comment, String subject) {
    return toWorkflowStatus(
        workflow.cancel(
            group,
            required(configId, "configId"),
            required(layerId, "layerId"),
            Strings.trimToNull(comment),
            Strings.trimToNull(subject)));
  }

  private ConfigAdmin.WorkflowStatus toWorkflowStatus(DefinitionConfigChange change) {
    if (change == null) {
      return null;
    }
    List<ConfigAdmin.AuditEvent> audits = new ArrayList<>();
    if (change.audit() != null) {
      for (DefinitionConfigChange.AuditEntry entry : change.audit()) {
        if (entry == null) {
          continue;
        }
        audits.add(
            new ConfigAdmin.AuditEvent(
                Strings.trimToNull(entry.timeUtc()),
                Strings.trimToNull(entry.subject()),
                toClientAction(entry.action()),
                Strings.trimToNull(entry.message()),
                Strings.trimToNull(entry.fromState()),
                Strings.trimToNull(entry.toState()),
                Strings.trimToNull(entry.targetConfigId())));
      }
    }
    return new ConfigAdmin.WorkflowStatus(
        Strings.trimToNull(change.group()),
        Strings.trimToNull(change.configId()),
        Strings.trimToNull(change.layerId()),
        Strings.trimToNull(change.schemaKey()),
        toClientState(change.state()),
        toClientMode(change.mode()),
        Strings.trimToNull(change.effectiveAtUtc()),
        Strings.trimToNull(change.expiresAtUtc()),
        Strings.trimToNull(change.baseConfigId()),
        Strings.trimToNull(change.baseEffectiveConfigId()),
        Strings.trimToNull(change.lastPublishedConfigId()),
        Strings.trimToNull(change.createdTimeUtc()),
        Strings.trimToNull(change.createdBySubject()),
        Strings.trimToNull(change.updatedTimeUtc()),
        Strings.trimToNull(change.updatedBySubject()),
        Strings.trimToNull(change.rationale()),
        Strings.trimToNull(change.decisionMessage()),
        audits.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(audits));
  }

  private ConfigAdmin.PublishedConfig toPublishedConfig(
      DefinitionConfigLayer published, String configId, String layerId) {
    if (published == null) {
      return null;
    }
    DefinitionEnvelope envelope = published.envelope();
    DefinitionConfigLayer payload = published;

    List<ConfigAdmin.EffectiveEntry> effectiveEntries = new ArrayList<>();
    List<DefinitionConfigLayer.Effective> effective = payload == null ? null : payload.effective();
    if (effective != null) {
      for (DefinitionConfigLayer.Effective entry : effective) {
        if (entry == null) {
          continue;
        }
        effectiveEntries.add(
            new ConfigAdmin.EffectiveEntry(
                Strings.trimToNull(entry.effectiveTimeUtc()),
                Strings.trimToNull(entry.expiresAtUtc()),
                deepCopy(entry.declared())));
      }
    }

    return new ConfigAdmin.PublishedConfig(
        resolveGroup(envelope, group),
        configId,
        layerId,
        Strings.trimToNull(payload == null ? null : payload.schemaKey()),
        Strings.trimToNull(published.configId()),
        Strings.trimToNull(published.effectiveConfigId()),
        Strings.trimToNull(envelope == null ? null : envelope.updatedTimeUtc()),
        Strings.trimToNull(envelope == null ? null : envelope.updatedBy()),
        deepCopy(payload == null ? null : payload.declared()),
        effectiveEntries.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(effectiveEntries));
  }

  private static String resolveGroup(
      DefinitionEnvelope envelope, String fallbackGroup) {
    String fromEnvelope = Strings.trimToNull(envelope == null ? null : envelope.group());
    return fromEnvelope == null ? Strings.trimToNull(fallbackGroup) : fromEnvelope;
  }

  private static JsonNode deepCopy(JsonNode value) {
    return value == null ? null : value.deepCopy();
  }

  private static ObjectNode requireObject(JsonNode value, String field) {
    if (value == null || !value.isObject()) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(field + " must be a JSON object");
    }
    return (ObjectNode) value;
  }

  private static String required(String value, String field) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(field + " is required");
    }
    return normalized;
  }

  private static boolean isPending(DefinitionConfigChange change) {
    if (change == null) {
      return false;
    }
    DefinitionConfigChange.ChangeState state = change.state();
    if (state == DefinitionConfigChange.ChangeState.DRAFT
        || state == DefinitionConfigChange.ChangeState.PROPOSED
        || state == DefinitionConfigChange.ChangeState.APPROVED) {
      return true;
    }
    if (change.mode() != DefinitionConfigChange.ChangeMode.SCHEDULED) {
      return false;
    }
    Instant effectiveAt = parseInstant(change.effectiveAtUtc());
    if (effectiveAt == null) {
      return false;
    }
    Instant now = Instant.now();
    Instant expiresAt = parseInstant(change.expiresAtUtc());
    if (expiresAt != null && !now.isBefore(expiresAt)) {
      return false;
    }
    return effectiveAt.isAfter(now);
  }

  private static Instant parseInstant(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return null;
    }
    try {
      return Instant.parse(normalized);
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      return null;
    }
  }

  private static DefinitionConfigChange.ChangeMode toInternalMode(ConfigAdmin.ChangeMode mode) {
    if (mode == null) {
      return null;
    }
    return switch (mode) {
      case IMMEDIATE -> DefinitionConfigChange.ChangeMode.IMMEDIATE;
      case SCHEDULED -> DefinitionConfigChange.ChangeMode.SCHEDULED;
    };
  }

  private static ConfigAdmin.ChangeMode toClientMode(DefinitionConfigChange.ChangeMode mode) {
    if (mode == null) {
      return ConfigAdmin.ChangeMode.IMMEDIATE;
    }
    return switch (mode) {
      case IMMEDIATE -> ConfigAdmin.ChangeMode.IMMEDIATE;
      case SCHEDULED -> ConfigAdmin.ChangeMode.SCHEDULED;
      case UNKNOWN ->
          throw new IllegalArgumentException("Unsupported config change mode UNKNOWN");
    };
  }

  private static ConfigAdmin.ChangeState toClientState(DefinitionConfigChange.ChangeState state) {
    if (state == null) {
      return ConfigAdmin.ChangeState.NONE;
    }
    return switch (state) {
      case NONE -> ConfigAdmin.ChangeState.NONE;
      case DRAFT -> ConfigAdmin.ChangeState.DRAFT;
      case PROPOSED -> ConfigAdmin.ChangeState.PROPOSED;
      case APPROVED -> ConfigAdmin.ChangeState.APPROVED;
      case REJECTED -> ConfigAdmin.ChangeState.REJECTED;
      case UNKNOWN ->
          throw new IllegalArgumentException("Unsupported config change state UNKNOWN");
    };
  }

  private static ConfigAdmin.DecisionAction toClientAction(
      DefinitionConfigChange.DecisionAction action) {
    if (action == null) {
      return null;
    }
    return switch (action) {
      case PROPOSE -> ConfigAdmin.DecisionAction.PROPOSE;
      case APPROVE -> ConfigAdmin.DecisionAction.APPROVE;
      case REJECT -> ConfigAdmin.DecisionAction.REJECT;
      case CANCEL -> ConfigAdmin.DecisionAction.CANCEL;
      case PUBLISH -> ConfigAdmin.DecisionAction.PUBLISH;
      case UNKNOWN ->
          throw new IllegalArgumentException("Unsupported config decision action UNKNOWN");
    };
  }
}

import com.fasterxml.jackson.annotation.JsonCreator;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.annotation.JsonValue;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public enum ConfigEventType {
  CONFIG_RESOLVED,
  CONFIG_SUBSCRIBED,
  CONFIG_UPDATE_CALLBACK,
  CONFIG_UNSUBSCRIBED,
  CONFIG_GENERATED;

  @JsonCreator
  public static ConfigEventType fromJson(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return null;
    }
    try {
      return ConfigEventType.valueOf(normalized.toUpperCase());
    } catch (IllegalArgumentException ex) {
      return null;
    }
  }

  @JsonValue
  public String toJson() {
    return name();
  }
}

FILE: ConfigPublisherAmp.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.configs.audit;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.concurrent.ExecutorService;
import java.util.concurrent.Executors;
import java.util.concurrent.RejectedExecutionException;
import java.util.concurrent.TimeUnit;
import java.util.concurrent.atomic.AtomicInteger;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.ControlConnection;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.cache.DiscoveryTopics;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.codec.DiscoveryCodec;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

public final class ConfigPublisherAmp implements ConfigPublisher {
  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(ConfigPublisherAmp.class);
  private static final AtomicInteger THREAD_ID = new AtomicInteger(0);
  private static final ObjectMapper MAPPER = DiscoveryCodec.mapper();

  private final ControlConnection controlConnection;
  private final Settings settings;
  private final ExecutorService publishExecutor;

  public ConfigPublisherAmp(ControlConnection controlConnection) {
    this(controlConnection, Settings.defaults());
  }

  public ConfigPublisherAmp(ControlConnection controlConnection, String topic) {
    this(controlConnection, new Settings("amps-fabric-discovery", topic, 3, 100L, 2_000L, 2.0d));
  }

  public ConfigPublisherAmp(ControlConnection controlConnection, Settings settings) {
    this.controlConnection = Objects.requireNonNull(controlConnection, "controlConnection");
    this.settings = settings == null ? Settings.defaults() : settings.normalized();
    this.publishExecutor =
        Executors.newSingleThreadExecutor(
            runnable -> {
              Thread thread =
                  new Thread(
                      runnable,
                      "config-usage-audit-" + THREAD_ID.incrementAndGet());
              thread.setDaemon(true);
              return thread;
            });
  }

  @Override
  public void publish(ConfigEvent event) {
    if (event == null) {
        return;
    }
    try {
      publishExecutor.execute(
          () -> {
            String payload;
            try {
              payload = MAPPER.writeValueAsString(event);
            } catch (Exception ex) {
              LOGGER.warn("[ConfigUsageAudit][AMPS] encode failed topic={} eventType={} message={}", settings.topic(), event.envelope() == null ? null : event.envelope().eventType(), ex.toString());
              return;
            }
            long backoff = settings.initialBackoffMillis();
            for (int attempt = 0; ; attempt++) {
              try {
                controlConnection.amps().publish(settings.topic(), payload);
                return;
              } catch (Exception ex) {
                if (attempt >= settings.maxRetries()) {
                  LOGGER.warn("[ConfigUsageAudit][AMPS] publish failed topic={} eventType={} retries={} message={}", settings.topic(), event.envelope() == null ? null : event.envelope().eventType(), settings.maxRetries(), ex.toString());
                  return;
                }
                LOGGER.warn("[ConfigUsageAudit][AMPS] publish retry topic={} eventType={} attempt={} backoffMs={} message={}", settings.topic(), event.envelope() == null ? null : event.envelope().eventType(), attempt + 1, backoff, ex.toString());
                sleep(backoff);
                backoff = nextBackoff(backoff, settings.maxBackoffMillis(), settings.backoffMultiplier());
              }
            }
          });
    } catch (RejectedExecutionException ex) {
      LOGGER.debug("[ConfigUsageAudit][AMPS] publish skipped topic={} reason=executor-closed message={}", settings.topic(), ex.toString());
    }
  }

  @Override
  public void close() {
    publishExecutor.shutdown();
    try {
      publishExecutor.awaitTermination(500L, TimeUnit.MILLISECONDS);
    } catch (InterruptedException ex) {
      Thread.currentThread().interrupt();
    } finally {
      publishExecutor.shutdownNow();
    }
  }

  private static long nextBackoff(long current, long maxBackoffMillis, double multiplier) {
    long scaled = Math.max(1L, (long) Math.ceil(current * multiplier));
    return Math.min(maxBackoffMillis, scaled);
  }

  private static void sleep(long millis) {
    try {
      Thread.sleep(Math.max(0L, millis));
    } catch (InterruptedException ex) {
      Thread.currentThread().interrupt();
    }
  }

  public record Settings(
      String connection,
      String topic,
      int maxRetries,
      long initialBackoffMillis,
      long maxBackoffMillis,
      double backoffMultiplier) {

    public Settings normalized() {
      String normalizedConnection = Strings.firstNonBlank(connection, "amps-fabric-discovery");
      String normalizedTopic = Strings.firstNonBlank(topic, DiscoveryTopics.EVENTS_CONFIG);
      int normalizedRetries = Math.max(0, maxRetries);
      long normalizedInitial = Math.max(1L, initialBackoffMillis);
      long normalizedMax = Math.max(normalizedInitial, maxBackoffMillis);
      double normalizedMultiplier = backoffMultiplier <= 1.0d ? 2.0d : backoffMultiplier;
      return new Settings(
          normalizedConnection,
          normalizedTopic,
          normalizedRetries,
          normalizedInitial,
          normalizedMax,
          normalizedMultiplier);
    }

    public static Settings defaults() {
      return new Settings("amps-fabric-discovery", DiscoveryTopics.EVENTS_CONFIG, 3, 100L, 2_000L, 2.0d);
    }
  }
}

FILE: ConfigPresentation.java

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.configs.presentation;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonNode;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.node.NullNode;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.node.ObjectNode;
import java.time.Instant;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.codec.DiscoveryCodec;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionConfigLayer;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class ConfigPresentation {

  private static final String UNGROUPED = "__ungrouped__";
  private static final List<String> FABRIC_KEYS =
      List.of(
          "group",
          "configName",
          "layerId",
          "schemaKey",
          "resolvedAtUtc",
          "effectiveAtUtc",
          "expiresAtUtc",
          "configId",
          "effectiveConfigId");

  private ConfigPresentation() {}

  public static ObjectNode grouped(
      ConfigSchemaDoc schema,
      JsonNode values,
      FabricMetadata fabricMetadata,
      Options options) {
    return grouped(schema, valuesByKey(values), fabricMetadata, options);
  }

  public static ObjectNode grouped(
      JsonNode schema,
      JsonNode values,
      FabricMetadata fabricMetadata,
      Options options) {
    return grouped(parseSchema(schema), valuesByKey(values), fabricMetadata, options);
  }

  public static ObjectNode grouped(
      ConfigSchemaDoc schema,
      Map<String, JsonNode> valuesByKey,
      FabricMetadata fabricMetadata,
      Options options) {
    Options resolvedOptions = options == null ? Options.defaults() : options;
    FabricMetadata resolvedFabric = normalizeFabric(fabricMetadata);
    ObjectNode root = DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode();
    root.set("fabric", toFabricNode(resolvedFabric));
    root.set(
        "config",
        toGroupedConfigNode(
            schema == null ? emptySchema() : schema,
            valuesByKey == null ? Map.of() : valuesByKey,
            resolvedOptions.includeAllFields()));
    return root;
  }

  public static ObjectNode flat(
      ConfigSchemaDoc schema,
      JsonNode values,
      FabricMetadata fabricMetadata,
      Options options) {
    return flat(schema, valuesByKey(values), fabricMetadata, options);
  }

  public static ObjectNode flat(
      JsonNode schema,
      JsonNode values,
      FabricMetadata fabricMetadata,
      Options options) {
    return flat(parseSchema(schema), valuesByKey(values), fabricMetadata, options);
  }

  public static ObjectNode flat(
      ConfigSchemaDoc schema,
      Map<String, JsonNode> valuesByKey,
      FabricMetadata fabricMetadata,
      Options options) {
    Options resolvedOptions = options == null ? Options.defaults() : options;
    FabricMetadata resolvedFabric = normalizeFabric(fabricMetadata);
    ObjectNode root = DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode();
    ObjectNode fabricNode = toFabricNode(resolvedFabric);
    for (String key : FABRIC_KEYS) {
      root.set("fabric." + key, deepCopyOrNull(fabricNode.get(key)));
    }
    for (FieldSpec field :
        orderedFields(schema == null ? emptySchema() : schema)) {
      JsonNode value = readValue(valuesByKey == null ? Map.of() : valuesByKey, field.key());
      if (!resolvedOptions.includeAllFields()) {
        if (value == null || value.isNull()) {
          continue;
        }
      }
      root.set(field.groupId() + "." + field.key(), value == null ? NullNode.getInstance() : value.deepCopy());
    }
    return root;
  }

  public static Map<String, JsonNode> valuesByKey(JsonNode values) {
    if (values == null || !values.isObject()) {
      return Map.of();
    }
    Map<String, JsonNode> out = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    values
        .fields()
        .forEachRemaining(
            entry -> {
              String key = Strings.trimToNull(entry.getKey());
              if (key == null) {
                return;
              }
              out.put(key, deepCopyOrNull(entry.getValue()));
            });
    return Map.copyOf(out);
  }

  public static FabricMetadata fabricMetadata(
      String group,
      String configName,
      String layerId,
      String schemaKey,
      Instant resolvedAtUtc,
      Instant effectiveAtUtc,
      List<DefinitionConfigLayer.Effective> effective,
      String configId,
      String effectiveConfigId) {
    Instant asOf = effectiveAtUtc == null ? resolvedAtUtc : effectiveAtUtc;
    String expiresAtUtc = activeExpiryUtc(effective, asOf);
    return new FabricMetadata(
        Strings.trimToNull(group),
        Strings.trimToNull(configName),
        Strings.trimToNull(layerId),
        Strings.trimToNull(schemaKey),
        toUtcText(resolvedAtUtc),
        toUtcText(effectiveAtUtc),
        expiresAtUtc,
        Strings.trimToNull(configId),
        Strings.trimToNull(effectiveConfigId));
  }

  public static String activeExpiryUtc(List<DefinitionConfigLayer.Effective> effective, Instant asOfUtc) {
    if (effective == null || effective.isEmpty() || asOfUtc == null) {
      return null;
    }
    Instant winnerEffectiveAt = null;
    String winnerExpiresAtUtc = null;
    for (DefinitionConfigLayer.Effective row : effective) {
      if (row == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String effectiveUtc = Strings.trimToNull(row.effectiveTimeUtc());
      if (effectiveUtc == null) {
        continue;
      }
      Instant effectiveAt;
      try {
        effectiveAt = Instant.parse(effectiveUtc);
      } catch (Exception ignore) {
        continue;
      }
      if (effectiveAt.isAfter(asOfUtc)) {
        continue;
      }
      Instant expiresAt = null;
      String expiresAtUtc = Strings.trimToNull(row.expiresAtUtc());
      if (expiresAtUtc != null) {
        try {
          expiresAt = Instant.parse(expiresAtUtc);
        } catch (Exception ignore) {
          continue;
        }
        if (!expiresAt.isAfter(effectiveAt) || !asOfUtc.isBefore(expiresAt)) {
          continue;
        }
      }
      if (winnerEffectiveAt == null || effectiveAt.isAfter(winnerEffectiveAt)) {
        winnerEffectiveAt = effectiveAt;
        winnerExpiresAtUtc = expiresAtUtc;
      }
    }
    return winnerExpiresAtUtc;
  }

  private static ObjectNode toGroupedConfigNode(
      ConfigSchemaDoc schema, Map<String, JsonNode> valuesByKey, boolean includeAllFields) {
    ObjectNode configNode = DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode();
    Map<String, ObjectNode> groupNodes = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (FieldSpec field : orderedFields(schema)) {
      JsonNode value = readValue(valuesByKey, field.key());
      if (!includeAllFields && (value == null || value.isNull())) {
        continue;
      }
      ObjectNode groupNode =
          groupNodes.computeIfAbsent(field.groupId(), ignored -> DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode());
      groupNode.set(field.key(), value == null ? NullNode.getInstance() : value.deepCopy());
    }
    for (Map.Entry<String, ObjectNode> entry : groupNodes.entrySet()) {
      configNode.set(entry.getKey(), entry.getValue());
    }
    return configNode;
  }

  private static ObjectNode toFabricNode(FabricMetadata metadata) {
    ObjectNode node = DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode();
    for (String key : FABRIC_KEYS) {
      node.set(key, toTextOrNull(metadataValue(metadata, key)));
    }
    return node;
  }

  private static String metadataValue(FabricMetadata metadata, String key) {
    return switch (key) {
      case "group" -> metadata.group();
      case "configName" -> metadata.configName();
      case "configId" -> metadata.configId();
      case "layerId" -> metadata.layerId();
      case "schemaKey" -> metadata.schemaKey();
      case "resolvedAtUtc" -> metadata.resolvedAtUtc();
      case "effectiveAtUtc" -> metadata.effectiveAtUtc();
      case "expiresAtUtc" -> metadata.expiresAtUtc();
      case "effectiveConfigId" -> metadata.effectiveConfigId();
      default -> null;
    };
  }

  private static ConfigSchemaDoc parseSchema(JsonNode schema) {
    if (schema == null || schema.isNull()) {
      return emptySchema();
    }
    return ConfigSchemaCodec.parse(schema);
  }

  private static ConfigSchemaDoc emptySchema() {
    return new ConfigSchemaDoc(null, null, List.of(), List.of(), List.of(), List.of());
  }

  private static List<FieldSpec> orderedFields(ConfigSchemaDoc schema) {
    List<ConfigSchemaDoc.Group> groups = safeGroups(schema.groups());
    Map<String, Integer> groupOrderById = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (ConfigSchemaDoc.Group group : groups) {
      if (group == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String id = Strings.trimToNull(group.id());
      if (id == null) {
        continue;
      }
      groupOrderById.put(id, group.order() == null ? Integer.MAX_VALUE : group.order());
    }
    List<FieldSpec> fields = new ArrayList<>();
    for (ConfigSchemaDoc.Field field : safeFields(schema.fields())) {
      if (field == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String key = Strings.trimToNull(field.key());
      if (key == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String groupId = Strings.trimToNull(field.groupId());
      String normalizedGroupId = groupId == null ? UNGROUPED : groupId;
      int groupOrder = groupOrderById.getOrDefault(normalizedGroupId, Integer.MAX_VALUE);
      int fieldOrder = field.order() == null ? Integer.MAX_VALUE : field.order();
      fields.add(new FieldSpec(normalizedGroupId, key, groupOrder, fieldOrder));
    }
    fields.sort(
        Comparator.comparingInt(FieldSpec::groupOrder)
            .thenComparing(FieldSpec::groupId)
            .thenComparingInt(FieldSpec::fieldOrder)
            .thenComparing(FieldSpec::key));
    return List.copyOf(fields);
  }

  private static List<ConfigSchemaDoc.Group> safeGroups(List<ConfigSchemaDoc.Group> values) {
    return values == null ? List.of() : values;
  }

  private static List<ConfigSchemaDoc.Field> safeFields(List<ConfigSchemaDoc.Field> values) {
    return values == null ? List.of() : values;
  }

  private static JsonNode readValue(Map<String, JsonNode> valuesByKey, String key) {
    if (valuesByKey == null || valuesByKey.isEmpty()) {
      return null;
    }
    JsonNode value = valuesByKey.get(key);
    return deepCopyOrNull(value);
  }

  private static JsonNode deepCopyOrNull(JsonNode value) {
    return value == null ? null : value.deepCopy();
  }

  private static JsonNode toTextOrNull(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return NullNode.getInstance();
    }
    return DiscoveryCodec.mapper().getNodeFactory().textNode(normalized);
  }

  private static String toUtcText(Instant instant) {
    return instant == null ? null : instant.toString();
  }

  private static FabricMetadata normalizeFabric(FabricMetadata value) {
    return value == null ? new FabricMetadata(null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null) : value;
  }

  public record Options(boolean includeAllFields) {
    public static Options defaults() {
      return new Options(false);
    }
  }

  public record FabricMetadata(
      String group,
      String configName,
      String layerId,
      String schemaKey,
      String resolvedAtUtc,
      String effectiveAtUtc,
      String expiresAtUtc,
      String configId,
      String effectiveConfigId) {}

  private record FieldSpec(String groupId, String key, int groupOrder, int fieldOrder) {}
}

FILE: ConfigHistoryUtil.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.configs.workflow;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonNode;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.node.ArrayNode;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.node.DecimalNode;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.node.JsonNodeFactory;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.node.NullNode;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.node.ObjectNode;
import java.math.BigDecimal;
import java.time.Instant;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.TreeSet;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionEnvelope;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionConfigLayer;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class ConfigHistoryUtil {

  public static final int DEFAULT_HISTORY_LIMIT = 50;

  private ConfigHistoryUtil() {}

  public static DefinitionConfigLayer.History snapshotFromCurrent(
      DefinitionConfigLayer definition, String mode, Instant effectiveAt, String updatedBy) {
    if (definition == null) {
      return null;
    }
    DefinitionConfigLayer payload = definition;
    DefinitionEnvelope envelope = definition.envelope();
    String resolvedUpdatedBy = Strings.trimToNull(updatedBy);
    if (resolvedUpdatedBy == null && envelope != null) {
      resolvedUpdatedBy = Strings.trimToNull(envelope.updatedBy());
    }
    if (resolvedUpdatedBy == null) {
      resolvedUpdatedBy = "unknown";
    }
    String updatedTimeUtc =
        Strings.trimToNull(envelope == null ? null : envelope.updatedTimeUtc());
    if (updatedTimeUtc == null) {
      updatedTimeUtc = Instant.now().toString();
    }
    return new DefinitionConfigLayer.History(
        Strings.trimToNull(definition.configId()),
        updatedTimeUtc,
        resolvedUpdatedBy,
        Strings.trimToNull(mode),
        effectiveAt == null ? null : effectiveAt.toString(),
        deepCopy(payload.declared()),
        copyEffective(payload.effective()));
  }

  public static JsonNode normalizeForCompare(JsonNode node) {
    if (node == null || node.isMissingNode()) {
      return NullNode.instance;
    }
    if (node.isNull()) {
      return NullNode.instance;
    }
    if (node.isObject()) {
      ObjectNode normalized = JsonNodeFactory.instance.objectNode();
      TreeSet<String> names = new TreeSet<>();
      node.fieldNames().forEachRemaining(names::add);
      for (String fieldName : names) {
        normalized.set(fieldName, normalizeForCompare(node.get(fieldName)));
      }
      return normalized;
    }
    if (node.isArray()) {
      ArrayNode normalized = JsonNodeFactory.instance.arrayNode();
      for (JsonNode element : node) {
        normalized.add(normalizeForCompare(element));
      }
      return normalized;
    }
    if (node.isNumber()) {
      BigDecimal decimal = node.decimalValue();
      return DecimalNode.valueOf(decimal.stripTrailingZeros());
    }
    return node.deepCopy();
  }

  public static boolean isSamePayload(
      JsonNode declaredA,
      List<DefinitionConfigLayer.Effective> effectiveA,
      JsonNode declaredB,
      List<DefinitionConfigLayer.Effective> effectiveB) {
    JsonNode leftDeclared = normalizeForCompare(declaredA);
    JsonNode rightDeclared = normalizeForCompare(declaredB);
    if (!Objects.equals(leftDeclared, rightDeclared)) {
      return false;
    }
    return Objects.equals(normalizeEffective(effectiveA), normalizeEffective(effectiveB));
  }

  public static List<DefinitionConfigLayer.History> trimHistory(
      List<DefinitionConfigLayer.History> history, int max) {
    if (history == null || history.isEmpty() || max <= 0) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<DefinitionConfigLayer.History> trimmed = new ArrayList<>(Math.min(history.size(), max));
    for (DefinitionConfigLayer.History entry : history) {
      if (entry == null) {
        continue;
      }
      trimmed.add(copyHistory(entry));
      if (trimmed.size() >= max) {
        break;
      }
    }
    return List.copyOf(trimmed);
  }

  public static List<DefinitionConfigLayer.History> appendSnapshot(
      List<DefinitionConfigLayer.History> existing,
      DefinitionConfigLayer.History snapshot,
      int max) {
    if (snapshot == null || max <= 0) {
      return trimHistory(existing, max);
    }
    List<DefinitionConfigLayer.History> rewritten = new ArrayList<>();
    DefinitionConfigLayer.History latest =
        existing == null || existing.isEmpty() ? null : existing.getFirst();
    if (latest == null
        || !isSamePayload(
            latest.declared(), latest.effective(), snapshot.declared(), snapshot.effective())) {
      rewritten.add(copyHistory(snapshot));
    }
    if (existing != null) {
      for (DefinitionConfigLayer.History entry : existing) {
        if (entry == null) {
          continue;
        }
        rewritten.add(copyHistory(entry));
        if (rewritten.size() >= max) {
          break;
        }
      }
    }
    return trimHistory(rewritten, max);
  }

  public static List<DefinitionConfigLayer.Effective> copyEffective(List<DefinitionConfigLayer.Effective> values) {
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<DefinitionConfigLayer.Effective> copied = new ArrayList<>(values.size());
    for (DefinitionConfigLayer.Effective value : values) {
      if (value == null) {
        continue;
      }
      copied.add(
          new DefinitionConfigLayer.Effective(
              value.effectiveTimeUtc(), value.expiresAtUtc(), deepCopy(value.declared())));
    }
    return List.copyOf(copied);
  }

  private static DefinitionConfigLayer.History copyHistory(
      DefinitionConfigLayer.History history) {
    return new DefinitionConfigLayer.History(
        history.configId(),
        history.updatedTimeUtc(),
        history.updatedBy(),
        history.mode(),
        history.effectiveAtUtc(),
        deepCopy(history.declared()),
        copyEffective(history.effective()));
  }

  private static ArrayNode normalizeEffective(List<DefinitionConfigLayer.Effective> entries) {
    ArrayNode normalized = JsonNodeFactory.instance.arrayNode();
    if (entries == null || entries.isEmpty()) {
      return normalized;
    }
    List<DefinitionConfigLayer.Effective> sorted = new ArrayList<>();
    for (DefinitionConfigLayer.Effective entry : entries) {
      if (entry != null) {
        sorted.add(entry);
      }
    }
    sorted.sort(
        Comparator.comparing(
            value -> Strings.trimToNull(value.effectiveTimeUtc()), Comparator.nullsFirst(String::compareTo)));
    for (DefinitionConfigLayer.Effective entry : sorted) {
      ObjectNode row = JsonNodeFactory.instance.objectNode();
      row.put("effectiveTimeUtc", Strings.trimToNull(entry.effectiveTimeUtc()));
      row.put("expiresAtUtc", Strings.trimToNull(entry.expiresAtUtc()));
      row.set("declared", normalizeForCompare(entry.declared()));
      normalized.add(row);
    }
    return normalized;
  }

  private static JsonNode deepCopy(JsonNode value) {
    return value == null ? null : value.deepCopy();
  }
}






FILE: ConfigJsonDiff.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.configs.workflow;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonNode;
import java.math.BigDecimal;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Set;
import java.util.TreeSet;

public final class ConfigJsonDiff {

  private ConfigJsonDiff() {}

  public enum Change {
    ADDED,
    REMOVED,
    MODIFIED
  }

  public record DiffRow(String path, Change change, JsonNode oldValue, JsonNode newValue) {}

  public static List<DiffRow> diff(JsonNode oldPayload, JsonNode newPayload) {
    Map<String, JsonNode> oldFlat = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    Map<String, JsonNode> newFlat = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    flatten(oldPayload, "", oldFlat);
    flatten(newPayload, "", newFlat);

    Set<String> paths = new TreeSet<>();
    paths.addAll(oldFlat.keySet());
    paths.addAll(newFlat.keySet());

    List<DiffRow> rows = new ArrayList<>();
    for (String path : paths) {
      boolean hasOld = oldFlat.containsKey(path);
      boolean hasNew = newFlat.containsKey(path);
      JsonNode oldValue = oldFlat.get(path);
      JsonNode newValue = newFlat.get(path);
      if (!hasOld && hasNew) {
        rows.add(new DiffRow(path, Change.ADDED, null, newValue));
      } else if (hasOld && !hasNew) {
        rows.add(new DiffRow(path, Change.REMOVED, oldValue, null));
      } else if (hasOld && hasNew && !jsonEquals(oldValue, newValue)) {
        rows.add(new DiffRow(path, Change.MODIFIED, oldValue, newValue));
      }
    }
    return List.copyOf(rows);
  }

  public static boolean jsonEquals(JsonNode left, JsonNode right) {
    if (left == right) {
      return true;
    }
    if (left == null || right == null) {
      return false;
    }
    if (left.isNumber() && right.isNumber()) {
      BigDecimal leftValue = left.decimalValue();
      BigDecimal rightValue = right.decimalValue();
      return leftValue.compareTo(rightValue) == 0;
    }
    return left.equals(right);
  }

  public static String formatJsonScalar(JsonNode value) {
    if (value == null || value.isNull() || value.isMissingNode()) {
      return "null";
    }
    if (value.isTextual()) {
      return value.asText();
    }
    if (value.isBoolean()) {
      return Boolean.toString(value.booleanValue());
    }
    if (value.isNumber()) {
      if (value.isIntegralNumber()) {
        return value.bigIntegerValue().toString();
      }
      BigDecimal normalized = value.decimalValue().stripTrailingZeros();
      return normalized.toPlainString();
    }
    return value.toString();
  }

  private static void flatten(JsonNode node, String path, Map<String, JsonNode> output) {
    if (node == null || node.isMissingNode() || node.isNull()) {
      output.put(pathOrRoot(path), node);
      return;
    }
    if (node.isObject()) {
      if (!node.fields().hasNext()) {
        output.put(pathOrRoot(path), node);
        return;
      }
      node.fields()
          .forEachRemaining(
              entry -> flatten(entry.getValue(), appendPath(path, entry.getKey()), output));
      return;
    }
    if (node.isArray()) {
      if (node.isEmpty()) {
        output.put(pathOrRoot(path), node);
        return;
      }
      for (int i = 0; i < node.size(); i++) {
        flatten(node.get(i), appendArrayPath(path, i), output);
      }
      return;
    }
    output.put(pathOrRoot(path), node);
  }

  private static String pathOrRoot(String path) {
    return path == null || path.isEmpty() ? "<root>" : path;
  }

  private static String appendPath(String path, String field) {
    if (path == null || path.isEmpty()) {
      return field;
    }
    return path + "." + field;
  }

  private static String appendArrayPath(String path, int index) {
    return (path == null ? "" : path) + "[" + index + "]";
  }
}

FILE: ConfigSchemaRequiredKeys.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.configs.workflow;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonNode;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Set;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.codec.DiscoveryCodec;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionSchema;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class ConfigSchemaRequiredKeys {

  private ConfigSchemaRequiredKeys() {}

  public static List<String> explicitRequiredKeys(DefinitionSchema schema) {
    String schemaText = Strings.trimToNull(schema == null ? null : schema.schema());
    if (schemaText == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("schema text is required");
    }
    try {
      JsonNode root = DiscoveryCodec.mapper().readTree(schemaText);
      return explicitRequiredKeys(root);
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("invalid config schema json", ex);
    }
  }

  public static List<String> explicitRequiredKeys(JsonNode schema) {
    if (schema == null) {
      return List.of();
    }
    JsonNode required = schema.get("requiredKeys");
    if (required == null || !required.isArray()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<String> keys = new ArrayList<>();
    for (JsonNode node : required) {
      if (node == null || !node.isTextual()) {
        continue;
      }
      String key = Strings.trimToNull(node.asText());
      if (key != null) {
        keys.add(key);
      }
    }
    return List.copyOf(keys);
  }

  public static List<String> mergedRequiredKeys(JsonNode schema) {
    if (schema == null) {
      return List.of();
    }
    Set<String> keys = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    for (String key : explicitRequiredKeys(schema)) {
      if (key != null && !key.isBlank()) {
        keys.add(key.trim());
      }
    }
    JsonNode fields = schema.get("fields");
    if (fields != null && fields.isArray()) {
      for (JsonNode fieldNode : fields) {
        if (fieldNode == null || !fieldNode.isObject()) {
          continue;
        }
        JsonNode keyNode = fieldNode.get("key");
        JsonNode requiredNode = fieldNode.get("required");
        if (keyNode != null
            && keyNode.isTextual()
            && requiredNode != null
            && requiredNode.isBoolean()
            && requiredNode.booleanValue()) {
          String key = Strings.trimToNull(keyNode.asText());
          if (key != null) {
            keys.add(key);
          }
        }
      }
    }
    return List.copyOf(keys);
  }

  public static List<String> missingRequiredKeys(List<String> requiredKeys, JsonNode payload) {
    if (requiredKeys == null || requiredKeys.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    if (payload == null || !payload.isObject()) {
      return List.copyOf(requiredKeys);
    }
    List<String> missing = new ArrayList<>();
    for (String key : requiredKeys) {
      if (key == null || key.isBlank()) {
        continue;
      }
      if (!payload.has(key)) {
        missing.add(key);
      }
    }
    return List.copyOf(missing);
  }
}

FILE: AmpsFactoryClient.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.connectors.amps.factory;

import com.crankuptheamps.client.ExponentialDelayStrategy;
import com.crankuptheamps.client.HAClient;
import java.net.URI;
import java.time.Duration;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Arrays;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

public final class AmpsFactoryClient {

  private static final String DEFAULT_HOSTPORT_PATH = "/amps";
  private static final String KERBEROS_MECHANISM = "GSSAPI";
  private static final String KERBEROS_SERVICE_NAME = "AMPS";

  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(AmpsFactoryClient.class);

  private AmpsFactoryClient() {}

  public static HAClient create(String clientName, AmpsFactoryOptions options) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(clientName, "clientName");
    return new HAClient(clientName);
  }

  public static void connect(HAClient client, Iterable<String> endpoints, AmpsFactoryOptions options) throws Exception {
    Objects.requireNonNull(client, "client");
    Objects.requireNonNull(endpoints, "endpoints");
    AmpsFactoryOptions effective = AmpsFactoryOptions.merge(options);
    AmpsFactoryOptions.Kerberos kerberos = effective.kerberos();
    if (kerberos.enabled()) {
      AmpsFactoryKerberos.ensureRuntimeContext(kerberos);
      kerberos.mechanism(KERBEROS_MECHANISM);
      kerberos.service(KERBEROS_SERVICE_NAME);
    }

    applyConnectionSettings(client, effective);
    List<String> trimmed = trimEndpoints(endpoints);
    if (trimmed.isEmpty()) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("endpoints must contain at least one non-blank value");
    }

    List<String> normalized = normalizeEndpoints(trimmed, DEFAULT_HOSTPORT_PATH);
    List<String> effectiveEndpoints = sanitizeEndpoints(normalized);
    List<String> connectEndpoints = effectiveEndpoints;
    if (kerberos.enabled()) {
      String shortUser = AmpsFactoryKerberos.shortUser(kerberos.getPrincipal());
      connectEndpoints = applyKerberosUserInfo(effectiveEndpoints, shortUser);
    }
    if (kerberos.enabled() && LOGGER.isDebugEnabled()) {
      String saslHost = AmpsFactoryKerberos.resolveSaslHost(kerberos, effectiveEndpoints);
      LOGGER.debug("[AMPS] Kerberos config principal={} keytab={} mechanism={} service={} host={} endpoints={}", kerberos.getPrincipal(), AmpsFactoryKerberos.keytabBasename(kerberos.getKeytab()), kerberos.mechanism(), kerberos.service(), saslHost, connectEndpoints);
    }
    validateUris(connectEndpoints);
    AmpsFactoryServerChooser.ConfigurableServerChooser chooser =
        AmpsFactoryServerChooser.ensureServerChooser(client);
    AmpsFactoryServerChooser.AuthenticatorFactory factory =
        AmpsFactoryServerChooser.authenticatorFactory(kerberos);
    chooser.setEndpoints(connectEndpoints, factory);

    if (kerberos.enabled()) {
      client.setLogonOptions(kerberos.logonOptions());
    } else {
      client.setLogonOptions(null);
    }
    client.connect();
  }

  public static void logon(HAClient client, AmpsFactoryOptions options) throws Exception {
    Objects.requireNonNull(client, "client");
    AmpsFactoryOptions effective = AmpsFactoryOptions.merge(options);
    if (effective.kerberos().enabled()) {
      AmpsFactoryKerberos.ensureRuntimeContext(effective.kerberos());
    }
    // HAClient performs logon during connect().
  }

  static void applyConnectionSettings(HAClient client, AmpsFactoryOptions options) {
    AmpsFactoryOptions.Connection connection = options.connection();
    int timeoutMillis = positiveMillis(connection.connectTimeout(), 5000);
    if (timeoutMillis > 0) {
      client.setTimeout(timeoutMillis);
    }
    ExponentialDelayStrategy strategy =
        new ExponentialDelayStrategy()
            .setInitialDelay(positiveMillis(connection.initialDelay(), 200))
            .setMaximumDelay(positiveMillis(connection.maximumDelay(), 2000))
            .setBackoffExponent(connection.backoffExponent())
            .setMaximumRetryTime(positiveMillis(connection.maximumRetryTime(), 15000))
            .setJitter(connection.jitter());
    client.setReconnectDelayStrategy(strategy);
  }

  public static List<String> normalizeEndpoints(Iterable<String> endpoints, String defaultPath) {
    List<String> normalized = new ArrayList<>();
    for (String endpoint : trimEndpoints(endpoints)) {
      if (!endpoint.contains("://")) {
        String[] parts = endpoint.split(":");
        if (parts.length != 2 || parts[0].isBlank() || parts[1].isBlank()) {
          throw new IllegalArgumentException("AMPS endpoint '" + endpoint + "' must include host:port");
        }
        try {
          Integer.parseInt(parts[1]);
        } catch (NumberFormatException ex) {
          throw new IllegalArgumentException("AMPS endpoint '" + endpoint + "' has an invalid port", ex);
        }
        String normalizedPath =
            Strings.isBlank(defaultPath)
                ? "/amps"
                : defaultPath.startsWith("/") ? defaultPath : "/" + defaultPath;
        normalized.add("tcp://" + parts[0] + ":" + parts[1] + normalizedPath);
      } else {
        normalized.add(endpoint);
      }
    }
    return normalized;
  }

  static void validateUris(List<String> uris) {
    for (String uri : uris) {
      try {
        if (!uri.contains("://")) {
          String[] parts = uri.split(":");
          if (parts.length != 2 || parts[0].isBlank() || parts[1].isBlank()) {
            throw new IllegalArgumentException("AMPS endpoint '" + uri + "' must include host:port");
          }
          continue;
        }
        URI parsed = URI.create(uri);
        String path = parsed.getPath();
        if (Strings.isBlank(path)) {
          throw new IllegalArgumentException("AMPS endpoint '" + uri + "' is missing a path segment");
        }
      } catch (IllegalArgumentException ex) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("Invalid AMPS endpoint URI: " + uri, ex);
      }
    }
  }

  static List<String> sanitizeEndpoints(List<String> endpoints) {
    if (Strings.isEmpty(endpoints)) {
      return endpoints;
    }
    List<String> sanitized = new ArrayList<>(endpoints.size());
    for (String endpoint : endpoints) {
      sanitized.add(stripUserInfo(endpoint));
    }
    return sanitized;
  }

  static List<String> applyKerberosUserInfo(List<String> endpoints, String user) {
    if (Strings.isEmpty(endpoints) || Strings.isBlank(user)) {
      return endpoints;
    }
    List<String> updated = new ArrayList<>(endpoints.size());
    for (String endpoint : endpoints) {
      updated.add(injectUserInfo(endpoint, user));
    }
    return updated;
  }

  static String injectUserInfo(String endpoint, String user) {
    if (Strings.isBlank(endpoint) || Strings.isBlank(user)) {
      return endpoint;
    }
    try {
      URI uri = URI.create(endpoint);
      if (Strings.isNotBlank(uri.getUserInfo())) {
        return endpoint;
      }
      String scheme = uri.getScheme();
      if (scheme == null) {
        return endpoint;
      }
      String host = uri.getHost();
      int port = uri.getPort();
      String path = uri.getPath();
      String query = uri.getQuery();
      String fragment = uri.getFragment();
      if (host != null) {
        return new URI(scheme, user, host, port, path, query, fragment).toString();
      }
      String marker = scheme + "://";
      int idx = endpoint.indexOf(marker);
      if (idx >= 0) {
        int start = idx + marker.length();
        return endpoint.substring(0, start) + user + "@" + endpoint.substring(start);
      }
      return endpoint;
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      return endpoint;
    }
  }

  static String stripUserInfo(String endpoint) {
    if (Strings.isBlank(endpoint)) {
      return endpoint;
    }
    int schemeIdx = endpoint.indexOf("://");
    if (schemeIdx < 0) {
      return endpoint;
    }
    int start = schemeIdx + 3;
    int end = endpoint.indexOf('/', start);
    if (end < 0) {
      end = endpoint.length();
    }
    int at = endpoint.lastIndexOf('@', end - 1);
    if (at < start) {
      return endpoint;
    }
    return endpoint.substring(0, start) + endpoint.substring(at + 1);
  }

  static List<String> splitEndpoints(String value) {
    return trimEndpoints(Arrays.asList(value.split(",")));
  }

  static List<String> trimEndpoints(Iterable<String> endpoints) {
    List<String> normalized = new ArrayList<>();
    for (String endpoint : endpoints) {
      if (endpoint == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String trimmed = endpoint.trim();
      if (!trimmed.isEmpty()) {
        normalized.add(trimmed);
      }
    }
    return normalized;
  }

  private static int positiveMillis(Duration duration, int defaultMillis) {
    Duration effective = duration == null ? Duration.ofMillis(defaultMillis) : duration;
    long millis = effective.toMillis();
    if (millis <= 0) {
      millis = defaultMillis;
    }
    return millis >= Integer.MAX_VALUE ? Integer.MAX_VALUE : (int) millis;
  }
}


FILE: AmpsFactoryKerberos.java
