package org.pronzato.fabric.api.connectors.amps.factory;

import java.net.URI;
import java.nio.file.Path;
import java.util.List;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.kerberos.KerberosClient;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.kerberos.KerberosConfig;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.kerberos.KerberosKrb5Source;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

final class AmpsFactoryKerberos {
  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(AmpsFactoryKerberos.class);

  private AmpsFactoryKerberos() {}

  static KerberosClient ensureRuntimeContext(AmpsFactoryOptions.Kerberos kerberos) {
    if (kerberos == null || !kerberos.enabled()) {
      return null;
    }
    kerberos.validate();

    KerberosClient existing = kerberos.runtimeContext();
    if (existing != null) {
      existing.start();
      if (Strings.isBlank(kerberos.getPrincipal())) {
        kerberos.principal(existing.getConfig().getEffectivePrincipal());
      }
      logKerberosEnabled(kerberos, existing.getConfig().getKrb5ConfigSource());
      return existing;
    }

    Path keytabPath = null;
    byte[] keytabBytes = null;
    if (Strings.isNotBlank(kerberos.getKeytab())) {
      keytabPath = Path.of(kerberos.getKeytab());
    } else {
      keytabBytes = kerberos.getKeytabBytes();
    }

    KerberosKrb5Source krb5Source;
    if (Strings.isNotBlank(kerberos.getKrb5ConfPath())) {
      krb5Source = KerberosKrb5Source.filePath(Path.of(kerberos.getKrb5ConfPath()));
    } else {
      byte[] krb5Data = kerberos.getKrb5ConfData();
      if (krb5Data != null && krb5Data.length > 0) {
        krb5Source = KerberosKrb5Source.bytes(krb5Data);
      } else {
        krb5Source = KerberosKrb5Source.DEFAULT;
      }
    }

    KerberosConfig config =
        new KerberosConfig(
            KerberosConfig.DEFAULT_CONTEXT_NAME,
            true,
            kerberos.getPrincipal(),
            keytabPath,
            keytabBytes,
            krb5Source,
            kerberos.realm(),
            kerberos.debug(),
            true);
    KerberosClient created = new KerberosClient(config).start();
    kerberos.runtimeContext(created);
    kerberos.principal(created.getConfig().getEffectivePrincipal());
    logKerberosEnabled(kerberos, created.getConfig().getKrb5ConfigSource());
    return created;
  }

  static String resolveSaslHost(AmpsFactoryOptions.Kerberos kerberos, List<String> endpoints) {
    if (kerberos != null && Strings.isNotBlank(kerberos.saslHost())) {
      return defaultSaslHost(kerberos.saslHost());
    }
    if (Strings.isEmpty(endpoints)) {
      return null;
    }
    try {
      URI uri = URI.create(endpoints.get(0));
      String host = uri.getHost();
      if (Strings.isNotBlank(host)) {
        return defaultSaslHost(host);
      }
      String authority = uri.getAuthority();
      if (Strings.isNotBlank(authority)) {
        int at = authority.indexOf('@');
        String hostPart = at >= 0 ? authority.substring(at + 1) : authority;
        int colon = hostPart.indexOf(':');
        host = colon >= 0 ? hostPart.substring(0, colon) : hostPart;
      }
      if (Strings.isBlank(host)) {
        return null;
      }
      return defaultSaslHost(host);
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      return null;
    }
  }

  static String resolveSaslHost(AmpsFactoryOptions.Kerberos kerberos, URI uri)
      throws com.crankuptheamps.client.exception.AuthenticationException {
    if (kerberos != null && Strings.isNotBlank(kerberos.saslHost())) {
      return defaultSaslHost(kerberos.saslHost());
    }
    return defaultSaslHost(resolveHost(uri));
  }

  static String defaultSaslHost(String host) {
    if (Strings.isBlank(host)) {
      return "localhost";
    }
    return isIpAddress(host) ? "localhost" : host;
  }

  static String shortUser(String principal) {
    return principal == null ? null : principal.split("@")[0];
  }

  static String keytabBasename(String keytabPath) {
    if (Strings.isBlank(keytabPath)) {
      return "<inline>";
    }
    try {
      Path path = Path.of(keytabPath);
      Path name = path.getFileName();
      return name == null ? keytabPath : name.toString();
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      return keytabPath;
    }
  }

  private static String resolveHost(URI uri)
      throws com.crankuptheamps.client.exception.AuthenticationException {
    if (uri == null) {
      throw new com.crankuptheamps.client.exception.AuthenticationException(
          "Kerberos requires a connected HAClient URI");
    }
    String host = uri.getHost();
    if (Strings.isBlank(host)) {
      String authority = uri.getAuthority();
      if (Strings.isNotBlank(authority)) {
        int at = authority.indexOf('@');
        String hostPart = at >= 0 ? authority.substring(at + 1) : authority;
        int colon = hostPart.indexOf(':');
        host = colon >= 0 ? hostPart.substring(0, colon) : hostPart;
      }
    }
    if (Strings.isBlank(host)) {
      throw new com.crankuptheamps.client.exception.AuthenticationException(
          "Unable to determine broker host for Kerberos handshake");
    }
    return host;
  }

  private static boolean isIpAddress(String host) {
    if (Strings.isBlank(host)) {
      return false;
    }
    if (host.indexOf(':') >= 0) {
      return true;
    }
    String[] parts = host.split("\\.");
    if (parts.length != 4) {
      return false;
    }
    for (String part : parts) {
      if (part.isEmpty() || part.length() > 3) {
        return false;
      }
      int value = 0;
      for (int i = 0; i < part.length(); i++) {
        char ch = part.charAt(i);
        if (ch < '0' || ch > '9') {
          return false;
        }
        value = value * 10 + (ch - '0');
      }
      if (value > 255) {
        return false;
      }
    }
    return true;
  }

  private static void logKerberosEnabled(
      AmpsFactoryOptions.Kerberos kerberos, KerberosKrb5Source krb5Source) {
    if (!LOGGER.isDebugEnabled()) {
      return;
    }
    LOGGER.debug("[AMPS] Kerberos enabled principal={} keytab={} krb5Source={}", kerberos.getPrincipal(), keytabBasename(kerberos.getKeytab()), describeKrb5Source(krb5Source));
  }

  private static String describeKrb5Source(KerberosKrb5Source source) {
    if (source == null || source == KerberosKrb5Source.SYSTEM_DEFAULT) {
      return "SYSTEM_DEFAULT";
    }
    if (source instanceof KerberosKrb5Source.FilePath filePath) {
      return "FILE_PATH(" + filePath.getPath().toAbsolutePath() + ")";
    }
    if (source instanceof KerberosKrb5Source.Bytes bytes) {
      return "BYTES(" + bytes.getData().length + " bytes)";
    }
    if (source instanceof KerberosKrb5Source.Classpath resource) {
      return "CLASSPATH_RESOURCE(" + resource.getResourcePath() + ")";
    }
    return source.toString();
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.connectors.amps.factory;

import com.crankuptheamps.client.Authenticator;
import com.crankuptheamps.client.exception.AuthenticationException;
import java.net.URI;
import java.util.Base64;
import java.util.HashMap;
import java.util.Map;
import javax.security.sasl.Sasl;
import javax.security.sasl.SaslClient;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.kerberos.KerberosClient;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

final class AmpsFactorySasl {
  private AmpsFactorySasl() {}

  static final class KerberosAuthenticator implements Authenticator {
    private final AmpsFactoryOptions.Kerberos kerberos;
    private final SaslClient sasl;

    KerberosAuthenticator(AmpsFactoryOptions.Kerberos kerberos, URI uri) throws AuthenticationException {
      this.kerberos = kerberos;
      String host = AmpsFactoryKerberos.resolveSaslHost(kerberos, uri);
      this.sasl = createSaslClient(kerberos, host);
    }

    @Override
    public String authenticate(String username, String password) throws AuthenticationException {
      return respond(password);
    }

    @Override
    public String retry(String username, String password) throws AuthenticationException {
      return respond(password);
    }

    @Override
    public void completed(String username, String password, int reason) throws AuthenticationException {
      try {
        sasl.dispose();
      } catch (Exception ignore) {
      }
    }

    private String respond(String challengeBase64) throws AuthenticationException {
      byte[] challenge = decode(challengeBase64);
      try {
        byte[] response =
            runInKerberosContext(
                kerberos,
                () -> sasl.evaluateChallenge(challenge),
                "Kerberos SASL evaluation failed");
        if (response == null || response.length == 0) {
          return "";
        }
        return Base64.getEncoder().encodeToString(response);
      } catch (AuthenticationException ex) {
        throw ex;
      } catch (Exception ex) {
        throw new AuthenticationException("Kerberos SASL evaluation failed", ex);
      }
    }

    private static <T> T runInKerberosContext(
        AmpsFactoryOptions.Kerberos kerberos, CheckedSupplier<T> supplier, String errorMessage)
        throws AuthenticationException {
      try {
        KerberosClient context = kerberos == null ? null : kerberos.runtimeContext();
        if (context == null) {
          return supplier.get();
        }
        return context.doAs(() -> supplier.get());
      } catch (AuthenticationException ex) {
        throw ex;
      } catch (Exception ex) {
        throw new AuthenticationException(errorMessage, ex);
      }
    }

    @FunctionalInterface
    private interface CheckedSupplier<T> {
      T get() throws Exception;
    }

    private static SaslClient createSaslClient(AmpsFactoryOptions.Kerberos kerberos, String host)
        throws AuthenticationException {
      Map<String, String> props = new HashMap<>();
      if (Strings.isNotBlank(kerberos.qop())) {
        props.put(Sasl.QOP, kerberos.qop());
      }
      SaslClient client =
          runInKerberosContext(
              kerberos,
              () ->
                  Sasl.createSaslClient(
                      new String[] {kerberos.mechanism()},
                      kerberos.authorizationId(),
                      kerberos.service(),
                      host,
                      props,
                      null),
              "Failed to create Kerberos SASL client");
      if (client == null) {
        throw new AuthenticationException(
            "No SASL client available for mechanism " + kerberos.mechanism());
      }
      return client;
    }

    private static byte[] decode(String value) {
      if (Strings.isBlank(value)) {
        return new byte[0];
      }
      return Base64.getDecoder().decode(value);
    }

  }
}


FILE: AmpsFactoryServerChooser.java

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.connectors.amps.factory;

import com.crankuptheamps.client.Authenticator;
import com.crankuptheamps.client.ConnectionInfo;
import com.crankuptheamps.client.HAClient;
import com.crankuptheamps.client.ServerChooser;
import com.crankuptheamps.client.exception.AuthenticationException;
import java.net.URI;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;

final class AmpsFactoryServerChooser {
  private AmpsFactoryServerChooser() {}

  static ConfigurableServerChooser ensureServerChooser(HAClient client) {
    ServerChooser chooser = client.getServerChooser();
    if (chooser instanceof ConfigurableServerChooser configurableServerChooser) {
      return configurableServerChooser;
    }
    ConfigurableServerChooser configured = new ConfigurableServerChooser();
    client.setServerChooser(configured);
    return configured;
  }

  static AuthenticatorFactory authenticatorFactory(AmpsFactoryOptions.Kerberos kerberos)
      throws Exception {
    if (kerberos == null || !kerberos.enabled()) {
      return AuthenticatorFactory.NOOP;
    }
    return endpoint -> {
      try {
        URI endpointUri = URI.create(endpoint);
        return new AmpsFactorySasl.KerberosAuthenticator(kerberos, endpointUri);
      } catch (IllegalArgumentException ex) {
        throw new AuthenticationException("Invalid AMPS endpoint URI: " + endpoint, ex);
      }
    };
  }

  static final class ConfigurableServerChooser implements ServerChooser {
    private final List<String> endpoints = new ArrayList<>();
    private int current;
    private String lastError = "";
    private AuthenticatorFactory factory = AuthenticatorFactory.NOOP;

    void setEndpoints(List<String> uris, AuthenticatorFactory factory) {
      endpoints.clear();
      if (uris != null) {
        endpoints.addAll(uris);
      }
      current = 0;
      lastError = "";
      this.factory = factory == null ? AuthenticatorFactory.NOOP : factory;
    }

    @Override
    public String getCurrentURI() {
      if (endpoints.isEmpty()) {
        return null;
      }
      if (current >= endpoints.size()) {
        current = 0;
      }
      return endpoints.get(current);
    }

    @Override
    public Authenticator getCurrentAuthenticator() throws Exception {
      String uri = getCurrentURI();
      if (uri == null) {
        return null;
      }
      return factory.create(uri);
    }

    @Override
    public void reportFailure(Exception exception, ConnectionInfo info) {
      if (exception != null) {
        lastError = exception.toString();
      }
      if (!endpoints.isEmpty()) {
        current = (current + 1) % endpoints.size();
      }
    }

    @Override
    public String getError() {
      return lastError == null ? "" : lastError;
    }

    @Override
    public void reportSuccess(ConnectionInfo info) {
      lastError = "";
    }
  }

  @FunctionalInterface
  interface AuthenticatorFactory {
    Authenticator create(String uri) throws Exception;

    AuthenticatorFactory NOOP = uri -> null;
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.connectors.s3;

import java.net.URI;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class S3Connection implements AutoCloseable {
  private final String name;
  private final String region;
  private final String bucket;
  private final String endpoint;
  private final boolean pathStyleAccess;
  private final String basePrefix;
  private final Map<String, String> attributes;
  private final String accessKeyId;
  private final String secretAccessKey;
  private final String sessionToken;
  private final S3Admin admin;
  private final boolean shared;

  public S3Connection(
      String name,
      String region,
      String bucket,
      String endpoint,
      boolean pathStyleAccess,
      String basePrefix,
      Map<String, String> attributes,
      String accessKeyId,
      String secretAccessKey,
      String sessionToken) {
    this.name = Objects.requireNonNull(name, "name");
    this.region = Strings.requireNonBlank(region, "s3.region");
    this.bucket = Strings.requireNonBlank(bucket, "s3.bucket");
    URI endpointUri = toEndpointUri(endpoint);
    this.endpoint = endpointUri == null ? null : endpointUri.toString();
    this.pathStyleAccess = pathStyleAccess;
    this.basePrefix = normalizePrefix(basePrefix);
    this.attributes = attributes == null ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(attributes);
    this.accessKeyId = Strings.requireNonBlank(accessKeyId, "s3.accessKeyId");
    this.secretAccessKey = Strings.requireNonBlank(secretAccessKey, "s3.secretAccessKey");
    this.sessionToken = Strings.trimToNull(sessionToken);
    this.admin =
        new S3Admin(
            this.name,
            this.region,
            this.bucket,
            this.endpoint,
            this.pathStyleAccess,
            this.basePrefix,
            this.attributes,
            this.accessKeyId,
            this.secretAccessKey,
            this.sessionToken);
    this.shared = false;
  }

  private S3Connection(S3Connection source, boolean shared) {
    this.name = source.name;
    this.region = source.region;
    this.bucket = source.bucket;
    this.endpoint = source.endpoint;
    this.pathStyleAccess = source.pathStyleAccess;
    this.basePrefix = source.basePrefix;
    this.attributes = source.attributes;
    this.accessKeyId = source.accessKeyId;
    this.secretAccessKey = source.secretAccessKey;
    this.sessionToken = source.sessionToken;
    this.admin = source.admin;
    this.shared = shared;
  }

  public String name() {
    return name;
  }

  public String region() {
    return region;
  }

  public String bucket() {
    return bucket;
  }

  public String endpoint() {
    return endpoint;
  }

  public boolean pathStyleAccess() {
    return pathStyleAccess;
  }

  public String basePrefix() {
    return basePrefix;
  }

  public Map<String, String> attributes() {
    return attributes;
  }

  public String bucketUri() {
    if (basePrefix == null) {
      return "s3://" + bucket;
    }
    return "s3://" + bucket + "/" + basePrefix;
  }

  public S3Admin admin() {
    return admin;
  }

  public S3Connection shared() {
    return new S3Connection(this, true);
  }

  public List<String> listFolders(String path) {
    return listFolders(path, false);
  }

  public List<String> listFolders(String path, boolean recursive) {
    String normalizedPath = normalizeListPath(path);
    if (!recursive) {
      S3ListResult page =
          admin.listObjects(
              S3ListRequest.builder()
                  .withPrefix(normalizedPath)
                  .withDelimiter("/")
                  .withMaxKeys(1000)
                  .build());
      return page.commonPrefixes().stream()
          .map(this::toClientPath)
          .map(S3Connection::trimTrailingSlash)
          .filter(Objects::nonNull)
          .filter(value -> !value.isBlank())
          .toList();
    }
    List<String> folders = new ArrayList<>();
    List<String> pending = new ArrayList<>();
    pending.add(normalizedPath);
    int offset = 0;
    while (offset < pending.size()) {
      String currentPrefix = pending.get(offset++);
      String continuationToken = null;
      do {
        S3ListResult page =
            admin.listObjects(
                S3ListRequest.builder()
                    .withPrefix(currentPrefix)
                    .withDelimiter("/")
                    .withContinuationToken(continuationToken)
                    .withMaxKeys(1000)
                    .build());
        for (String prefix : page.commonPrefixes()) {
          String display = trimTrailingSlash(toClientPath(prefix));
          if (display != null && !display.isBlank() && !folders.contains(display)) {
            folders.add(display);
          }
          pending.add(prefix);
        }
        continuationToken = page.nextContinuationToken();
      } while (hasText(continuationToken));
    }
    return List.copyOf(folders);
  }

  public List<S3ObjectSummary> listObjects(String path) {
    return listObjects(path, false);
  }

  public List<S3ObjectSummary> listObjects(String path, boolean recursive) {
    String normalizedPath = normalizeListPath(path);
    String continuationToken = null;
    List<S3ObjectSummary> objects = new ArrayList<>();
    do {
      S3ListResult page =
          admin.listObjects(
              S3ListRequest.builder()
                  .withPrefix(normalizedPath)
                  .withDelimiter(recursive ? null : "/")
                  .withContinuationToken(continuationToken)
                  .withMaxKeys(1000)
                  .build());
      objects.addAll(page.objects());
      continuationToken = page.nextContinuationToken();
    } while (hasText(continuationToken));
    return List.copyOf(objects);
  }

  private static String normalizePrefix(String value) {
    String trimmed = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (trimmed == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String normalized = trimmed.replace('\\', '/');
    while (normalized.startsWith("/")) {
      normalized = normalized.substring(1);
    }
    while (normalized.endsWith("/")) {
      normalized = normalized.substring(0, normalized.length() - 1);
    }
    return Strings.trimToNull(normalized);
  }

  private static String normalizeListPath(String value) {
    String normalized = normalizePrefix(value);
    if (!hasText(normalized)) {
      return null;
    }
    return normalized.endsWith("/") ? normalized : normalized + "/";
  }

  private String toClientPath(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return null;
    }
    if (!hasText(basePrefix)) {
      return normalized;
    }
    if (normalized.equals(basePrefix)) {
      return "";
    }
    String prefixed = basePrefix + "/";
    if (normalized.startsWith(prefixed)) {
      return normalized.substring(prefixed.length());
    }
    return normalized;
  }

  private static String trimTrailingSlash(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return null;
    }
    while (normalized.endsWith("/")) {
      normalized = normalized.substring(0, normalized.length() - 1);
    }
    return Strings.trimToNull(normalized);
  }

  private static URI toEndpointUri(String value) {
    String trimmed = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (trimmed == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String normalized = trimmed.contains("://") ? trimmed : "https://" + trimmed;
    try {
      return URI.create(normalized);
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Invalid s3.endpoint value: " + value, ex);
    }
  }

  private static boolean hasText(String value) {
    return !Strings.isBlank(value);
  }

  @Override
  public void close() {
    if (!shared) {
      admin.close();
    }
  }
}

FILE: S3OperationException.java

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.connectors.s3;

import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

/** Fabric-level exception describing a failed S3 operation without exposing AWS SDK types. */
public class S3OperationException extends RuntimeException {

  private final String operation;
  private final String key;
  private final int statusCode;
  private final String errorCode;

  public S3OperationException(
      String operation, String key, int statusCode, String errorCode, String message) {
    this(operation, key, statusCode, errorCode, message, null);
  }

  public S3OperationException(
      String operation,
      String key,
      int statusCode,
      String errorCode,
      String message,
      Throwable cause) {
    super(message, cause);
    this.operation = requireText(operation, "operation");
    this.key = key;
    this.statusCode = statusCode;
    this.errorCode = errorCode;
  }

  public String operation() {
    return operation;
  }

  public String key() {
    return key;
  }

  public int statusCode() {
    return statusCode;
  }

  public String errorCode() {
    return errorCode;
  }

  private static String requireText(String value, String name) {
    String trimmed = value == null ? null : value.trim();
    if (Strings.isEmpty(trimmed)) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(name + " is required");
    }
    return trimmed;
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.connectors.s3;

import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;


/** Request used when reading an object. */
public class S3ReadObjectRequest {
  private final String key;
  private final Long rangeStart;
  private final Long rangeEnd;

  private S3ReadObjectRequest(Builder builder) {
    this.key = requireKey(builder.key);
    this.rangeStart = builder.rangeStart;
    this.rangeEnd = builder.rangeEnd;
  }

  public static Builder builder() {
    return new Builder();
  }

  public String key() {
    return key;
  }

  public Long rangeStart() {
    return rangeStart;
  }

  public Long rangeEnd() {
    return rangeEnd;
  }

  private static String requireKey(String value) {
    if (Strings.isBlank(value)) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("object key is required");
    }
    return value;
  }

  public static final class Builder {
    private String key;
    private Long rangeStart;
    private Long rangeEnd;

    private Builder() {}

    public Builder withKey(String value) {
      this.key = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withRange(long startInclusive, long endInclusive) {
      this.rangeStart = startInclusive;
      this.rangeEnd = endInclusive;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withRangeStart(long startInclusive) {
      this.rangeStart = startInclusive;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withRangeEnd(long endInclusive) {
      this.rangeEnd = endInclusive;
      return this;
    }

    public S3ReadObjectRequest build() {
      if (rangeStart != null && rangeStart < 0) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("range start must be >= 0");
      }
      if (rangeEnd != null && rangeEnd < 0) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("range end must be >= 0");
      }
      if (rangeStart != null && rangeEnd != null && rangeEnd < rangeStart) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("range end must be >= range start");
      }
      return new S3ReadObjectRequest(this);
    }
  }
}





FILE: S3UploadRequest.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.connectors.s3;

import java.io.InputStream;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

/** Request used when uploading an object. */
public class S3UploadRequest {
  private final String key;
  private final byte[] bytes;
  private final InputStream stream;
  private final long contentLength;
  private final boolean closeStream;
  private final String contentType;
  private final Map<String, String> metadata;

  private S3UploadRequest(Builder builder) {
    this.key = requireKey(builder.key);
    this.bytes = builder.bytes == null ? null : builder.bytes.clone();
    this.stream = builder.stream;
    this.contentLength = builder.contentLength == null ? -1 : builder.contentLength;
    this.closeStream = builder.closeStream;
    this.contentType = builder.contentType;
    this.metadata =
        builder.metadata == null || builder.metadata.isEmpty()
            ? Map.of()
            : Map.copyOf(builder.metadata);
    if (bytes == null && stream == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("either bytes or stream must be supplied");
    }
    if (bytes != null && stream != null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("only one of bytes or stream may be supplied");
    }
    if (stream != null && contentLength < 0) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("contentLength must be >= 0 for stream uploads");
    }
  }

  public static Builder builder() {
    return new Builder();
  }

  public String key() {
    return key;
  }

  public byte[] bytes() {
    return bytes == null ? null : bytes.clone();
  }

  public InputStream stream() {
    return stream;
  }

  public long contentLength() {
    return contentLength;
  }

  public boolean closeStream() {
    return closeStream;
  }

  public String contentType() {
    return contentType;
  }

  public Map<String, String> metadata() {
    return metadata;
  }

  private static String requireKey(String value) {
    if (Strings.isBlank(value)) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("object key is required");
    }
    return value;
  }

  public static final class Builder {
    private String key;
    private byte[] bytes;
    private InputStream stream;
    private Long contentLength;
    private boolean closeStream;
    private String contentType;
    private Map<String, String> metadata;

    private Builder() {}

    public Builder withKey(String value) {
      this.key = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withBytes(byte[] value) {
      this.bytes = value == null ? null : value.clone();
      this.stream = null;
      this.contentLength = null;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withStream(InputStream value, long length) {
      return withStream(value, length, false);
    }

    public Builder withStream(InputStream value, long length, boolean close) {
      this.stream = Objects.requireNonNull(value, "stream");
      this.contentLength = length;
      this.closeStream = close;
      this.bytes = null;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder closeStream(boolean value) {
      this.closeStream = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withContentType(String value) {
      this.contentType = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withMetadata(Map<String, String> value) {
      if (Strings.isEmpty(value)) {
        this.metadata = null;
      } else {
        this.metadata = new LinkedHashMap<>(value);
      }
      return this;
    }

    public Builder putMetadata(String name, String value) {
      if (metadata == null) {
        metadata = new LinkedHashMap<>();
      }
      metadata.put(name, value);
      return this;
    }

    public S3UploadRequest build() {
      return new S3UploadRequest(this);
    }
  }
}

PACKAGE: org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery

FILE: CanonicalIds.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery;

import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.regex.Pattern;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

/**
 * Strict canonical ID utilities for config/discovery and runtime code paths.
 *
 * <p>Supported formats:</p>
 * <ul>
 *   <li>user:{id}</li>
 *   <li>group:{name} </li>
 *   <li>namespace:{group}/{namespace}</li>
 *   <li>app:{group}/{name}</li>
 *   <li>role:{name}</li>
 *   <li>dataset:{group}/{namespace}/{name}</li>
 *   <li>stream:{group}/{namespace}/{name}</li>
 *   <li>service:{group}/{name}</li>
 *   <li>endpoint:{group}/{name}</li>
 *   <li>endpoint:{group}/{namespace}/{name}</li>
 *   <li>materialized:{group}/{namespace}/{name}</li>
 *   <li>feed:{group}/{name}</li>
 *   <li>feed:{group}/{namespace}/{name}</li>
 *   <li>config:{group}/{configId}/{layerId}</li>
 * </ul>
 */
public final class CanonicalIds {
  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(CanonicalIds.class);
  private static final boolean DEBUG_STACKTRACES = debugStacktracesEnabled();
  private static final String EXPECTED_FORMATS_STRING =
      "dataset:<group>/<namespace>/<name>, "
          + "stream:<group>/<namespace>/<name>, materialized:<group>/<namespace>/<name>, "
          + "feed:<group>/<name> or feed:<group>/<namespace>/<name>, "
          + "namespace:<group>/<namespace>, service:<group>/<name>, "
          + "endpoint:<group>/<name>, endpoint:<group>/<namespace>/<name>, "
          + "config:<group>/<configId>/<layerId>, "
          + "user:<name>, group:<name>, app:<group>/<name>, or role:<name>";

  private static final Pattern USER = Pattern.compile("^user:[a-zA-Z0-9._-]+$");
  private static final Pattern GROUP = Pattern.compile("^group:[a-zA-Z0-9._-]+$");
  private static final Pattern NAMESPACE =
      Pattern.compile("^namespace:[a-zA-Z0-9._-]+/[a-zA-Z0-9._-]+$");
  private static final Pattern APP =
      Pattern.compile("^app:[a-zA-Z0-9._-]+/[a-zA-Z0-9._-]+$");
  private static final Pattern ROLE = Pattern.compile("^role:[a-zA-Z0-9._-]+$");
  private static final Pattern DATASET =
      Pattern.compile("^dataset:[a-zA-Z0-9._-]+/[a-zA-Z0-9._-]+/[a-zA-Z0-9._-]+$");
  private static final Pattern STREAM =
      Pattern.compile("^stream:[a-zA-Z0-9._-]+/[a-zA-Z0-9._-]+/[a-zA-Z0-9._-]+$");
  private static final Pattern SERVICE =
      Pattern.compile("^service:[a-zA-Z0-9._-]+/[a-zA-Z0-9._-]+$");
  private static final Pattern FEED =
      Pattern.compile("^feed:[a-zA-Z0-9._-]+/[a-zA-Z0-9._-]+(?:/[a-zA-Z0-9._-]+)?$");
  private static final Pattern ENDPOINT =
      Pattern.compile("^endpoint:[a-zA-Z0-9._-]+/[a-zA-Z0-9._-]+(?:/[a-zA-Z0-9._-]+)?$");
  private static final Pattern MATERIALIZED =
      Pattern.compile("^materialized:[a-zA-Z0-9._-]+/[a-zA-Z0-9._-]+/[a-zA-Z0-9._-]+$");
  private static final Pattern CONFIG =
      Pattern.compile("^config:[a-zA-Z0-9._-]+/[a-zA-Z0-9._-]+/[a-zA-Z0-9._-]+$");

  private CanonicalIds() {}

  public static boolean isUser(String id) {
    return id != null && USER.matcher(id.trim()).matches();
  }

  public static boolean isGroup(String id) {
    return id != null && GROUP.matcher(id.trim()).matches();
  }

  public static boolean isNamespace(String id) {
    return id != null && NAMESPACE.matcher(id.trim()).matches();
  }

  public static boolean isApp(String id) {
    return id != null && APP.matcher(id.trim()).matches();
  }

  public static boolean isRole(String id) {
    return id != null && ROLE.matcher(id.trim()).matches();
  }

  public static boolean isDataset(String id) {
    return id != null && DATASET.matcher(id.trim()).matches();
  }

  public static boolean isStream(String id) {
    return id != null && STREAM.matcher(id.trim()).matches();
  }

  public static boolean isService(String id) {
    return id != null && SERVICE.matcher(id.trim()).matches();
  }

  public static boolean isFeed(String id) {
    return id != null && FEED.matcher(id.trim()).matches();
  }

  public static boolean isEndpoint(String id) {
    return id != null && ENDPOINT.matcher(id.trim()).matches();
  }

  public static boolean isMaterialized(String id) {
    return id != null && MATERIALIZED.matcher(id.trim()).matches();
  }

  public static boolean isConfig(String id) {
    return id != null && CONFIG.matcher(id.trim()).matches();
  }

  public static String appPrincipal(String group, String appName) {
    String trimmedGroup = trim(group);
    String trimmedApp = trim(appName);
    if (trimmedGroup == null || trimmedApp == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("app group/name is required");
    }
    String canonical = "app:" + trimmedGroup + "/" + trimmedApp;
    validate(canonical);
    return canonical;
  }

  public static void validate(String id) {
    parse(id);
  }

  public static ParsedId parse(String id) {
    if (id == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("canonical id is required");
    }
    String trimmed = id.trim();
    if (trimmed.isEmpty()) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("canonical id is required");
    }
    if (isUser(trimmed)) {
      String name = trimmed.substring("user:".length());
      return new ParsedId("user", null, null, name, trimmed);
    }
    if (isGroup(trimmed)) {
      String name = trimmed.substring("group:".length());
      return new ParsedId("group", name, null, name, trimmed);
    }
    if (isNamespace(trimmed)) {
      String payload = trimmed.substring("namespace:".length());
      int slash = payload.indexOf('/');
      String group = payload.substring(0, slash);
      String namespace = payload.substring(slash + 1);
      return new ParsedId("namespace", group, namespace, namespace, trimmed);
    }
    if (isApp(trimmed)) {
      String payload = trimmed.substring("app:".length());
      int slash = payload.indexOf('/');
      String group = payload.substring(0, slash);
      String name = payload.substring(slash + 1);
      return new ParsedId("app", group, null, name, trimmed);
    }
    if (isRole(trimmed)) {
      String name = trimmed.substring("role:".length());
      return new ParsedId("role", null, null, name, trimmed);
    }
    if (isConfig(trimmed)) {
      String payload = trimmed.substring("config:".length());
      int firstSlash = payload.indexOf('/');
      String group = payload.substring(0, firstSlash);
      String remainder = payload.substring(firstSlash + 1);
      int secondSlash = remainder.indexOf('/');
      String configId = remainder.substring(0, secondSlash);
      String layerId = remainder.substring(secondSlash + 1);
      return new ParsedId("config", group, configId, layerId, trimmed);
    }
    if (isDataset(trimmed)
        || isService(trimmed)
        || isMaterialized(trimmed)
        || isStream(trimmed)
        || isFeed(trimmed)) {
      String prefix;
      String type;
      if (trimmed.startsWith("dataset:")) {
        prefix = "dataset:";
        type = "dataset";
      } else if (trimmed.startsWith("service:")) {
        prefix = "service:";
        type = "service";
      } else if (trimmed.startsWith("materialized:")) {
        prefix = "materialized:";
        type = "materialized";
      } else if (trimmed.startsWith("feed:")) {
        prefix = "feed:";
        type = "feed";
      } else {
        prefix = "stream:";
        type = "stream";
      }
      String payload = trimmed.substring(prefix.length());
      int firstSlash = payload.indexOf('/');
      if (firstSlash < 0) {
        throw invalidCanonicalFormat(trimmed, "Invalid canonical ID format: missing group segment");
      }
      String group = payload.substring(0, firstSlash);
      String remainder = payload.substring(firstSlash + 1);
      if ("service".equals(type)) {
        return new ParsedId(type, group, null, remainder, trimmed);
      }
      int secondSlash = remainder.indexOf('/');
      if ("feed".equals(type) && secondSlash < 0) {
        return new ParsedId(type, group, null, remainder, trimmed);
      }
      if (secondSlash < 0) {
        throw invalidCanonicalFormat(trimmed, "Invalid canonical ID format: namespace is required");
      }
      String namespace = remainder.substring(0, secondSlash);
      String name = remainder.substring(secondSlash + 1);
      return new ParsedId(type, group, namespace, name, trimmed);
    }
    if (isEndpoint(trimmed)) {
      String payload = trimmed.substring("endpoint:".length());
      String[] parts = payload.split("/");
      if (parts.length == 2) {
        return new ParsedId("endpoint", parts[0], null, parts[1], trimmed);
      }
      if (parts.length == 3) {
        return new ParsedId("endpoint", parts[0], parts[1], parts[2], trimmed);
      }
      throw invalidCanonicalFormat(
          trimmed,
          "Invalid canonical ID format: endpoint must be endpoint:<group>/<name> or endpoint:<group>/<namespace>/<name>");
    }
    throw invalidCanonicalFormat(trimmed, "Invalid canonical ID format. Expected " + EXPECTED_FORMATS_STRING);
  }

  public record ParsedId(String type, String group, String namespace, String name, String canonical) {
    public ParsedId {
      Objects.requireNonNull(type, "type");
      Objects.requireNonNull(name, "name");
      Objects.requireNonNull(canonical, "canonical");
    }

    public boolean isIdentity() {
      return "user".equals(type)
          || "group".equals(type)
          || "app".equals(type)
          || "role".equals(type);
    }

    public boolean isDataset() {
      return "dataset".equals(type);
    }

    public boolean isStream() {
      return "stream".equals(type);
    }

    public boolean isNamespace() {
      return "namespace".equals(type);
    }

    public boolean isGroup() {
      return "group".equals(type);
    }

    public boolean isService() {
      return "service".equals(type);
    }

    public boolean isFeed() {
      return "feed".equals(type);
    }

    public boolean isEndpoint() {
      return "endpoint".equals(type);
    }

    public boolean isMaterialized() {
      return "materialized".equals(type);
    }

  }

  private static String trim(String value) {
    if (value == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String trimmed = value.trim();
    return trimmed.isEmpty() ? null : trimmed;
  }

  private static IllegalArgumentException invalidCanonicalFormat(String value, String message) {
    IllegalArgumentException ex = new IllegalArgumentException(message);
    StackTraceElement[] stack = ex.getStackTrace();
    String caller = stack.length > 1 ? stack[1].toString() : "<unknown>";
    LOGGER.error("[CanonicalIds][Invalid] value='{}' expected='{}' caller='{}'", value, EXPECTED_FORMATS_STRING, caller);
    LOGGER.error("[CanonicalIds][Invalid][Cause] {}", ex.toString());
    if (DEBUG_STACKTRACES) {
      LOGGER.error("[CanonicalIds][Invalid][Stacktrace] value='{}'", value, ex);
    } else {
      LOGGER.error("[CanonicalIds][Invalid][StackTop] {}", compactOrgStack(stack, 5));
    }
    return ex;
  }

  private static boolean debugStacktracesEnabled() {
    return readFlag("fabric.debugStacktraces")
        || readFlag("studio.debugStacktraces")
        || readFlagFromEnv("FABRIC_DEBUG_STACKTRACES")
        || readFlagFromEnv("STUDIO_DEBUG_STACKTRACES");
  }

  private static boolean readFlag(String key) {
    String value = trim(System.getProperty(key));
    return value != null && "true".equalsIgnoreCase(value);
  }

  private static boolean readFlagFromEnv(String key) {
    String value = trim(System.getenv(key));
    return value != null && "true".equalsIgnoreCase(value);
  }

  private static String compactOrgStack(StackTraceElement[] stack, int maxFrames) {
    if (stack == null || stack.length == 0) {
      return "<no stack>";
    }
    StringBuilder out = new StringBuilder();
    int count = 0;
    int limit = Math.max(2, maxFrames);
    for (StackTraceElement frame : stack) {
      if (frame == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String className = frame.getClassName();
      if (className == null || !className.startsWith("org.pronzato.")) {
        continue;
      }
      if (count > 0) {
        out.append(" | ");
      }
      out.append(frame);
      count++;
      if (count >= limit) {
        break;
      }
    }
    return count == 0 ? "<no org.pronzato stack frames>" : out.toString();
  }
}


FILE: DeleteManager.java

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Set;
import java.util.function.Supplier;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.Definition;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionType;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.lifecycle.AssetLifecycleGraph;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.lifecycle.AssetLifecycleGraphBuilder;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.lifecycle.AssetLifecycleNode;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.lifecycle.DeleteOptions;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.lifecycle.DeleteOutcome;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.lifecycle.DeletePlan;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.lifecycle.DeletePlanner;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.lifecycle.DeleteResult;

public final class DeleteManager implements AutoCloseable {
  private final Supplier<List<Definition>> definitionsSupplier;
  private final DefinitionDeleteExecutor deleteExecutor;

  public DeleteManager(List<Definition> definitions) {
    List<Definition> snapshot = definitions == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(definitions);
    this.definitionsSupplier = () -> snapshot;
    this.deleteExecutor = null;
  }

  public DeleteManager(
      Supplier<List<Definition>> definitionsSupplier, DefinitionDeleteExecutor deleteExecutor) {
    this.definitionsSupplier = definitionsSupplier == null ? List::of : definitionsSupplier;
    this.deleteExecutor = deleteExecutor;
  }

  public DeletePlan planDelete(String assetIdOrToken) {
    return planDelete(assetIdOrToken, DeleteOptions.defaults());
  }

  public DeletePlan planDelete(String assetIdOrToken, DeleteOptions options) {
    DeleteOptions resolved = options == null ? DeleteOptions.defaults() : options;
    AssetLifecycleGraph graph = buildGraph();
    return DeletePlanner.plan(graph, assetIdOrToken, resolved);
  }

  public DeleteResult delete(String assetIdOrToken) {
    return delete(assetIdOrToken, null);
  }

  public DeleteResult delete(String assetIdOrToken, DeleteOptions options) {
    DeleteOptions requested =
        options == null ? DeleteOptions.defaults().forExecution() : options;
    DeleteOptions resolved = requested.dryRun() ? requested : requested.forExecution();
    AssetLifecycleGraph graph = buildGraph();
    DeletePlan plan = DeletePlanner.plan(graph, assetIdOrToken, resolved);

    if (resolved.dryRun()) {
      return new DeleteResult(
          plan.rootAssetId(),
          resolved,
          DeleteOutcome.DRY_RUN,
          plan,
          List.of(),
          List.of(),
          plan.assetsToDetach(),
          plan.assetsRetained(),
          List.of(),
          List.of(),
          plan.blockers(),
          plan.warnings(),
          plan.manualActions(),
          List.of());
    }

    if (!plan.blockers().isEmpty() && !resolved.force()) {
      return new DeleteResult(
          plan.rootAssetId(),
          resolved,
          DeleteOutcome.BLOCKED,
          plan,
          List.of(),
          List.of(),
          plan.assetsToDetach(),
          plan.assetsRetained(),
          List.of(),
          List.of(),
          plan.blockers(),
          plan.warnings(),
          plan.manualActions(),
          List.of());
    }

    if (deleteExecutor == null) {
      List<String> warnings = new ArrayList<>(plan.warnings());
      warnings.add("Delete execution is not available in this manager instance.");
      return new DeleteResult(
          plan.rootAssetId(),
          resolved,
          DeleteOutcome.BLOCKED,
          plan,
          List.of(),
          plan.assetsToDelete(),
          plan.assetsToDetach(),
          plan.assetsRetained(),
          List.of(),
          List.of(),
          plan.blockers(),
          warnings,
          plan.manualActions(),
          List.of());
    }

    Set<String> selected = new LinkedHashSet<>(plan.assetsToDelete());
    List<String> deleted = new ArrayList<>();
    List<String> skipped = new ArrayList<>();
    List<String> attempted = new ArrayList<>();
    List<String> warnings = new ArrayList<>(plan.warnings());
    List<String> manualActions = new ArrayList<>(plan.manualActions());

    for (String assetId : plan.executionOrder()) {
      if (!selected.contains(assetId)) {
        continue;
      }
      attempted.add(assetId);
      java.util.Optional<AssetLifecycleNode> maybeNode = graph.node(assetId);
      if (maybeNode.isEmpty()) {
        skipped.add(assetId);
        warnings.add("Skipping delete for unknown asset node: " + assetId);
        continue;
      }
      AssetLifecycleNode node = maybeNode.orElseThrow();
      if (!isSupportedDefinitionType(node.type())) {
        skipped.add(assetId);
        manualActions.add(
            "Manual delete required for unsupported asset type "
                + node.type().name().toLowerCase()
                + ": "
                + node.assetId());
        continue;
      }
      try {
        deleteExecutor.delete(node.type(), node.group(), node.name());
        deleted.add(assetId);
      } catch (RuntimeException ex) {
        skipped.add(assetId);
        warnings.add(
            "Delete failed for "
                + assetId
                + " ("
                + node.type().name().toLowerCase()
                + "): "
                + ex.getMessage());
      }
    }

    if (resolved.deleteData() && !plan.storageToDelete().isEmpty()) {
      for (String storageTarget : plan.storageToDelete()) {
        manualActions.add(
            "Storage delete requested but not executed automatically: " + storageTarget);
      }
    }
    if (resolved.deleteHistory() && !plan.historyToDelete().isEmpty()) {
      for (String historyTarget : plan.historyToDelete()) {
        manualActions.add(
            "History delete requested but not executed automatically: " + historyTarget);
      }
    }

    DeleteOutcome outcome = skipped.isEmpty() ? DeleteOutcome.COMPLETED : DeleteOutcome.PARTIAL;
    return new DeleteResult(
        plan.rootAssetId(),
        resolved,
        outcome,
        plan,
        List.copyOf(deleted),
        List.copyOf(skipped),
        plan.assetsToDetach(),
        plan.assetsRetained(),
        List.of(),
        List.of(),
        plan.blockers(),
        List.copyOf(warnings),
        List.copyOf(manualActions),
        List.copyOf(attempted));
  }

  @Override
  public void close() {}

  private AssetLifecycleGraph buildGraph() {
    List<Definition> definitions = definitionsSupplier.get();
    return AssetLifecycleGraphBuilder.build(definitions == null ? List.of() : definitions);
  }

  private static boolean isSupportedDefinitionType(DefinitionType type) {
    if (type == null) {
      return false;
    }
    return switch (type) {
      case DATASET,
          SERVICE,
          STREAM,
          SCHEMA,
          INGEST,
          INGEST_SOURCE,
          CONFIG,
          ENTITLEMENT,
          CONNECTION -> true;
      default -> false;
    };
  }

  @FunctionalInterface
  public interface DefinitionDeleteExecutor {
    void delete(DefinitionType type, String group, String name);
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery;

import java.time.Duration;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.CloseSupport;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.function.Supplier;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.ControlConnection;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.cache.DiscoveryCache;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.cache.DiscoveryTopics;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.scope.DiscoveryScope;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.scope.DiscoveryScopeDiff;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.scope.DiscoveryScopeResolver;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.scope.DiscoveryVisibilityManager;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.status.app.AppStatusCache;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.status.data.DataStatusCache;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.status.service.ServiceStatusCache;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

public final class DiscoveryManager implements AutoCloseable {
  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(DiscoveryManager.class);
  private static final String STATUS_SUBSCRIPTION_FILTER =
      "(/type='STATUS_APP' OR /type='STATUS_SERVICE' OR /type='STATUS_DATA')";
  private final Object lifecycleLock = new Object();
  private final ControlConnection controlConnection;
  private final DiscoveryCache preloadedDiscoveryCache;
  private final String sessionGroup;
  private final boolean configCacheAdmin;
  private final boolean verbose;
  private final Supplier<String> subjectSupplier;
  private final Supplier<String> delegatedSubjectSupplier;

  private volatile DiscoveryCache discoveryCache;
  private volatile AppStatusCache appStatusCache;
  private volatile ServiceStatusCache serviceStatusCache;
  private volatile DataStatusCache dataStatusCache;
  private volatile DiscoveryVisibilityManager discoveryVisibilityManager;
  private volatile DiscoveryScope discoveryScope;
  private volatile DiscoveryScopeDiff discoveryScopeDiff;
  private volatile ControlConnection.Subscription statusSubscription;

  public DiscoveryManager(
      ControlConnection controlConnection,
      String sessionGroup,
      boolean configCacheAdmin,
      boolean verbose,
      Supplier<String> subjectSupplier,
      Supplier<String> delegatedSubjectSupplier) {
    this(
        Objects.requireNonNull(controlConnection, "controlConnection"),
        null,
        sessionGroup,
        configCacheAdmin,
        verbose,
        subjectSupplier,
        delegatedSubjectSupplier);
  }

  public static DiscoveryManager recoveredSnapshot(
      DiscoveryCache recoveredDiscoveryCache,
      String sessionGroup,
      Supplier<String> subjectSupplier,
      Supplier<String> delegatedSubjectSupplier) {
    return new DiscoveryManager(
        null,
        Objects.requireNonNull(recoveredDiscoveryCache, "recoveredDiscoveryCache"),
        sessionGroup,
        true,
        false,
        subjectSupplier,
        delegatedSubjectSupplier);
  }

  private DiscoveryManager(
      ControlConnection controlConnection,
      DiscoveryCache preloadedDiscoveryCache,
      String sessionGroup,
      boolean configCacheAdmin,
      boolean verbose,
      Supplier<String> subjectSupplier,
      Supplier<String> delegatedSubjectSupplier) {
    this.controlConnection = controlConnection;
    this.preloadedDiscoveryCache = preloadedDiscoveryCache;
    this.sessionGroup = sessionGroup;
    this.configCacheAdmin = configCacheAdmin;
    this.verbose = verbose;
    this.subjectSupplier = Objects.requireNonNull(subjectSupplier, "subjectSupplier");
    this.delegatedSubjectSupplier =
        delegatedSubjectSupplier == null ? () -> null : delegatedSubjectSupplier;
  }

  public void start() {
    synchronized (lifecycleLock) {
      if (discoveryCache != null) {
        return;
      }
      long managerStartNanos = System.nanoTime();
      long phaseStartNanos = System.nanoTime();
      DiscoveryCache createdCache =
          preloadedDiscoveryCache == null
              ? createDiscoveryCache(controlConnection)
              : startPreloadedDiscoveryCache(preloadedDiscoveryCache);
      discoveryCache = createdCache;
      LOGGER.info(
          "[Session][StartupTiming] phase=discovery-manager.discovery-cache elapsedMs={} recovered={} offline={}",
          elapsedMillis(phaseStartNanos),
          createdCache.recovered(),
          createdCache.offlineMode());

      phaseStartNanos = System.nanoTime();
      DiscoveryVisibilityManager visibilityManager =
          new DiscoveryVisibilityManager(
              createdCache,
              new DiscoveryScopeResolver(),
              () -> sessionGroup,
              subjectSupplier,
              delegatedSubjectSupplier);
      visibilityManager.start();
      discoveryVisibilityManager = visibilityManager;
      discoveryScope = visibilityManager.currentScope();
      discoveryScopeDiff = visibilityManager.lastDiff();
      LOGGER.info(
          "[Session][StartupTiming] phase=discovery-manager.visibility elapsedMs={}",
          elapsedMillis(phaseStartNanos));

      phaseStartNanos = System.nanoTime();
      appStatusCache = controlConnection == null ? null : createSharedAppStatusCache(controlConnection);
      LOGGER.info(
          "[Session][StartupTiming] phase=discovery-manager.app-status-cache elapsedMs={} enabled={}",
          elapsedMillis(phaseStartNanos),
          appStatusCache != null);
      phaseStartNanos = System.nanoTime();
      serviceStatusCache =
          controlConnection == null ? null : createSharedServiceStatusCache(controlConnection);
      LOGGER.info(
          "[Session][StartupTiming] phase=discovery-manager.service-status-cache elapsedMs={} enabled={}",
          elapsedMillis(phaseStartNanos),
          serviceStatusCache != null);
      phaseStartNanos = System.nanoTime();
      dataStatusCache = controlConnection == null ? null : createSharedDataStatusCache(controlConnection);
      if (controlConnection != null) {
        statusSubscription =
            createSharedStatusSubscription(
                controlConnection, appStatusCache, serviceStatusCache, dataStatusCache);
      }
      LOGGER.info(
          "[Session][StartupTiming] phase=discovery-manager.data-status-cache elapsedMs={} enabled={}",
          elapsedMillis(phaseStartNanos),
          dataStatusCache != null);
      LOGGER.info(
          "[Session][StartupTiming] phase=discovery-manager.complete elapsedMs={}",
          elapsedMillis(managerStartNanos));
    }
  }

  public DiscoveryCache discoveryCache() {
    return discoveryCache;
  }

  public AppStatusCache appStatusCache() {
    return appStatusCache;
  }

  public ServiceStatusCache serviceStatusCache() {
    return serviceStatusCache;
  }

  public DataStatusCache dataStatusCache() {
    return dataStatusCache;
  }

  public DiscoveryScope currentScope() {
    DiscoveryVisibilityManager manager = discoveryVisibilityManager;
    return manager == null ? discoveryScope : manager.currentScope();
  }

  public DiscoveryScopeDiff lastScopeDiff() {
    DiscoveryVisibilityManager manager = discoveryVisibilityManager;
    return manager == null ? discoveryScopeDiff : manager.lastDiff();
  }

  @Override
  public void close() {
    synchronized (lifecycleLock) {
      CloseSupport.closeQuietly(discoveryVisibilityManager);
      discoveryVisibilityManager = null;
      discoveryScope = null;
      discoveryScopeDiff = null;
      CloseSupport.closeQuietly(statusSubscription);
      statusSubscription = null;
      CloseSupport.closeQuietly(appStatusCache);
      appStatusCache = null;
      CloseSupport.closeQuietly(serviceStatusCache);
      serviceStatusCache = null;
      CloseSupport.closeQuietly(dataStatusCache);
      dataStatusCache = null;
      CloseSupport.closeQuietly(discoveryCache);
      discoveryCache = null;
    }
  }

  private DiscoveryCache createDiscoveryCache(ControlConnection connection) {
    DiscoveryCache created = new DiscoveryCache(connection, sessionGroup, configCacheAdmin, verbose);
    try {
      created.start();
      return created;
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      CloseSupport.closeQuietly(created);
      throw new IllegalStateException("Failed to initialize DiscoveryCache", ex);
    }
  }

  private static DiscoveryCache startPreloadedDiscoveryCache(DiscoveryCache preloaded) {
    try {
      preloaded.start();
      return preloaded;
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      CloseSupport.closeQuietly(preloaded);
      throw new IllegalStateException("Failed to initialize recovered DiscoveryCache", ex);
    }
  }

  private AppStatusCache createSharedAppStatusCache(ControlConnection connection) {
    AppStatusCache created = new AppStatusCache(connection);
    try {
      created.startShared();
      return created;
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      CloseSupport.closeQuietly(created);
      throw new IllegalStateException("Failed to initialize AppStatusCache", ex);
    }
  }

  private ServiceStatusCache createSharedServiceStatusCache(ControlConnection connection) {
    ServiceStatusCache created = new ServiceStatusCache(connection);
    try {
      created.startShared();
      return created;
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      CloseSupport.closeQuietly(created);
      throw new IllegalStateException("Failed to initialize ServiceStatusCache", ex);
    }
  }

  private DataStatusCache createSharedDataStatusCache(ControlConnection connection) {
    DataStatusCache created = new DataStatusCache(connection);
    try {
      created.startShared();
      return created;
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      CloseSupport.closeQuietly(created);
      throw new IllegalStateException("Failed to initialize DataStatusCache", ex);
    }
  }

  private ControlConnection.Subscription createSharedStatusSubscription(
      ControlConnection connection,
      AppStatusCache appCache,
      ServiceStatusCache serviceCache,
      DataStatusCache dataCache) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(connection, "connection");
    Objects.requireNonNull(appCache, "appCache");
    Objects.requireNonNull(serviceCache, "serviceCache");
    Objects.requireNonNull(dataCache, "dataCache");
    ControlConnection.Subscription subscription = null;
    boolean success = false;
    try {
      subscription =
          connection.sowAndSubscribe(
              DiscoveryTopics.STATUS,
              "oof",
              STATUS_SUBSCRIPTION_FILTER,
              message -> {
                com.crankuptheamps.client.Message raw = message.raw();
                appCache.onStatusMessage(raw);
                serviceCache.onStatusMessage(raw);
                dataCache.onStatusMessage(raw);
              });
      Duration recoveryTimeout = Duration.ofSeconds(30);
      appCache.awaitRecovery(recoveryTimeout);
      serviceCache.awaitRecovery(recoveryTimeout);
      dataCache.awaitRecovery(recoveryTimeout);
      success = true;
      return subscription;
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Failed to initialize shared status subscription", ex);
    } finally {
      if (!success) {
        CloseSupport.closeQuietly(subscription);
        CloseSupport.closeQuietly(appCache);
        CloseSupport.closeQuietly(serviceCache);
        CloseSupport.closeQuietly(dataCache);
      }
    }
  }

  private static long elapsedMillis(long startNanos) {
    return Math.max(0L, (System.nanoTime() - startNanos) / 1_000_000L);
  }

}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.codec;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.annotation.JsonInclude;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.DeserializationFeature;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonNode;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.SerializationFeature;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.node.ObjectNode;
import java.io.IOException;
import java.util.concurrent.ConcurrentHashMap;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.Definition;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionApp;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionConnection;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionDataset;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionEntitlement;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionEnvelope;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionEnvironment;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionHbService;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionIngest;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionIngestSource;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionConfig;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionConfigLayer;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionConfigChange;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionPlatform;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionSchema;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionService;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionStatusApp;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionStatusData;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionStatusService;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionStream;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionType;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

public final class DiscoveryCodec {
  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(DiscoveryCodec.class);
  private static final long UNKNOWN_TYPE_LOG_WINDOW_MS = 30_000L;
  private static final ConcurrentHashMap<String, Long> UNKNOWN_TYPE_LAST_LOG =
      new ConcurrentHashMap<>();
  private static final ObjectMapper MAPPER =
      new ObjectMapper()
          .setSerializationInclusion(JsonInclude.Include.NON_NULL)
          .disable(DeserializationFeature.FAIL_ON_UNKNOWN_PROPERTIES)
          .enable(DeserializationFeature.READ_UNKNOWN_ENUM_VALUES_USING_DEFAULT_VALUE)
          .disable(SerializationFeature.FAIL_ON_EMPTY_BEANS)
          .findAndRegisterModules();

  private DiscoveryCodec() {}

  public static ObjectMapper mapper() {
    return MAPPER;
  }

  public static Definition decode(String json) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(json);
    if (normalized == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("definition data is required");
    }
    try {
      return decode(MAPPER.readTree(normalized));
    } catch (IOException ex) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("definition data must be valid JSON", ex);
    }
  }

  public static Definition decode(byte[] data) {
    if (data == null || data.length == 0) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("definition data is required");
    }
    try {
      return decode(MAPPER.readTree(data));
    } catch (IOException ex) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("definition data must be valid JSON", ex);
    }
  }

  public static Definition decode(JsonNode node) {
    if (node == null || node.isNull() || node.isMissingNode() || !node.isObject()) {
      return null;
    }
    ObjectNode root = (ObjectNode) node;
    JsonNode envelopeNode = root.get("envelope");
    if (envelopeNode == null || envelopeNode.isNull() || !envelopeNode.isObject()) {
      return null;
    }
    ObjectNode envelopeRoot = (ObjectNode) envelopeNode;
    String typeText = asText(envelopeRoot.get("type"));
    String group = asText(envelopeRoot.get("group"));
    String name = asText(envelopeRoot.get("name"));
    String uuid = asText(envelopeRoot.get("uuid"));
    DefinitionType type = parseType(typeText);
    if (type == DefinitionType.UNKNOWN || !isSupportedDecodeType(type)) {
      logUnknownTypeWithDedupe(group, typeText, name, uuid);
      return null;
    }
    DefinitionEnvelope envelope = decodeEnvelope(envelopeRoot, type);
    if (envelope == null) {
      return null;
    }
    try {
      Definition decoded =
          switch (type) {
            case APP -> MAPPER.treeToValue(root, DefinitionApp.class);
            case ENVIRONMENT -> MAPPER.treeToValue(root, DefinitionEnvironment.class);
            case CONNECTION -> MAPPER.treeToValue(root, DefinitionConnection.class);
            case DATASET -> MAPPER.treeToValue(root, DefinitionDataset.class);
            case STREAM -> MAPPER.treeToValue(root, DefinitionStream.class);
            case INGEST -> MAPPER.treeToValue(root, DefinitionIngest.class);
            case INGEST_SOURCE -> MAPPER.treeToValue(root, DefinitionIngestSource.class);
            case PLATFORM -> MAPPER.treeToValue(root, DefinitionPlatform.class);
            case SCHEMA -> MAPPER.treeToValue(root, DefinitionSchema.class);
            case SERVICE -> MAPPER.treeToValue(root, DefinitionService.class);
            case ENTITLEMENT -> MAPPER.treeToValue(root, DefinitionEntitlement.class);
            case CONFIG -> MAPPER.treeToValue(root, DefinitionConfig.class);
            case CONFIG_LAYER -> MAPPER.treeToValue(root, DefinitionConfigLayer.class);
            case CONFIG_CHANGE -> MAPPER.treeToValue(root, DefinitionConfigChange.class);
            case STATUS_APP -> MAPPER.treeToValue(root, DefinitionStatusApp.class);
            case STATUS_SERVICE -> MAPPER.treeToValue(root, DefinitionStatusService.class);
            case STATUS_DATA -> MAPPER.treeToValue(root, DefinitionStatusData.class);
            case HEARTBEAT_SERVICE -> MAPPER.treeToValue(root, DefinitionHbService.class);
            default -> throw new IllegalArgumentException("Unsupported definition type=" + type);
          };
      if (decoded.envelope() == null) {
        throw new DefinitionDecodeException(
            "Decoded definition missing envelope for type=" + type, envelope, root.deepCopy(), null);
      }
      return decoded;
    } catch (DefinitionDecodeException ex) {
      throw ex;
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      throw new DefinitionDecodeException(
          "Unable to decode definition for type=" + type, envelope, root.deepCopy(), ex);
    }
  }

  private static DefinitionEnvelope decodeEnvelope(ObjectNode envelopeNode, DefinitionType type) {
    String group = asText(envelopeNode.get("group"));
    String name = asText(envelopeNode.get("name"));
    if (isBlank(group) || isBlank(name)) {
      return null;
    }
    DefinitionEnvelope envelope =
        new DefinitionEnvelope(
            group,
            type,
            name,
            asText(envelopeNode.get("uuid")),
            asBoolean(envelopeNode.get("enabled")),
            asText(envelopeNode.get("lifecycleStatus")),
            asText(envelopeNode.get("createdTimeUtc")),
            asText(envelopeNode.get("createdBy")),
            asText(envelopeNode.get("updatedTimeUtc")),
            asText(envelopeNode.get("updatedBy")));
    return envelope;
  }

  private static DefinitionType parseType(String value) {
    if (isBlank(value)) {
      return DefinitionType.UNKNOWN;
    }
    try {
      return DefinitionType.valueOf(value);
    } catch (IllegalArgumentException ex) {
      return DefinitionType.UNKNOWN;
    }
  }

  private static String asText(JsonNode node) {
    if (node == null || node.isNull() || !node.isTextual()) {
      return null;
    }
    return node.textValue();
  }

  private static Boolean asBoolean(JsonNode node) {
    return node == null || node.isNull() || !node.isBoolean() ? null : node.booleanValue();
  }

  private static boolean isBlank(String value) {
    return value == null || value.isBlank();
  }

  private static void logUnknownTypeWithDedupe(
      String group, String typeText, String name, String uuid) {
    String key = safe(group) + "|" + safe(typeText) + "|" + safe(name) + "|" + safe(uuid);
    long now = System.currentTimeMillis();
    Long last = UNKNOWN_TYPE_LAST_LOG.get(key);
    if (last != null && now - last <= UNKNOWN_TYPE_LOG_WINDOW_MS) {
      return;
    }
    UNKNOWN_TYPE_LAST_LOG.put(key, now);
    LOGGER.debug("[Discovery][UnknownType][Ignored] group={} typeText={} name={} uuid={}", group, typeText, name, uuid);
  }

  private static String safe(String value) {
    return value == null ? "" : value;
  }

  private static boolean isSupportedDecodeType(DefinitionType type) {
    if (type == null) {
      return false;
    }
    return switch (type) {
      case APP,
          ENVIRONMENT,
          CONNECTION,
          DATASET,
          STREAM,
          INGEST,
          INGEST_SOURCE,
          PLATFORM,
          SCHEMA,
          SERVICE,
          ENTITLEMENT,
          CONFIG,
          CONFIG_LAYER,
          CONFIG_CHANGE,
          STATUS_APP,
          STATUS_SERVICE,
          STATUS_DATA,
          HEARTBEAT_SERVICE -> true;
      default -> false;
    };
  }

  public static final class DefinitionDecodeException extends RuntimeException {
    private final DefinitionEnvelope envelope;
    private final JsonNode payload;

    public DefinitionDecodeException(
        String message, DefinitionEnvelope envelope, JsonNode payload, Throwable cause) {
      super(message, cause);
      this.envelope = envelope;
      this.payload = payload;
    }

    public DefinitionEnvelope getEnvelope() {
      return envelope;
    }

    public JsonNode getPayload() {
      return payload;
    }
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.scope;

import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Set;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public record DiscoveryScope(
    String primaryGroup,
    Set<String> visibleGroups,
    Set<String> visibleAssetIds,
    Map<String, List<String>> visibilityReasons,
    String subject,
    String delegatedSubject) {
  private static final String PLATFORM_GROUP = "platform";

  public DiscoveryScope {
    String normalizedPrimary = normalize(primaryGroup);
    String normalizedSubject = normalize(subject);
    String normalizedDelegated = normalize(delegatedSubject);

    LinkedHashSet<String> normalizedGroups = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    if (visibleGroups != null) {
      for (String group : visibleGroups) {
        String normalizedGroup = normalize(group);
        if (normalizedGroup != null) {
          normalizedGroups.add(normalizedGroup);
        }
      }
    }
    if (normalizedPrimary != null) {
      normalizedGroups.add(normalizedPrimary);
    }
    normalizedGroups.add(PLATFORM_GROUP);

    LinkedHashSet<String> normalizedAssets = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    if (visibleAssetIds != null) {
      for (String assetId : visibleAssetIds) {
        String normalizedAsset = normalize(assetId);
        if (normalizedAsset != null) {
          normalizedAssets.add(normalizedAsset);
        }
      }
    }

    LinkedHashMap<String, List<String>> normalizedReasons = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    if (visibilityReasons != null) {
      for (Map.Entry<String, List<String>> entry : visibilityReasons.entrySet()) {
        String group = normalize(entry.getKey());
        if (group == null) {
          continue;
        }
        LinkedHashSet<String> reasons = new LinkedHashSet<>();
        List<String> values = entry.getValue();
        if (values != null) {
          for (String reason : values) {
            String normalizedReason = normalize(reason);
            if (normalizedReason != null) {
              reasons.add(normalizedReason);
            }
          }
        }
        normalizedReasons.put(group, reasons.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(reasons));
      }
    }

    for (String group : normalizedGroups) {
      normalizedReasons.computeIfAbsent(group, ignored -> defaultReasons(group, normalizedPrimary));
    }

    primaryGroup = normalizedPrimary;
    visibleGroups = Set.copyOf(normalizedGroups);
    visibleAssetIds = Set.copyOf(normalizedAssets);
    visibilityReasons = Map.copyOf(normalizedReasons);
    subject = normalizedSubject;
    delegatedSubject = normalizedDelegated;
  }

  public static DiscoveryScope primaryOnly(String primaryGroup, String subject, String delegatedSubject) {
    return new DiscoveryScope(primaryGroup, Set.of(), Set.of(), Map.of(), subject, delegatedSubject);
  }

  public boolean includesGroup(String group) {
    String normalizedGroup = normalize(group);
    return normalizedGroup != null && visibleGroups.contains(normalizedGroup);
  }

  public DiscoveryScope withGroupVisibility(
      Set<String> groups, Set<String> assetIds, Map<String, List<String>> reasons) {
    return new DiscoveryScope(primaryGroup, groups, assetIds, reasons, subject, delegatedSubject);
  }

  private static List<String> defaultReasons(String group, String primaryGroup) {
    if (Objects.equals(group, PLATFORM_GROUP)) {
      return List.of("platform-model");
    }
    if (primaryGroup != null && Objects.equals(group, primaryGroup)) {
      return List.of("session-primary-group");
    }
    return List.of();
  }

  private static String normalize(String value) {
    return Strings.trimToNull(value);
  }
}


FILE: DiscoveryScopeDiff.java

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.scope;

import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Set;

public record DiscoveryScopeDiff(
    DiscoveryScope previous,
    DiscoveryScope current,
    Set<String> addedGroups,
    Set<String> removedGroups,
    Set<String> addedAssetIds,
    Set<String> removedAssetIds) {

  public DiscoveryScopeDiff {
    addedGroups = addedGroups == null ? Set.of() : Set.copyOf(addedGroups);
    removedGroups = removedGroups == null ? Set.of() : Set.copyOf(removedGroups);
    addedAssetIds = addedAssetIds == null ? Set.of() : Set.copyOf(addedAssetIds);
    removedAssetIds = removedAssetIds == null ? Set.of() : Set.copyOf(removedAssetIds);
  }

  public static DiscoveryScopeDiff between(DiscoveryScope previous, DiscoveryScope current) {
    DiscoveryScope baseline = previous == null ? DiscoveryScope.primaryOnly(null, null, null) : previous;
    DiscoveryScope next = current == null ? DiscoveryScope.primaryOnly(null, null, null) : current;

    Set<String> addedGroups = difference(next.visibleGroups(), baseline.visibleGroups());
    Set<String> removedGroups = difference(baseline.visibleGroups(), next.visibleGroups());
    Set<String> addedAssetIds = difference(next.visibleAssetIds(), baseline.visibleAssetIds());
    Set<String> removedAssetIds = difference(baseline.visibleAssetIds(), next.visibleAssetIds());
    return new DiscoveryScopeDiff(previous, current, addedGroups, removedGroups, addedAssetIds, removedAssetIds);
  }

  public boolean changed() {
    return !addedGroups.isEmpty()
        || !removedGroups.isEmpty()
        || !addedAssetIds.isEmpty()
        || !removedAssetIds.isEmpty()
        || !Objects.equals(previous, current);
  }

  private static Set<String> difference(Set<String> left, Set<String> right) {
    LinkedHashSet<String> values = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    if (left != null) {
      values.addAll(left);
    }
    if (right != null) {
      values.removeAll(right);
    }
    return values.isEmpty() ? Set.of() : Set.copyOf(values);
  }
}


FILE: DiscoveryVisibilityManager.java
