package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.scope;

import java.util.List;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.concurrent.ExecutorService;
import java.util.concurrent.Executors;
import java.util.concurrent.ThreadFactory;
import java.util.concurrent.atomic.AtomicBoolean;
import java.util.concurrent.atomic.AtomicReference;
import java.util.function.Supplier;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.cache.DiscoveryCache;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.cache.DiscoveryListener;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.Definition;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionEnvelope;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionType;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

public final class DiscoveryVisibilityManager implements AutoCloseable {
  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(DiscoveryVisibilityManager.class);

  private final DiscoveryCache discoveryCache;
  private final DiscoveryScopeResolver scopeResolver;
  private final Supplier<String> primaryGroupSupplier;
  private final Supplier<String> subjectSupplier;
  private final Supplier<String> delegatedSubjectSupplier;
  private final AtomicBoolean started = new AtomicBoolean(false);
  private final AtomicBoolean refreshQueued = new AtomicBoolean(false);
  private final AtomicReference<DiscoveryScope> currentScope = new AtomicReference<>();
  private final AtomicReference<DiscoveryScopeDiff> lastDiff = new AtomicReference<>();
  private final ExecutorService refreshExecutor = Executors.newSingleThreadExecutor(new RefreshThreadFactory());
  private final DiscoveryListener listener =
      new DiscoveryListener() {
        @Override
        public void onUpsert(Definition definition) {
          if (!shouldRefresh(definition == null ? null : definition.envelope())) {
            return;
          }
          requestRefresh("upsert");
        }

        @Override
        public void onDelete(DefinitionEnvelope envelope) {
          if (!shouldRefresh(envelope)) {
            return;
          }
          requestRefresh("delete");
        }
      };

  public DiscoveryVisibilityManager(
      DiscoveryCache discoveryCache,
      DiscoveryScopeResolver scopeResolver,
      Supplier<String> primaryGroupSupplier,
      Supplier<String> subjectSupplier,
      Supplier<String> delegatedSubjectSupplier) {
    this.discoveryCache = Objects.requireNonNull(discoveryCache, "discoveryCache");
    this.scopeResolver = Objects.requireNonNull(scopeResolver, "scopeResolver");
    this.primaryGroupSupplier = Objects.requireNonNull(primaryGroupSupplier, "primaryGroupSupplier");
    this.subjectSupplier = Objects.requireNonNull(subjectSupplier, "subjectSupplier");
    this.delegatedSubjectSupplier =
        Objects.requireNonNull(delegatedSubjectSupplier, "delegatedSubjectSupplier");
  }

  public void start() {
    if (!started.compareAndSet(false, true)) {
      return;
    }
    discoveryCache.addListener(listener);
    refreshNow("initial");
  }

  public DiscoveryScope currentScope() {
    DiscoveryScope scope = currentScope.get();
    if (scope != null) {
      return scope;
    }
    return discoveryCache.discoveryScope();
  }

  public DiscoveryScopeDiff lastDiff() {
    return lastDiff.get();
  }

  public void refreshNow(String reason) {
    if (!started.get()) {
      return;
    }
    synchronized (this) {
      String primaryGroup = normalize(primaryGroupSupplier.get());
      String subject = normalize(subjectSupplier.get());
      String delegatedSubject = normalize(delegatedSubjectSupplier.get());
      List<Definition> definitions = discoveryCache.allDefinitions();
      DiscoveryScope resolvedScope =
          scopeResolver.resolve(primaryGroup, subject, delegatedSubject, definitions);
      DiscoveryScope previous = currentScope.get();
      DiscoveryScopeDiff diff = DiscoveryScopeDiff.between(previous, resolvedScope);
      if (previous != null && !diff.changed()) {
        return;
      }
      discoveryCache.updateDiscoveryScope(resolvedScope);
      currentScope.set(resolvedScope);
      lastDiff.set(diff);
      LOGGER.info("[DiscoveryScope] reason={} visibleGroups={} addedGroups={} removedGroups={} visibleAssets={}", normalize(reason), resolvedScope.visibleGroups().size(), diff.addedGroups().size(), diff.removedGroups().size(), resolvedScope.visibleAssetIds().size());
    }
  }

  @Override
  public void close() {
    discoveryCache.removeListener(listener);
    refreshExecutor.shutdownNow();
    started.set(false);
  }

  private void requestRefresh(String reason) {
    if (!started.get()) {
      return;
    }
    if (!refreshQueued.compareAndSet(false, true)) {
      return;
    }
    refreshExecutor.execute(
        () -> {
          try {
            refreshNow(reason);
          } finally {
            refreshQueued.set(false);
          }
        });
  }

  private static boolean shouldRefresh(DefinitionEnvelope envelope) {
    DefinitionType type = envelope == null ? null : envelope.type();
    return type == DefinitionType.ENTITLEMENT || type == DefinitionType.PLATFORM;
  }

  private static String normalize(String value) {
    return Strings.trimToNull(value);
  }

  private static final class RefreshThreadFactory implements ThreadFactory {
    @Override
    public Thread newThread(Runnable runnable) {
      Thread thread = new Thread(runnable, "fabric-discovery-scope-refresh");
      thread.setDaemon(true);
      return thread;
    }
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.core.data;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Set;
import java.util.regex.Matcher;
import java.util.regex.Pattern;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.core.EntitlementObligations;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.schemas.SchemaModel;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class DataColumnMaskPlanner {
  private static final Comparator<String> NAME_ORDER =
      Comparator.comparing((String value) -> value.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT))
          .thenComparing(Comparator.naturalOrder());
  private static final Pattern PREFIX_PATTERN =
      Pattern.compile("^PREFIX\\s*[(:_]\\s*(\\d+)\\s*[)]?$", Pattern.CASE_INSENSITIVE);

  private DataColumnMaskPlanner() {}

  public static ColumnMaskPlan planRead(
      DataEntitlements entitlements,
      DataEntitlements.Identity identity,
      String datasetCanonicalId,
      SchemaModel schema) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(entitlements, "entitlements");
    String datasetId = trimToNull(datasetCanonicalId);
    if (datasetId == null) {
      return denied("DENIED: no column mask decision for dataset <unknown>");
    }

    DataEntitlements.Decision decision;
    try {
      decision = entitlements.authorizeRead(identity, datasetId);
    } catch (RuntimeException ex) {
      return denied("DENIED: no column mask decision for dataset " + datasetId);
    }
    if (decision == null) {
      return denied("DENIED: no column mask decision for dataset " + datasetId);
    }
    if (!decision.allowed()) {
      return denied(denyReason(datasetId, decision.reason()));
    }

    EntitlementObligations obligations =
        decision.obligations() == null ? EntitlementObligations.empty() : decision.obligations();
    Map<String, String> maskByColumn = normalizeMaskMap(obligations.columnsMask());
    Set<String> allowColumns = normalizeAllowList(obligations.columnsAllow());
    boolean hasAllowList = !allowColumns.isEmpty();
    if (!hasAllowList && maskByColumn.isEmpty()) {
      return new ColumnMaskPlan(true, null, List.of(), List.of(), List.of("ALLOW: no column masks"));
    }

    List<SchemaModel.Field> orderedFields = orderedFields(schema);
    if (orderedFields.isEmpty()) {
      return denied("DENIED: schema required for column masking dataset=" + datasetId);
    }

    List<String> projection = new ArrayList<>(orderedFields.size());
    List<String> maskedColumns = new ArrayList<>();
    List<String> deniedColumns = new ArrayList<>();
    Set<String> schemaColumns = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    for (SchemaModel.Field field : orderedFields) {
      String columnName = Strings.requireNonBlank(field == null ? null : field.name(), "schema.field.name");
      schemaColumns.add(columnName.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT));
      String columnKey = columnName.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
      String expression = quoteIdentifier(columnName);
      boolean masked = false;
      if (hasAllowList && !allowColumns.contains(columnKey)) {
        expression = "NULL";
        masked = true;
        deniedColumns.add(columnName);
      } else {
        String rawMask = maskByColumn.get(columnKey);
        if (rawMask != null) {
          MaskRender render = renderMaskExpression(columnName, field.type(), rawMask);
          if (render.error() != null) {
            return denied("DENIED: " + render.error() + " dataset=" + datasetId);
          }
          expression = render.expression();
          masked = true;
        }
      }
      if (masked) {
        maskedColumns.add(columnName);
      }
      projection.add(expression + " as " + quoteIdentifier(columnName));
    }

    for (Map.Entry<String, String> entry : maskByColumn.entrySet()) {
      if (!schemaColumns.contains(entry.getKey())) {
        return denied(
            "DENIED: schema required for column masking dataset="
                + datasetId
                + " column="
                + entry.getKey());
      }
    }

    return new ColumnMaskPlan(
        true,
        String.join(", ", projection),
        List.copyOf(maskedColumns),
        List.copyOf(deniedColumns),
        List.of("ALLOW"));
  }

  private static List<SchemaModel.Field> orderedFields(SchemaModel schema) {
    if (schema == null || schema.getFields() == null || schema.getFields().isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<SchemaModel.Field> fields = new ArrayList<>();
    for (SchemaModel.Field field : schema.getFields()) {
      if (field != null && trimToNull(field.name()) != null) {
        fields.add(field);
      }
    }
    return List.copyOf(fields);
  }

  private static String denyReason(String datasetId, String decisionReason) {
    String reason = trimToNull(decisionReason);
    if (reason == null) {
      return "DENIED: no column mask decision for dataset " + datasetId;
    }
    if (reason.regionMatches(true, 0, "DENIED:", 0, "DENIED:".length())) {
      return reason;
    }
    return "DENIED: " + reason;
  }

  private static Set<String> normalizeAllowList(List<String> columnsAllow) {
    if (columnsAllow == null || columnsAllow.isEmpty()) {
      return Set.of();
    }
    List<String> normalized = new ArrayList<>();
    for (String column : columnsAllow) {
      String value = trimToNull(column);
      if (value != null) {
        normalized.add(value.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT));
      }
    }
    normalized.sort(NAME_ORDER);
    return Set.copyOf(new LinkedHashSet<>(normalized));
  }

  private static Map<String, String> normalizeMaskMap(Map<String, String> columnsMask) {
    if (columnsMask == null || columnsMask.isEmpty()) {
      return Map.of();
    }
    List<String> keys = new ArrayList<>();
    for (String key : columnsMask.keySet()) {
      String normalized = trimToNull(key);
      if (normalized != null) {
        keys.add(normalized);
      }
    }
    keys.sort(NAME_ORDER);
    Map<String, String> normalized = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (String key : keys) {
      String lower = key.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
      if (normalized.containsKey(lower)) {
        continue;
      }
      String raw = trimToNull(columnsMask.get(key));
      normalized.put(lower, raw == null ? "NULL" : raw);
    }
    return Map.copyOf(normalized);
  }

  private static MaskRender renderMaskExpression(
      String columnName, SchemaModel.FieldType type, String maskSpecRaw) {
    String maskSpec = trimToNull(maskSpecRaw);
    if (maskSpec == null) {
      return new MaskRender("NULL", null);
    }
    String upper = maskSpec.toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT);
    String ref = quoteIdentifier(columnName);
    if ("NULL".equals(upper)) {
      return new MaskRender("NULL", null);
    }
    if ("REDACT".equals(upper) || "REDACTED".equals(upper)) {
      if (isString(type)) {
        return new MaskRender("'REDACTED'", null);
      }
      if (isNumber(type)) {
        return new MaskRender("0", null);
      }
      return new MaskRender("NULL", null);
    }
    if ("HASH".equals(upper) || "SHA256".equals(upper)) {
      if (isString(type)) {
        return new MaskRender("sha256(cast(" + ref + " as varchar))", null);
      }
      return new MaskRender("NULL", null);
    }
    if (upper.startsWith("PREFIX")) {
      Matcher matcher = PREFIX_PATTERN.matcher(maskSpec);
      if (!matcher.matches()) {
        return new MaskRender(
            null, "unsupported column mask column=" + columnName + " mask=" + maskSpecRaw);
      }
      int length;
      try {
        length = Integer.parseInt(matcher.group(1));
      } catch (RuntimeException ex) {
        return new MaskRender(
            null, "unsupported column mask column=" + columnName + " mask=" + maskSpecRaw);
      }
      if (length < 0) {
        return new MaskRender(
            null, "unsupported column mask column=" + columnName + " mask=" + maskSpecRaw);
      }
      if (!isString(type)) {
        return new MaskRender("NULL", null);
      }
      return new MaskRender("left(cast(" + ref + " as varchar), " + length + ") || '***'", null);
    }
    return new MaskRender(
        null, "unsupported column mask column=" + columnName + " mask=" + maskSpecRaw);
  }

  private static boolean isString(SchemaModel.FieldType type) {
    return type == SchemaModel.FieldType.STRING;
  }

  private static boolean isNumber(SchemaModel.FieldType type) {
    return type == SchemaModel.FieldType.INT32
        || type == SchemaModel.FieldType.INT64
        || type == SchemaModel.FieldType.FLOAT64;
  }

  private static ColumnMaskPlan denied(String reason) {
    return new ColumnMaskPlan(false, null, List.of(), List.of(), List.of(reason));
  }

  private static String quoteIdentifier(String value) {
    String identifier = Strings.requireNonBlank(value, "identifier");
    return "\"" + identifier.replace("\"", "\"\"") + "\"";
  }

  private static String trimToNull(String value) {
    if (value == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String trimmed = value.trim();
    return trimmed.isEmpty() ? null : trimmed;
  }

  public record ColumnMaskPlan(
      boolean allowed,
      String projectionSql,
      List<String> maskedColumns,
      List<String> deniedColumns,
      List<String> reasons) {
    public ColumnMaskPlan {
      maskedColumns = maskedColumns == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(maskedColumns);
      deniedColumns = deniedColumns == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(deniedColumns);
      reasons = reasons == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(reasons);
    }
  }

  private record MaskRender(String expression, String error) {}
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.core.data;

import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.CanonicalIds;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.core.EntitlementObligations;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Namespaces;

public interface DataEntitlements {
  String READ_ACTION = "read";

  record Identity(String subject, String delegatedSubject) {}

  record Decision(
      boolean allowed,
      String reason,
      String rewritePayload,
      EntitlementObligations obligations) {
    public Decision {
      obligations = obligations == null ? EntitlementObligations.empty() : obligations;
    }

    public Decision(boolean allowed, String reason, String rewritePayload) {
      this(allowed, reason, rewritePayload, EntitlementObligations.empty());
    }
  }

  Decision authorizeRead(Identity identity, String datasetCanonicalId);

  default Decision authorizeWrite(Identity identity, String datasetCanonicalId) {
    return new Decision(false, "DENIED write is not implemented", null);
  }

  default void requireReadAllowed(Identity identity, String datasetCanonicalId) {
    Decision decision = authorizeRead(identity, datasetCanonicalId);
    if (decision == null || !decision.allowed()) {
      String reason = decision == null ? null : decision.reason();
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(reason == null ? "DENIED" : reason);
    }
  }

  static String readAction() {
    return READ_ACTION;
  }

  static String canonicalDatasetResourceId(String group, String namespace, String name) {
    String trimmedGroup = trim(group);
    String trimmedNamespace = Namespaces.resolveNamespace(namespace);
    String trimmedName = trim(name);
    if (trimmedGroup == null || trimmedNamespace == null || trimmedName == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("dataset group/namespace/name is required");
    }
    String resourceId = "dataset:" + trimmedGroup + "/" + trimmedNamespace + "/" + trimmedName;
    CanonicalIds.validate(resourceId);
    return resourceId;
  }

  static String requireDatasetResourceId(String resourceId) {
    String trimmed = trim(resourceId);
    if (trimmed == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("resourceId is required");
    }
    CanonicalIds.ParsedId parsed = CanonicalIds.parse(trimmed);
    if (!parsed.isDataset()) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("resourceId must be canonical dataset:<group>/<namespace>/<name>");
    }
    return parsed.canonical();
  }

  private static String trim(String value) {
    if (value == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String trimmed = value.trim();
    return trimmed.isEmpty() ? null : trimmed;
  }

  static String subject(Identity identity) {
    if (identity == null || identity.subject() == null || identity.subject().isBlank()) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("identity.subject is required");
    }
    if (identity.delegatedSubject() != null && identity.delegatedSubject().isBlank()) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("identity.delegatedSubject is blank");
    }
    return identity.delegatedSubject() == null ? identity.subject() : identity.delegatedSubject();
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.core.data;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Set;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.core.EntitlementObligations;

public final class DataRowFilterPlanner {
  private static final Comparator<String> PREDICATE_ORDER =
      Comparator.comparing((String value) -> value.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT))
          .thenComparing(Comparator.naturalOrder());

  private DataRowFilterPlanner() {}

  public static RowFilterPlan planRead(
      DataEntitlements entitlements, DataEntitlements.Identity identity, String datasetCanonicalId) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(entitlements, "entitlements");
    String datasetId = trimToNull(datasetCanonicalId);
    if (datasetId == null) {
      return denied("DENIED: no row filter decision for dataset <unknown>");
    }

    DataEntitlements.Decision decision;
    try {
      decision = entitlements.authorizeRead(identity, datasetId);
    } catch (RuntimeException ex) {
      return denied("DENIED: no row filter decision for dataset " + datasetId);
    }
    if (decision == null) {
      return denied("DENIED: no row filter decision for dataset " + datasetId);
    }
    if (!decision.allowed()) {
      return denied(denyReason(datasetId, decision.reason()));
    }

    List<String> predicates = normalizePredicates(decision.obligations());
    String predicateSql = mergePredicates(predicates);
    List<String> reasons = predicateSql == null ? List.of("ALLOW: no row filters") : List.of("ALLOW");
    return new RowFilterPlan(true, predicateSql, reasons);
  }

  private static String denyReason(String datasetId, String decisionReason) {
    String reason = trimToNull(decisionReason);
    if (reason == null) {
      return "DENIED: no row filter decision for dataset " + datasetId;
    }
    if (reason.regionMatches(true, 0, "DENIED:", 0, "DENIED:".length())) {
      return reason;
    }
    return "DENIED: " + reason;
  }

  private static List<String> normalizePredicates(EntitlementObligations obligations) {
    if (obligations == null || obligations.rowFilters().isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<String> ordered = new ArrayList<>();
    for (String predicate : obligations.rowFilters()) {
      String normalized = trimToNull(predicate);
      if (normalized != null) {
        ordered.add(normalized);
      }
    }
    ordered.sort(PREDICATE_ORDER);
    Set<String> deduped = new LinkedHashSet<>(ordered);
    return List.copyOf(deduped);
  }

  private static String mergePredicates(List<String> predicates) {
    if (predicates == null || predicates.isEmpty()) {
      return null;
    }
    StringBuilder combined = new StringBuilder();
    for (int index = 0; index < predicates.size(); index++) {
      if (index > 0) {
        combined.append(" OR ");
      }
      combined.append("(").append(predicates.get(index)).append(")");
    }
    return combined.toString();
  }

  private static RowFilterPlan denied(String reason) {
    return new RowFilterPlan(false, null, List.of(reason));
  }

  private static String trimToNull(String value) {
    if (value == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String trimmed = value.trim();
    return trimmed.isEmpty() ? null : trimmed;
  }

  public record RowFilterPlan(boolean allowed, String predicateSql, List<String> reasons) {
    public RowFilterPlan {
      reasons = reasons == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(reasons);
    }
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.core.data;

import java.util.List;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class DataWriteAuthorization {
  private static final String WRITE_DENIED_PREFIX = "WRITE_DENIED";
  private static final String WRITE_NO_DECISION = "no decision";

  private DataWriteAuthorization() {}

  public static void requireWrite(
      DataEntitlements entitlements,
      DataEntitlements.Identity identity,
      String datasetId,
      String operation,
      List<String> columnsOrNull) {
    String canonicalDatasetId = DataEntitlements.requireDatasetResourceId(datasetId);
    DataWritePlanner.WritePlan plan =
        DataWritePlanner.planWrite(
            entitlements,
            identity,
            canonicalDatasetId,
            new DataWritePlanner.WriteRequest(operation, columnsOrNull));
    if (plan.allowed()) {
      return;
    }
    String reason =
        plan.reasons() == null || plan.reasons().isEmpty()
            ? WRITE_NO_DECISION
            : Strings.firstNonBlank(plan.reasons().get(0), WRITE_NO_DECISION);
    throw new IllegalStateException(
        WRITE_DENIED_PREFIX
            + " dataset="
            + canonicalDatasetId
            + " subject="
            + effectiveSubject(identity)
            + " reason="
            + reason);
  }

  private static String effectiveSubject(DataEntitlements.Identity identity) {
    if (identity == null) {
      return "<unknown>";
    }
    try {
      return DataEntitlements.subject(identity);
    } catch (RuntimeException ex) {
      return "<unknown>";
    }
  }
}


FILE: DataWritePlanner.java

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.core.data;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Objects;

public final class DataWritePlanner {
  private static final Comparator<String> REASON_ORDER =
      Comparator.comparing((String value) -> value.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT))
          .thenComparing(Comparator.naturalOrder());

  private DataWritePlanner() {}

  public static WritePlan planWrite(
      DataEntitlements entitlements,
      DataEntitlements.Identity identity,
      String datasetId,
      WriteRequest request) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(entitlements, "entitlements");
    Objects.requireNonNull(request, "request");
    String canonicalDatasetId = DataEntitlements.requireDatasetResourceId(datasetId);
    DataEntitlements.Decision decision;
    try {
      decision = entitlements.authorizeWrite(identity, canonicalDatasetId);
    } catch (RuntimeException ex) {
      return denied("no decision");
    }
    if (decision == null) {
      return denied("no decision");
    }
    String reason = normalizeReason(decision.reason());
    if (!decision.allowed()) {
      return denied(reason);
    }
    return new WritePlan(true, reason == null ? List.of() : normalizeReasons(List.of(reason)));
  }

  private static WritePlan denied(String reason) {
    return new WritePlan(false, normalizeReasons(List.of(reason)));
  }

  private static String normalizeReason(String reason) {
    String trimmed = trimToNull(reason);
    return trimmed == null ? null : trimmed;
  }

  private static List<String> normalizeReasons(List<String> reasons) {
    if (reasons == null || reasons.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of("no decision");
    }
    List<String> ordered = new ArrayList<>();
    for (String reason : reasons) {
      String normalized = trimToNull(reason);
      if (normalized != null) {
        ordered.add(normalized);
      }
    }
    if (ordered.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of("no decision");
    }
    ordered.sort(REASON_ORDER);
    return List.copyOf(new LinkedHashSet<>(ordered));
  }

  private static String trimToNull(String value) {
    if (value == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String trimmed = value.trim();
    return trimmed.isEmpty() ? null : trimmed;
  }

  public record WriteRequest(String operation, List<String> columns) {
    public WriteRequest {
      operation = trimToNull(operation);
      if (operation == null) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("operation is required");
      }
      columns = columns == null ? null : List.copyOf(columns);
    }
  }

  public record WritePlan(boolean allowed, List<String> reasons) {
    public WritePlan {
      reasons = reasons == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(reasons);
    }
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.core.services;

import java.util.HashMap;
import java.util.Map;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.core.EntitlementsAction;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.core.EntitlementsScopeType;

public interface ServiceEntitlements {
  enum Transport {
    GRPC,
    ARROW_FLIGHT,
    ARROW_FLIGHT_INGEST,
    ARROW_FLIGHT_SQL,
    AMPS
  }

  enum Action {
    START(EntitlementsAction.START),
    INVOKE(EntitlementsAction.INVOKE),
    READ(EntitlementsAction.READ),
    WRITE(EntitlementsAction.WRITE);

    private final EntitlementsAction canonical;

    Action(EntitlementsAction canonical) {
      this.canonical = canonical;
    }

    public EntitlementsAction canonical() {
      return canonical;
    }
  }

  record Identity(String subject, String delegatedSubject) {}

  record Request(
      Transport transport,
      Action action,
      String serviceResourceId,
      String operationName,
      String datasetId,
      String requestPayload,
      Map<String, String> bindings,
      Map<String, String> metadata) {
    public Request {
      bindings = safeMap(bindings);
      metadata = safeMap(metadata);
    }
  }

  record Decision(boolean allowed, String reason, String rewritePayload) {}

  Decision authorize(Identity identity, Request request);

  default void requireAllowed(Identity identity, Request request) {
    Decision decision = authorize(identity, request);
    if (decision == null || !decision.allowed()) {
      String reason = decision == null ? null : decision.reason();
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(reason == null ? "DENIED" : reason);
    }
  }

  static Map<String, String> safeMap(Map<String, String> m) {
    if (m == null || m.isEmpty()) {
      return Map.of();
    }
    return Map.copyOf(m);
  }

  static Map<String, String> emptyMap() {
    return Map.of();
  }

  static EntitlementsScopeType scopeTypeEnum() {
    return EntitlementsScopeType.SERVICE;
  }

  static String scopeType() {
    return scopeTypeEnum().toWire();
  }

  static String policyAction(EntitlementsAction action) {
    if (action == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("action is required");
    }
    return switch (action) {
      case START -> "service.start";
      case INVOKE, READ, WRITE -> "service.invoke";
    };
  }

  static String policyAction(Action action) {
    if (action == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("action is required");
    }
    return policyAction(action.canonical());
  }

  static ContextBuilder context(String transport) {
    return new ContextBuilder(transport);
  }

  static String canonicalServiceResourceId(String group, String name) {
    String trimmedGroup = trim(group);
    String trimmedName = trim(name);
    if (trimmedGroup == null || trimmedName == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("service group/name is required");
    }
    String resourceId = "service:" + trimmedGroup + "/" + trimmedName;
    return requireServiceResourceId(resourceId);
  }

  static String requireServiceResourceId(String resourceId) {
    String trimmed = requireAssetResourceId(resourceId);
    if (!"service".equals(assetTypePrefix(trimmed))) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(
          "service resourceId must be canonical service:<group>/<name>");
    }
    return trimmed;
  }

  static String canonicalAppResourceId(String group, String name) {
    String trimmedGroup = trim(group);
    String trimmedName = trim(name);
    if (trimmedGroup == null || trimmedName == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("app group/name is required");
    }
    return requireAppResourceId("app:" + trimmedGroup + "/" + trimmedName);
  }

  static String requireAppResourceId(String resourceId) {
    String trimmed = requireAssetResourceId(resourceId);
    if (!"app".equals(assetTypePrefix(trimmed))) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("app resourceId must be canonical app:<group>/<name>");
    }
    return trimmed;
  }

  static String canonicalConfigResourceId(String group, String configId) {
    String trimmedGroup = trim(group);
    String trimmedConfigId = trim(configId);
    if (trimmedGroup == null || trimmedConfigId == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("config group/configId is required");
    }
    return requireConfigResourceId("config:" + trimmedGroup + "/" + trimmedConfigId);
  }

  static String canonicalConfigLayerResourceId(String group, String configId, String layerId) {
    String trimmedGroup = trim(group);
    String trimmedConfigId = trim(configId);
    String trimmedLayerId = trim(layerId);
    if (trimmedGroup == null || trimmedConfigId == null || trimmedLayerId == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("config group/configId/layerId is required");
    }
    return requireConfigResourceId(
        "config:" + trimmedGroup + "/" + trimmedConfigId + "/" + trimmedLayerId);
  }

  static String requireConfigResourceId(String resourceId) {
    String trimmed = requireAssetResourceId(resourceId);
    if (!"config".equals(assetTypePrefix(trimmed))) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(
          "config resourceId must be canonical config:<group>/<configId> or config:<group>/<configId>/<layerId>");
    }
    return trimmed;
  }

  static String requireAssetResourceId(String resourceId) {
    String trimmed = trim(resourceId);
    if (trimmed == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("resourceId is required");
    }
    if (!isCanonicalServiceResourceId(trimmed)
        && !isCanonicalAppResourceId(trimmed)
        && !isCanonicalConfigResourceId(trimmed)
        && !isCanonicalConfigLayerResourceId(trimmed)) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(
          "resourceId must be canonical service:<group>/<name>, app:<group>/<name>, config:<group>/<configId>, or config:<group>/<configId>/<layerId>");
    }
    return trimmed;
  }

  static String assetTypePrefix(String resourceId) {
    String canonical = requireAssetResourceId(resourceId);
    int separator = canonical.indexOf(':');
    return separator <= 0 ? "" : canonical.substring(0, separator);
  }

  private static boolean isCanonicalServiceResourceId(String resourceId) {
    return resourceId.matches("^service:[a-zA-Z0-9._-]+/[a-zA-Z0-9._-]+$");
  }

  private static boolean isCanonicalAppResourceId(String resourceId) {
    return resourceId.matches("^app:[a-zA-Z0-9._-]+/[a-zA-Z0-9._-]+$");
  }

  private static boolean isCanonicalConfigResourceId(String resourceId) {
    return resourceId.matches("^config:[a-zA-Z0-9._-]+/[a-zA-Z0-9._-]+$");
  }

  private static boolean isCanonicalConfigLayerResourceId(String resourceId) {
    return resourceId.matches("^config:[a-zA-Z0-9._-]+/[a-zA-Z0-9._-]+/[a-zA-Z0-9._-]+$");
  }

  private static String trim(String value) {
    if (value == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String trimmed = value.trim();
    return trimmed.isEmpty() ? null : trimmed;
  }

  final class Noop implements ServiceEntitlements {
    public static final Noop INSTANCE = new Noop();

    private Noop() {}

    @Override
    public Decision authorize(Identity identity, Request request) {
      return new Decision(true, "NOOP", null);
    }
  }

  final class ContextBuilder {
    private final Map<String, String> context = new HashMap<>();

    private ContextBuilder(String transport) {
      putIfPresent("transport", transport);
    }

    public ContextBuilder withMethod(String methodName) {
      putIfPresent("method", methodName);
      return this;
    }

    public ContextBuilder withServiceGroup(String group) {
      putIfPresent("serviceGroup", group);
      return this;
    }

    public ContextBuilder withServiceName(String name) {
      putIfPresent("serviceName", name);
      return this;
    }

    public ContextBuilder withAttribute(String key, String value) {
      putIfPresent(key, value);
      return this;
    }

    public Map<String, String> build() {
      return context.isEmpty() ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(context);
    }

    private void putIfPresent(String key, String value) {
      String trimmedKey = trim(key);
      String trimmedValue = trim(value);
      if (trimmedKey == null || trimmedValue == null) {
        return;
      }
      context.put(trimmedKey, trimmedValue);
    }
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.provider;

import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Optional;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.cache.DiscoveryCache;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionEnvironment;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionEnvironment.Entitlements.ProviderRegistration;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

public final class DefaultEntitlementProviderRegistry implements EntitlementProviderRegistry {
  private static final Logger LOGGER =
      LoggerFactory.getLogger(DefaultEntitlementProviderRegistry.class);
  private static final String PLATFORM_GROUP = "platform";
  private static final String ENVIRONMENT_NAME = "environment";
  public static final String DEMO_STATIC_PROVIDER_ID = "demo-static";
  public static final String PLATFORM_MODEL_PROVIDER_ID = "platform-model";

  private final Map<String, EntitlementSubjectProvider> providers;
  private final EntitlementSubjectProvider defaultProvider;
  private final String defaultProviderId;

  public DefaultEntitlementProviderRegistry(DiscoveryCache DiscoveryCache) {
    this(
        Objects.requireNonNull(DiscoveryCache, "DiscoveryCache"),
        new EntitlementSubjectProviderPlatform(DiscoveryCache),
        null);
  }

  public DefaultEntitlementProviderRegistry(
      DiscoveryCache DiscoveryCache, EntitlementSubjectProvider platformModelProvider) {
    this(
        Objects.requireNonNull(DiscoveryCache, "DiscoveryCache"),
        Objects.requireNonNull(platformModelProvider, "platformModelProvider"),
        null);
  }

  public DefaultEntitlementProviderRegistry(EntitlementSubjectProvider platformModelProvider) {
    EntitlementSubjectProvider platform =
        Objects.requireNonNull(platformModelProvider, "platformModelProvider");
    this.providers = Map.of(PLATFORM_MODEL_PROVIDER_ID, platform);
    this.defaultProviderId = PLATFORM_MODEL_PROVIDER_ID;
    this.defaultProvider = platform;
    logInitialization(this.providers);
  }

  private DefaultEntitlementProviderRegistry(
      DiscoveryCache DiscoveryCache,
      EntitlementSubjectProvider platformModelProvider,
      String fixedDefaultProviderId) {
    RegistryState state =
        buildRegistryState(
            DiscoveryCache,
            platformModelProvider,
            normalizeProviderId(fixedDefaultProviderId));
    this.providers = state.providers();
    this.defaultProviderId = state.defaultProviderId();
    this.defaultProvider = state.defaultProvider();
    logInitialization(this.providers);
  }

  @Override
  public EntitlementSubjectProvider defaultProvider() {
    return defaultProvider;
  }

  @Override
  public EntitlementSubjectProvider provider(String id) {
    String normalized = normalizeProviderId(id);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return null;
    }
    return providers.get(normalized);
  }

  String defaultProviderIdHint() {
    return defaultProviderId;
  }

  private static RegistryState buildRegistryState(
      DiscoveryCache DiscoveryCache,
      EntitlementSubjectProvider platformModelProvider,
      String fixedDefaultProviderId) {
    LinkedHashMap<String, EntitlementSubjectProvider> built = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    LinkedHashSet<String> knownIds = new LinkedHashSet<>();

    DefinitionEnvironment environment = environmentDefinition(DiscoveryCache);
    DefinitionEnvironment.Entitlements entitlements = environment == null ? null : environment.entitlements();
    String environmentDefaultProviderId =
        entitlements == null ? null : normalizeProviderId(entitlements.defaultProviderId());

    if (entitlements != null && entitlements.providers() != null) {
      for (ProviderRegistration registration : entitlements.providers()) {
        if (registration == null || !enabled(registration.enabled())) {
          continue;
        }

        String providerId = normalizeProviderId(registration.id());
        if (providerId == null) {
          throw new IllegalStateException("Entitlement provider id is required");
        }
        if (!knownIds.add(providerId)) {
          throw new IllegalStateException("Duplicate entitlement provider id: " + providerId);
        }

        String providerType = normalizeProviderId(registration.type());
        if (providerType == null) {
          throw new IllegalStateException("Unknown entitlement provider type: " + registration.type());
        }

        validateProviderConfig(providerId, registration);

        EntitlementSubjectProvider provider =
            createProvider(DiscoveryCache, providerId, providerType, platformModelProvider);
        built.put(providerId, provider);
      }
    }

    built.putIfAbsent(PLATFORM_MODEL_PROVIDER_ID, platformModelProvider);
    knownIds.add(PLATFORM_MODEL_PROVIDER_ID);

    String resolvedDefaultId =
        fixedDefaultProviderId != null
            ? fixedDefaultProviderId
            : environmentDefaultProviderId != null ? environmentDefaultProviderId : PLATFORM_MODEL_PROVIDER_ID;
    EntitlementSubjectProvider resolvedDefaultProvider = built.get(resolvedDefaultId);
    return new RegistryState(
        Map.copyOf(built),
        resolvedDefaultProvider,
        resolvedDefaultId);
  }

  private static EntitlementSubjectProvider createProvider(
      DiscoveryCache DiscoveryCache,
      String providerId,
      String providerType,
      EntitlementSubjectProvider platformModelProvider) {
    if (PLATFORM_MODEL_PROVIDER_ID.equals(providerType)) {
      if (PLATFORM_MODEL_PROVIDER_ID.equals(providerId)) {
        return platformModelProvider;
      }
      return new EntitlementSubjectProviderPlatform(DiscoveryCache);
    }
    if (DEMO_STATIC_PROVIDER_ID.equals(providerType)) {
      return new EntitlementSubjectProviderDemoStatic(DiscoveryCache, providerId);
    }
    throw new IllegalStateException("Unknown entitlement provider type: " + providerType);
  }

  private static void validateProviderConfig(
      String providerId, ProviderRegistration registration) {
    if (registration == null) {
      return;
    }
    Object config = registration.config();
    if (config != null && !(config instanceof Map<?, ?>)) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "Invalid entitlement provider config for provider " + providerId);
    }
  }

  private static DefinitionEnvironment environmentDefinition(DiscoveryCache DiscoveryCache) {
    if (DiscoveryCache == null) {
      return null;
    }
    Optional<DefinitionEnvironment> definition =
        DiscoveryCache.get(DefinitionEnvironment.class, PLATFORM_GROUP, ENVIRONMENT_NAME);
    return definition.orElse(null);
  }

  private static boolean enabled(Boolean value) {
    return value == null || value.booleanValue();
  }

  private static String normalizeProviderId(String value) {
    if (value == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String normalized = value.trim();
    if (normalized.isEmpty()) {
      return null;
    }
    return normalized.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
  }

  private static void logInitialization(Map<String, EntitlementSubjectProvider> providers) {
    List<String> ids = providers == null ? List.of() : providers.keySet().stream().sorted().toList();
    LOGGER.info(
        "[Entitlements][ProvidersInitialized] count={} providers=[{}]",
        ids.size(),
        String.join(",", ids));
  }

  private record RegistryState(
      Map<String, EntitlementSubjectProvider> providers,
      EntitlementSubjectProvider defaultProvider,
      String defaultProviderId) {}
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.provider;

import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.Set;

public final class EntitlementSubjectCandidates {
  private EntitlementSubjectCandidates() {}

  public static Set<String> membershipSubjectCandidates(String subject) {
    String normalized = trimToNull(subject);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return Set.of();
    }
    LinkedHashSet<String> candidates = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    addCandidateVariants(candidates, normalized);
    return Set.copyOf(candidates);
  }

  private static void addCandidateVariants(LinkedHashSet<String> candidates, String value) {
    String normalized = trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return;
    }
    candidates.add(normalized);
    String withoutPrefix = stripUserPrefix(normalized);
    if (withoutPrefix != null) {
      candidates.add(withoutPrefix);
    }
    String beforeRealm = beforeRealm(normalized);
    if (beforeRealm != null) {
      candidates.add(beforeRealm);
    }
    if (withoutPrefix != null) {
      String withoutPrefixBeforeRealm = beforeRealm(withoutPrefix);
      if (withoutPrefixBeforeRealm != null) {
        candidates.add(withoutPrefixBeforeRealm);
      }
    }
  }

  private static String stripUserPrefix(String value) {
    if (value.regionMatches(true, 0, "user:", 0, "user:".length()) && value.length() > "user:".length()) {
      return trimToNull(value.substring("user:".length()));
    }
    return null;
  }

  private static String beforeRealm(String value) {
    int realmSeparator = value.indexOf('@');
    if (realmSeparator > 0) {
      return trimToNull(value.substring(0, realmSeparator));
    }
    return null;
  }

  private static String trimToNull(String value) {
    if (value == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String normalized = value.trim();
    return normalized.isEmpty() ? null : normalized;
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.provider;

import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Optional;
import java.util.Set;
import java.util.concurrent.atomic.AtomicReference;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.cache.DiscoveryCache;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionEnvironment;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionEnvironment.Entitlements.ProviderRegistration;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionEnvelope;

public final class EntitlementSubjectProviderDemoStatic implements EntitlementSubjectProvider {
  private static final String PLATFORM_GROUP = "platform";
  private static final String ENVIRONMENT_NAME = "environment";
  private static final String MISSING_VERSION = "MISSING";

  private final DiscoveryCache DiscoveryCache;
  private final String providerId;
  private final AtomicReference<Snapshot> snapshotRef = new AtomicReference<>(Snapshot.missing());

  public EntitlementSubjectProviderDemoStatic(DiscoveryCache DiscoveryCache, String providerId) {
    this.DiscoveryCache = Objects.requireNonNull(DiscoveryCache, "DiscoveryCache");
    this.providerId = requireProviderId(providerId);
  }

  @Override
  public SubjectContext resolve(ResolveRequest request) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(request, "request");
    Snapshot snapshot = snapshot();
    String subjectId = effectiveSubject(request.subject(), request.delegatedSubject());
    Set<String> candidates = EntitlementSubjectCandidates.membershipSubjectCandidates(subjectId);

    LinkedHashSet<String> directGroups = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    LinkedHashSet<String> effectiveGroups = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> attributes = new LinkedHashMap<>(snapshot.attributes());
    boolean serviceAccount = false;

    for (String candidate : candidates) {
      SubjectEntry entry = snapshot.subjects().get(candidate);
      if (entry == null) {
        continue;
      }
      directGroups.addAll(entry.directGroups());
      effectiveGroups.addAll(entry.effectiveGroups());
      for (Map.Entry<String, String> attr : entry.attributes().entrySet()) {
        attributes.putIfAbsent(attr.getKey(), attr.getValue());
      }
      serviceAccount = serviceAccount || entry.serviceAccount();
    }

    if (directGroups.isEmpty() && !effectiveGroups.isEmpty()) {
      directGroups.addAll(effectiveGroups);
    }
    if (effectiveGroups.isEmpty() && !directGroups.isEmpty()) {
      effectiveGroups.addAll(directGroups);
    }
    if (!serviceAccount) {
      serviceAccount = containsAny(snapshot.serviceAccounts(), candidates);
    }

    return new SubjectContext(
        subjectId,
        directGroups.isEmpty() ? Set.of() : Set.copyOf(directGroups),
        effectiveGroups.isEmpty() ? Set.of() : Set.copyOf(effectiveGroups),
        attributes.isEmpty() ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(attributes),
        serviceAccount);
  }

  @Override
  public String versionKey() {
    return snapshot().versionKey();
  }

  private Snapshot snapshot() {
    Snapshot current = snapshotRef.get();
    Optional<DefinitionEnvironment> definition =
        DiscoveryCache.get(DefinitionEnvironment.class, PLATFORM_GROUP, ENVIRONMENT_NAME);
    if (definition.isEmpty()) {
      if (!MISSING_VERSION.equals(current.versionKey())) {
        Snapshot missing = Snapshot.missing();
        snapshotRef.set(missing);
        return missing;
      }
      return current;
    }

    DefinitionEnvironment environment = definition.get();
    ProviderRegistration registration = findRegistration(environment, providerId);
    if (registration == null) {
      Snapshot missing = Snapshot.missing();
      snapshotRef.set(missing);
      return missing;
    }

    String nextVersion = versionKey(environment.envelope(), registration);
    if (nextVersion.equals(current.versionKey())) {
      return current;
    }

    Snapshot next = snapshotFromRegistration(nextVersion, registration);
    snapshotRef.set(next);
    return next;
  }

  private static Snapshot snapshotFromRegistration(
      String versionKey, ProviderRegistration registration) {
    if (registration == null) {
      return Snapshot.missing();
    }
    Map<String, Object> config = registration.config();
    if (config == null) {
      config = Map.of();
    }

    Map<String, SubjectEntry> subjects = parseSubjects(config.get("subjects"));
    Set<String> serviceAccounts = parseStringSet(config.get("serviceAccounts"));
    Map<String, String> attributes = parseStringMap(config.get("attributes"));
    return new Snapshot(versionKey, subjects, serviceAccounts, attributes);
  }

  private static ProviderRegistration findRegistration(
      DefinitionEnvironment environment, String providerId) {
    if (environment == null || environment.entitlements() == null) {
      return null;
    }
    List<ProviderRegistration> providers = environment.entitlements().providers();
    if (providers == null || providers.isEmpty()) {
      return null;
    }
    for (ProviderRegistration registration : providers) {
      if (registration == null || !enabled(registration.enabled())) {
        continue;
      }
      String id = normalizeProviderId(registration.id());
      if (Objects.equals(providerId, id)) {
        return registration;
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  private static Map<String, SubjectEntry> parseSubjects(Object value) {
    if (!(value instanceof Map<?, ?> rawMap) || rawMap.isEmpty()) {
      return Map.of();
    }
    LinkedHashMap<String, SubjectEntry> parsed = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (Map.Entry<?, ?> rawEntry : rawMap.entrySet()) {
      if (!(rawEntry.getKey() instanceof String rawSubject)) {
        continue;
      }
      String subject = trimToNull(rawSubject);
      if (subject == null) {
        continue;
      }
      SubjectEntry entry = parseSubjectEntry(rawEntry.getValue());
      parsed.put(subject, entry);
    }
    return parsed.isEmpty() ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(parsed);
  }

  private static SubjectEntry parseSubjectEntry(Object value) {
    if (value instanceof Map<?, ?> map) {
      Set<String> directGroups = parseStringSet(map.get("directGroups"));
      Set<String> effectiveGroups = parseStringSet(map.get("effectiveGroups"));
      Map<String, String> attributes = parseStringMap(map.get("attributes"));
      boolean serviceAccount = parseBoolean(map.get("serviceAccount"));
      return new SubjectEntry(directGroups, effectiveGroups, attributes, serviceAccount);
    }
    Set<String> groups = parseStringSet(value);
    return new SubjectEntry(groups, groups, Map.of(), false);
  }

  private static Set<String> parseStringSet(Object value) {
    if (value instanceof String stringValue) {
      String normalized = trimToNull(stringValue);
      return normalized == null ? Set.of() : Set.of(normalized);
    }
    if (!(value instanceof List<?> list) || list.isEmpty()) {
      return Set.of();
    }
    LinkedHashSet<String> parsed = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    for (Object item : list) {
      if (!(item instanceof String stringItem)) {
        continue;
      }
      String normalized = trimToNull(stringItem);
      if (normalized != null) {
        parsed.add(normalized);
      }
    }
    return parsed.isEmpty() ? Set.of() : Set.copyOf(parsed);
  }

  private static Map<String, String> parseStringMap(Object value) {
    if (!(value instanceof Map<?, ?> rawMap) || rawMap.isEmpty()) {
      return Map.of();
    }
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> parsed = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (Map.Entry<?, ?> entry : rawMap.entrySet()) {
      if (!(entry.getKey() instanceof String key) || !(entry.getValue() instanceof String stringValue)) {
        continue;
      }
      String normalizedKey = trimToNull(key);
      String normalizedValue = trimToNull(stringValue);
      if (normalizedKey != null && normalizedValue != null) {
        parsed.put(normalizedKey, normalizedValue);
      }
    }
    return parsed.isEmpty() ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(parsed);
  }

  private static boolean parseBoolean(Object value) {
    if (value instanceof Boolean bool) {
      return bool;
    }
    if (value instanceof String stringValue) {
      return Boolean.parseBoolean(stringValue.trim());
    }
    return false;
  }

  private static boolean containsAny(Set<String> values, Set<String> candidates) {
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty() || candidates == null || candidates.isEmpty()) {
      return false;
    }
    for (String candidate : candidates) {
      if (values.contains(candidate)) {
        return true;
      }
    }
    return false;
  }

  private static String versionKey(
      DefinitionEnvelope envelope, ProviderRegistration registration) {
    String uuid = envelope == null ? null : envelope.uuid();
    String updated = envelope == null ? null : envelope.updatedTimeUtc();
    return String.valueOf(uuid)
        + "|"
        + String.valueOf(updated)
        + "|"
        + String.valueOf(registration.id())
        + "|"
        + String.valueOf(registration.type())
        + "|"
        + String.valueOf(registration.config().hashCode());
  }

  private static String effectiveSubject(String subject, String delegatedSubject) {
    String normalizedSubject = trimToNull(subject);
    if (normalizedSubject == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("request.subject is required");
    }
    if (delegatedSubject == null) {
      return normalizedSubject;
    }
    String normalizedDelegated = trimToNull(delegatedSubject);
    if (normalizedDelegated == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("request.delegatedSubject is blank");
    }
    return normalizedDelegated;
  }

  private static String normalizeProviderId(String value) {
    String normalized = trimToNull(value);
    return normalized == null ? null : normalized.toLowerCase(java.util.Locale.ROOT);
  }

  private static String requireProviderId(String value) {
    String normalized = normalizeProviderId(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("providerId is required");
    }
    return normalized;
  }

  private static boolean enabled(Boolean value) {
    return value == null || value.booleanValue();
  }

  private static String trimToNull(String value) {
    if (value == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String normalized = value.trim();
    return normalized.isEmpty() ? null : normalized;
  }

  private record Snapshot(
      String versionKey,
      Map<String, SubjectEntry> subjects,
      Set<String> serviceAccounts,
      Map<String, String> attributes) {
    private Snapshot {
      subjects = subjects == null || subjects.isEmpty() ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(subjects);
      serviceAccounts =
          serviceAccounts == null || serviceAccounts.isEmpty() ? Set.of() : Set.copyOf(serviceAccounts);
      attributes = attributes == null || attributes.isEmpty() ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(attributes);
    }

    private static Snapshot missing() {
      return new Snapshot(MISSING_VERSION, Map.of(), Set.of(), Map.of());
    }
  }

  private record SubjectEntry(
      Set<String> directGroups,
      Set<String> effectiveGroups,
      Map<String, String> attributes,
      boolean serviceAccount) {
    private SubjectEntry {
      directGroups = directGroups == null || directGroups.isEmpty() ? Set.of() : Set.copyOf(directGroups);
      effectiveGroups =
          effectiveGroups == null || effectiveGroups.isEmpty() ? Set.of() : Set.copyOf(effectiveGroups);
      attributes = attributes == null || attributes.isEmpty() ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(attributes);
    }
  }
}


FILE: EntitlementSubjectProviderPlatform.java

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.provider;

import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Optional;
import java.util.Set;
import java.util.concurrent.atomic.AtomicReference;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.cache.DiscoveryCache;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionEnvelope;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionPlatform;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.simple.PlatformModelMembership;

public final class EntitlementSubjectProviderPlatform implements EntitlementSubjectProvider {
  private static final String PLATFORM_GROUP = "platform";
  private static final String PLATFORM_NAME = "platform";
  private static final String MISSING_VERSION = "MISSING";

  private final DiscoveryCache DiscoveryCache;
  private final AtomicReference<Snapshot> snapshotRef = new AtomicReference<>(Snapshot.missing());

  public EntitlementSubjectProviderPlatform(DiscoveryCache DiscoveryCache) {
    this.DiscoveryCache = Objects.requireNonNull(DiscoveryCache, "DiscoveryCache");
  }

  @Override
  public SubjectContext resolve(ResolveRequest request) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(request, "request");
    Snapshot snapshot = snapshot();
    String subjectId = effectiveSubject(request.subject(), request.delegatedSubject());
    Set<String> candidates = EntitlementSubjectCandidates.membershipSubjectCandidates(subjectId);
    Set<String> groups = groupsForCandidates(snapshot.membershipIndex(), candidates);
    return new SubjectContext(
        subjectId,
        groups,
        groups,
        request.attributes(),
        isServiceAccount(snapshot.serviceAccounts(), subjectId, candidates));
  }

  @Override
  public String versionKey() {
    return snapshot().versionKey();
  }

  public Map<String, Set<String>> membershipIndex() {
    return snapshot().membershipIndex();
  }

  private Snapshot snapshot() {
    Snapshot current = snapshotRef.get();

    Optional<DefinitionPlatform> platformModel =
        DiscoveryCache.get(DefinitionPlatform.class, PLATFORM_GROUP, PLATFORM_NAME);
    if (platformModel.isEmpty()) {
      if (!MISSING_VERSION.equals(current.versionKey())) {
        Snapshot missing = Snapshot.missing();
        snapshotRef.set(missing);
        return missing;
      }
      return current;
    }

    DefinitionPlatform model = platformModel.get();
    String nextVersionKey = platformModelVersionKey(model);
    if (nextVersionKey.equals(current.versionKey())) {
      return current;
    }

    Snapshot next =
        new Snapshot(
            nextVersionKey,
            PlatformModelMembership.buildMembershipIndex(model),
            extractServiceAccounts(model));
    snapshotRef.set(next);
    return next;
  }

  private static Set<String> groupsForCandidates(
      Map<String, Set<String>> membershipIndex, Set<String> candidates) {
    if (membershipIndex == null || membershipIndex.isEmpty() || candidates == null || candidates.isEmpty()) {
      return Set.of();
    }
    LinkedHashSet<String> groups = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    for (String candidate : candidates) {
      Set<String> candidateGroups = membershipIndex.get(candidate);
      if (candidateGroups != null && !candidateGroups.isEmpty()) {
        groups.addAll(candidateGroups);
      }
    }
    return groups.isEmpty() ? Set.of() : Set.copyOf(groups);
  }

  private static boolean isServiceAccount(
      Set<String> serviceAccounts, String subjectId, Set<String> candidates) {
    if (serviceAccounts == null || serviceAccounts.isEmpty()) {
      return false;
    }
    if (serviceAccounts.contains(subjectId)) {
      return true;
    }
    if (candidates == null || candidates.isEmpty()) {
      return false;
    }
    for (String candidate : candidates) {
      if (serviceAccounts.contains(candidate)) {
        return true;
      }
    }
    return false;
  }

  private static Set<String> extractServiceAccounts(DefinitionPlatform model) {
    if (model == null) {
      return Set.of();
    }
    LinkedHashSet<String> values = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    Map<String, DefinitionPlatform.PlatformService> services = model.services();
    if (services != null && !services.isEmpty()) {
      for (Map.Entry<String, DefinitionPlatform.PlatformService> entry : services.entrySet()) {
        String key = trimToNull(entry.getKey());
        if (key != null) {
          values.add(key);
        }
        DefinitionPlatform.PlatformService service = entry.getValue();
        String id = service == null ? null : trimToNull(service.id());
        if (id != null) {
          values.add(id);
        }
      }
    }
    collectServiceAccounts(model.root(), values);
    return values.isEmpty() ? Set.of() : Set.copyOf(values);
  }

  private static void collectServiceAccounts(
      DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode node, LinkedHashSet<String> collected) {
    if (node == null || collected == null) {
      return;
    }
    List<DefinitionPlatform.OrgGroup> groups = node.groups();
    if (groups != null) {
      for (DefinitionPlatform.OrgGroup group : groups) {
        if (group == null || group.serviceIds() == null) {
          continue;
        }
        for (String serviceId : group.serviceIds()) {
          String normalized = trimToNull(serviceId);
          if (normalized != null) {
            collected.add(normalized);
          }
        }
      }
    }
    List<DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode> children = node.ous();
    if (children == null) {
      return;
    }
    for (DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode child : children) {
      collectServiceAccounts(child, collected);
    }
  }

  private static String effectiveSubject(String subject, String delegatedSubject) {
    String normalizedSubject = trimToNull(subject);
    if (normalizedSubject == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("request.subject is required");
    }
    if (delegatedSubject == null) {
      return normalizedSubject;
    }
    String normalizedDelegated = trimToNull(delegatedSubject);
    if (normalizedDelegated == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("request.delegatedSubject is blank");
    }
    return normalizedDelegated;
  }

  private static String platformModelVersionKey(DefinitionPlatform model) {
    DefinitionEnvelope envelope = model == null ? null : model.envelope();
    String uuid = envelope == null ? null : envelope.uuid();
    String updated = envelope == null ? null : envelope.updatedTimeUtc();
    return String.valueOf(uuid) + "|" + String.valueOf(updated);
  }

  private static String trimToNull(String value) {
    if (value == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String normalized = value.trim();
    return normalized.isEmpty() ? null : normalized;
  }

  private record Snapshot(
      String versionKey, Map<String, Set<String>> membershipIndex, Set<String> serviceAccounts) {
    private Snapshot {
      membershipIndex =
          membershipIndex == null || membershipIndex.isEmpty() ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(membershipIndex);
      serviceAccounts =
          serviceAccounts == null || serviceAccounts.isEmpty() ? Set.of() : Set.copyOf(serviceAccounts);
    }

    private static Snapshot missing() {
      return new Snapshot(MISSING_VERSION, Map.of(), Set.of());
    }
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security;

import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Optional;

/**
 * Thread-local user context for core API components.
 */
public final class UserContext {

  private static final ThreadLocal<UserPrincipal> CURRENT = new ThreadLocal<>();

  private UserContext() {}

  public static void set(UserPrincipal principal) {
    if (principal == null) {
      CURRENT.remove();
      return;
    }
    CURRENT.set(principal);
  }

  public static Optional<UserPrincipal> get() {
    return Optional.ofNullable(CURRENT.get());
  }

  public static String getUsernameOrDefault(String fallback) {
    UserPrincipal principal = CURRENT.get();
    if (principal != null && principal.username() != null && !principal.username().isBlank()) {
      return principal.username().trim();
    }
    return fallback;
  }

  public static Map<String, Object> getAttributesOrEmpty() {
    UserPrincipal principal = CURRENT.get();
    return principal == null ? Map.of() : principal.attributes();
  }

  public static void clear() {
    CURRENT.remove();
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security;

import java.util.Collections;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.Map;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

/**
 * Neutral user principal representation for core API components.
 */
public final class UserPrincipal {

  private final String username;
  private final Map<String, Object> attributes;

  public UserPrincipal(String username, Map<String, Object> attributes) {
    this.username = Strings.isBlank(username) ? null : username.trim();
    Map<String, Object> clone = attributes == null ? Map.of() : new LinkedHashMap<>(attributes);
    this.attributes = Collections.unmodifiableMap(clone);
  }

  public String username() {
    return username;
  }

  public Map<String, Object> attributes() {
    return attributes;
  }

  public boolean hasUsername() {
    return Strings.isNotBlank(username);
  }

  public static UserPrincipal anonymous() {
    return new UserPrincipal("anonymous", Map.of());
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.identity;

import java.util.Optional;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class CallerAppContext {
  private static final ThreadLocal<ContextValue> CURRENT = new ThreadLocal<>();

  private CallerAppContext() {}

  public static void set(ContextValue value) {
    if (value == null) {
      CURRENT.remove();
      return;
    }
    CURRENT.set(value);
  }

  public static void set(RequestIdentity identity) {
    if (identity == null) {
      CURRENT.remove();
      return;
    }
    set(new ContextValue(identity.callerAppSubject(), identity.requestId(), identity.traceId()));
  }

  public static Optional<ContextValue> get() {
    return Optional.ofNullable(CURRENT.get());
  }

  public static void clear() {
    CURRENT.remove();
  }

  public record ContextValue(String callerAppSubject, String requestId, String traceId) {
    public ContextValue {
      callerAppSubject = Strings.trimToNull(callerAppSubject);
      requestId = Strings.requireNonBlank(requestId, "requestId");
      traceId = Strings.trimToNull(traceId);
    }

    public boolean hasCallerAppSubject() {
      return Strings.isNotBlank(callerAppSubject);
    }

    public static ContextValue of(
        String callerAppSubject, String requestId, String traceId) {
      return new ContextValue(callerAppSubject, requestId, traceId);
    }
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.identity;

import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public record CallerAppIdentity(String group, String name, String instance) {

  public CallerAppIdentity {
    group = Strings.trimToNull(group);
    name = Strings.trimToNull(name);
    instance = Strings.trimToNull(instance);
  }

  public boolean isPresent() {
    return group != null && name != null;
  }

  public String asSubject() {
    if (!isPresent()) {
      return null;
    }
    return "app:" + group + "/" + name;
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.kerberos;

import java.nio.file.Path;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public record KerberosConfig(
    String getName,
    boolean isEnabled,
    String getPrincipal,
    Path getKeytabPath,
    byte[] getKeytabBytes,
    KerberosKrb5Source getKrb5ConfigSource,
    String getRealm,
    boolean isDebug,
    boolean isAllowSpnegoFallbackToKrb5) {

  public static final String DEFAULT_REALM = "FABRIC.TEST.REALM";
  public static final String DEFAULT_CONTEXT_NAME = "default";

  public KerberosConfig {
    getName = Strings.trimToNull(getName);
    if (getName == null) {
      getName = DEFAULT_CONTEXT_NAME;
    }
    getPrincipal = Strings.trimToNull(getPrincipal);
    getRealm = Strings.trimToNull(getRealm);
    getKeytabPath = getKeytabPath == null ? null : getKeytabPath.toAbsolutePath().normalize();
    getKeytabBytes = getKeytabBytes == null ? null : getKeytabBytes.clone();
    getKrb5ConfigSource = getKrb5ConfigSource == null ? KerberosKrb5Source.DEFAULT : getKrb5ConfigSource;
    validate();
  }

  public KerberosConfig(
      String getName,
      boolean isEnabled,
      String getPrincipal,
      Path getKeytabPath,
      byte[] getKeytabBytes,
      KerberosKrb5Source getKrb5ConfigSource,
      String getRealm,
      boolean isDebug) {
    this(
        getName,
        isEnabled,
        getPrincipal,
        getKeytabPath,
        getKeytabBytes,
        getKrb5ConfigSource,
        getRealm,
        isDebug,
        true);
  }

  @Override
  public byte[] getKeytabBytes() {
    return getKeytabBytes == null ? null : getKeytabBytes.clone();
  }

  public String getEffectivePrincipal() {
    return KerberosSpn.normalizePrincipal(
        Objects.requireNonNull(getPrincipal, "principal"),
        Strings.trimToNull(getRealm) == null ? DEFAULT_REALM : getRealm);
  }

  public void validate() {
    if (!isEnabled) {
      return;
    }
    if (Strings.isBlank(getPrincipal)) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Kerberos principal is required when enabled");
    }
    boolean hasPath = getKeytabPath != null;
    boolean hasBytes = getKeytabBytes != null && getKeytabBytes.length > 0;
    if (hasPath == hasBytes) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Exactly one of keytabPath or keytabBytes is required");
    }
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.kerberos;

import java.nio.file.Path;
import java.util.Objects;

public sealed interface KerberosKrb5Source
    permits KerberosKrb5Source.Classpath,
        KerberosKrb5Source.FilePath,
        KerberosKrb5Source.Bytes {
  String DEFAULT_RESOURCE = "krb5.conf";
  KerberosKrb5Source DEFAULT = new Classpath(DEFAULT_RESOURCE);
  KerberosKrb5Source SYSTEM_DEFAULT = DEFAULT;

  static KerberosKrb5Source defaultSource() {
    return DEFAULT;
  }

  static KerberosKrb5Source filePath(Path path) {
    return new FilePath(path);
  }

  static KerberosKrb5Source bytes(byte[] data) {
    return new Bytes(data);
  }

  static KerberosKrb5Source classpathResource(String resourcePath) {
    return new Classpath(resourcePath);
  }

  record FilePath(Path getPath) implements KerberosKrb5Source {
    public FilePath {
      getPath = Objects.requireNonNull(getPath, "path");
    }
  }

  record Bytes(byte[] getData) implements KerberosKrb5Source {
    public Bytes {
      Objects.requireNonNull(getData, "data");
      if (getData.length == 0) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("krb5 bytes cannot be empty");
      }
      getData = getData.clone();
    }

    @Override
    public byte[] getData() {
      return getData.clone();
    }
  }

  record Classpath(String getResourcePath) implements KerberosKrb5Source {
    public Classpath {
      getResourcePath = trim(getResourcePath);
      if (getResourcePath == null) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("resourcePath is required");
      }
    }
  }

  private static String trim(String value) {
    String v = value == null ? null : value.trim();
    return v == null || v.isEmpty() ? null : v;
  }
}

FILE: KerberosRuntimeRegistry.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.kerberos;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Collections;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Optional;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class KerberosRuntimeRegistry implements AutoCloseable {
  private static final String DEFAULT_CONTEXT_NAME = KerberosConfig.DEFAULT_CONTEXT_NAME;
  private final Map<String, KerberosClient> contexts = new LinkedHashMap<>();
  private String defaultContextName = DEFAULT_CONTEXT_NAME;

  public synchronized KerberosRuntimeRegistry register(String name, KerberosIdentity identity) {
    if (identity == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("identity is required");
    }
    KerberosConfig config =
        new KerberosConfig(
            normalize(name),
            true,
            identity.getPrincipal(),
            identity.getKeytabPath(),
            null,
            identity.getKrb5ConfPath() == null
                ? KerberosKrb5Source.DEFAULT
                : KerberosKrb5Source.filePath(identity.getKrb5ConfPath()),
            null,
            false,
            true);
    return register(name, config);
  }

  public synchronized KerberosRuntimeRegistry register(String name, KerberosConfig config) {
    String normalized = normalize(name);
    if (config == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("config is required");
    }
    KerberosClient old = contexts.put(normalized, new KerberosClient(config));
    if (old != null) {
      old.close();
    }
    if (contexts.size() == 1) {
      defaultContextName = normalized;
    }
    return this;
  }

  public synchronized Optional<KerberosIdentity> resolve(String name) {
    KerberosClient context = contexts.get(normalize(name));
    return context == null ? Optional.empty() : Optional.of(toIdentity(context.getConfig()));
  }

  public synchronized Optional<KerberosIdentity> lookup(String name) {
    return resolve(name);
  }

  public synchronized KerberosRuntimeRegistry setDefault(String name) {
    String normalized = normalize(name);
    if (!contexts.containsKey(normalized)) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Kerberos context is not registered: " + normalized);
    }
    defaultContextName = normalized;
    return this;
  }

  public synchronized Optional<KerberosIdentity> defaultIdentity() {
    KerberosClient context = contexts.get(defaultContextName);
    return context == null ? Optional.empty() : Optional.of(toIdentity(context.getConfig()));
  }

  public synchronized Optional<KerberosIdentity> getDefaultIdentity() {
    return defaultIdentity();
  }

  public synchronized KerberosClient context(String name) {
    KerberosClient context = contexts.get(normalize(name));
    if (context == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Kerberos context is not registered: " + name);
    }
    return context;
  }

  public synchronized KerberosClient getContext(String name) {
    return context(name);
  }

  public synchronized KerberosClient defaultContext() {
    return context(defaultContextName);
  }

  public synchronized KerberosClient getDefaultContext() {
    return defaultContext();
  }

  public synchronized Map<String, KerberosClient> contexts() {
    return Collections.unmodifiableMap(new LinkedHashMap<>(contexts));
  }

  public synchronized Map<String, KerberosClient> getContexts() {
    return contexts();
  }

  public synchronized String defaultContextName() {
    return defaultContextName;
  }

  public synchronized String getDefaultContextName() {
    return defaultContextName;
  }

  public synchronized void startAll() {
    for (KerberosClient context : contexts.values()) {
      context.start();
    }
  }

  public synchronized void closeAll() {
    List<KerberosClient> reverse = new ArrayList<>(contexts.values());
    Collections.reverse(reverse);
    for (KerberosClient context : reverse) {
      context.close();
    }
  }

  @Override
  public synchronized void close() {
    closeAll();
  }

  private static KerberosIdentity toIdentity(KerberosConfig config) {
    java.nio.file.Path krb5 = null;
    if (config.getKrb5ConfigSource() instanceof KerberosKrb5Source.FilePath filePath) {
      krb5 = filePath.getPath();
    }
    return new KerberosIdentity(config.getEffectivePrincipal(), config.getKeytabPath(), krb5);
  }

  private static String normalize(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Kerberos context name is required");
    }
    return normalized;
  }
}
