FILE: KerberosSpn.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.kerberos;

import java.security.Principal;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Set;
import javax.security.auth.Subject;
import javax.security.auth.kerberos.KerberosPrincipal;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.common.ServiceAdvertise;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

/** SPN helpers enforcing Fabric host-based Kerberos convention. */
public final class KerberosSpn {
  private static final String HTTP_PREFIX = "HTTP/";
  private static final String HTTP_ERR =
      "SPN must be of the form HTTP/<host> or HTTP/<host>@REALM (example: HTTP/myhost.example.com)";

  private KerberosSpn() {}

  public static String canonicalizeAdvertiseHost(String host) {
    return ServiceAdvertise.requireRoutableHost(host, "kerberos advertise host")
        .toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
  }

  public static String httpSpnForHost(String host) {
    return HTTP_PREFIX + canonicalizeAdvertiseHost(host);
  }

  public static String resolveAdvertiseHost(String advertiseHost, String runtimePlacementHost) {
    return ServiceAdvertise.resolveAdvertiseHost(advertiseHost, runtimePlacementHost);
  }

  public static String resolveSpn(String configuredSpn, String advertiseHost) {
    String spn = Strings.trimToNull(configuredSpn);
    if (spn != null) {
      validateHttpSpn(spn);
      return spn;
    }
    return httpSpnForHost(advertiseHost);
  }

  public static void validateHttpSpn(String spn) {
    String value = require(spn, "spn");
    String withoutRealm = stripRealm(value);
    if (withoutRealm == null || !withoutRealm.startsWith(HTTP_PREFIX)) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(HTTP_ERR + ". Received: " + value);
    }
    String host = Strings.trimToNull(withoutRealm.substring(HTTP_PREFIX.length()));
    if (ServiceAdvertise.isWildcardHost(host)) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(
          HTTP_ERR + ". Wildcard/blank host is not allowed: " + value);
    }
  }

  public static String normalizePrincipal(String principalOrUsername, String realm) {
    String principal = require(principalOrUsername, "principalOrUsername");
    if (principal.indexOf('@') >= 0) {
      return principal;
    }
    String resolvedRealm = Strings.trimToNull(realm);
    return principal + "@" + (resolvedRealm == null ? KerberosConfig.DEFAULT_REALM : resolvedRealm);
  }

  public static String normalizeSpnWithRealm(String spn, String realm) {
    String value = require(spn, "spn");
    if (value.indexOf('@') >= 0) {
      return value;
    }
    String resolvedRealm = Strings.trimToNull(realm);
    return resolvedRealm == null ? value : value + "@" + resolvedRealm;
  }

  public static String resolveRealm(String configuredRealm, Subject subject) {
    String explicit = Strings.trimToNull(configuredRealm);
    if (explicit != null) {
      return explicit;
    }
    String fromSubject = extractRealm(firstSubjectPrincipal(subject));
    return fromSubject == null ? KerberosConfig.DEFAULT_REALM : fromSubject;
  }

  public static String extractRealm(String principal) {
    String value = Strings.trimToNull(principal);
    if (value == null) {
      return null;
    }
    int at = value.indexOf('@');
    return at < 0 || at >= value.length() - 1 ? null : Strings.trimToNull(value.substring(at + 1));
  }

  public static String stripRealm(String principal) {
    String value = Strings.trimToNull(principal);
    if (value == null) {
      return null;
    }
    int at = value.indexOf('@');
    return at < 0 ? value : value.substring(0, at);
  }

  public static boolean principalsMatchIgnoringRealm(String left, String right) {
    String normalizedLeft = stripRealm(left);
    String normalizedRight = stripRealm(right);
    return normalizedLeft != null
        && normalizedRight != null
        && normalizedLeft.equalsIgnoreCase(normalizedRight);
  }

  public static String firstSubjectPrincipal(Subject subject) {
    if (subject == null) {
      return null;
    }
    Set<KerberosPrincipal> kerberosPrincipals = subject.getPrincipals(KerberosPrincipal.class);
    for (KerberosPrincipal principal : kerberosPrincipals) {
      String name = Strings.trimToNull(principal == null ? null : principal.getName());
      if (name != null) {
        return name;
      }
    }
    for (Principal principal : subject.getPrincipals()) {
      String name = Strings.trimToNull(principal == null ? null : principal.getName());
      if (name != null) {
        return name;
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  private static String require(String value, String label) {
    String trimmed = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (trimmed == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(label + " is required");
    }
    return trimmed;
  }
}

PACKAGE: org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.sso

FILE: DefaultSsoService.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.sso;

import com.nimbusds.jwt.JWTClaimsSet;
import java.net.URI;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.sso.oidc.FabricOidcConfig;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.sso.oidc.FabricOidcHandler;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.sso.oidc.FabricOidcSession;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.sso.oidc.OidcIdTokenVerifier;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

/** Default framework-agnostic SSO implementation. */
public final class DefaultSsoService implements SsoService {

  private static final Logger LOG = LoggerFactory.getLogger(DefaultSsoService.class);
  private static final String HEADER_USER = "fabric-user";
  private static final String LEGACY_HEADER_USER = "X-Fabric-User";
  private static final String QUERY_SPOOF_USER = "spoofUser";

  private final SsoConfig config;
  private final SsoMode mode;
  private final FabricOidcHandler oidcHandler;
  private final OidcIdTokenVerifier idTokenVerifier;

  public DefaultSsoService(SsoConfig config) {
    this.config = config == null ? SsoConfig.builder().withMode(SsoMode.NONE).build() : config;
    this.mode = this.config.mode();
    if (this.config.oidc() == null) {
      this.oidcHandler = null;
      this.idTokenVerifier = null;
    } else {
      this.oidcHandler = new FabricOidcHandler(this.config.oidc());
      this.idTokenVerifier = this.oidcHandler.idTokenVerifier();
    }
  }

  @Override
  public SsoResult resolve(FabricSsoRequest request, FabricSsoResponse response) {
    if (!config.enabled() || mode == SsoMode.NONE) {
      return SsoResult.empty(mode);
    }
    if (config.spoofEnabled()) {
      SsoPrincipal spoofPrincipal = resolveSpoofPrincipal(request);
      if (spoofPrincipal != null && spoofPrincipal.hasUsername()) {
        return buildResult(spoofPrincipal, SsoMode.SPOOF);
      }
    }
    if (mode == SsoMode.OIDC) {
      SsoPrincipal principal = resolveOidcPrincipal(request, response);
      SsoResult result = buildResult(principal, mode);
      if (!result.authenticated() && shouldRedirectToLogin(request)) {
        FabricOidcConfig oidcConfig = config.oidc();
        if (oidcConfig != null) {
          FabricOidcSession session = FabricOidcSession.from(request);
          String requested = buildRequestedPath(request);
          if (requested != null) {
            session.setPostLoginRedirect(request, response, requested);
          }
          response.redirect(oidcConfig.loginPath());
          response.halt();
        }
      }
      return result;
    }
    if (mode == SsoMode.SPOOF) {
      SsoPrincipal principal = resolveSpoofPrincipal(request);
      return buildResult(principal, SsoMode.SPOOF);
    }
    return SsoResult.empty(mode);
  }

  @Override
  public void handleLogin(FabricSsoRequest request, FabricSsoResponse response) {
    if (!config.enabled() || mode != SsoMode.OIDC || oidcHandler == null) {
      response.setStatus(404);
      response.setText("OIDC not enabled");
      return;
    }
    oidcHandler.handleLogin(request, response);
  }

  @Override
  public void handleCallback(FabricSsoRequest request, FabricSsoResponse response) {
    if (!config.enabled() || mode != SsoMode.OIDC || oidcHandler == null) {
      response.setStatus(404);
      response.setText("OIDC not enabled");
      return;
    }
    oidcHandler.handleCallback(request, response);
  }

  @Override
  public SsoResult handleSpoof(
      FabricSsoRequest request, FabricSsoResponse response, String username) {
    if (!config.spoofEnabled() || config.spoof() == null) {
      response.setStatus(400);
      response.setText("Spoof mode is not enabled");
      return SsoResult.empty(mode);
    }
    SsoConfig.Spoof spoof = config.spoof();
    String normalized = canonicalSpoofSubject(username);
    if (!spoof.allowEditing() && username != null) {
      response.setStatus(400);
      response.setText("Editing spoof user is disabled");
      return SsoResult.empty(mode);
    }
    boolean cleared = Strings.isBlank(normalized);
    if (Strings.isNotBlank(spoof.cookieName())) {
      SsoCookieAttributes.Builder cookie =
          SsoCookieAttributes.builder(spoof.cookieName())
              .withValue(cleared ? "" : normalized)
              .withMaxAgeSeconds(cleared ? 0 : spoof.cookieMaxAgeSeconds())
              .withSecure(isSecureRequest(request))
              .withHttpOnly(false)
              .withSameSite("Lax");
      response.addCookie(cookie.build());
    }
    if (cleared) {
      return SsoResult.empty(mode);
    }
    SsoPrincipal principal = buildSpoofPrincipal(normalized, spoof);
    return buildResult(principal, SsoMode.SPOOF);
  }

  @Override
  public Map<String, Object> buildCurrentUserPayload(SsoContext context) {
    SsoPrincipal principal = context == null ? null : context.principal();
    String subject = context == null ? null : context.subject();
    String actor = context == null ? null : context.actor();
    List<String> groups = groupsFrom(principal);
    boolean authenticated = context != null && context.authenticated();
    boolean allowEditing = config.spoofEnabled() && config.spoof().allowEditing();
    Map<String, Object> payload = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    payload.put("mode", (context == null ? mode : context.mode()).name());
    payload.put("subject", subject);
    payload.put("actor", actor);
    payload.put("authenticated", authenticated);
    payload.put("username", usernameFromSubject(subject));
    payload.put("groups", groups);
    payload.put("allowEditing", allowEditing);
    payload.put("attributes", principal == null ? Map.of() : principal.attributes());
    return payload;
  }

  @Override
  public SsoMode mode() {
    return mode;
  }

  @Override
  public SsoConfig config() {
    return config;
  }

  private SsoResult buildResult(SsoPrincipal principal, SsoMode mode) {
    boolean authenticated = principal != null && principal.hasUsername();
    String subject = principal == null ? null : principal.username();
    SsoContext context = new SsoContext(principal, mode, authenticated, subject, null);
    return new SsoResult(context, SsoAttributes.create());
  }

  private SsoPrincipal resolveSpoofPrincipal(FabricSsoRequest request) {
    SsoConfig.Spoof spoof = config.spoof();
    if (spoof == null || !spoof.enabled()) {
      return null;
    }
    String username = null;
    if (Strings.isNotBlank(spoof.cookieName())) {
      username = request.cookie(spoof.cookieName());
    }
    if (Strings.isBlank(username)) {
      username = request.header(HEADER_USER);
    }
    if (Strings.isBlank(username)) {
      username = request.header(LEGACY_HEADER_USER);
    }
    if (Strings.isBlank(username)) {
      username = request.queryParam(QUERY_SPOOF_USER);
    }
    if (Strings.isBlank(username)) {
      username = spoof.defaultUsername();
    }
    return buildSpoofPrincipal(username, spoof);
  }

  private SsoPrincipal buildSpoofPrincipal(String username, SsoConfig.Spoof spoof) {
    String canonical = canonicalSpoofSubject(username);
    if (Strings.isBlank(canonical)) {
      return null;
    }
    Map<String, Object> attributes = spoof == null ? Map.of() : spoof.attributesFor(canonical);
    return new SsoPrincipal(canonical, attributes);
  }

  private SsoPrincipal resolveOidcPrincipal(
      FabricSsoRequest request, FabricSsoResponse response) {
    if (config.oidc() == null || idTokenVerifier == null) {
      return null;
    }
    FabricOidcSession session = FabricOidcSession.from(request);
    String idToken = session.idToken();
    if (Strings.isBlank(idToken)) {
      return null;
    }
    try {
      JWTClaimsSet claims = idTokenVerifier.verify(idToken);
      String username = FabricOidcHandler.resolveUsername(claims, config.oidc().usernameClaim());
      if (Strings.isBlank(username)) {
        return null;
      }
      String canonical = canonicalSpoofSubject(username);
      if (Strings.isBlank(canonical)) {
        return null;
      }
      List<String> groups = FabricOidcHandler.extractGroups(claims, config.oidc().groupClaims());
      return new SsoPrincipal(canonical, Map.of("groups", groups));
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      LOG.warn("OIDC ID token verification failed: {}", ex.getMessage());
      session.clearIdToken(request, response);
      return null;
    }
  }

  private boolean shouldRedirectToLogin(FabricSsoRequest request) {
    if (request == null || config.oidc() == null) {
      return false;
    }
    String method = request.method();
    if (Strings.isBlank(method) || !"GET".equalsIgnoreCase(method.trim())) {
      return false;
    }
    String path = request.path();
    if (Strings.isBlank(path)) {
      return false;
    }
    return !isAllowlisted(path, config.oidc().allowAnonPaths());
  }

  private static boolean isAllowlisted(String path, List<String> allowlist) {
    if (Strings.isBlank(path) || allowlist == null || allowlist.isEmpty()) {
      return false;
    }
    String normalized = path.trim();
    for (String entry : allowlist) {
      if (Strings.isBlank(entry)) {
        continue;
      }
      String rule = entry.trim();
      if (rule.equals(normalized)) {
        return true;
      }
      if (rule.endsWith("*")) {
        String prefix = rule.substring(0, rule.length() - 1);
        if (normalized.startsWith(prefix)) {
          return true;
        }
      }
    }
    return false;
  }

  private static String buildRequestedPath(FabricSsoRequest request) {
    if (request == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String path = request.path();
    if (Strings.isBlank(path)) {
      return null;
    }
    String fullUrl = request.fullUrl();
    if (Strings.isBlank(fullUrl)) {
      return path;
    }
    try {
      URI uri = URI.create(fullUrl);
      String query = uri.getRawQuery();
      if (Strings.isBlank(query)) {
        return path;
      }
      return path + "?" + query;
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      return path;
    }
  }

  private static String canonicalSpoofSubject(String value) {
    String normalized = value == null ? null : value.trim();
    if (Strings.isBlank(normalized)) {
      return null;
    }
    String lower = normalized.toLowerCase();
    if (lower.startsWith("user:")) {
      String id = normalized.substring("user:".length()).trim();
      if (id.isEmpty()) {
        return null;
      }
      return "user:" + id;
    }
    return "user:" + normalized;
  }

  private static List<String> groupsFrom(SsoPrincipal principal) {
    if (principal == null || principal.attributes() == null) {
      return List.of();
    }
    Object groups = principal.attributes().get("groups");
    if (groups instanceof List<?> values) {
      return values.stream()
          .filter(String.class::isInstance)
          .map(String.class::cast)
          .map(String::trim)
          .filter(value -> !value.isEmpty())
          .toList();
    }
    if (groups instanceof String value && !value.isBlank()) {
      return List.of(value.trim());
    }
    return List.of();
  }

  private static String usernameFromSubject(String subject) {
    if (Strings.isBlank(subject)) {
      return null;
    }
    String normalized = subject.trim();
    if (normalized.toLowerCase().startsWith("user:")) {
      String id = normalized.substring("user:".length()).trim();
      return id.isEmpty() ? null : id;
    }
    return normalized;
  }

  private static boolean isSecureRequest(FabricSsoRequest request) {
    if (request == null) {
      return false;
    }
    String fullUrl = request.fullUrl();
    if (Strings.isBlank(fullUrl)) {
      return false;
    }
    try {
      URI uri = URI.create(fullUrl);
      String scheme = uri.getScheme();
      return scheme != null && scheme.equalsIgnoreCase("https");
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      return false;
    }
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.sso;

import java.util.Collections;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.concurrent.ConcurrentHashMap;

/** Request-scoped attributes related to SSO evaluation. */
public final class SsoAttributes {

  public static final String CURRENT_PRINCIPAL = "fabric.sso.current.principal";
  public static final String CURRENT_CONTEXT = "fabric.sso.current.context";
  public static final String CURRENT_ATTRIBUTES = "fabric.sso.current.attributes";

  private final Map<String, Object> values = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();

  public static SsoAttributes create() {
    return new SsoAttributes();
  }

  public void put(String key, Object value) {
    if (key == null) {
      return;
    }
    if (value == null) {
      values.remove(key);
      return;
    }
    values.put(key, value);
  }

  public Object get(String key) {
    return key == null ? null : values.get(key);
  }

  @SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
  public <T> T get(String key, Class<T> type) {
    Object value = get(key);
    if (type == null || value == null) {
      return null;
    }
    if (type.isInstance(value)) {
      return (T) value;
    }
    return null;
  }

  public Map<String, Object> snapshot() {
    return Collections.unmodifiableMap(values);
  }
}

      return sessionAttribute;

      return cookieMaxAgeSeconds;
    }

    public Map<String, Object> attributesFor(String username) {
      Map<String, Object> resolved = attributeResolver == null ? Map.of() : attributeResolver.apply(username);
      return resolved == null ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(resolved);
    }

    public static Builder builder() {
      return new Builder();
    }

    public static final class Builder {
      private boolean enabled = true;
      private String defaultUsername;
      private boolean allowEditing = true;
      private String cookieName = "fabric_spoof_user";
      private String sessionAttribute = "fabric.sso.spoof.username";
      private int cookieMaxAgeSeconds = 60 * 60 * 24 * 30;
      private Function<String, Map<String, Object>> attributeResolver = username -> Map.of();

      Builder() {
      }

        return this;

        }
        return this;
      }

        return this;

        }

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.sso;

import java.util.Optional;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.UserContext;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.UserPrincipal;

/** Thread-local holder for the current SSO identity and state. */
public final class SsoContext {

  private static final ThreadLocal<SsoContext> CURRENT = new ThreadLocal<>();

  private final SsoPrincipal principal;
  private final SsoMode mode;
  private final boolean authenticated;
  private final String subject;
  private final String actor;

  public SsoContext(
      SsoPrincipal principal,
      SsoMode mode,
      boolean authenticated,
      String subject,
      String actor) {
    this.principal = principal;
    this.mode = mode == null ? SsoMode.NONE : mode;
    this.authenticated = authenticated;
    this.subject = subject;
    this.actor = actor;
  }

  public SsoPrincipal principal() {
    return principal;
  }

  public SsoMode mode() {
    return mode;
  }

  public boolean authenticated() {
    return authenticated;
  }

  public String subject() {
    return subject;
  }

  public String actor() {
    return actor;
  }

  public static void set(SsoPrincipal principal) {
    if (principal == null) {
      set((SsoContext) null);
      return;
    }
    set(new SsoContext(principal, SsoMode.NONE, true, principal.username(), null));
  }

  public static void set(SsoContext context) {
    if (context == null) {
      CURRENT.remove();
      UserContext.clear();
      return;
    }
    CURRENT.set(context);
    if (context.principal == null) {
      UserContext.clear();
      return;
    }
    UserContext.set(new UserPrincipal(context.principal.username(), context.principal.attributes()));
  }

  public static Optional<SsoContext> current() {
    return Optional.ofNullable(CURRENT.get());
  }

  /** Backwards-compatible accessor for the current principal. */
  public static Optional<SsoPrincipal> get() {
    return currentPrincipal();
  }

  public static Optional<SsoPrincipal> currentPrincipal() {
    SsoContext ctx = CURRENT.get();
    return Optional.ofNullable(ctx == null ? null : ctx.principal);
  }

  public static String getUsernameOrDefault(String fallback) {
    SsoContext ctx = CURRENT.get();
    SsoPrincipal principal = ctx == null ? null : ctx.principal;
    if (principal != null && principal.username() != null && !principal.username().isBlank()) {
      return principal.username().trim();
    }
    return fallback;
  }

  public static String currentSubject() {
    SsoContext ctx = CURRENT.get();
    if (ctx == null || ctx.subject == null || ctx.subject.isBlank()) {
      return null;
    }
    return ctx.subject.trim();
  }

  public static void clear() {
    CURRENT.remove();
    UserContext.clear();
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.sso;

/** Supported SSO modes for Fabric web applications. */
public enum SsoMode {
  /** No authentication is enforced; the application may operate anonymously. */
  NONE,

  /** OpenID Connect (OIDC) powered authentication. */
  OIDC,

  /** Developer/spoof mode that allows selecting an arbitrary username for demos. */
  SPOOF
}

    this.username = Strings.isBlank(username) ? null : username.trim();
    Map<String, Object> clone = attributes == null ? Map.of() : new LinkedHashMap<>(attributes);
    this.attributes = Collections.unmodifiableMap(clone);

  }

  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.sso;

import java.util.Map;

/** Public SSO service API for framework integrations. */
public interface SsoService {

  SsoResult resolve(FabricSsoRequest request, FabricSsoResponse response);

}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.sso.oidc;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonNode;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import com.nimbusds.jwt.JWTClaimsSet;
import com.nimbusds.jwt.SignedJWT;
import com.nimbusds.jwt.proc.ConfigurableJWTProcessor;
import com.nimbusds.jwt.proc.DefaultJWTProcessor;
import com.nimbusds.jose.JWSAlgorithm;
import com.nimbusds.jose.jwk.source.JWKSource;
import com.nimbusds.jose.jwk.source.RemoteJWKSet;
import com.nimbusds.jose.proc.JWSKeySelector;
import com.nimbusds.jose.proc.JWSVerificationKeySelector;
import com.nimbusds.jose.proc.SecurityContext;
import com.nimbusds.jose.util.DefaultResourceRetriever;
import com.nimbusds.oauth2.sdk.AuthorizationCode;
import com.nimbusds.oauth2.sdk.AuthorizationCodeGrant;
import com.nimbusds.oauth2.sdk.ErrorObject;
import com.nimbusds.oauth2.sdk.ResponseType;
import com.nimbusds.oauth2.sdk.Scope;
import com.nimbusds.oauth2.sdk.TokenRequest;
import com.nimbusds.oauth2.sdk.TokenResponse;
import com.nimbusds.oauth2.sdk.auth.ClientAuthentication;
import com.nimbusds.oauth2.sdk.auth.ClientSecretBasic;
import com.nimbusds.oauth2.sdk.auth.Secret;
import com.nimbusds.oauth2.sdk.http.HTTPResponse;
import com.nimbusds.oauth2.sdk.id.ClientID;
import com.nimbusds.oauth2.sdk.id.State;
import com.nimbusds.openid.connect.sdk.AuthenticationRequest;
import com.nimbusds.openid.connect.sdk.Nonce;
import com.nimbusds.openid.connect.sdk.OIDCTokenResponse;
import com.nimbusds.openid.connect.sdk.OIDCTokenResponseParser;
import com.nimbusds.openid.connect.sdk.token.OIDCTokens;
import java.io.InputStream;
import java.net.HttpURLConnection;
import java.net.URI;
import java.net.URL;
import java.time.Instant;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Set;
import java.util.UUID;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.sso.FabricSsoRequest;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.sso.FabricSsoResponse;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

/** OIDC authorization code flow handler with login and callback endpoints. */
public final class FabricOidcHandler {

  private static final Logger LOG = LoggerFactory.getLogger(FabricOidcHandler.class);

  private final FabricOidcConfig config;
  private final OidcTokenExchanger tokenExchanger;
  private final OidcIdTokenVerifier idTokenVerifier;

  public FabricOidcHandler(FabricOidcConfig config) {
    this(config, new NimbusOidcTokenExchanger(config), new NimbusOidcIdTokenVerifier(config));
  }

  public FabricOidcHandler(
      FabricOidcConfig config,
      OidcTokenExchanger tokenExchanger,
      OidcIdTokenVerifier idTokenVerifier) {
    this.config = Objects.requireNonNull(config, "config");
    this.tokenExchanger = Objects.requireNonNull(tokenExchanger, "tokenExchanger");
    this.idTokenVerifier = Objects.requireNonNull(idTokenVerifier, "idTokenVerifier");
  }

  public OidcIdTokenVerifier idTokenVerifier() {
    return idTokenVerifier;
  }

  public void handleLogin(FabricSsoRequest request, FabricSsoResponse response) {
    try {
      FabricOidcSession session = FabricOidcSession.from(request);
      String stateValue = UUID.randomUUID().toString();
      String nonceValue = UUID.randomUUID().toString();
      session.storeStateNonce(request, response, stateValue, nonceValue);
      String redirectOverride = safeRelativeRedirect(request.queryParam("redirect"));
      if (redirectOverride != null) {
        session.setPostLoginRedirect(request, response, redirectOverride);
      }
      State state = new State(stateValue);
      Nonce nonce = new Nonce(nonceValue);
      ResponseType responseType = new ResponseType(ResponseType.Value.CODE);
      Scope scope = Scope.parse(config.scope());
      ClientID clientId = new ClientID(config.clientId());
      AuthenticationRequest authRequest =
          new AuthenticationRequest.Builder(
                  responseType, scope, clientId, URI.create(config.redirectUri()))
              .endpointURI(URI.create(config.authorizationUrl()))
              .state(state)
              .nonce(nonce)
              .build();
      response.redirect(authRequest.toURI().toString());
      response.halt();
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      LOG.error("Failed to initiate OIDC login", ex);
      response.setStatus(500);
      response.setText("Unable to start login");
    }
  }

  public void handleCallback(FabricSsoRequest request, FabricSsoResponse response) {
    FabricOidcSession session = FabricOidcSession.from(request);
    String error = request.queryParam("error");
    if (Strings.isNotBlank(error)) {
      String description = request.queryParam("error_description");
      LOG.warn("OIDC callback error: {} {}", error, safeValue(description));
      response.setStatus(400);
      response.setText("Authentication failed");
      return;
    }
    String expectedState = session.consumeState(request, response);
    String providedState = request.queryParam("state");
    if (expectedState == null || providedState == null || !expectedState.equals(providedState)) {
      response.setStatus(400);
      response.setText("Invalid authentication state");
      return;
    }
    String codeParam = request.queryParam("code");
    if (Strings.isBlank(codeParam)) {
      response.setStatus(400);
      response.setText("Missing authorization code");
      return;
    }
    try {
      OidcTokens tokens = tokenExchanger.exchange(codeParam.trim());
      if (tokens == null || Strings.isBlank(tokens.idToken())) {
        throw new IllegalStateException("Missing ID token in OIDC response");
      }
      JWTClaimsSet claims = idTokenVerifier.verify(tokens.idToken());
      if (claims == null) {
        throw new IllegalStateException("ID token claims missing");
      }
      String expectedNonce = session.consumeNonce(request, response);
      String tokenNonce = claims.getStringClaim("nonce");
      if (Strings.isBlank(expectedNonce)
          || Strings.isBlank(tokenNonce)
          || !expectedNonce.equals(tokenNonce)) {
        response.setStatus(400);
        response.setText("Invalid ID token nonce");
        return;
      }
      String username = resolveUsername(claims, config.usernameClaim());
      if (Strings.isBlank(username)) {
        throw new IllegalStateException(
            "OIDC token missing username claim: " + config.usernameClaim());
      }
      List<String> groups = extractGroups(claims, config.groupClaims());
      FabricWebIdentity identity = new FabricWebIdentity(
          username,
          groups,
          claims.getSubject(),
          toInstant(claims.getIssueTime()),
          toInstant(claims.getExpirationTime()));
      session.storeIdToken(request, response, tokens.idToken());
      String redirect = safeRelativeRedirect(session.consumePostLoginRedirect(request, response));
      response.redirect(redirect == null ? "/" : redirect);
      response.halt();
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      LOG.warn("OIDC callback failed", ex);
      response.setStatus(500);
      response.setText("Authentication failed");
    }
  }

  public static String resolveUsername(JWTClaimsSet claims, String claimName) {
    if (claims == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String primary = null;
    if (claimName != null) {
      try {
        primary = claims.getStringClaim(claimName);
      } catch (java.text.ParseException ignored) {
        primary = null;
      }
    }
    if (Strings.isNotBlank(primary)) {
      return primary.trim();
    }
    String fallback = null;
    try {
      fallback = claims.getStringClaim("sub");
    } catch (java.text.ParseException ignored) {
      fallback = null;
    }
    return Strings.isBlank(fallback) ? null : fallback.trim();
  }

  public static List<String> extractGroups(JWTClaimsSet claims, List<String> claimNames) {
    if (claims == null || claimNames == null || claimNames.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    Set<String> groups = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    for (String claimName : claimNames) {
      if (Strings.isBlank(claimName)) {
        continue;
      }
      Object claim = claims.getClaim(claimName);
      if (claim instanceof List<?> list) {
        for (Object value : list) {
          if (value instanceof String text && !text.isBlank()) {
            groups.add(text.trim());
          }
        }
      } else if (claim instanceof String text && !text.isBlank()) {
        groups.add(text.trim());
      }
    }
    if (groups.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    return List.copyOf(groups);
  }

  private static Instant toInstant(java.util.Date date) {
    if (date == null) {
      return null;
    }
    return Instant.ofEpochMilli(date.getTime());
  }

  private static String safeRelativeRedirect(String value) {
    if (Strings.isBlank(value)) {
      return null;
    }
    String trimmed = value.trim();
    if (!trimmed.startsWith("/")) {
      return null;
    }
    return trimmed;
  }

  private static String safeValue(String value) {
    if (Strings.isBlank(value)) {
      return "<none>";
    }
    return value.length() > 120 ? value.substring(0, 120) + "..." : value;
  }

  public static final class NimbusOidcTokenExchanger implements OidcTokenExchanger {

    private final FabricOidcConfig config;

    public NimbusOidcTokenExchanger(FabricOidcConfig config) {
      this.config = Objects.requireNonNull(config, "config");
    }

    @Override
    public OidcTokens exchange(String codeValue) throws Exception {
      AuthorizationCode code = new AuthorizationCode(codeValue);
      AuthorizationCodeGrant grant = new AuthorizationCodeGrant(code, URI.create(config.redirectUri()));
      ClientAuthentication clientAuth =
          new ClientSecretBasic(new ClientID(config.clientId()), new Secret(config.clientSecret()));
      TokenRequest request = new TokenRequest(URI.create(config.tokenUrl()), clientAuth, grant);
      HTTPResponse response = request.toHTTPRequest().send();
      TokenResponse parsed = OIDCTokenResponseParser.parse(response);
      if (!parsed.indicatesSuccess()) {
        ErrorObject error = parsed.toErrorResponse().getErrorObject();
        throw new IllegalStateException("Token exchange failed: " + error);
      }
      OIDCTokens tokens = ((OIDCTokenResponse) parsed).getOIDCTokens();
      if (tokens == null) {
        throw new IllegalStateException("Token exchange returned no tokens");
      }
      String idToken = tokens.getIDToken() == null ? null : tokens.getIDToken().serialize();
      String accessToken = tokens.getAccessToken() == null ? null : tokens.getAccessToken().getValue();
      String refreshToken = tokens.getRefreshToken() == null ? null : tokens.getRefreshToken().getValue();
      return new OidcTokens(idToken, accessToken, refreshToken);
    }
  }

  public static final class NimbusOidcIdTokenVerifier implements OidcIdTokenVerifier {

    private static final int CONNECT_TIMEOUT_MS = 5000;
    private static final int READ_TIMEOUT_MS = 5000;
    private static final int RESOURCE_SIZE_LIMIT = 1024 * 1024;

    private final FabricOidcConfig config;
    private final ObjectMapper mapper = new ObjectMapper();
    private volatile URL jwksUrl;

    public NimbusOidcIdTokenVerifier(FabricOidcConfig config) {
      this.config = Objects.requireNonNull(config, "config");
    }

    @Override
    public JWTClaimsSet verify(String idToken) throws Exception {
      if (Strings.isBlank(idToken)) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("ID token is required");
      }
      SignedJWT jwt = SignedJWT.parse(idToken);
      JWSAlgorithm alg = jwt.getHeader().getAlgorithm();
      if (alg == null || JWSAlgorithm.NONE.equals(alg)) {
        throw new IllegalStateException("Unsupported ID token signing algorithm");
      }
      JWKSource<SecurityContext> jwkSource = new RemoteJWKSet<>(resolveJwksUrl(),
          new DefaultResourceRetriever(CONNECT_TIMEOUT_MS, READ_TIMEOUT_MS, RESOURCE_SIZE_LIMIT));
      JWSKeySelector<SecurityContext> keySelector = new JWSVerificationKeySelector<>(alg, jwkSource);
      ConfigurableJWTProcessor<SecurityContext> processor = new DefaultJWTProcessor<>();
      processor.setJWSKeySelector(keySelector);
      JWTClaimsSet claims = processor.process(jwt, null);
      validateClaims(claims);
      return claims;
    }

    private void validateClaims(JWTClaimsSet claims) {
      if (claims == null) {
        throw new IllegalStateException("ID token claims missing");
      }
      String issuer = claims.getIssuer();
      if (Strings.isBlank(issuer) || !issuer.equals(config.issuerBaseUrl())) {
        throw new IllegalStateException("ID token issuer mismatch");
      }
      List<String> audience = claims.getAudience();
      if (audience == null || audience.isEmpty() || !audience.contains(config.clientId())) {
        throw new IllegalStateException("ID token audience mismatch");
      }
      Instant now = Instant.now();
      int skew = Math.max(0, config.clockSkewSeconds());
      if (claims.getExpirationTime() == null) {
        throw new IllegalStateException("ID token expiration missing");
      }
      Instant exp = Instant.ofEpochMilli(claims.getExpirationTime().getTime());
      if (exp.plusSeconds(skew).isBefore(now)) {
        throw new IllegalStateException("ID token expired");
      }
      if (claims.getNotBeforeTime() != null) {
        Instant nbf = Instant.ofEpochMilli(claims.getNotBeforeTime().getTime());
        if (nbf.minusSeconds(skew).isAfter(now)) {
          throw new IllegalStateException("ID token not yet valid");
        }
      }
      if (claims.getIssueTime() != null) {
        Instant iat = Instant.ofEpochMilli(claims.getIssueTime().getTime());
        if (iat.minusSeconds(skew).isAfter(now)) {
          throw new IllegalStateException("ID token issued in the future");
        }
      }
    }

    private URL resolveJwksUrl() throws Exception {
      URL cached = jwksUrl;
      if (cached != null) {
        return cached;
      }
      synchronized (this) {
        if (jwksUrl != null) {
          return jwksUrl;
        }
        if (Strings.isNotBlank(config.jwksEndpoint())) {
          jwksUrl = new URL(config.jwksEndpoint());
          return jwksUrl;
        }
        String discoveryUrl = config.discoveryUrl();
        if (Strings.isBlank(discoveryUrl)) {
          throw new IllegalStateException("OIDC discovery URL not configured");
        }
        HttpURLConnection connection = (HttpURLConnection) new URL(discoveryUrl).openConnection();
        connection.setRequestMethod("GET");
        connection.setConnectTimeout(CONNECT_TIMEOUT_MS);
        connection.setReadTimeout(READ_TIMEOUT_MS);
        int status = connection.getResponseCode();
        if (status >= 400) {
          throw new IllegalStateException("OIDC discovery request failed with status " + status);
        }
        try (InputStream in = connection.getInputStream()) {
          JsonNode node = mapper.readTree(in);
          String jwksUri = node.path("jwks_uri").asText(null);
          if (Strings.isBlank(jwksUri)) {
            throw new IllegalStateException("OIDC discovery missing jwks_uri");
          }
          jwksUrl = new URL(jwksUri);
          return jwksUrl;
        }
      }
    }
  }
}


FILE: FabricOidcSession.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.sso.oidc;

import java.net.URI;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.sso.FabricSsoRequest;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.sso.FabricSsoResponse;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.sso.SsoCookieAttributes;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

/** Cookie-backed holder for OIDC state, nonce, and identity. */
public final class FabricOidcSession {

  static final String STATE_COOKIE = "fabric.oidc.state";
  static final String NONCE_COOKIE = "fabric.oidc.nonce";
  static final String ID_TOKEN_COOKIE = "fabric.oidc.id_token";
  static final String REDIRECT_COOKIE = "fabric.oidc.redirect";
  static final int STATE_TTL_SECONDS = 300;
  static final int NONCE_TTL_SECONDS = 300;
  static final int REDIRECT_TTL_SECONDS = 600;

  private final String state;
  private final String nonce;
  private final String idToken;
  private final String postLoginRedirect;

  private FabricOidcSession(String state, String nonce, String idToken, String postLoginRedirect) {
    this.state = state;
    this.nonce = nonce;
    this.idToken = idToken;
    this.postLoginRedirect = postLoginRedirect;
  }

  public static FabricOidcSession from(FabricSsoRequest request) {
    if (request == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("request is required");
    }
    String state = request.cookie(STATE_COOKIE);
    String nonce = request.cookie(NONCE_COOKIE);
    String idToken = request.cookie(ID_TOKEN_COOKIE);
    String redirect = request.cookie(REDIRECT_COOKIE);
    return new FabricOidcSession(state, nonce, idToken, redirect);
  }

  public String state() {
    return state;
  }

  public String nonce() {
    return nonce;
  }

  public String idToken() {
    return idToken;
  }

  public String postLoginRedirect() {
    return postLoginRedirect;
  }

  public void storeStateNonce(FabricSsoRequest request, FabricSsoResponse response, String state, String nonce) {
    boolean secure = isSecureRequest(request);
    response.addCookie(cookie(STATE_COOKIE, state, STATE_TTL_SECONDS, secure));
    response.addCookie(cookie(NONCE_COOKIE, nonce, NONCE_TTL_SECONDS, secure));
  }

  public String consumeState(FabricSsoRequest request, FabricSsoResponse response) {
    boolean secure = isSecureRequest(request);
    response.addCookie(cookie(STATE_COOKIE, "", 0, secure));
    return state;
  }

  public String consumeNonce(FabricSsoRequest request, FabricSsoResponse response) {
    boolean secure = isSecureRequest(request);
    response.addCookie(cookie(NONCE_COOKIE, "", 0, secure));
    return nonce;
  }

  public void setPostLoginRedirect(FabricSsoRequest request, FabricSsoResponse response, String redirect) {
    if (Strings.isBlank(redirect)) {
      return;
    }
    boolean secure = isSecureRequest(request);
    response.addCookie(cookie(REDIRECT_COOKIE, redirect, REDIRECT_TTL_SECONDS, secure));
  }

  public String consumePostLoginRedirect(FabricSsoRequest request, FabricSsoResponse response) {
    boolean secure = isSecureRequest(request);
    response.addCookie(cookie(REDIRECT_COOKIE, "", 0, secure));
    return postLoginRedirect;
  }

  public void storeIdToken(FabricSsoRequest request, FabricSsoResponse response, String idToken) {
    boolean secure = isSecureRequest(request);
    response.addCookie(cookie(ID_TOKEN_COOKIE, idToken, null, secure));
  }

  public void clearIdToken(FabricSsoRequest request, FabricSsoResponse response) {
    boolean secure = isSecureRequest(request);
    response.addCookie(cookie(ID_TOKEN_COOKIE, "", 0, secure));
  }

  private static boolean isSecureRequest(FabricSsoRequest request) {
    if (request == null) {
      return false;
    }
    String fullUrl = request.fullUrl();
    if (Strings.isNotBlank(fullUrl)) {
      try {
        URI uri = URI.create(fullUrl);
        String scheme = uri.getScheme();
        if (scheme != null && scheme.equalsIgnoreCase("https")) {
          return true;
        }
      } catch (Exception ignore) {
      }
    }
    return false;
  }

  private static SsoCookieAttributes cookie(
      String name, String value, Integer maxAgeSeconds, boolean secure) {
    return SsoCookieAttributes.builder(name)
        .withValue(value)
        .withMaxAgeSeconds(maxAgeSeconds)
        .withSecure(secure)
        .withHttpOnly(true)
        .withSameSite("Lax")
        .build();
  }
}

FILE: DataStatusCache.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.status.data;

import com.crankuptheamps.client.Command;
import com.crankuptheamps.client.Message;
import java.time.Clock;
import java.time.Duration;
import java.time.Instant;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.concurrent.ConcurrentHashMap;
import java.util.concurrent.CountDownLatch;
import java.util.concurrent.TimeUnit;
import java.util.concurrent.atomic.AtomicBoolean;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.ControlConnection;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.cache.DiscoveryTopics;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.codec.DiscoveryCodec;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.Definition;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionStatusData;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

public final class DataStatusCache implements AutoCloseable {
  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(DataStatusCache.class);
  private static final String TOPIC_STATUS = DiscoveryTopics.STATUS;
  private static final String FILTER_STATUS_DATA = "/type='STATUS_DATA'";
  private static final Duration DEFAULT_STALE_AFTER = Duration.ofSeconds(15);
  private static final String UNKNOWN = "-";

  private final ControlConnection control;
  private final Clock clock;
  private final Duration staleAfter;
  private final ConcurrentHashMap<Key, StatusSnapshot> statuses = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();
  private final AtomicBoolean started = new AtomicBoolean(false);
  private final AtomicBoolean recovered = new AtomicBoolean(false);
  private final CountDownLatch recoveryLatch = new CountDownLatch(1);
  private volatile ControlConnection.Subscription subscription;

  public DataStatusCache(ControlConnection control) {
    this(control, Clock.systemUTC(), DEFAULT_STALE_AFTER);
  }

  DataStatusCache(ControlConnection control, Clock clock, Duration staleAfter) {
    this.control = Objects.requireNonNull(control, "control");
    this.clock = Objects.requireNonNull(clock, "clock");
    this.staleAfter =
        staleAfter == null || staleAfter.isNegative() || staleAfter.isZero()
            ? DEFAULT_STALE_AFTER
            : staleAfter;
  }

  public void start() throws Exception {
    if (!started.compareAndSet(false, true)) {
      awaitRecovery(Duration.ofSeconds(30));
      return;
    }
    Command command = new Command(Message.Command.SOWAndSubscribe);
    command.setTopic(TOPIC_STATUS);
    command.setOptions("oof");
    command.setFilter(FILTER_STATUS_DATA);
    subscription =
        control
            .sowAndSubscribe(
                command.getTopic(),
                command.getOptions(),
                command.getFilter(),
                message -> handleMessage(message.raw()));
    awaitRecovery(Duration.ofSeconds(30));
    LOGGER.debug(
        "Data status cache ready topics={} enabledTypes={} instanceCount={}",
        List.of(TOPIC_STATUS),
        List.of("STATUS_DATA"),
        statuses.size());
  }

  public void startShared() {
    if (!started.compareAndSet(false, true)) {
      awaitRecovery(Duration.ofSeconds(30));
    }
  }

  public boolean recovered() {
    return recovered.get();
  }

  public int size() {
    return statuses.size();
  }

  public List<DataStatusRow> snapshot() {
    long nowMs = clock.millis();
    return statuses.entrySet().stream()
        .map(entry -> toRow(entry.getKey(), entry.getValue(), nowMs))
        .sorted(
            Comparator.comparing(
                    (DataStatusRow row) ->
                        Strings.trimToEmpty(row.group()), String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER)
                .thenComparing(
                    row -> Strings.trimToEmpty(row.name()), String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER)
                .thenComparing(
                    row -> Strings.trimToEmpty(row.instanceName()), String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER))
        .toList();
  }

  public void stop() {
    ControlConnection.Subscription id = subscription;
    if (id != null) {
      try {
        id.close();
      } catch (Exception ignore) {
      }
      subscription = null;
    }
    statuses.clear();
  }

  @Override
  public void close() {
    stop();
  }

  private DataStatusRow toRow(Key key, StatusSnapshot snapshot, long nowMs) {
    DefinitionStatusData status = snapshot.status();
    Long heartbeatMs = positive(status.lastHeartbeatEpochMs());
    Instant lastHeartbeatUtc = heartbeatMs == null ? null : Instant.ofEpochMilli(heartbeatMs);
    Instant lastSeenUtc = snapshot.receivedTimeUtc();
    String state = deriveState(status.state(), heartbeatMs, snapshot.receivedTimeUtc(), nowMs);
    String producerType =
        status.producerType() == null ? "UNKNOWN" : status.producerType().name();
    return new DataStatusRow(
        key.group(),
        key.name(),
        key.instanceName(),
        producerType,
        state,
        defaultText(status.producerId()),
        defaultText(status.datasetId()),
        defaultText(status.host()),
        defaultText(status.message()),
        lastHeartbeatUtc,
        lastSeenUtc);
  }

  private String deriveState(
      DefinitionStatusData.State rawState, Long heartbeatMs, Instant lastSeenUtc, long nowMs) {
    if (isOfflineState(rawState)) {
      return "OFFLINE";
    }
    if (isErrorState(rawState)) {
      return "ERROR";
    }
    if (isStale(heartbeatMs, lastSeenUtc, nowMs)) {
      return "STALE";
    }
    if (isOnlineState(rawState)) {
      return "ONLINE";
    }
    return "UNKNOWN";
  }

  private boolean isStale(Long heartbeatMs, Instant lastSeenUtc, long nowMs) {
    long referenceMs = heartbeatMs == null ? 0L : heartbeatMs;
    if (referenceMs <= 0L && lastSeenUtc != null) {
      referenceMs = lastSeenUtc.toEpochMilli();
    }
    if (referenceMs <= 0L) {
      return true;
    }
    return nowMs - referenceMs > staleAfter.toMillis();
  }

  private boolean isOnlineState(DefinitionStatusData.State state) {
    return switch (state == null ? DefinitionStatusData.State.UNKNOWN : state) {
      case ONLINE -> true;
      default -> false;
    };
  }

  private boolean isOfflineState(DefinitionStatusData.State state) {
    return switch (state == null ? DefinitionStatusData.State.UNKNOWN : state) {
      case OFFLINE -> true;
      default -> false;
    };
  }

  private boolean isErrorState(DefinitionStatusData.State state) {
    return switch (state == null ? DefinitionStatusData.State.UNKNOWN : state) {
      case ERROR -> true;
      default -> false;
    };
  }

  public void awaitRecovery(Duration timeout) {
    long millis = timeout == null ? 30000L : Math.max(1L, timeout.toMillis());
    try {
      boolean done = recoveryLatch.await(millis, TimeUnit.MILLISECONDS);
      if (!done) {
        throw new IllegalStateException(
            "DataStatusCache initial recovery did not complete (GroupEnd not observed)");
      }
    } catch (InterruptedException ex) {
      Thread.currentThread().interrupt();
      throw new IllegalStateException("Interrupted while waiting for DataStatusCache recovery", ex);
    }
  }

  private void handleMessage(Message message) {
    if (message == null) {
      return;
    }
    int command = message.getCommand();
    if (command == Message.Command.GroupEnd) {
      recovered.set(true);
      recoveryLatch.countDown();
      return;
    }
    if (command != Message.Command.SOW
        && command != Message.Command.Publish
        && command != Message.Command.OOF
        && command != Message.Command.SOWDelete) {
      return;
    }
    String payload = message.getData();
    if (Strings.isBlank(payload)) {
      return;
    }
    try {
      Definition definition = DiscoveryCodec.decode(payload);
      if (!(definition instanceof DefinitionStatusData status)) {
        return;
      }
      Key key = key(status.group(), status.name(), status.instance());
      if (key == null) {
        return;
      }
      if (command == Message.Command.OOF || command == Message.Command.SOWDelete) {
        statuses.remove(key);
        return;
      }
      statuses.put(key, new StatusSnapshot(status, Instant.now(clock)));
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      LOGGER.debug("Data status decode failed payload={} reason={}", payload, ex.toString());
    }
  }

  public void onStatusMessage(Message message) {
    handleMessage(message);
  }

  private static Key key(String group, String name, String instanceName) {
    String normalizedGroup = Strings.trimToNull(group);
    String normalizedName = Strings.trimToNull(name);
    String normalizedInstance = Strings.trimToNull(instanceName);
    if (normalizedGroup == null || normalizedName == null || normalizedInstance == null) {
      return null;
    }
    return new Key(normalizedGroup, normalizedName, normalizedInstance);
  }

  private static Long positive(Long value) {
    return value == null || value <= 0L ? null : value;
  }

  private static String defaultText(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    return normalized == null ? UNKNOWN : normalized;
  }

  private record Key(String group, String name, String instanceName) {}

  private record StatusSnapshot(DefinitionStatusData status, Instant receivedTimeUtc) {}
}


FILE: DataStatusPublisher.java

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.status.data;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.SerializationFeature;
import java.io.Closeable;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.concurrent.ConcurrentHashMap;
import java.util.concurrent.Executors;
import java.util.concurrent.ScheduledExecutorService;
import java.util.concurrent.ScheduledFuture;
import java.util.concurrent.TimeUnit;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.ControlConnection;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.cache.DiscoveryTopics;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.codec.DiscoveryCodec;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionEnvelope;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionStatusData;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionType;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

public final class DataStatusPublisher implements Closeable {
  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(DataStatusPublisher.class);
  private static final boolean STATUS_DEBUG = false;
  private static final long DEFAULT_INTERVAL_SECONDS = 30L;

  private final ObjectMapper om =
      DiscoveryCodec.mapper().copy().configure(SerializationFeature.ORDER_MAP_ENTRIES_BY_KEYS, true);
  private final ControlConnection control;
  private final ScheduledExecutorService ses;
  private final boolean ownsScheduler;
  private final long intervalSec;
  private final String group;
  private final String name;
  private final String instance;
  private final DefinitionStatusData.ProducerType producerType;
  private final String producerId;
  private final String datasetId;
  private final String host;
  private final String appName;
  private final String appInstance;
  private final String appGroup;
  private final long startEpochMs;
  private final Map<String, String> tags;

  private volatile String message;
  private volatile DefinitionStatusData.State state = DefinitionStatusData.State.ONLINE;
  private volatile boolean open = true;
  private volatile ScheduledFuture<?> heartbeatTask;

  public DataStatusPublisher(
      ControlConnection control,
      String group,
      String name,
      String instance,
      DefinitionStatusData.ProducerType producerType,
      String producerId,
      String datasetId,
      String host,
      String appName,
      String appInstance,
      String appGroup,
      Map<String, String> tags,
      long heartbeatSeconds,
      ScheduledExecutorService scheduler) {
    this.control = Objects.requireNonNull(control, "control");
    this.group = Strings.requireNonBlank(group, "group");
    this.name = Strings.requireNonBlank(name, "name");
    this.instance = Strings.requireNonBlank(instance, "instance");
    this.producerType =
        producerType == null ? DefinitionStatusData.ProducerType.UNKNOWN : producerType;
    this.producerId = Strings.trimToNull(producerId);
    this.datasetId = Strings.trimToNull(datasetId);
    this.host = Strings.trimToNull(host);
    this.appName = Strings.trimToNull(appName);
    this.appInstance = Strings.trimToNull(appInstance);
    this.appGroup = Strings.trimToNull(appGroup);
    this.startEpochMs = System.currentTimeMillis();
    this.tags = new ConcurrentHashMap<>(sanitizeTags(tags));
    this.intervalSec = heartbeatSeconds <= 0 ? DEFAULT_INTERVAL_SECONDS : heartbeatSeconds;
    if (scheduler == null) {
      this.ses = Executors.newSingleThreadScheduledExecutor();
      this.ownsScheduler = true;
    } else {
      this.ses = scheduler;
      this.ownsScheduler = false;
    }
  }

  public void start() {
    publishSafe(state, message);
    heartbeatTask =
        ses.scheduleAtFixedRate(
            () -> publishSafe(state, message), intervalSec, intervalSec, TimeUnit.SECONDS);
  }

  public void publishOnline(String detail) {
    publishState(DefinitionStatusData.State.ONLINE, detail);
  }

  public void publishError(String detail) {
    publishState(DefinitionStatusData.State.ERROR, detail);
  }

  public void publishState(DefinitionStatusData.State state, String detail) {
    this.state = state == null ? DefinitionStatusData.State.UNKNOWN : state;
    this.message = Strings.trimToNull(detail);
    publishSafe(this.state, this.message);
  }

  public void putTag(String key, String value) {
    String normalizedKey = Strings.trimToNull(key);
    if (normalizedKey == null) {
      return;
    }
    String normalizedValue = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalizedValue == null) {
      tags.remove(normalizedKey);
      return;
    }
    tags.put(normalizedKey, normalizedValue);
  }

  @Override
  public void close() {
    if (!open) {
      return;
    }
    open = false;
    publishSafe(DefinitionStatusData.State.OFFLINE, "stopped");
    ScheduledFuture<?> task = heartbeatTask;
    heartbeatTask = null;
    if (task != null) {
      task.cancel(true);
    }
    if (ownsScheduler) {
      ses.shutdownNow();
    }
  }

  private void publishSafe(DefinitionStatusData.State state, String detail) {
    try {
      publish(buildStatus(state, detail));
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      LOGGER.debug(
          "Data status publish failed group={} name={} instance={} reason={}",
          group,
          name,
          instance,
          ex.toString());
    }
  }

  private void publish(DefinitionStatusData status) throws Exception {
    if (status == null) {
      return;
    }
    String payload = om.writeValueAsString(status);
    if (STATUS_DEBUG) {
      LOGGER.debug("[DataStatus] publish topic={} payload={}", DiscoveryTopics.STATUS, payload);
    }
    control.amps().publish(DiscoveryTopics.STATUS, payload);
  }

  private DefinitionStatusData buildStatus(DefinitionStatusData.State state, String detail) {
    DefinitionEnvelope envelope =
        new DefinitionEnvelope(
            group, DefinitionType.STATUS_DATA, name, null, null, null, null, null, null, null);
    long now = System.currentTimeMillis();
    return new DefinitionStatusData(
        envelope,
        group,
        DefinitionType.STATUS_DATA,
        name,
        instance,
        producerType,
        state == null ? DefinitionStatusData.State.UNKNOWN : state,
        producerId,
        datasetId,
        startEpochMs > 0L ? startEpochMs : null,
        now,
        Strings.trimToNull(detail),
        host,
        appName,
        appInstance,
        appGroup,
        tags.isEmpty() ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(tags));
  }

  private static Map<String, String> sanitizeTags(Map<String, String> tags) {
    if (Strings.isEmpty(tags)) {
      return Map.of();
    }
    Map<String, String> normalized = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();
    for (Map.Entry<String, String> entry : tags.entrySet()) {
      if (entry == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String key = Strings.trimToNull(entry.getKey());
      String value = Strings.trimToNull(entry.getValue());
      if (key != null && value != null) {
        normalized.put(key, value);
      }
    }
    return normalized.isEmpty() ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(normalized);
  }
}

FILE: ServiceStatusCache.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.status.service;

import com.crankuptheamps.client.Command;
import com.crankuptheamps.client.Message;
import java.time.Clock;
import java.time.Duration;
import java.time.Instant;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.concurrent.ConcurrentHashMap;
import java.util.concurrent.CountDownLatch;
import java.util.concurrent.TimeUnit;
import java.util.concurrent.atomic.AtomicBoolean;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.ControlConnection;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.cache.DiscoveryTopics;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.codec.DiscoveryCodec;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.Definition;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionStatusService;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

public final class ServiceStatusCache implements AutoCloseable {
  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(ServiceStatusCache.class);
  private static final String TOPIC_STATUS = DiscoveryTopics.STATUS;
  private static final String FILTER_STATUS_SERVICE = "/type='STATUS_SERVICE'";
  private static final Duration DEFAULT_STALE_AFTER = Duration.ofSeconds(15);
  private static final String UNKNOWN = "-";

  private final ControlConnection control;
  private final Clock clock;
  private final Duration staleAfter;
  private final ConcurrentHashMap<Key, StatusSnapshot> statuses = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();
  private final AtomicBoolean started = new AtomicBoolean(false);
  private final AtomicBoolean recovered = new AtomicBoolean(false);
  private final CountDownLatch recoveryLatch = new CountDownLatch(1);
  private volatile ControlConnection.Subscription subscription;

  public ServiceStatusCache(ControlConnection control) {
    this(control, Clock.systemUTC(), DEFAULT_STALE_AFTER);
  }

  ServiceStatusCache(ControlConnection control, Clock clock, Duration staleAfter) {
    this.control = Objects.requireNonNull(control, "control");
    this.clock = Objects.requireNonNull(clock, "clock");
    this.staleAfter =
        staleAfter == null || staleAfter.isNegative() || staleAfter.isZero()
            ? DEFAULT_STALE_AFTER
            : staleAfter;
  }

  public void start() throws Exception {
    if (!started.compareAndSet(false, true)) {
      awaitRecovery(Duration.ofSeconds(30));
      return;
    }
    Command command = new Command(Message.Command.SOWAndSubscribe);
    command.setTopic(TOPIC_STATUS);
    command.setOptions("oof");
    command.setFilter(FILTER_STATUS_SERVICE);
    subscription =
        control
            .sowAndSubscribe(
                command.getTopic(),
                command.getOptions(),
                command.getFilter(),
                message -> handleMessage(message.raw()));
    awaitRecovery(Duration.ofSeconds(30));
    LOGGER.debug("Service status cache ready topics={} enabledTypes={} instanceCount={}", List.of(TOPIC_STATUS), List.of("STATUS_SERVICE"), statuses.size());
  }

  public void startShared() {
    if (!started.compareAndSet(false, true)) {
      awaitRecovery(Duration.ofSeconds(30));
    }
  }

  public boolean recovered() {
    return recovered.get();
  }

  public int size() {
    return statuses.size();
  }

  public List<ServiceStatusRow> snapshot() {
    long nowMs = clock.millis();
    return statuses.entrySet().stream()
        .map(entry -> toRow(entry.getKey(), entry.getValue(), nowMs))
        .sorted(
            Comparator.comparing(
                    (ServiceStatusRow row) ->
                        Strings.trimToEmpty(row.group()), String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER)
                .thenComparing(
                    row -> Strings.trimToEmpty(row.name()), String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER)
                .thenComparing(
                    row -> Strings.trimToEmpty(row.instanceName()), String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER))
        .toList();
  }

  public List<DefinitionStatusService> snapshotDefinitions() {
    return statuses.values().stream().map(StatusSnapshot::status).toList();
  }

  public void stop() {
    ControlConnection.Subscription id = subscription;
    if (id != null) {
      try {
        id.close();
      } catch (Exception ignore) {
      }
      subscription = null;
    }
    statuses.clear();
  }

  @Override
  public void close() {
    stop();
  }

  private ServiceStatusRow toRow(Key key, StatusSnapshot snapshot, long nowMs) {
    DefinitionStatusService status = snapshot.status();
    Map<String, String> tags = status.tags() == null ? Map.of() : status.tags();
    Long heartbeatMs = positive(status.lastHeartbeatEpochMs());
    Instant lastHeartbeatUtc = heartbeatMs == null ? null : Instant.ofEpochMilli(heartbeatMs);
    Instant lastSeenUtc = snapshot.receivedTimeUtc();
    String state = deriveState(status.state(), heartbeatMs, snapshot.receivedTimeUtc(), nowMs);
    String host =
        defaultText(
            firstNonBlank(
                status.host(),
                status.advertiseHost(),
                status.routeHost(),
                tags.get("host"),
                tags.get("hostname")));
    String user =
        defaultText(
            firstNonBlank(
                tags.get("user"),
                tags.get("username"),
                tags.get("runAsUser"),
                tags.get("owner")));
    String pid =
        defaultText(firstNonBlank(tags.get("pid"), tags.get("processId"), tags.get("process.id")));
    String runtime =
        defaultText(
            firstNonBlank(
                status.transport(),
                tags.get("runtime"),
                tags.get("serviceType"),
                tags.get("protocol"),
                tags.get("transport"),
                status.uri()));
    String cpu = defaultText(formatPercent(firstNonBlank(tags.get("cpu"), tags.get("cpuPercent"))));
    String heap =
        defaultText(
            firstNonBlank(
                formatBytes(parseLong(tags.get("heapUsedBytes"))),
                formatBytes(parseLong(tags.get("heapBytes"))),
                tags.get("heap")));
    String uptime =
        defaultText(
            firstNonBlank(
                renderUptimeFromStart(status.startTimestampEpochMs(), nowMs),
                formatDuration(parseLong(tags.get("uptimeMs"))),
                tags.get("uptime")));
    return new ServiceStatusRow(
        key.group(),
        key.name(),
        key.instanceName(),
        state,
        host,
        user,
        pid,
        runtime,
        cpu,
        heap,
        uptime,
        lastHeartbeatUtc,
        lastSeenUtc);
  }

  private String deriveState(
      DefinitionStatusService.State rawState, Long heartbeatMs, Instant lastSeenUtc, long nowMs) {
    if (isOfflineState(rawState)) {
      return "OFFLINE";
    }
    if (isStale(heartbeatMs, lastSeenUtc, nowMs)) {
      return "STALE";
    }
    if (isOnlineState(rawState)) {
      return "ONLINE";
    }
    return "UNKNOWN";
  }

  private boolean isStale(Long heartbeatMs, Instant lastSeenUtc, long nowMs) {
    long referenceMs = heartbeatMs == null ? 0L : heartbeatMs;
    if (referenceMs <= 0L && lastSeenUtc != null) {
      referenceMs = lastSeenUtc.toEpochMilli();
    }
    if (referenceMs <= 0L) {
      return true;
    }
    return nowMs - referenceMs > staleAfter.toMillis();
  }

  private boolean isOnlineState(DefinitionStatusService.State state) {
    return switch (state == null ? DefinitionStatusService.State.UNKNOWN : state) {
      case ONLINE -> true;
      default -> false;
    };
  }

  private boolean isOfflineState(DefinitionStatusService.State state) {
    return switch (state == null ? DefinitionStatusService.State.UNKNOWN : state) {
      case OFFLINE -> true;
      default -> false;
    };
  }

  public void awaitRecovery(Duration timeout) {
    long millis = timeout == null ? 30000L : Math.max(1L, timeout.toMillis());
    try {
      boolean done = recoveryLatch.await(millis, TimeUnit.MILLISECONDS);
      if (!done) {
        throw new IllegalStateException(
            "ServiceStatusCache initial recovery did not complete (GroupEnd not observed)");
      }
    } catch (InterruptedException ex) {
      Thread.currentThread().interrupt();
      throw new IllegalStateException("Interrupted while waiting for ServiceStatusCache recovery", ex);
    }
  }

  private void handleMessage(Message message) {
    if (message == null) {
      return;
    }
    int command = message.getCommand();
    if (command == Message.Command.GroupEnd) {
      recovered.set(true);
      recoveryLatch.countDown();
      return;
    }
    if (command != Message.Command.SOW
        && command != Message.Command.Publish
        && command != Message.Command.OOF
        && command != Message.Command.SOWDelete) {
      return;
    }
    String payload = message.getData();
    if (Strings.isBlank(payload)) {
      return;
    }
    try {
      Definition definition = DiscoveryCodec.decode(payload);
      if (!(definition instanceof DefinitionStatusService status)) {
        return;
      }
      Key key = key(status.group(), status.name(), status.instance());
      if (key == null) {
        return;
      }
      if (command == Message.Command.OOF || command == Message.Command.SOWDelete) {
        statuses.remove(key);
        return;
      }
      statuses.put(key, new StatusSnapshot(status, Instant.now(clock)));
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      LOGGER.warn("Ignoring malformed service status message command={} reason={}", command, ex.toString());
    }
  }

  private static String renderUptimeFromStart(Long startEpochMs, long nowMs) {
    if (startEpochMs == null || startEpochMs <= 0L || nowMs < startEpochMs) {
      return null;
    }
    return formatDuration(nowMs - startEpochMs);
  }

  private static String formatPercent(String value) {
    if (Strings.isBlank(value)) {
      return null;
    }
    String trimmed = value.trim();
    if (trimmed.endsWith("%")) {
      return trimmed;
    }
    return trimmed + "%";
  }

  private static String formatBytes(Long bytes) {
    if (bytes == null || bytes < 0) {
      return null;
    }
    String[] units = {"B", "KiB", "MiB", "GiB", "TiB"};
    double scaled = bytes;
    int unit = 0;
    while (scaled >= 1024.0 && unit < units.length - 1) {
      scaled /= 1024.0;
      unit++;
    }
    return unit == 0
        ? bytes + " B"
        : String.format(java.util.Locale.ROOT, "%.1f %s", scaled, units[unit]);
  }

  private static String formatDuration(Long millis) {
    if (millis == null || millis <= 0L) {
      return null;
    }
    long totalSeconds = millis / 1000L;
    if (totalSeconds <= 0L) {
      return "0s";
    }
    long days = totalSeconds / 86_400;
    long remainder = totalSeconds % 86_400;
    long hours = remainder / 3_600;
    remainder %= 3_600;
    long minutes = remainder / 60;
    long seconds = remainder % 60;
    List<String> parts = new java.util.ArrayList<>(4);
    if (days > 0) {
      parts.add(days + "d");
    }
    if (hours > 0) {
      parts.add(hours + "h");
    }
    if (minutes > 0) {
      parts.add(minutes + "m");
    }
    if (seconds > 0 && parts.isEmpty()) {
      parts.add(seconds + "s");
    }
    return parts.isEmpty() ? "0s" : String.join(" ", parts);
  }

  private static Long parseLong(String value) {
    if (Strings.isBlank(value)) {
      return null;
    }
    try {
      return Long.parseLong(value.trim());
    } catch (NumberFormatException ignore) {
      return null;
    }
  }

  private static Long positive(Long value) {
    return value == null || value <= 0L ? null : value;
  }

  private static String firstNonBlank(String... values) {
    if (values == null) {
      return null;
    }
    for (String value : values) {
      if (Strings.isNotBlank(value)) {
        return value.trim();
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  private static String defaultText(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    return normalized == null ? UNKNOWN : normalized;
  }

  public void onStatusMessage(Message message) {
    handleMessage(message);
  }

  private static Key key(String group, String name, String instanceName) {
    String normalizedGroup = normalizeKey(group);
    String normalizedName = normalizeKey(name);
    String normalizedInstance = normalizeKey(instanceName);
    if (normalizedGroup == null || normalizedName == null || normalizedInstance == null) {
      return null;
    }
    return new Key(normalizedGroup, normalizedName, normalizedInstance);
  }

  private static String normalizeKey(String value) {
    return Strings.trimToNull(value);
  }

  private record Key(String group, String name, String instanceName) {}

  private record StatusSnapshot(DefinitionStatusService status, Instant receivedTimeUtc) {}
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.status.service;

import java.time.Instant;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class ServiceStatusInstance {
  public final String instanceId;
  public final String host;
  public final int port;
  public final String region;
  public final long tsEpochMs;
  public final String status;
  public final boolean tlsRequired;
  public final String routeHost;
  public final Integer routePort;
  public final String routeAuthority;
  public final Map<String, String> attrs;

  public ServiceStatusInstance(
      String instanceId,
      String host,
      int port,
      String region,
      long tsEpochMs,
      String status,
      boolean tlsRequired,
      String routeHost,
      Integer routePort,
      String routeAuthority,
      Map<String, String> attrs) {
    this.instanceId = instanceId;
    this.host = host;
    this.port = port;
    this.region = region;
    this.tsEpochMs = tsEpochMs;
    this.status = status == null ? "ONLINE" : status;
    this.tlsRequired = tlsRequired;
    this.routeHost = Strings.emptyToNull(routeHost);
    this.routePort = routePort;
    this.routeAuthority = Strings.emptyToNull(routeAuthority);
    this.attrs = Strings.isEmpty(attrs) ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(attrs);
  }

  public ServiceHbCache.Target asTarget() {
    return new ServiceHbCache.Target(instanceId, host, port, tlsRequired, null);
  }

  @Override
  public String toString() {
    String base = host + ":" + port + (tlsRequired ? " (TLS)" : "");
    String route =
        (routeHost == null ? "" : " via " + routeHost + ":" + (routePort == null ? 443 : routePort));
    return "ServiceStatusInstance{"
        + instanceId
        + " "
        + base
        + route
        + " status="
        + status
        + " attrs="
        + attrs
        + " ts="
        + Instant.ofEpochMilli(tsEpochMs)
        + "}";
  }

  @Override
  public boolean equals(Object o) {
    if (this == o) {
      return true;
    }
    if (!(o instanceof ServiceStatusInstance that)) {
      return false;
    }
    return port == that.port
        && tlsRequired == that.tlsRequired
        && Objects.equals(instanceId, that.instanceId)
        && Objects.equals(host, that.host)
        && Objects.equals(region, that.region)
        && Objects.equals(status, that.status)
        && Objects.equals(routeHost, that.routeHost)
        && Objects.equals(routePort, that.routePort)
        && Objects.equals(routeAuthority, that.routeAuthority)
        && Objects.equals(attrs, that.attrs);
  }

  @Override
  public int hashCode() {
    return Objects.hash(
        instanceId,
        host,
        port,
        region,
        status,
        tlsRequired,
        routeHost,
        routePort,
        routeAuthority,
        attrs);
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.dataset;

public sealed interface DatasetBinding
    permits DatasetBinding.DuckdbDatasetBinding,
        DatasetBinding.ParquetDatasetBinding,
        DatasetBinding.ExternalDatasetBinding {

  DatasetId id();

  DatasetType type();

  record DuckdbDatasetBinding(DatasetId id, String relationName) implements DatasetBinding {
    @Override
    public DatasetType type() {
      return DatasetType.DUCKDB;
    }
  }

  record ParquetDatasetBinding(
      DatasetId id, String uri, String glob, Boolean hivePartitioning, String connectionName)
      implements DatasetBinding {
    public ParquetDatasetBinding(DatasetId id, String uri, String glob, Boolean hivePartitioning) {
      this(id, uri, glob, hivePartitioning, null);
    }

    @Override
    public DatasetType type() {
      return DatasetType.PARQUET;
    }
  }

  record ExternalDatasetBinding(DatasetId id, String externalType, String reference)
      implements DatasetBinding {
    @Override
    public DatasetType type() {
      return DatasetType.EXTERNAL;
    }
  }
