package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.dataset;

import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.CanonicalIds;

public record DatasetId(String group, String namespace, String name) {
  private static final String PREFIX = "dataset:";
  private static final String EXPECTED_FORMAT = "dataset:<group>/<namespace>/<name>";

  public DatasetId {
    group = requireSegment("group", group);
    namespace = requireSegment("namespace", namespace);
    name = requireSegment("name", name);
  }

  public static DatasetId of(String group, String namespace, String name) {
    return new DatasetId(group, namespace, name);
  }

  public static DatasetId parse(String canonical) {
    final CanonicalIds.ParsedId parsed;
    try {
      parsed = CanonicalIds.parse(canonical);
    } catch (IllegalArgumentException ex) {
      throw invalid(canonical, ex);
    }
    if (!parsed.isDataset()) {
      throw invalid(canonical, null);
    }
    return new DatasetId(parsed.group(), parsed.namespace(), parsed.name());
  }

  public static DatasetId parse(
      String datasetIdOrName, String defaultGroup, String defaultNamespace) {
    String normalized = trimToNull(datasetIdOrName);
    if (normalized == null) {
      throw invalid(datasetIdOrName, null);
    }
    if (normalized.regionMatches(true, 0, PREFIX, 0, PREFIX.length())) {
      return parse(normalized);
    }
    String[] segments = normalized.split("/", -1);
    if (segments.length == 1) {
      return new DatasetId(
          requireSegment("group", defaultGroup),
          requireSegment("namespace", defaultNamespace),
          requireSegment("name", segments[0]));
    }
    if (segments.length == 2) {
      return new DatasetId(
          requireSegment("group", defaultGroup),
          requireSegment("namespace", segments[0]),
          requireSegment("name", segments[1]));
    }
    if (segments.length == 3) {
      return new DatasetId(
          requireSegment("group", segments[0]),
          requireSegment("namespace", segments[1]),
          requireSegment("name", segments[2]));
    }
    throw invalid(datasetIdOrName, null);
  }

  @Override
  public String toString() {
    return PREFIX + group + "/" + namespace + "/" + name;
  }

  private static String requireSegment(String label, String value) {
    String normalized = trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("dataset " + label + " is required");
    }
    return normalized;
  }

  private static String trimToNull(String value) {
    if (value == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String trimmed = value.trim();
    return trimmed.isEmpty() ? null : trimmed;
  }

  private static IllegalArgumentException invalid(String canonical, Throwable cause) {
    String message = "Invalid dataset id '" + canonical + "'. Expected format " + EXPECTED_FORMAT;
    return cause == null ? new IllegalArgumentException(message) : new IllegalArgumentException(message, cause);
  }
}


FILE: DatasetResolver.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.dataset;

import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.cache.DiscoveryCache;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionDataset;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionEnvelope;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionType;

public final class DatasetResolver {
  private final DiscoveryCache DiscoveryCache;

  public DatasetResolver(DiscoveryCache DiscoveryCache) {
    this.DiscoveryCache = Objects.requireNonNull(DiscoveryCache, "DiscoveryCache");
  }

  public DatasetBinding resolve(DatasetId id) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(id, "id");
    DefinitionDataset definition = resolveDefinition(id);
    DefinitionEnvelope envelope = definition.envelope();
    String baseName = requireDatasetBaseName(definition);
    DatasetId resolvedId = DatasetId.of(envelope.group(), definition.namespace(), baseName);

    DatasetType type = definition.type();
    if (type == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Dataset definition has null type: " + definition);
    }
    DefinitionDataset.Binding binding = definition.binding();
    return switch (type) {
      case DUCKDB -> {
        if (binding == null || binding.duckdb() == null) {
          throw new IllegalStateException("Dataset definition missing DUCKDB binding: " + definition);
        }
        yield new DatasetBinding.DuckdbDatasetBinding(resolvedId, binding.duckdb().relationName());
      }
      case PARQUET -> {
        if (binding == null || binding.parquet() == null) {
          throw new IllegalStateException("Dataset definition missing PARQUET binding: " + definition);
        }
        yield new DatasetBinding.ParquetDatasetBinding(
            resolvedId,
            binding.parquet().uri(),
            binding.parquet().glob(),
            binding.parquet().hivePartitioning(),
            binding.parquet().connectionName());
      }
      case EXTERNAL -> {
        if (binding == null) {
          throw new IllegalStateException("Dataset definition missing EXTERNAL binding: " + definition);
        }
        if (binding.odbc() != null) {
          yield new DatasetBinding.ExternalDatasetBinding(
              resolvedId, "ODBC", binding.odbc().connectionName());
        }
        if (binding.external() != null) {
          yield new DatasetBinding.ExternalDatasetBinding(
              resolvedId, binding.external().externalType(), binding.external().reference());
        }
        throw new IllegalStateException("Dataset definition missing EXTERNAL binding: " + definition);
      }
    };
  }

  public DefinitionDataset resolveDefinition(DatasetId id) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(id, "id");
    return DiscoveryCache.list(DefinitionDataset.class, id.group()).stream()
        .filter(candidate -> matches(candidate, id))
        .findFirst()
        .orElseThrow(() -> new IllegalStateException("Dataset definition not found: " + id));
  }

  private boolean matches(DefinitionDataset definition, DatasetId id) {
    requireIdentity(definition);
    DefinitionEnvelope envelope = definition.envelope();
    if (envelope.type() != DefinitionType.DATASET) {
      return false;
    }
    String baseName = requireDatasetBaseName(definition);
    return id.group().equals(envelope.group())
        && id.namespace().equals(definition.namespace())
        && id.name().equals(baseName);
  }

  private void requireIdentity(DefinitionDataset definition) {
    if (definition == null || definition.envelope() == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Dataset definition missing envelope/group/name/namespace: " + definition);
    }
    DefinitionEnvelope envelope = definition.envelope();
    if (isBlank(envelope.group()) || isBlank(envelope.name()) || isBlank(definition.namespace())) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Dataset definition missing envelope/group/name/namespace: " + definition);
    }
  }

  private String requireDatasetBaseName(DefinitionDataset definition) {
    DefinitionEnvelope envelope = definition.envelope();
    String namespace = definition.namespace();
    String envelopeName = envelope.name();
    String prefix = namespace + "/";

    if (!envelopeName.startsWith(prefix)) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "Dataset definition invalid envelope.name. Expected namespace/baseName with namespace='"
              + namespace
              + "' and envelope.name='"
              + envelopeName
              + "': "
              + definition);
    }
    String baseName = envelopeName.substring(prefix.length());
    if (isBlank(baseName) || baseName.indexOf('/') >= 0) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "Dataset definition invalid envelope.name. Expected namespace/baseName with namespace='"
              + namespace
              + "' and envelope.name='"
              + envelopeName
              + "': "
              + definition);
    }
    return baseName;
  }

  private static boolean isBlank(String value) {
    return value == null || value.isBlank();
  }
}

FILE: DuckdbEngine.java

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.duckdb;

import java.sql.Connection;
import java.sql.DriverManager;
import java.sql.ResultSet;
import java.sql.SQLException;
import java.sql.Statement;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

public final class DuckdbEngine implements AutoCloseable {
  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(DuckdbEngine.class);
  private final Connection systemConnection;
  private volatile boolean closed;

  public DuckdbEngine() {
    ensureDriverLoaded();
    DuckdbExtensions.requireDefaultExtensionDir();
    this.systemConnection = openConnection();
    try {
      if (!ping(systemConnection)) {
        throw new IllegalStateException("DuckDB engine ping failed");
      }
      LOGGER.debug("DuckDB engine started dbPath=:memory:");
    } catch (RuntimeException ex) {
      closeConnection(systemConnection);
      throw ex;
    }
  }

  public synchronized DuckdbSession openSession() {
    requireOpen();
    return new DuckdbSession(openConnection());
  }

  public synchronized DuckdbSession openSession(String databasePath) {
    requireOpen();
    String normalizedPath = Strings.requireNonBlank(databasePath, "databasePath");
    return new DuckdbSession(openConnection(normalizedPath));
  }

  @Override
  public synchronized void close() {
    if (closed) {
      return;
    }
    closed = true;
    closeConnection(systemConnection);
  }

  private static Connection openConnection() {
    try {
      return DriverManager.getConnection("jdbc:duckdb:");
    } catch (SQLException ex) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Failed to open DuckDB connection", ex);
    }
  }

  private static Connection openConnection(String databasePath) {
    try {
      return DriverManager.getConnection("jdbc:duckdb:" + databasePath);
    } catch (SQLException ex) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "Failed to open DuckDB connection for databasePath=" + databasePath, ex);
    }
  }

  private static void ensureDriverLoaded() {
    try {
      Class.forName("org.duckdb.DuckDBDriver");
    } catch (ClassNotFoundException ex) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("DuckDB JDBC driver not found on classpath", ex);
    }
  }

  private static void closeConnection(Connection connection) {
    if (connection == null) {
      return;
    }
    try {
      connection.close();
    } catch (SQLException ex) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Failed to close DuckDB connection", ex);
    }
  }

  private static boolean ping(Connection connection) {
    try (Statement statement = connection.createStatement();
        ResultSet result = statement.executeQuery("select 1")) {
      return result.next() && result.getInt(1) == 1;
    } catch (SQLException ex) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("DuckDB ping failed: " + ex.getMessage(), ex);
    }
  }

  private void requireOpen() {
    if (closed) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("DuckDB engine is closed");
    }
  }
}


FILE: DuckdbExtensions.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.duckdb;

import java.nio.file.Path;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class DuckdbExtensions {
  private static final String HTTPFS_EXTENSION = "httpfs";
  private static final String ODBC_EXTENSION = "odbc";
  private static final String ODBC_FALLBACK_EXTENSION = "odbc_scanner";
  private static volatile boolean httpfsLoaded;

  private DuckdbExtensions() {}

  public static String requireDefaultExtensionDir() {
    return requireDefaultExtensionDir(System.getProperty("user.home"));
  }

  static String requireDefaultExtensionDir(String userHome) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(userHome);
    if (normalized == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("DuckDB default extensionDir requires user.home");
    }
    return Path.of(normalized, ".fabric", "duckdb", "extensions").toString();
  }

  public static synchronized void requireHttpfs(DuckdbSession session) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(session, "session");
    if (httpfsLoaded) {
      return;
    }
    String extensionDir = requireDefaultExtensionDir();
    try {
      configureSession(session, extensionDir);
      session.exec("INSTALL '" + HTTPFS_EXTENSION + "'");
      session.exec("LOAD '" + HTTPFS_EXTENSION + "'");
      httpfsLoaded = true;
    } catch (RuntimeException ex) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "DuckDB httpfs extension is required for S3 access. extensionDir="
              + extensionDir
              + " error="
              + ex.getMessage(),
          ex);
    }
  }

  public static synchronized void requireOdbc(DuckdbSession session) {
    loadOdbc(session);
  }

  public static synchronized OdbcExtensionLoadResult loadOdbc(DuckdbSession session) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(session, "session");
    String extensionDir = requireDefaultExtensionDir();
    try {
      configureSession(session, extensionDir);
      session.exec("INSTALL '" + ODBC_EXTENSION + "'");
      session.exec("LOAD '" + ODBC_EXTENSION + "'");
      return new OdbcExtensionLoadResult(
          ODBC_EXTENSION,
          false,
          true,
          "ODBC_EXTENSION_READY extension=" + ODBC_EXTENSION);
    } catch (RuntimeException ex) {
      String reason =
          Strings.firstNonBlank(
              Strings.trimToNull(ex.getMessage()), ex.getClass().getSimpleName());
      if (isUnavailable(reason, ODBC_EXTENSION)) {
        try {
          session.exec("INSTALL '" + ODBC_FALLBACK_EXTENSION + "'");
          session.exec("LOAD '" + ODBC_FALLBACK_EXTENSION + "'");
          return new OdbcExtensionLoadResult(
              ODBC_FALLBACK_EXTENSION,
              true,
              true,
              "ODBC_EXTENSION_READY extension="
                  + ODBC_FALLBACK_EXTENSION
                  + " fallbackFrom="
                  + ODBC_EXTENSION);
        } catch (RuntimeException fallbackEx) {
          String fallbackReason =
              Strings.firstNonBlank(
                  Strings.trimToNull(fallbackEx.getMessage()),
                  fallbackEx.getClass().getSimpleName());
          if (isUnavailable(fallbackReason, ODBC_FALLBACK_EXTENSION)) {
            throw new IllegalStateException("ODBC_EXTENSION_UNAVAILABLE extension=odbc", ex);
          }
          throw new IllegalStateException(
              "ODBC_EXTENSION_LOAD_FAILED extension=odbc reason="
                  + compactReason(fallbackReason),
              fallbackEx);
        }
      }
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "ODBC_EXTENSION_LOAD_FAILED extension=odbc reason=" + compactReason(reason), ex);
    }
  }

  private static boolean isUnavailable(String reason, String extensionName) {
    String normalized = Strings.firstNonBlank(reason, "").toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
    return normalized.contains(extensionName.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT))
        && (normalized.contains("missing")
            || normalized.contains("not found")
            || normalized.contains("no such file")
            || normalized.contains("could not")
            || normalized.contains("cannot open")
            || normalized.contains("autoload")
            || normalized.contains("install")
            || normalized.contains("extension"));
  }

  private static void configureSession(DuckdbSession session, String extensionDir) {
    session.exec("SET extension_directory='" + escapeSql(extensionDir) + "'");
    session.exec("SET autoinstall_known_extensions=false");
    session.exec("SET autoload_known_extensions=false");
  }

  private static String escapeSql(String value) {
    return value.replace("'", "''");
  }

  private static String compactReason(String reason) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(reason);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return "unknown";
    }
    return normalized.replace('\n', ' ').replace('\r', ' ');
  }

  public record OdbcExtensionLoadResult(
      String extensionNameUsed,
      boolean fallbackInUse,
      boolean extensionLoaded,
      String message) {}
}


FILE: DuckdbNotifier.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.duckdb;

import java.util.OptionalLong;
import java.util.concurrent.ConcurrentHashMap;
import java.util.concurrent.ConcurrentMap;
import java.util.concurrent.TimeUnit;
import java.util.concurrent.atomic.LongAdder;
import java.util.concurrent.locks.Condition;
import java.util.concurrent.locks.ReentrantLock;
import java.util.function.BooleanSupplier;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class DuckdbNotifier {
  private static final DuckdbNotifier SHARED = new DuckdbNotifier();

  private final ConcurrentMap<String, State> states = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();
  private final LongAdder awaitCount = new LongAdder();
  private final LongAdder wakeupCount = new LongAdder();

  public static DuckdbNotifier shared() {
    return SHARED;
  }

  public void notifyChanged(String datasetId, long newSeq) {
    String key = normalizeDatasetId(datasetId);
    if (newSeq <= 0L) {
      return;
    }
    State state = states.computeIfAbsent(key, ignored -> new State());
    state.lock.lock();
    try {
      if (newSeq > state.lastSeq) {
        state.lastSeq = newSeq;
        state.changed.signalAll();
      }
    } finally {
      state.lock.unlock();
    }
  }

  public OptionalLong awaitNextSeq(
      String datasetId, long afterSeq, long timeoutMillis, BooleanSupplier cancelToken) {
    String key = normalizeDatasetId(datasetId);
    long threshold = Math.max(0L, afterSeq);
    long timeoutNanos = TimeUnit.MILLISECONDS.toNanos(Math.max(1L, timeoutMillis));
    State state = states.computeIfAbsent(key, ignored -> new State());
    if (state.lastSeq > threshold) {
      wakeupCount.increment();
      return OptionalLong.of(state.lastSeq);
    }
    state.lock.lock();
    try {
      while (state.lastSeq <= threshold) {
        if (cancelToken != null && cancelToken.getAsBoolean()) {
          return OptionalLong.empty();
        }
        if (timeoutNanos <= 0L) {
          return OptionalLong.empty();
        }
        awaitCount.increment();
        try {
          timeoutNanos = state.changed.awaitNanos(timeoutNanos);
        } catch (InterruptedException ex) {
          Thread.currentThread().interrupt();
          return OptionalLong.empty();
        }
      }
      wakeupCount.increment();
      return OptionalLong.of(state.lastSeq);
    } finally {
      state.lock.unlock();
    }
  }

  public long awaitCount() {
    return awaitCount.sum();
  }

  public long wakeupCount() {
    return wakeupCount.sum();
  }

  public void resetForTests() {
    states.clear();
    awaitCount.reset();
    wakeupCount.reset();
  }

  private static String normalizeDatasetId(String datasetId) {
    return Strings.requireNonBlank(datasetId, "datasetId").trim();
  }

  private static final class State {
    private final ReentrantLock lock = new ReentrantLock();
    private final Condition changed = lock.newCondition();
    private volatile long lastSeq;
  }
}



FILE: DuckdbSession.java

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.duckdb;

import java.sql.Connection;
import java.sql.PreparedStatement;
import java.sql.ResultSet;
import java.sql.SQLException;
import java.sql.Statement;
import java.util.Objects;

public final class DuckdbSession implements AutoCloseable {
  private final Connection connection;
  private volatile boolean closed;

  DuckdbSession(Connection connection) {
    this.connection = Objects.requireNonNull(connection, "connection");
  }

  public void exec(String sql) {
    requireOpen();
    String normalized = Objects.requireNonNull(sql, "sql").trim();
    if (normalized.isEmpty()) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("sql is required");
    }
    try (Statement statement = connection.createStatement()) {
      statement.execute(normalized);
    } catch (SQLException ex) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "DuckDB SQL failed: " + normalized + " error=" + ex.getMessage(), ex);
    }
  }

  public void execSensitive(String sql) {
    requireOpen();
    String normalized = Objects.requireNonNull(sql, "sql").trim();
    if (normalized.isEmpty()) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("sql is required");
    }
    try (Statement statement = connection.createStatement()) {
      statement.execute(normalized);
    } catch (SQLException ex) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("DuckDB SQL failed for sensitive statement");
    }
  }

  public boolean ping() {
    requireOpen();
    try (Statement statement = connection.createStatement();
        ResultSet result = statement.executeQuery("select 1")) {
      return result.next() && result.getInt(1) == 1;
    } catch (SQLException ex) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("DuckDB ping failed: " + ex.getMessage(), ex);
    }
  }

  public Statement createStatement() throws SQLException {
    requireOpen();
    return connection.createStatement();
  }

  public PreparedStatement prepareStatement(String sql) throws SQLException {
    requireOpen();
    return connection.prepareStatement(sql);
  }

  @Override
  public void close() {
    if (closed) {
      return;
    }
    closed = true;
    try {
      connection.close();
    } catch (SQLException ex) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Failed to close DuckDB session", ex);
    }
  }

  private void requireOpen() {
    if (closed) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("DuckDB session is closed");
    }
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.duckdb;

import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionConnection;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionDataset;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionIngestSource;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class OdbcRuntimeGuard {
  private static final String ODBC = "ODBC";

  private OdbcRuntimeGuard() {}

  public static boolean isOdbcType(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    return normalized != null && ODBC.equalsIgnoreCase(normalized);
  }

  public static void failDatasetRuntime(String datasetId, String databaseType) {
    throw new IllegalStateException(
        "ODBC_RUNTIME_NOT_AVAILABLE datasetId="
            + Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(datasetId), "<unknown>")
            + " databaseType="
            + Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(databaseType), "OTHER"));
  }

  public static void failDatasetRuntime(String datasetId, DefinitionDataset.OdbcBinding odbc) {
    failDatasetRuntime(
        datasetId, odbc == null || odbc.databaseType() == null ? null : odbc.databaseType().name());
  }

  public static void failIngestRuntime(String ingestName, String databaseType) {
    throw new IllegalStateException(
        "ODBC_INGEST_RUNTIME_NOT_AVAILABLE ingestName="
            + Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(ingestName), "<unknown>")
            + " databaseType="
            + Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(databaseType), "OTHER"));
  }

  public static void failIngestRuntime(String ingestName, DefinitionIngestSource.OdbcSource odbc) {
    failIngestRuntime(
        ingestName, odbc == null || odbc.databaseType() == null ? null : odbc.databaseType().name());
  }

  public static void failIngestRuntime(
      String ingestName, DefinitionConnection.Odbc.DatabaseType databaseType) {
    failIngestRuntime(ingestName, databaseType == null ? null : databaseType.name());
  }

  public static void failConnectionRuntime(String connectionName, String databaseType) {
    throw new IllegalStateException(
        "ODBC_RUNTIME_NOT_AVAILABLE connectionName="
            + Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(connectionName), "<unknown>")
            + " databaseType="
            + Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(databaseType), "OTHER"));
  }

  public static void failConnectionRuntime(
      String connectionName, DefinitionConnection.Odbc odbc) {
    failConnectionRuntime(
        connectionName, odbc == null || odbc.databaseType() == null ? null : odbc.databaseType().name());
  }
}

FILE: NamespaceEntitlementDefaults.java

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.entitlements;

import java.time.Instant;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.CanonicalIds;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.cache.DiscoveryCache;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionDataset;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionEntitlement;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionEnvelope;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionType;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

/** Applies default namespace entitlement policy at first dataset registration. */
public final class NamespaceEntitlementDefaults {
  private static final String PLATFORM_GROUP = "platform";

  private NamespaceEntitlementDefaults() {}

  public static void ensureDefaultNamespaceAccess(
      DiscoveryCache cache,
      DiscoveryCache.ConfigCacheTx tx,
      DefinitionDataset datasetDefinition,
      String actor) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(cache, "cache");
    Objects.requireNonNull(tx, "tx");
    Objects.requireNonNull(datasetDefinition, "datasetDefinition");

    NamespaceIdentity identity = resolveNamespaceIdentity(datasetDefinition);
    if (identity == null) {
      return;
    }

    String namespaceScopeId = "namespace:" + identity.group() + "/" + identity.namespace();
    if (hasDirectNamespaceEntitlement(cache, identity.group(), namespaceScopeId)) {
      return;
    }

    DefinitionEntitlement definition = buildDefaultDefinition(identity, namespaceScopeId, actor);
    cache.upsertTx(tx, definition);
  }

  private static boolean hasDirectNamespaceEntitlement(
      DiscoveryCache cache, String group, String namespaceScopeId) {
    for (DefinitionEntitlement entitlement : cache.list(DefinitionEntitlement.class, group)) {
      if (entitlement == null || entitlement.envelope() == null) {
        continue;
      }
      if (Boolean.FALSE.equals(entitlement.envelope().enabled())) {
        continue;
      }
      String scopeType = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(entitlement.scopeType()), "namespace");
      if (!"namespace".equalsIgnoreCase(scopeType)) {
        continue;
      }
      String canonicalScope = canonicalNamespaceScope(entitlement.scopeId());
      if (namespaceScopeId.equals(canonicalScope)) {
        return true;
      }
    }
    return false;
  }

  private static String canonicalNamespaceScope(String scopeId) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(scopeId);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return null;
    }
    try {
      CanonicalIds.ParsedId parsed = CanonicalIds.parse(normalized);
      if (!parsed.isNamespace()) {
        return null;
      }
      return parsed.canonical();
    } catch (RuntimeException ex) {
      return null;
    }
  }

  private static DefinitionEntitlement buildDefaultDefinition(
      NamespaceIdentity identity, String namespaceScopeId, String actor) {
    String now = Instant.now().toString();
    String normalizedActor = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(actor), "fabric-lite");
    String entitlementName = "overrides/namespaces/" + identity.namespace();
    DefinitionEnvelope envelope =
        new DefinitionEnvelope(
            identity.group(),
            DefinitionType.ENTITLEMENT,
            entitlementName,
            "ent-namespace-" + identity.namespace() + "-" + identity.group(),
            true,
            "ACTIVE",
            now,
            normalizedActor,
            now,
            normalizedActor);

    DefinitionEntitlement.ObligationSet emptyObligations =
        new DefinitionEntitlement.ObligationSet(
            List.of(), List.of(), List.of(), List.of(), List.of(), Map.of());
    List<DefinitionEntitlement.PolicyBinding> bindings =
        List.of(
            new DefinitionEntitlement.PolicyBinding(
                "namespace-read-allow-group-0",
                "group:" + identity.group(),
                "read",
                "ALLOW",
                true,
                emptyObligations,
                Map.of(),
                Map.of()),
            new DefinitionEntitlement.PolicyBinding(
                "namespace-read-allow-group-1",
                "group:" + PLATFORM_GROUP,
                "read",
                "ALLOW",
                true,
                emptyObligations,
                Map.of(),
                Map.of()),
            new DefinitionEntitlement.PolicyBinding(
                "namespace-write-allow-group-0",
                "group:" + identity.group(),
                "write",
                "ALLOW",
                true,
                emptyObligations,
                Map.of(),
                Map.of()));

    DefinitionEntitlement.PolicyDocument policy =
        new DefinitionEntitlement.PolicyDocument(
            "1.0",
            namespaceScopeId,
            identity.group(),
            identity.namespace(),
            "NAMESPACE",
            "NAMESPACE",
            namespaceScopeId,
            "DATASET",
            "namespace-" + identity.namespace(),
            "Namespace entitlements",
            "1",
            true,
            "ACTIVE",
            Map.of(),
            bindings);
    return new DefinitionEntitlement(
        envelope,
        "namespace",
        namespaceScopeId,
        List.of(policy),
        List.of(),
        Map.of("managedBy", "fabric-lite-defaults", "defaultPlatformRead", "true"),
        List.of("Auto-created namespace entitlement"));
  }

  private static NamespaceIdentity resolveNamespaceIdentity(DefinitionDataset definition) {
    DefinitionEnvelope envelope = definition == null ? null : definition.envelope();
    String group = Strings.trimToNull(envelope == null ? null : envelope.group());
    String namespace =
        Strings.firstNonBlank(
            Strings.trimToNull(definition == null ? null : definition.namespace()),
            namespaceFromEnvelopeName(envelope));
    if (group == null || namespace == null) {
      return null;
    }
    return new NamespaceIdentity(group, namespace);
  }

  private static String namespaceFromEnvelopeName(DefinitionEnvelope envelope) {
    String name = Strings.trimToNull(envelope == null ? null : envelope.name());
    if (name == null) {
      return null;
    }
    int split = name.indexOf('/');
    if (split <= 0) {
      return null;
    }
    return Strings.trimToNull(name.substring(0, split));
  }

  private record NamespaceIdentity(String group, String namespace) {}
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.format;

public interface FormatDecoder {
  byte[] decodeToArrowIpc(FormatDecodeRequest request);
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.format;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonNode;
import java.io.ByteArrayOutputStream;
import java.io.IOException;
import java.nio.charset.StandardCharsets;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import org.apache.arrow.memory.RootAllocator;
import org.apache.arrow.vector.BigIntVector;
import org.apache.arrow.vector.BitVector;
import org.apache.arrow.vector.DateDayVector;
import org.apache.arrow.vector.FieldVector;
import org.apache.arrow.vector.Float8Vector;
import org.apache.arrow.vector.IntVector;
import org.apache.arrow.vector.TimeStampMicroVector;
import org.apache.arrow.vector.VarCharVector;
import org.apache.arrow.vector.VectorSchemaRoot;
import org.apache.arrow.vector.ipc.ArrowStreamWriter;
import org.apache.arrow.vector.types.DateUnit;
import org.apache.arrow.vector.types.FloatingPointPrecision;
import org.apache.arrow.vector.types.TimeUnit;
import org.apache.arrow.vector.types.pojo.ArrowType;
import org.apache.arrow.vector.types.pojo.Field;
import org.apache.arrow.vector.types.pojo.FieldType;
import org.apache.arrow.vector.types.pojo.Schema;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.codec.DiscoveryCodec;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionSchema;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class FormatDecoderArrowBuilder {
  private static final long MAX_ALLOCATOR_BYTES = 64L * 1024L * 1024L;

  public BuildSession open(FormatDecodeRequest request) {
    if (request == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("request is required");
    }
    return open(describeFields(request.ingestName(), request.outputSchemaId(), request.schemaDefinition()));
  }

  public BuildSession open(List<FormatField> fields) {
    if (fields == null || fields.isEmpty()) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("fields are required");
    }
    return new BuildSession(List.copyOf(fields));
  }

  public List<FormatField> describeFields(
      String ingestName, String outputSchemaId, DefinitionSchema schemaDefinition) {
    return parseFields(schemaDefinition, ingestName, outputSchemaId);
  }

  private static List<FormatField> parseFields(
      DefinitionSchema schemaDefinition, String ingestName, String outputSchemaId) {
    String schemaText = Strings.trimToNull(schemaDefinition == null ? null : schemaDefinition.schema());
    if (schemaText == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "Expected schema payload is empty for ingest="
              + ingestName
              + " expectedSchema="
              + outputSchemaId);
    }
    try {
      JsonNode root = DiscoveryCodec.mapper().readTree(schemaText);
      JsonNode fieldsNode = root.path("fields");
      if (!fieldsNode.isArray()) {
        fieldsNode = root.path("columns");
      }
      if (!fieldsNode.isArray() || fieldsNode.isEmpty()) {
        throw new IllegalStateException(
            "Expected schema has no fields for ingest="
                + ingestName
                + " expectedSchema="
                + outputSchemaId);
      }
      List<FormatField> fields = new ArrayList<>();
      Map<String, Integer> byName = new LinkedHashMap<>();
      int index = 0;
      for (JsonNode fieldNode : fieldsNode) {
        String fieldName = Strings.trimToNull(fieldNode.path("name").asText(null));
        if (fieldName == null) {
          throw new IllegalStateException(
              "Expected schema field name is required at index "
                  + index
                  + " for ingest="
                  + ingestName
                  + " expectedSchema="
                  + outputSchemaId);
        }
        if (byName.containsKey(fieldName)) {
          throw new IllegalStateException(
              "Expected schema has duplicate field name '"
                  + fieldName
                  + "' for ingest="
                  + ingestName
                  + " expectedSchema="
                  + outputSchemaId);
        }
        ValueKind valueKind =
            parseValueKind(fieldNode.path("type"), fieldName, ingestName, outputSchemaId);
        fields.add(
            new FormatField(
                index,
                fieldName,
                fieldNode.path("nullable").asBoolean(true),
                valueKind.expectedTypeLabel(),
                valueKind));
        byName.put(fieldName, index);
        index++;
      }
      return List.copyOf(fields);
    } catch (IOException ex) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "Expected schema payload is not valid JSON for ingest="
              + ingestName
              + " expectedSchema="
              + outputSchemaId,
          ex);
    }
  }

  private static ValueKind parseValueKind(
      JsonNode typeNode, String fieldName, String ingestName, String outputSchemaId) {
    if (typeNode != null && typeNode.isObject()) {
      String name = normalize(typeNode.path("name").asText(null));
      if ("UTF8".equals(name)) {
        return ValueKind.UTF8;
      }
      if ("BOOL".equals(name) || "BOOLEAN".equals(name)) {
        return ValueKind.BOOL;
      }
      if ("INT".equals(name)) {
        int bitWidth = typeNode.path("bitWidth").asInt(32);
        boolean signed = !typeNode.has("isSigned") || typeNode.path("isSigned").asBoolean(true);
        if (!signed) {
          throw unsupportedType(fieldName, ingestName, outputSchemaId, typeNode.toString());
        }
        return switch (bitWidth) {
          case 32 -> ValueKind.INT32;
          case 64 -> ValueKind.INT64;
          default -> throw unsupportedType(fieldName, ingestName, outputSchemaId, typeNode.toString());
        };
      }
      if ("FLOATINGPOINT".equals(name)) {
        String precision = normalize(typeNode.path("precision").asText(null));
        if ("DOUBLE".equals(precision)) {
          return ValueKind.FLOAT64;
        }
      }
      if ("DATE".equals(name)) {
        String unit = normalize(typeNode.path("unit").asText("DAY"));
        if ("DAY".equals(unit)) {
          return ValueKind.DATE_DAY;
        }
      }
      if ("TIMESTAMP".equals(name)) {
        String unit = normalize(typeNode.path("unit").asText("MICROSECOND"));
        if ("MICROSECOND".equals(unit)) {
          return ValueKind.TIMESTAMP_MICROSECOND;
        }
      }
      throw unsupportedType(fieldName, ingestName, outputSchemaId, typeNode.toString());
    }

    String token = Strings.trimToNull(typeNode == null ? null : typeNode.asText(null));
    String normalized = normalize(token);
    if (normalized == null) {
      throw unsupportedType(fieldName, ingestName, outputSchemaId, String.valueOf(typeNode));
    }
    if ("UTF8".equals(normalized)
        || "STRING".equals(normalized)
        || "VARCHAR".equals(normalized)
        || "CHAR".equals(normalized)
        || "TEXT".equals(normalized)) {
      return ValueKind.UTF8;
    }
    if ("BOOL".equals(normalized) || "BOOLEAN".equals(normalized)) {
      return ValueKind.BOOL;
    }
    if ("INT32".equals(normalized)
        || "INT".equals(normalized)
        || "INTEGER".equals(normalized)
        || "INT(32)".equals(normalized)) {
      return ValueKind.INT32;
    }
    if ("INT64".equals(normalized)
        || "LONG".equals(normalized)
        || "BIGINT".equals(normalized)
        || "INT(64)".equals(normalized)) {
      return ValueKind.INT64;
    }
    if ("FLOAT64".equals(normalized)
        || "DOUBLE".equals(normalized)
        || "FLOAT".equals(normalized)
        || "REAL".equals(normalized)
        || "FLOATINGPOINT(DOUBLE)".equals(normalized)) {
      return ValueKind.FLOAT64;
    }
    if ("DATE32".equals(normalized) || "DATE".equals(normalized) || "DATE(DAY)".equals(normalized)) {
      return ValueKind.DATE_DAY;
    }
    if ("TIMESTAMP".equals(normalized)
        || "TIMESTAMP(MICROSECOND)".equals(normalized)
        || "TIMESTAMP[US]".equals(normalized)
        || normalized.contains("MICROSECOND")) {
      return ValueKind.TIMESTAMP_MICROSECOND;
    }
    throw unsupportedType(fieldName, ingestName, outputSchemaId, token);
  }

  private static IllegalStateException unsupportedType(
      String fieldName, String ingestName, String outputSchemaId, String typeToken) {
    return new IllegalStateException(
        "Unsupported schema type for field="
            + fieldName
            + " ingest="
            + ingestName
            + " expectedSchema="
            + outputSchemaId
            + " type="
            + typeToken);
  }

  private static String normalize(String value) {
    return value == null ? null : value.toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT).replace(" ", "");
  }

  public record FormatField(
      int index, String name, boolean nullable, String expectedType, ValueKind valueKind) {}

  public enum ValueKind {
    UTF8("Utf8"),
    INT32("Int32"),
    INT64("Int64"),
    FLOAT64("Float64"),
    DATE_DAY("Date(DAY)"),
    TIMESTAMP_MICROSECOND("Timestamp(MICROSECOND)"),
    BOOL("Bool");

    private final String expectedTypeLabel;

    ValueKind(String expectedTypeLabel) {
      this.expectedTypeLabel = expectedTypeLabel;
    }

    public String expectedTypeLabel() {
      return expectedTypeLabel;
    }
  }

  public static final class BuildSession implements AutoCloseable {
    private final RootAllocator allocator;
    private final VectorSchemaRoot root;
    private final ArrowStreamWriter writer;
    private final ByteArrayOutputStream out;
    private final List<FormatField> fields;
    private final List<FieldVector> vectors;
    private boolean finished;

    private BuildSession(List<FormatField> fields) {
      this.fields = fields;
      List<Field> arrowFields = new ArrayList<>(fields.size());
      for (FormatField field : fields) {
        arrowFields.add(
            new Field(
                field.name(),
                new FieldType(field.nullable(), arrowType(field.valueKind()), null, null),
                null));
      }
      allocator = new RootAllocator(MAX_ALLOCATOR_BYTES);
      root = VectorSchemaRoot.create(new Schema(arrowFields), allocator);
      root.allocateNew();
      out = new ByteArrayOutputStream();
      writer = new ArrowStreamWriter(root, null, out);
      try {
        writer.start();
      } catch (IOException ex) {
        throw new IllegalStateException("Failed to start Arrow stream writer", ex);
      }
      vectors = List.copyOf(root.getFieldVectors());
    }

    public List<FormatField> fields() {
      return fields;
    }

    public void setNull(FormatField field, int rowIndex) {
      FieldVector vector = vector(field);
      vector.setNull(rowIndex);
    }

    public void setValue(FormatField field, int rowIndex, Object value) {
      if (value == null) {
        setNull(field, rowIndex);
        return;
      }
      FieldVector vector = vector(field);
      switch (field.valueKind()) {
        case UTF8 ->
            requireVector(vector, VarCharVector.class, field)
                .setSafe(rowIndex, value.toString().getBytes(StandardCharsets.UTF_8));
        case INT32 -> requireVector(vector, IntVector.class, field).setSafe(rowIndex, (Integer) value);
        case INT64 -> requireVector(vector, BigIntVector.class, field).setSafe(rowIndex, (Long) value);
        case FLOAT64 -> requireVector(vector, Float8Vector.class, field).setSafe(rowIndex, (Double) value);
        case DATE_DAY -> requireVector(vector, DateDayVector.class, field).setSafe(rowIndex, (Integer) value);
        case TIMESTAMP_MICROSECOND ->
            requireVector(vector, TimeStampMicroVector.class, field).setSafe(rowIndex, (Long) value);
        case BOOL -> requireVector(vector, BitVector.class, field).setSafe(rowIndex, Boolean.TRUE.equals(value) ? 1 : 0);
      }
    }

    public byte[] finish(int rowCount) {
      if (finished) {
        throw new IllegalStateException("BuildSession already finished");
      }
      if (rowCount <= 0) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("rowCount must be > 0");
      }
      for (FieldVector vector : vectors) {
        vector.setValueCount(rowCount);
      }
      root.setRowCount(rowCount);
      try {
        writer.writeBatch();
        writer.end();
      } catch (IOException ex) {
        throw new IllegalStateException("Failed to write Arrow IPC batch", ex);
      }
      finished = true;
      return out.toByteArray();
    }

    private FieldVector vector(FormatField field) {
      if (field == null) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("field is required");
      }
      int index = field.index();
      if (index < 0 || index >= vectors.size()) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("Unknown field index: " + index);
      }
      return vectors.get(index);
    }

    private static ArrowType arrowType(ValueKind valueKind) {
      return switch (valueKind) {
        case UTF8 -> new ArrowType.Utf8();
        case INT32 -> new ArrowType.Int(32, true);
        case INT64 -> new ArrowType.Int(64, true);
        case FLOAT64 -> new ArrowType.FloatingPoint(FloatingPointPrecision.DOUBLE);
        case DATE_DAY -> new ArrowType.Date(DateUnit.DAY);
        case TIMESTAMP_MICROSECOND -> new ArrowType.Timestamp(TimeUnit.MICROSECOND, null);
        case BOOL -> new ArrowType.Bool();
      };
    }

    private static <T extends FieldVector> T requireVector(
        FieldVector vector, Class<T> expectedType, FormatField field) {
      if (expectedType.isInstance(vector)) {
        return expectedType.cast(vector);
      }
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "Unexpected vector type for field="
              + field.name()
              + " expected="
              + expectedType.getSimpleName()
              + " actual="
              + vector.getClass().getSimpleName());
    }

    @Override
    public void close() {
      try {
        writer.close();
      } catch (Exception ignore) {
      }
      try {
        root.close();
      } catch (Exception ignore) {
      }
      allocator.close();
    }
  }
}





FILE: FormatDecoderConversions.java

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.format;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonNode;
import java.time.Instant;
import java.time.LocalDate;
import java.time.format.DateTimeParseException;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.format.FormatDecoderArrowBuilder.FormatField;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

final class FormatDecoderConversions {
  private FormatDecoderConversions() {}

  static Object fromJson(JsonNode value, FormatField field, String ingestName) {
    if (value == null || value.isNull()) {
      return null;
    }
    return switch (field.valueKind()) {
      case UTF8 -> convertUtf8Json(value, field, ingestName);
      case INT32 -> convertInt32Json(value, field, ingestName);
      case INT64 -> convertInt64Json(value, field, ingestName);
      case FLOAT64 -> convertFloat64Json(value, field, ingestName);
      case DATE_DAY -> convertDateJson(value, field, ingestName);
      case TIMESTAMP_MICROSECOND -> convertTimestampJson(value, field, ingestName);
      case BOOL -> convertBoolJson(value, field, ingestName);
    };
  }

  static Object fromString(String value, FormatField field, String ingestName) {
    if (value == null) {
      return null;
    }
    return switch (field.valueKind()) {
      case UTF8 -> value;
      case INT32 -> parseInt32(value, field, ingestName);
      case INT64 -> parseInt64(value, field, ingestName);
      case FLOAT64 -> parseFloat64(value, field, ingestName);
      case DATE_DAY -> parseDateEpochDay(value, field, ingestName);
      case TIMESTAMP_MICROSECOND -> parseTimestampMicros(value, field, ingestName);
      case BOOL -> parseBoolean(value, field, ingestName);
    };
  }

  private static Object convertUtf8Json(JsonNode value, FormatField field, String ingestName) {
    if (value.isTextual() || value.isNumber() || value.isBoolean()) {
      return value.asText();
    }
    throw conversionError(ingestName, field, value.toString());
  }

  private static Integer convertInt32Json(JsonNode value, FormatField field, String ingestName) {
    if (value.isIntegralNumber()) {
      long parsed = value.longValue();
      if (parsed < Integer.MIN_VALUE || parsed > Integer.MAX_VALUE) {
        throw conversionError(ingestName, field, value.toString());
      }
      return (int) parsed;
    }
    if (value.isTextual()) {
      return parseInt32(value.textValue(), field, ingestName);
    }
    throw conversionError(ingestName, field, value.toString());
  }

  private static Long convertInt64Json(JsonNode value, FormatField field, String ingestName) {
    if (value.isIntegralNumber()) {
      return value.longValue();
    }
    if (value.isTextual()) {
      return parseInt64(value.textValue(), field, ingestName);
    }
    throw conversionError(ingestName, field, value.toString());
  }

  private static Double convertFloat64Json(JsonNode value, FormatField field, String ingestName) {
    if (value.isNumber()) {
      return value.doubleValue();
    }
    if (value.isTextual()) {
      return parseFloat64(value.textValue(), field, ingestName);
    }
    throw conversionError(ingestName, field, value.toString());
  }

  private static Integer convertDateJson(JsonNode value, FormatField field, String ingestName) {
    if (value.isTextual()) {
      return parseDateEpochDay(value.textValue(), field, ingestName);
    }
    if (value.isIntegralNumber()) {
      return parseDateEpochDay(String.valueOf(value.longValue()), field, ingestName);
    }
    throw conversionError(ingestName, field, value.toString());
  }

  private static Long convertTimestampJson(JsonNode value, FormatField field, String ingestName) {
    if (value.isIntegralNumber()) {
      return value.longValue();
    }
    if (value.isTextual()) {
      return parseTimestampMicros(value.textValue(), field, ingestName);
    }
    throw conversionError(ingestName, field, value.toString());
  }

  private static Boolean convertBoolJson(JsonNode value, FormatField field, String ingestName) {
    if (value.isBoolean()) {
      return value.booleanValue();
    }
    if (value.isTextual()) {
      return parseBoolean(value.textValue(), field, ingestName);
    }
    throw conversionError(ingestName, field, value.toString());
  }

  private static Integer parseInt32(String value, FormatField field, String ingestName) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      throw conversionError(ingestName, field, value);
    }
    try {
      return Integer.parseInt(normalized);
    } catch (NumberFormatException ex) {
      throw conversionError(ingestName, field, value, ex);
    }
  }

  private static Long parseInt64(String value, FormatField field, String ingestName) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      throw conversionError(ingestName, field, value);
    }
    try {
      return Long.parseLong(normalized);
    } catch (NumberFormatException ex) {
      throw conversionError(ingestName, field, value, ex);
    }
  }

  private static Double parseFloat64(String value, FormatField field, String ingestName) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      throw conversionError(ingestName, field, value);
    }
    try {
      return Double.parseDouble(normalized);
    } catch (NumberFormatException ex) {
      throw conversionError(ingestName, field, value, ex);
    }
  }

  private static Integer parseDateEpochDay(String value, FormatField field, String ingestName) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      throw conversionError(ingestName, field, value);
    }
    try {
      LocalDate date;
      if (normalized.matches("\\d{8}")) {
        int year = Integer.parseInt(normalized.substring(0, 4));
        int month = Integer.parseInt(normalized.substring(4, 6));
        int day = Integer.parseInt(normalized.substring(6, 8));
        date = LocalDate.of(year, month, day);
      } else {
        date = LocalDate.parse(normalized);
      }
      return Math.toIntExact(date.toEpochDay());
    } catch (RuntimeException ex) {
      throw conversionError(ingestName, field, value, ex);
    }
  }

  private static Long parseTimestampMicros(String value, FormatField field, String ingestName) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      throw conversionError(ingestName, field, value);
    }
    try {
      if (normalized.matches("[-+]?\\d+")) {
        return Long.parseLong(normalized);
      }
      Instant instant = Instant.parse(normalized);
      return Math.addExact(
          Math.multiplyExact(instant.getEpochSecond(), 1_000_000L), instant.getNano() / 1_000L);
    } catch (DateTimeParseException | NumberFormatException | ArithmeticException ex) {
      throw conversionError(ingestName, field, value, ex);
    }
  }

  private static Boolean parseBoolean(String value, FormatField field, String ingestName) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      throw conversionError(ingestName, field, value);
    }
    if ("true".equalsIgnoreCase(normalized)) {
      return true;
    }
    if ("false".equalsIgnoreCase(normalized)) {
      return false;
    }
    throw conversionError(ingestName, field, value);
  }

  static IllegalArgumentException missingRequiredField(String ingestName, FormatField field) {
    return new IllegalArgumentException(
        "Format decode missing required field ingest="
            + ingestName
            + " fieldName="
            + field.name()
            + " expectedType="
            + field.expectedType());
  }

  static IllegalArgumentException conversionError(
      String ingestName, FormatField field, String actualValueSnippet) {
    return conversionError(ingestName, field, actualValueSnippet, null);
  }

  static IllegalArgumentException conversionError(
      String ingestName, FormatField field, String actualValueSnippet, Throwable cause) {
    String message =
        "Format decode conversion failed ingest="
            + ingestName
            + " fieldName="
            + field.name()
            + " expectedType="
            + field.expectedType()
            + " actualValue="
            + snippet(actualValueSnippet);
    if (cause == null) {
      return new IllegalArgumentException(message);
    }
    return new IllegalArgumentException(message, cause);
  }

  private static String snippet(String value) {
    if (value == null) {
      return "null";
    }
    String normalized = value.replace('\n', ' ').replace('\r', ' ').trim();
    if (normalized.length() <= 96) {
      return normalized;
    }
    return normalized.substring(0, 96) + "...";
  }
}


FILE: FormatDecodeRequest.java

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.format;

import java.nio.charset.StandardCharsets;
import java.util.Arrays;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionIngest;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionSchema;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.format.FormatDecoderArrowBuilder.FormatField;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public record FormatDecodeRequest(
    String ingestName,
    String outputSchemaId,
    DefinitionSchema schemaDefinition,
    byte[] payloadUtf8Bytes,
    DefinitionIngest.SchemaMode schemaMode,
    int rowLimitPerBatch,
    SchemaEvolutionObserver schemaEvolutionObserver
) {
  public static final int DEFAULT_ROW_LIMIT_PER_BATCH = 5_000;

  public FormatDecodeRequest {
    ingestName = Strings.requireNonBlank(ingestName, "ingestName");
    outputSchemaId = Strings.requireNonBlank(outputSchemaId, "outputSchemaId");
    schemaDefinition = Objects.requireNonNull(schemaDefinition, "schemaDefinition");
    if (payloadUtf8Bytes == null || payloadUtf8Bytes.length == 0) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("payloadUtf8Bytes is required");
    }
    if (rowLimitPerBatch <= 0) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("rowLimitPerBatch must be > 0");
    }
    payloadUtf8Bytes = Arrays.copyOf(payloadUtf8Bytes, payloadUtf8Bytes.length);
    schemaMode = schemaMode == null ? DefinitionIngest.SchemaMode.STRICT : schemaMode;
  }

  public FormatDecodeRequest(
      String ingestName, String outputSchemaId, DefinitionSchema schemaDefinition, byte[] payloadUtf8Bytes) {
    this(
        ingestName,
        outputSchemaId,
        schemaDefinition,
        payloadUtf8Bytes,
        DefinitionIngest.SchemaMode.STRICT,
        DEFAULT_ROW_LIMIT_PER_BATCH,
        null);
  }

  public FormatDecodeRequest(
      String ingestName,
      String outputSchemaId,
      DefinitionSchema schemaDefinition,
      byte[] payloadUtf8Bytes,
      int rowLimitPerBatch) {
    this(
        ingestName,
        outputSchemaId,
        schemaDefinition,
        payloadUtf8Bytes,
        DefinitionIngest.SchemaMode.STRICT,
        rowLimitPerBatch,
        null);
  }

  public FormatDecodeRequest(
      String ingestName,
      String outputSchemaId,
      DefinitionSchema schemaDefinition,
      byte[] payloadUtf8Bytes,
      DefinitionIngest.SchemaMode schemaMode,
      int rowLimitPerBatch) {
    this(
        ingestName,
        outputSchemaId,
        schemaDefinition,
        payloadUtf8Bytes,
        schemaMode,
        rowLimitPerBatch,
        null);
  }

  public static FormatDecodeRequest fromUtf8String(
      String ingestName, String outputSchemaId, DefinitionSchema schemaDefinition, String payloadUtf8) {
    return new FormatDecodeRequest(
        ingestName,
        outputSchemaId,
        schemaDefinition,
        Strings.requireNonBlank(payloadUtf8, "payloadUtf8").getBytes(StandardCharsets.UTF_8),
        DefinitionIngest.SchemaMode.STRICT,
        DEFAULT_ROW_LIMIT_PER_BATCH,
        null);
  }

  public static FormatDecodeRequest fromUtf8String(
      String ingestName,
      String outputSchemaId,
      DefinitionSchema schemaDefinition,
      String payloadUtf8,
      DefinitionIngest.SchemaMode schemaMode) {
    return new FormatDecodeRequest(
        ingestName,
        outputSchemaId,
        schemaDefinition,
        Strings.requireNonBlank(payloadUtf8, "payloadUtf8").getBytes(StandardCharsets.UTF_8),
        schemaMode,
        DEFAULT_ROW_LIMIT_PER_BATCH,
        null);
  }

  public String payloadUtf8() {
    return new String(payloadUtf8Bytes, StandardCharsets.UTF_8);
  }

  @Override
  public byte[] payloadUtf8Bytes() {
    return Arrays.copyOf(payloadUtf8Bytes, payloadUtf8Bytes.length);
  }

  public void notifySchemaEvolution(SchemaEvolutionSummary summary) {
    if (schemaEvolutionObserver == null || summary == null) {
      return;
    }
    schemaEvolutionObserver.onSchemaEvolution(summary);
  }

  @FunctionalInterface
  public interface SchemaEvolutionObserver {
    void onSchemaEvolution(SchemaEvolutionSummary summary);
  }

  public record SchemaEvolutionSummary(
      List<FormatField> effectiveFields,
      List<String> addedColumns,
      List<String> defaultedFields,
      List<String> widenedFields,
      List<String> observedInputFields
  ) {
    public SchemaEvolutionSummary {
      effectiveFields = effectiveFields == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(effectiveFields);
      addedColumns = addedColumns == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(addedColumns);
      defaultedFields = defaultedFields == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(defaultedFields);
      widenedFields = widenedFields == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(widenedFields);
      observedInputFields = observedInputFields == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(observedInputFields);
    }
  }
}





FILE: FormatDecoderJson.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.format;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonNode;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.codec.DiscoveryCodec;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionIngestSource;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.format.FormatDecoderArrowBuilder.BuildSession;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class FormatDecoderJson implements FormatDecoder {
  public static final String MODE_OBJECT_PER_MESSAGE = "OBJECT_PER_MESSAGE";

  private final ObjectMapper mapper;
  private final FormatDecoderArrowBuilder arrowBuilder;
  private final String mode;
  private final String rootField;

  public FormatDecoderJson() {
    this(null, new FormatDecoderArrowBuilder(), DiscoveryCodec.mapper());
  }

  public FormatDecoderJson(DefinitionIngestSource.JsonConfig config) {
    this(config, new FormatDecoderArrowBuilder(), DiscoveryCodec.mapper());
  }

  FormatDecoderJson(
      DefinitionIngestSource.JsonConfig config,
      FormatDecoderArrowBuilder arrowBuilder,
      ObjectMapper mapper) {
    this.arrowBuilder = Objects.requireNonNull(arrowBuilder, "arrowBuilder");
    this.mapper = Objects.requireNonNull(mapper, "mapper");
    String configuredMode = Strings.trimToNull(config == null ? null : config.mode());
    mode =
        configuredMode == null
            ? MODE_OBJECT_PER_MESSAGE
            : configuredMode.toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT);
    rootField = Strings.trimToNull(config == null ? null : config.rootField());
  }

  @Override
  public byte[] decodeToArrowIpc(FormatDecodeRequest request) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(request, "request");
    if (!MODE_OBJECT_PER_MESSAGE.equals(mode)) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Unsupported JSON mode: " + mode);
    }

    String payload = request.payloadUtf8();
    ArrayList<Map<String, JsonNode>> inputRows =
        new ArrayList<>(
            FormatPayloadParsing.parseJsonRows(
                request.ingestName(),
                payload,
                rootField,
                request.rowLimitPerBatch(),
                mapper));

    SchemaEvolution.Result evolution =
        SchemaEvolution.resolveJson(
            request.ingestName(),
            request.schemaMode(),
            arrowBuilder.describeFields(
                request.ingestName(), request.outputSchemaId(), request.schemaDefinition()),
            inputRows);
    request.notifySchemaEvolution(
        new FormatDecodeRequest.SchemaEvolutionSummary(
            evolution.outputFields(),
            evolution.addedColumns(),
            evolution.defaultedFields(),
            evolution.widenedFields(),
            evolution.observedInputFields()));

    try (BuildSession buildSession = arrowBuilder.open(evolution.outputFields())) {
      for (int i = 0; i < evolution.outputRows().size(); i++) {
        Object[] values = evolution.outputRows().get(i);
        for (int f = 0; f < evolution.outputFields().size(); f++) {
          Object value = values[f];
          if (value == null) {
            buildSession.setNull(evolution.outputFields().get(f), i);
          } else {
            buildSession.setValue(evolution.outputFields().get(f), i, value);
          }
        }
      }
      return buildSession.finish(evolution.outputRows().size());
    }
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.format;

import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionIngestSource;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.connectors.amps.AmpsConnection;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.format.FormatDecoderArrowBuilder.BuildSession;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.format.FormatDecoderArrowBuilder.FormatField;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class FormatDecoderNvFix implements FormatDecoder {
  private final FormatDecoderArrowBuilder arrowBuilder;
  private final String pairDelimiter;
  private final String kvDelimiter;
  private final boolean trimKeys;
  private final boolean trimValues;

  public FormatDecoderNvFix() {
    this(null, new FormatDecoderArrowBuilder());
  }

  public FormatDecoderNvFix(DefinitionIngestSource.NvFixConfig config) {
    this(config, new FormatDecoderArrowBuilder());
  }

  FormatDecoderNvFix(DefinitionIngestSource.NvFixConfig config, FormatDecoderArrowBuilder arrowBuilder) {
    this.arrowBuilder = Objects.requireNonNull(arrowBuilder, "arrowBuilder");
    String configuredPairDelimiter = Strings.trimToNull(config == null ? null : config.pairDelimiter());
    String configuredKvDelimiter = Strings.trimToNull(config == null ? null : config.kvDelimiter());
    trimKeys = config == null || config.trimKeys() == null || config.trimKeys();
    trimValues = config == null || config.trimValues() == null || config.trimValues();
    String effectivePairDelimiter =
        configuredPairDelimiter == null ? String.valueOf(AmpsConnection.SOH) : configuredPairDelimiter;
    String effectiveKvDelimiter = configuredKvDelimiter == null ? "=" : configuredKvDelimiter;
    if (effectiveKvDelimiter.isEmpty()) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("kvDelimiter must not be empty");
    }
    this.pairDelimiter = effectivePairDelimiter;
    this.kvDelimiter = effectiveKvDelimiter;
  }

  @Override
  public byte[] decodeToArrowIpc(FormatDecodeRequest request) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(request, "request");
    String payload = request.payloadUtf8();
    List<Map<String, String>> inputRows =
        FormatPayloadParsing.parseNvFixRows(
            request.ingestName(),
            payload,
            pairDelimiter,
            kvDelimiter,
            trimKeys,
            trimValues,
            request.rowLimitPerBatch());

    SchemaEvolution.Result evolution =
        SchemaEvolution.resolveNvFix(
            request.ingestName(),
            request.schemaMode(),
            arrowBuilder.describeFields(
                request.ingestName(), request.outputSchemaId(), request.schemaDefinition()),
            inputRows);
    request.notifySchemaEvolution(
        new FormatDecodeRequest.SchemaEvolutionSummary(
            evolution.outputFields(),
            evolution.addedColumns(),
            evolution.defaultedFields(),
            evolution.widenedFields(),
            evolution.observedInputFields()));

    try (BuildSession buildSession = arrowBuilder.open(evolution.outputFields())) {
      for (int i = 0; i < evolution.outputRows().size(); i++) {
        Object[] values = evolution.outputRows().get(i);
        for (int f = 0; f < evolution.outputFields().size(); f++) {
          FormatField field = evolution.outputFields().get(f);
          Object value = values[f];
          if (value == null) {
            buildSession.setNull(field, i);
          } else {
            buildSession.setValue(field, i, value);
          }
        }
      }
      return buildSession.finish(evolution.outputRows().size());
    }
  }
}





FILE: FormatPayloadParsing.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.format;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonNode;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.regex.Pattern;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.connectors.amps.AmpsConnection;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class FormatPayloadParsing {
  private FormatPayloadParsing() {}

  public static List<Map<String, JsonNode>> parseJsonRows(
      String ingestName,
      String payload,
      String rootField,
      int rowLimitPerBatch,
      ObjectMapper mapper) {
    String resolvedIngestName = Strings.requireNonBlank(ingestName, "ingestName");
    if (Strings.isBlank(payload)) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(
          "Format decode payload did not contain any JSON messages ingest=" + resolvedIngestName);
    }
    if (rowLimitPerBatch <= 0) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("rowLimitPerBatch must be > 0");
    }
    ObjectMapper resolvedMapper = mapper == null ? org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.codec.DiscoveryCodec.mapper() : mapper;
    List<Map<String, JsonNode>> rows = new ArrayList<>();
    for (String line : payload.split("\\R", -1)) {
      String message = Strings.trimToNull(line);
      if (message == null) {
        continue;
      }
      if (rows.size() >= rowLimitPerBatch) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException(
            "Format decode row limit exceeded ingest="
                + resolvedIngestName
                + " rowLimitPerBatch="
                + rowLimitPerBatch);
      }
      JsonNode payloadNode = parseJsonMessage(resolvedMapper, message, resolvedIngestName);
      JsonNode rowNode = payloadNode;
      if (rootField != null) {
        rowNode = payloadNode.get(rootField);
        if (rowNode == null || rowNode.isNull() || !rowNode.isObject()) {
          throw new IllegalArgumentException(
              "JSON rootField is missing or not an object ingest="
                  + resolvedIngestName
                  + " rootField="
                  + rootField);
        }
      }
      if (!rowNode.isObject()) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException(
            "JSON message must be an object ingest="
                + resolvedIngestName
                + " actualValue="
                + rowNode);
      }
      Map<String, JsonNode> valuesByField = new LinkedHashMap<>();
      rowNode.fields().forEachRemaining(entry -> valuesByField.put(entry.getKey(), entry.getValue()));
      rows.add(valuesByField);
    }
    if (rows.isEmpty()) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(
          "Format decode payload did not contain any JSON messages ingest=" + resolvedIngestName);
    }
    return List.copyOf(rows);
  }

  public static List<Map<String, String>> parseNvFixRows(
      String ingestName,
      String payload,
      String pairDelimiter,
      String kvDelimiter,
      boolean trimKeys,
      boolean trimValues,
      int rowLimitPerBatch) {
    String resolvedIngestName = Strings.requireNonBlank(ingestName, "ingestName");
    String resolvedPayload = payload == null ? "" : payload;
    if (rowLimitPerBatch <= 0) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("rowLimitPerBatch must be > 0");
    }
    String effectivePairDelimiter = Strings.trimToNull(pairDelimiter);
    if (effectivePairDelimiter == null) {
      effectivePairDelimiter = String.valueOf(AmpsConnection.SOH);
    }
    String effectiveKvDelimiter = Strings.trimToNull(kvDelimiter);
    if (effectiveKvDelimiter == null) {
      effectiveKvDelimiter = "=";
    }
    if (effectiveKvDelimiter.isEmpty()) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("kvDelimiter must not be empty");
    }
    Pattern pairSplitPattern = Pattern.compile(Pattern.quote(effectivePairDelimiter));
    List<Map<String, String>> rows = new ArrayList<>();
    for (String line : resolvedPayload.split("\\R", -1)) {
      String message = Strings.trimToNull(line);
      if (message == null) {
        continue;
      }
      if (rows.size() >= rowLimitPerBatch) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException(
            "Format decode row limit exceeded ingest="
                + resolvedIngestName
                + " rowLimitPerBatch="
                + rowLimitPerBatch);
      }
      rows.add(
          parseNvFixLine(
              message,
              resolvedIngestName,
              pairSplitPattern,
              effectiveKvDelimiter,
              trimKeys,
              trimValues));
    }
    if (rows.isEmpty()) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(
          "Format decode payload did not contain any NVFIX messages ingest=" + resolvedIngestName);
    }
    return List.copyOf(rows);
  }

  public static Map<String, String> parseNvFixLine(
      String message,
      String ingestName,
      Pattern pairSplitPattern,
      String kvDelimiter,
      boolean trimKeys,
      boolean trimValues) {
    Map<String, String> parsed = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    String[] entries = pairSplitPattern.split(message, -1);
    for (String entry : entries) {
      if (entry == null || entry.isBlank()) {
        continue;
      }
      int delimiterIndex = entry.indexOf(kvDelimiter);
      if (delimiterIndex < 0) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException(
            "Invalid NVFIX key/value entry ingest="
                + ingestName
                + " entry="
                + entry.trim()
                + " kvDelimiter="
                + kvDelimiter);
      }
      String key = entry.substring(0, delimiterIndex);
      String value = entry.substring(delimiterIndex + kvDelimiter.length());
      if (trimKeys) {
        key = key.trim();
      }
      if (trimValues) {
        value = value.trim();
      }
      if (key.isEmpty()) {
        continue;
      }
      parsed.put(key, value);
    }
    return parsed;
  }

  private static JsonNode parseJsonMessage(ObjectMapper mapper, String message, String ingestName) {
    try {
      return mapper.readTree(message);
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(
          "Invalid JSON message ingest="
              + ingestName
              + " actualValue="
              + snippet(message),
          ex);
    }
  }

  private static String snippet(String value) {
    if (value == null) {
      return "null";
    }
    String normalized = value.replace('\n', ' ').replace('\r', ' ').trim();
    if (normalized.length() <= 96) {
      return normalized;
    }
    return normalized.substring(0, 96) + "...";
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.ingest.agent;

import java.util.Collection;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.Set;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.Fabric;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.IngestManager;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

/**
 * Internal ingest agent that materializes DefinitionIngestSource records into running AMPS ingest
 * pumps.
 */
public interface IngestAgent extends AutoCloseable {

  void start() throws Exception;

  boolean started();

  @Override
  void close();

  static Builder builder() {
    return new Builder();
  }

  static IngestAgent create(Fabric.Session session) {
    return create(session, Options.defaults());
  }

  static IngestAgent create(Fabric.Session session, Options options) {
    return new IngestAgentImpl(session, options);
  }

  record Options(
      Set<String> ingestAllowlist,
      boolean dryRun,
      boolean once,
      IngestManager.IngestRuntimeOptions ingestRuntimeOptions) {
    public Options {
      ingestAllowlist = normalizeAllowlist(ingestAllowlist);
    }

    public static Options defaults() {
      return new Options(Set.of(), false, false, null);
    }

    public Builder toBuilder() {
      return new Builder()
          .withIngestAllowlist(ingestAllowlist)
          .withDryRun(dryRun)
          .withOnce(once)
          .withIngestRuntimeOptions(ingestRuntimeOptions);
    }

    public boolean allowIngest(String ingestName) {
      String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(ingestName);
      if (normalized == null) {
        return false;
      }
      if (ingestAllowlist.isEmpty()) {
        return true;
      }
      if (ingestAllowlist.contains(normalized)) {
        return true;
      }
      int slash = normalized.indexOf('/');
      if (slash > 0 && slash < normalized.length() - 1) {
        return ingestAllowlist.contains(normalized.substring(slash + 1));
      }
      return false;
    }

    private static Set<String> normalizeAllowlist(Collection<String> values) {
      if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
        return Set.of();
      }
      LinkedHashSet<String> normalized = new LinkedHashSet<>();
      for (String value : values) {
        String trimmed = Strings.trimToNull(value);
        if (trimmed != null) {
          normalized.add(trimmed);
        }
      }
      return normalized.isEmpty() ? Set.of() : Set.copyOf(normalized);
    }
  }

  final class Builder {
    private Set<String> ingestAllowlist = Set.of();
    private boolean dryRun;
    private boolean once;
    private IngestManager.IngestRuntimeOptions ingestRuntimeOptions;

    public Builder withIngestAllowlist(Collection<String> values) {
      LinkedHashSet<String> normalized = new LinkedHashSet<>();
      if (values != null) {
        for (String value : values) {
          String trimmed = Strings.trimToNull(value);
          if (trimmed != null) {
            normalized.add(trimmed);
          }
        }
      }
      ingestAllowlist = normalized.isEmpty() ? Set.of() : Set.copyOf(normalized);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withDryRun(boolean value) {
      dryRun = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withOnce(boolean value) {
      once = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withIngestRuntimeOptions(IngestManager.IngestRuntimeOptions value) {
      ingestRuntimeOptions = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Options build() {
      return new Options(ingestAllowlist, dryRun, once, ingestRuntimeOptions);
    }
  }
}
