FILE: ArrowIpcRowDecoder.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.manager;

import java.io.ByteArrayInputStream;
import java.io.InputStream;
import java.nio.ByteBuffer;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Arrays;
import java.util.Collections;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.time.LocalDate;
import org.apache.arrow.memory.BufferAllocator;
import org.apache.arrow.vector.FieldVector;
import org.apache.arrow.vector.VectorSchemaRoot;
import org.apache.arrow.vector.ipc.ArrowStreamReader;
import org.apache.arrow.vector.types.DateUnit;
import org.apache.arrow.vector.types.pojo.ArrowType;
import org.apache.arrow.vector.util.Text;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.RowResult;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Bytes;

final class ArrowIpcRowDecoder {
  private ArrowIpcRowDecoder() {}

  static RowResult decodeToRowResult(byte[] ipcBytes, BufferAllocator allocator) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(allocator, "allocator");
    if (ipcBytes == null || ipcBytes.length == 0) {
      return new RowResult(List.of(), List.of());
    }
    return decodeToRowResult(new ByteArrayInputStream(ipcBytes), allocator);
  }

  static RowResult decodeToRowResult(ByteBuffer ipcBuffer, BufferAllocator allocator) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(allocator, "allocator");
    Objects.requireNonNull(ipcBuffer, "ipcBuffer");
    if (!ipcBuffer.hasRemaining()) {
      return new RowResult(List.of(), List.of());
    }
    return decodeToRowResult(Bytes.asInputStream(ipcBuffer), allocator);
  }

  private static RowResult decodeToRowResult(InputStream inputStream, BufferAllocator allocator) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(inputStream, "inputStream");
    List<String> columns = new ArrayList<>();
    List<List<Object>> rows = new ArrayList<>();
    try (ArrowStreamReader reader = new ArrowStreamReader(inputStream, allocator)) {
      VectorSchemaRoot root = reader.getVectorSchemaRoot();
      if (root.getSchema() != null && root.getSchema().getFields() != null) {
        root.getSchema().getFields().forEach(field -> columns.add(field.getName()));
      }
      while (reader.loadNextBatch()) {
        int rowCount = root.getRowCount();
        List<FieldVector> vectors = root.getFieldVectors();
        for (int rowIndex = 0; rowIndex < rowCount; rowIndex++) {
          List<Object> row = new ArrayList<>(vectors.size());
          for (FieldVector vector : vectors) {
            row.add(decodeValue(vector, rowIndex));
          }
          rows.add(List.copyOf(row));
        }
      }
      return new RowResult(List.copyOf(columns), List.copyOf(rows));
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Failed to decode Arrow IPC query result", ex);
    }
  }

  static List<Map<String, Object>> decodeToRowMaps(byte[] ipcBytes, BufferAllocator allocator) {
    RowResult result = decodeToRowResult(ipcBytes, allocator);
    return decodeToRowMaps(result);
  }

  static List<Map<String, Object>> decodeToRowMaps(ByteBuffer ipcBuffer, BufferAllocator allocator) {
    RowResult result = decodeToRowResult(ipcBuffer, allocator);
    return decodeToRowMaps(result);
  }

  private static List<Map<String, Object>> decodeToRowMaps(RowResult result) {
    List<String> columns = result.columns();
    if (columns == null || columns.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<Map<String, Object>> rows = new ArrayList<>();
    for (List<Object> row : result.rows()) {
      LinkedHashMap<String, Object> values = new LinkedHashMap<>(columns.size());
      for (int i = 0; i < columns.size(); i++) {
        Object value = row != null && i < row.size() ? row.get(i) : null;
        values.put(columns.get(i), value);
      }
      rows.add(Collections.unmodifiableMap(new LinkedHashMap<>(values)));
    }
    return List.copyOf(rows);
  }

  private static Object decodeValue(FieldVector vector, int rowIndex) {
    if (vector == null || vector.isNull(rowIndex)) {
      return null;
    }
    Object value = vector.getObject(rowIndex);
    value = convertArrowLogicalValue(vector, value);
    if (value instanceof Text text) {
      return text.toString();
    }
    if (value instanceof byte[] bytes) {
      return Arrays.copyOf(bytes, bytes.length);
    }
    return value;
  }

  private static Object convertArrowLogicalValue(FieldVector vector, Object value) {
    if (vector == null || value == null) {
      return value;
    }
    ArrowType type =
        vector.getField() == null ? null : (vector.getField().getType());
    if (type instanceof ArrowType.Date dateType && dateType.getUnit() == DateUnit.DAY) {
      if (value instanceof Number number) {
        return LocalDate.ofEpochDay(number.longValue());
      }
    }
    return value;
  }
}

public final class DataPlanesImpl implements DataManagers, AutoCloseable {

      "SERVICE_DATA_PLANE_DISABLED: configure data.service.*";

  public DataPlanesImpl(

      ControlConnection controlPlaneConnection,
      Supplier<ScheduledExecutorService> statusSchedulerSupplier,
      ConnectionManager connectionManager,
      DataEntitlements dataEntitlements,
      Fabric.Session session,
      CheckpointStore checkpointStore) {
    this.dataOptions = dataOptions == null ? DataOptions.builder().build() : dataOptions;
    this.discoveryCache = Objects.requireNonNull(discoveryCache, "discoveryCache");
    this.group = Strings.requireNonBlank(group, "group");
    this.appName = Strings.trimToNull(appName);
    this.kerberosUsername = Strings.trimToNull(kerberosUsername);
    this.kerberosPrincipal = Strings.trimToNull(kerberosPrincipal);
    this.kerberosKeytab = kerberosKeytab;
    this.trustCert = trustCert;
    this.controlPlaneConnection = controlPlaneConnection;
    this.statusSchedulerSupplier = Objects.requireNonNull(statusSchedulerSupplier, "statusSchedulerSupplier");
    this.connectionManager = Objects.requireNonNull(connectionManager, "connectionManager");
    this.dataEntitlements = Objects.requireNonNull(dataEntitlements, "dataEntitlements");
    this.session = Objects.requireNonNull(session, "session");
    this.checkpointStore = Objects.requireNonNull(checkpointStore, "checkpointStore");
    initialize();
  }

  @Override
  public DataManager direct() {
    return directDataPlane;
  }

  @Override
  public DataManager service() {
    return serviceDataPlane;
  }

  public ServiceInstanceResolver serviceInstanceResolverIfInitialized() {
    return serviceInstanceResolver;
  }

  @Override
  public void close() {
    synchronized (lifecycleLock) {
      CloseSupport.closeQuietly(serviceDataPlane instanceof AutoCloseable closeable ? closeable : null);
      serviceDataPlane = null;
      CloseSupport.closeQuietly(directDataPlane instanceof AutoCloseable closeable ? closeable : null);
      directDataPlane = null;
      CloseSupport.closeQuietly(serviceInstanceResolver);
      serviceInstanceResolver = null;
    }
  }

  private void initialize() {
    synchronized (lifecycleLock) {
      if (dataOptions.direct().enabled()) {
        directDataPlane =
            new DirectDataManagerImpl(
                discoveryCache,
                group,
                appName,
                kerberosUsername,
                dataEntitlements,
                connectionManager,
                session,
                checkpointStore);
      } else {
        directDataPlane = new DisabledDirectDataPlane();
      }

      if (dataOptions.service().enabled()) {
        DataOptions.ServiceOptions serviceOptions =
            withSessionTrustCertFallback(dataOptions.service(), trustCert);
        ServiceInstanceResolver resolver = createServiceInstanceResolver(serviceOptions);
        serviceDataPlane =
            new ServiceDataManagerImpl(
                discoveryCache,
                group,
                appName,
                session.context() == null ? null : session.context().getInstance(),
                session.context() == null ? null : session.context().getEnv(),
                session.context() == null ? null : session.context().getRegion(),
                session.context() == null ? null : session.context().getSite(),
                serviceOptions,
                kerberosPrincipal,
                kerberosKeytab,
                resolver,
                session,
                checkpointStore);
      } else {
        serviceDataPlane = new DisabledServiceDataPlane();
      }
    }
  }

  private static DataOptions.ServiceOptions withSessionTrustCertFallback(
      DataOptions.ServiceOptions serviceOptions, Path sessionTrustCert) {
    if (serviceOptions == null || sessionTrustCert == null) {
      return serviceOptions;
    }
    ServiceRunOptions runOptions =
        serviceOptions.serviceOptions() == null
            ? ServiceRunOptions.defaults()
            : serviceOptions.serviceOptions();
    if (runOptions.tlsTrustCert() != null && runOptions.clientTrustCert() != null) {
      return serviceOptions;
    }
    DataOptions.ServiceOptions.Builder builder = serviceOptions.toBuilder();
    if (runOptions.tlsTrustCert() == null) {
      builder.withTlsTrustCert(sessionTrustCert);
    }
    if (runOptions.clientTrustCert() == null) {
      builder.withTlsClientTrustCert(sessionTrustCert);
    }
    return builder.build();
  }

  private ServiceInstanceResolver createServiceInstanceResolver(DataOptions.ServiceOptions options) {
    ServiceInstanceResolver resolver = serviceInstanceResolver;
    if (resolver != null) {
      return resolver;
    }
    if (controlPlaneConnection == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Session control-plane client is not initialized");
    }
    resolver = new ServiceInstanceResolver(controlPlaneConnection, statusSchedulerSupplier.get());
    ServiceRunOptions runOptions =
        options.serviceOptions() == null ? ServiceRunOptions.defaults() : options.serviceOptions();
    String serviceGroup = Strings.firstNonBlank(runOptions.group(), group);
    String queryService = Strings.trimToNull(options.queryService());
    if (queryService != null) {
      resolver.ensureServiceCache(serviceGroup, queryService);
    }
    String ingestService = Strings.trimToNull(options.ingestService());
    if (ingestService != null) {
      resolver.ensureServiceCache(serviceGroup, ingestService);
    }
    serviceInstanceResolver = resolver;
    return resolver;
  }


  private static final class DisabledDirectDataPlane implements DataManager {
    @Override
    public RowManager rows() {
      throw new IllegalStateException(DIRECT_DISABLED_MESSAGE);
    }

    @Override
    public IngestManager ingest() {
      throw new IllegalStateException(DIRECT_DISABLED_MESSAGE);
    }

    @Override
    public TabularManager tabular() {
      throw new IllegalStateException(DIRECT_DISABLED_MESSAGE);
    }

    @Override
    public ViewManager views() {
      throw new IllegalStateException(DIRECT_DISABLED_MESSAGE);
    }

    @Override
    public ParquetManager parquet() {
      throw new IllegalStateException(DIRECT_DISABLED_MESSAGE);
    }

  }

  private static final class DisabledServiceDataPlane implements DataManager {
    @Override
    public RowManager rows() {
      throw new IllegalStateException(SERVICE_DISABLED_MESSAGE);
    }

    @Override
    public IngestManager ingest() {
      throw new IllegalStateException(SERVICE_DISABLED_MESSAGE);
    }

    @Override
    public TabularManager tabular() {
      throw new IllegalStateException(SERVICE_DISABLED_MESSAGE);
    }

    @Override
    public ViewManager views() {
      throw new IllegalStateException(SERVICE_DISABLED_MESSAGE);
    }

    @Override
    public ParquetManager parquet() {
      throw new IllegalStateException(SERVICE_DISABLED_MESSAGE);
    }

  }
}





FILE: DirectDataManagerImpl.java

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.manager;

import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.concurrent.Executors;
import java.util.concurrent.ScheduledExecutorService;
import java.util.concurrent.ThreadFactory;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.Fabric;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.connections.ConnectionManager;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.cache.DiscoveryCache;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.cache.DiscoveryListener;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.Definition;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionDataset;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionEnvelope;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionType;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.catalog.DuckdbCatalog;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.catalog.DuckdbCatalogImpl;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.checkpoints.CheckpointStore;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.DataManager;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.IngestManager;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.ParquetManager;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.RowManager;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.TabularManager;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.ViewManager;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.duckdb.DuckdbEngine;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.views.ViewManagerImpl;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.core.data.DataEntitlements;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.CloseSupport;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class DirectDataManagerImpl implements DataManager, AutoCloseable {
  private final Object lifecycleLock = new Object();
  private final DiscoveryCache discoveryCache;
  private final String group;
  private final String appName;
  private final String kerberosUsername;
  private final ConnectionManager connectionManager;
  private final Fabric.Session session;
  private final CheckpointStore checkpointStore;
  private final ScheduledExecutorService ingestRollScheduler;

  private volatile RowManager rowManager;
  private volatile IngestManager ingestManager;
  private volatile TabularManager tabularManager;
  private volatile ViewManager viewManager;
  private volatile ParquetManager parquetManager;
  private final DataEntitlements dataEntitlements;
  private volatile DuckdbCatalog duckdbCatalog;
  private volatile DiscoveryListener datasetCatalogListener;

  public DirectDataManagerImpl(
      DiscoveryCache discoveryCache,
      String group,
      String appName,
      String kerberosUsername,
      DataEntitlements dataEntitlements,
      ConnectionManager connectionManager,
      Fabric.Session session,
      CheckpointStore checkpointStore) {
    this.discoveryCache = Objects.requireNonNull(discoveryCache, "discoveryCache");
    this.group = Strings.requireNonBlank(group, "group");
    this.appName = Strings.trimToNull(appName);
    this.kerberosUsername = Strings.trimToNull(kerberosUsername);
    this.dataEntitlements = Objects.requireNonNull(dataEntitlements, "dataEntitlements");
    this.connectionManager = Objects.requireNonNull(connectionManager, "connectionManager");
    this.session = Objects.requireNonNull(session, "session");
    this.checkpointStore = Objects.requireNonNull(checkpointStore, "checkpointStore");
    this.ingestRollScheduler = newIngestRollScheduler(group);
    initialize();
  }

  @Override
  public RowManager rows() {
    return rowManager;
  }

  @Override
  public IngestManager ingest() {
    return ingestManager;
  }

  @Override
  public TabularManager tabular() {
    return tabularManager;
  }

  @Override
  public ViewManager views() {
    return viewManager;
  }

  @Override
  public ParquetManager parquet() {
    return parquetManager;
  }

  @Override
  public void close() {
    synchronized (lifecycleLock) {
      DiscoveryListener listener = datasetCatalogListener;
      datasetCatalogListener = null;
      if (listener != null) {
        discoveryCache.removeListener(listener);
      }
      CloseSupport.closeQuietly(duckdbCatalog);
      duckdbCatalog = null;
      CloseSupport.closeQuietly(viewManager instanceof AutoCloseable closeable ? closeable : null);
      viewManager = null;
      CloseSupport.closeQuietly(ingestManager instanceof AutoCloseable closeable ? closeable : null);
      ingestManager = null;
      CloseSupport.closeQuietly(tabularManager instanceof AutoCloseable closeable ? closeable : null);
      tabularManager = null;
      closeScheduler(ingestRollScheduler);
      CloseSupport.closeQuietly(rowManager);
      rowManager = null;
      parquetManager = null;
    }
  }

  private void initialize() {
    synchronized (lifecycleLock) {
      RowManagerImpl localManager = createRowManager();
      DuckdbCatalog catalog = new DuckdbCatalogImpl(discoveryCache, localManager, group);
      catalog.installAll();
      localManager.setSqlCatalog(catalog);
      DiscoveryListener catalogListener = createDatasetCatalogListener(catalog);
      discoveryCache.addListener(catalogListener);
      this.datasetCatalogListener = catalogListener;
      this.duckdbCatalog = catalog;
      this.rowManager = localManager;
      this.ingestManager =
          new IngestManagerImpl(
              localManager,
              discoveryCache,
              group,
              session,
              ingestRollScheduler,
              checkpointStore);
      this.tabularManager = new TabularManagerImpl(localManager, catalog);
      this.viewManager =
          new ViewManagerImpl(localManager, discoveryCache, group, session, checkpointStore);
      this.parquetManager = ingestManager.parquet();
    }
  }

  private RowManagerImpl createRowManager() {
    if (dataEntitlements == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("DataEntitlements is not available");
    }
    DuckdbEngine engine = new DuckdbEngine();
    return new RowManagerImpl(
        engine,
        () -> {
          try (var session = engine.openSession()) {
            return session.ping();
          }
        },
        discoveryCache,
        dataEntitlements,
        resolveDataIdentity(),
        connectionManager);
  }

  private DiscoveryListener createDatasetCatalogListener(DuckdbCatalog catalog) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(catalog, "catalog");
    return new DiscoveryListener() {
      @Override
      public void onUpsert(Definition definition) {
        if (!(definition instanceof DefinitionDataset dataset)) {
          return;
        }
        catalog.onDatasetUpsert(dataset);
      }

      @Override
      public void onDelete(DefinitionEnvelope envelope) {
        if (envelope == null || envelope.type() != DefinitionType.DATASET) {
          return;
        }
        String envelopeGroup = Strings.trimToNull(envelope.group());
        String encodedName = Strings.trimToNull(envelope.name());
        if (envelopeGroup == null || encodedName == null) {
          return;
        }
        int delimiter = encodedName.indexOf('/');
        if (delimiter <= 0 || delimiter >= encodedName.length() - 1) {
          return;
        }
        String namespace = encodedName.substring(0, delimiter);
        String name = encodedName.substring(delimiter + 1);
        catalog.onDatasetDelete(envelopeGroup, namespace, name);
      }
    };
  }

  private DataEntitlements.Identity resolveDataIdentity() {
    String subject = resolveDataSubject();
    return new DataEntitlements.Identity(subject == null ? "anonymous" : subject, null);
  }

  private String resolveDataSubject() {
    if (kerberosUsername != null) {
      return "user:" + kerberosUsername;
    }
    if (appName == null) {
      return null;
    }
    return "app:" + group + "/" + appName;
  }

  private static ScheduledExecutorService newIngestRollScheduler(String group) {
    String normalizedGroup =
        Strings.requireNonBlank(group, "group").replaceAll("[^A-Za-z0-9_-]", "_");
    ThreadFactory threadFactory =
        runnable -> {
          Thread thread = new Thread(runnable);
          thread.setName("fabric-ingest-roll-" + normalizedGroup);
          thread.setDaemon(true);
          return thread;
        };
    return Executors.newSingleThreadScheduledExecutor(threadFactory);
  }

  private static void closeScheduler(ScheduledExecutorService scheduler) {
    if (scheduler == null) {
      return;
    }
    scheduler.shutdownNow();
  }
}


FILE: DuckdbActiveChangeLog.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.manager;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.dataset.DatasetId;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

/** Shared DUCKDB_ACTIVE change-log SQL helpers used by ingest and streaming paths. */
public final class DuckdbActiveChangeLog {
  private static final String CHANGE_TABLE_PREFIX = "__fabric_changes_";

  private DuckdbActiveChangeLog() {}

  public static String tableName(DatasetId datasetId) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(datasetId, "datasetId");
    return CHANGE_TABLE_PREFIX
        + sanitizeToken(datasetId.namespace())
        + "__"
        + sanitizeToken(datasetId.name());
  }

  public static String primaryKeyTextExpression(List<String> primaryKeyColumns, String tableAlias) {
    List<String> columns = normalizedPrimaryKeyColumns(primaryKeyColumns);
    String aliasPrefix = tableAlias == null || tableAlias.isBlank() ? "" : tableAlias + ".";
    if (columns.size() == 1) {
      return "cast(" + aliasPrefix + quoteIdentifier(columns.get(0)) + " as varchar)";
    }
    List<String> parts = new ArrayList<>(columns.size());
    for (String column : columns) {
      parts.add(
          "coalesce(cast(" + aliasPrefix + quoteIdentifier(column) + " as varchar), '<null>')");
    }
    return "concat_ws('|', " + String.join(", ", parts) + ")";
  }

  public static String quoteIdentifier(String identifier) {
    return "\"" + Objects.requireNonNull(identifier, "identifier").replace("\"", "\"\"") + "\"";
  }

  public static String quoteSqlString(String value) {
    return "'" + escapeSqlLiteral(Objects.requireNonNull(value, "value")) + "'";
  }

  public static String escapeSqlLiteral(String value) {
    return Objects.requireNonNull(value, "value").replace("'", "''");
  }

  public static List<String> normalizedPrimaryKeyColumns(List<String> primaryKeyColumns) {
    if (primaryKeyColumns == null || primaryKeyColumns.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<String> normalized = new ArrayList<>(primaryKeyColumns.size());
    for (String column : primaryKeyColumns) {
      String candidate = Strings.trimToNull(column);
      if (candidate != null && normalized.stream().noneMatch(existing -> existing.equalsIgnoreCase(candidate))) {
        normalized.add(candidate);
      }
    }
    return List.copyOf(normalized);
  }

  private static String sanitizeToken(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.requireNonBlank(value, "value").trim();
    StringBuilder builder = new StringBuilder(normalized.length());
    for (int i = 0; i < normalized.length(); i++) {
      char current = normalized.charAt(i);
      if (Character.isLetterOrDigit(current) || current == '_' || current == '-') {
        builder.append(Character.toLowerCase(current));
      } else {
        builder.append('_');
      }
    }
    String token = builder.toString();
    if (token.isBlank()) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("value must contain identifier characters");
    }
    return token;
  }

  public record ChangeEvent(long seq, String pk, String op) {
    public ChangeEvent {
      if (seq < 0L) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("seq must be >= 0");
      }
      pk = Strings.trimToNull(pk);
      op = Strings.trimToNull(op);
      if (pk == null) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("pk is required");
      }
      if (op == null) {
        op = "UPSERT";
      } else {
        op = op.toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT);
      }
    }
  }
}

FILE: IngestSchemaResolver.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.manager;

import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Optional;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.cache.DiscoveryCache;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionSchema;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class IngestSchemaResolver {
  private IngestSchemaResolver() {}

  public static DefinitionSchema resolveExpectedSchema(
      DiscoveryCache DiscoveryCache, String group, String outputSchemaId, String ingestId) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(DiscoveryCache, "DiscoveryCache");
    String normalizedGroup = Strings.requireNonBlank(group, "group");
    String normalizedSchemaId = Strings.requireNonBlank(outputSchemaId, "outputSchemaId");
    String normalizedIngestId = Strings.requireNonBlank(ingestId, "ingestId");

    Optional<DefinitionSchema> schema =
        DiscoveryCache.get(DefinitionSchema.class, normalizedGroup, normalizedSchemaId);
    if (schema.isPresent()) {
      return schema.get();
    }
    for (DefinitionSchema candidate : DiscoveryCache.list(DefinitionSchema.class, normalizedGroup)) {
      if (candidate == null || candidate.envelope() == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String schemaUuid = Strings.trimToNull(candidate.envelope().uuid());
      if (normalizedSchemaId.equals(schemaUuid)) {
        return candidate;
      }
    }
    throw new IllegalStateException(
        "Expected schema was not found for ingest="
            + normalizedIngestId
            + " expectedSchema="
            + normalizedSchemaId);
  }
}







FILE: RemoteRowManager.java

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.manager;

import java.io.ByteArrayInputStream;
import java.nio.ByteBuffer;
import java.nio.charset.StandardCharsets;
import java.nio.file.Path;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Objects;
import io.opentelemetry.api.common.Attributes;
import io.opentelemetry.api.trace.Span;
import io.opentelemetry.api.trace.SpanKind;
import org.apache.arrow.flight.AsyncPutListener;
import org.apache.arrow.flight.CallOption;
import org.apache.arrow.flight.FlightClient;
import org.apache.arrow.flight.FlightDescriptor;
import org.apache.arrow.vector.VectorSchemaRoot;
import org.apache.arrow.vector.ipc.ArrowStreamReader;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.Fabric;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.cache.DiscoveryCache;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionIngest;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionService;

import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.UserContext;

import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.identity.CallerAppContext;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.identity.CallerAppIdentity;

import org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.ServiceRunOptions;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.common.ServiceInstanceResolver;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.common.routing.ServiceRoutingContext;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.common.routing.ServiceRoutingState;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.telemetry.manager.FabricOtelAttributes;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.telemetry.manager.FabricOtelEnablement;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.telemetry.OtelManager;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.telemetry.manager.FabricOtelSupport;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class RemoteRowManager implements RowManager {
  private final RemoteTabularManager tabularManager;
  private final DiscoveryCache DiscoveryCache;
  private final String group;
  private final String ingestServiceName;
  private final ServiceRunOptions options;
  private final String sessionKerberosPrincipal;
  private final Path sessionKerberosKeytab;
  private final ServiceInstanceResolver endpointResolver;
  private final CallerAppIdentity callerApp;
  private final String environment;
  private final String region;
  private final String site;
  private final SessionImpl session;
  private final ServiceRoutingState ingestRoutingState = new ServiceRoutingState();

  public RemoteRowManager(
      Fabric.Session session,
      RemoteTabularManager tabularManager,
      DiscoveryCache DiscoveryCache,
      String group,
      String callerAppName,
      String callerAppInstance,
      String environment,
      String region,
      String site,
      DataOptions.ServiceOptions dataOptions,
      String kerberosPrincipal,
      Path kerberosKeytab,
      ServiceInstanceResolver endpointResolver) {
    this.session = (SessionImpl) Objects.requireNonNull(session, "session");
    this.tabularManager = Objects.requireNonNull(tabularManager, "tabularManager");
    this.DiscoveryCache = Objects.requireNonNull(DiscoveryCache, "DiscoveryCache");
    this.group = Strings.requireNonBlank(group, "session group");
    DataOptions.ServiceOptions configured = Objects.requireNonNull(dataOptions, "dataOptions");
    if (!configured.enabled()) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(
          "RemoteRowManager requires DataOptions service.enabled=true");
    }
    this.ingestServiceName = Strings.trimToNull(configured.ingestService());
    this.options =
        configured.serviceOptions() == null
            ? ServiceRunOptions.defaults()
            : configured.serviceOptions();
    this.sessionKerberosPrincipal = Strings.trimToNull(kerberosPrincipal);
    this.sessionKerberosKeytab = kerberosKeytab;
    this.endpointResolver = endpointResolver;
    this.callerApp = new CallerAppIdentity(group, callerAppName, callerAppInstance);
    this.environment = Strings.trimToNull(environment);
    this.region = Strings.trimToNull(region);
    this.site = Strings.trimToNull(site);
  }

  @Override
  public boolean check() {
    return tabularManager.check();
  }

  @Override
  public RowResult query(DataQuery query) {
    ByteBuffer ipcBuffer = tabularManager.queryIpcBuffer(query);
    return decodeDataResult(ipcBuffer);
  }

  @Override
  public RowResult querySql(String sql) {
    return decodeDataResult(tabularManager.queryIpcBuffer(sql));
  }

  @Override
  public RowResult querySql(String sql, int limit) {
    return decodeDataResult(tabularManager.queryIpcBuffer(sql, limit));
  }

  void appendIpc(DatasetId datasetId, byte[] arrowIpcStreamBytes) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(datasetId, "datasetId");
    if (arrowIpcStreamBytes == null || arrowIpcStreamBytes.length == 0) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Arrow IPC stream bytes are required for append");
    }
    if (ingestServiceName == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "Remote ingest service name is not configured (DataOptions.ingestService)");
    }
    String ingestName = resolveIngestName(datasetId);
    RemoteFlightClientSupport.ServiceEndpoint endpoint = resolveIngestService();
    OtelManager otelRuntime = resolveClientRuntime(endpoint);
    Attributes otelAttrs = otelAttributes(endpoint);
    long otelStartedAt = System.nanoTime();
    Span otelSpan =
        FabricOtelSupport.startSpan(
            otelRuntime, "fabric.flight.client.append", SpanKind.CLIENT, otelAttrs);
    Throwable otelError = null;

    try (RemoteFlightClientSupport.ClientResources client =
            RemoteFlightClientSupport.openClient(
                endpoint, options, sessionKerberosPrincipal, sessionKerberosKeytab);
        ArrowStreamReader reader =
            new ArrowStreamReader(new ByteArrayInputStream(arrowIpcStreamBytes), client.allocator())) {
      VectorSchemaRoot root = reader.getVectorSchemaRoot();
      FlightDescriptor descriptor =
          FlightDescriptor.command(("ingest:" + ingestName).getBytes(StandardCharsets.UTF_8));
      CallOption[] callOptions =
          RemoteFlightClientSupport.buildCallOptions(
              callerApp, environment, region, site, client, null);
      AsyncPutListener putListener = new AsyncPutListener();
      FlightClient.ClientStreamListener stream =
          client.flightClient().startPut(descriptor, root, putListener, callOptions);
      while (reader.loadNextBatch()) {
        stream.putNext();
      }
      stream.completed();
      putListener.getResult();
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      otelError = ex;
      String kerberosDetails =
          RemoteFlightClientSupport.kerberosAuthFailureDetails(
              endpoint, ex, sessionKerberosPrincipal);
      String endpointContext = RemoteFlightClientSupport.endpointSecurityContext(endpoint);
      String detailSuffix = kerberosDetails == null ? "" : " " + kerberosDetails;
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "Remote ingest failed ["
              + endpointContext
              + "] ingest="
              + ingestName
              + ": "
              + ex.getMessage()
              + detailSuffix,
          ex);
    } finally {
      FabricOtelSupport.endSpan(otelRuntime, otelSpan, otelAttrs, otelStartedAt, otelError);
    }
  }

  @Override
  public void close() {
    tabularManager.close();
  }

  private OtelManager resolveClientRuntime(RemoteFlightClientSupport.ServiceEndpoint endpoint) {
    OtelManager runtime = session.telemetry();
    DefinitionService service = endpoint == null ? null : endpoint.definition();
    return FabricOtelEnablement.isArrowFlightClientTracingEnabled(service)
        ? runtime
        : null;
  }

  private Attributes otelAttributes(RemoteFlightClientSupport.ServiceEndpoint endpoint) {
    String endpointAddress =
        endpoint == null ? null : endpoint.connectHost() + ":" + endpoint.port();
    String serviceName = endpoint == null ? null : endpoint.serviceName();
    String serviceGroup = endpoint == null ? null : endpoint.group();
    return FabricOtelAttributes.common(
        serviceGroup,
        callerApp == null ? null : callerApp.name(),
        serviceName,
        "arrow-flight",
        callerApp == null ? null : callerApp.asSubject(),
        endpointAddress);
  }

  private RemoteFlightClientSupport.ServiceEndpoint resolveIngestService() {
    String serviceGroup = Strings.firstNonBlank(options.group(), group);
    return RemoteFlightClientSupport.resolveArrowService(
        DiscoveryCache,
        serviceGroup,
        ingestServiceName,
        DefinitionService.ServiceType.ARROW_FLIGHT_INGEST,
        endpointResolver,
        currentRoutingContext(),
        ingestRoutingState);
  }

  private ServiceRoutingContext currentRoutingContext() {
    UserPrincipal principal = UserContext.get().orElse(null);
    CallerAppContext.ContextValue callerContext = CallerAppContext.get().orElse(null);
    String effectiveSubject =
        Strings.firstNonBlank(
            principal == null ? null : Strings.trimToNull(principal.username()),
            sessionKerberosPrincipal);
    String callerAppSubject =
        Strings.firstNonBlank(
            callerContext == null ? null : callerContext.callerAppSubject(),
            callerApp == null ? null : callerApp.asSubject());
    return new ServiceRoutingContext(
        null,
        "ARROW_FLIGHT",
        effectiveSubject,
        callerAppSubject,
        options.routingKey(),
        callerContext == null ? null : callerContext.requestId(),
        null);
  }

  private String resolveIngestName(DatasetId datasetId) {
    String datasetCanonical = datasetId.toString();
    List<String> matches = new ArrayList<>();
    String ingestGroup = Strings.firstNonBlank(options.group(), group);
    for (DefinitionIngest ingest : DiscoveryCache.list(DefinitionIngest.class, ingestGroup)) {
      if (ingest == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String definitionDatasetId = Strings.trimToNull(ingest.datasetId());
      if (!Objects.equals(datasetCanonical, definitionDatasetId)) {
        continue;
      }
      String name =
          ingest.envelope() == null ? null : Strings.trimToNull(ingest.envelope().name());
      if (name != null) {
        matches.add(name);
      }
    }
    if (matches.isEmpty()) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("No ingest registered for dataset " + datasetId);
    }
    if (matches.size() > 1) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "Multiple ingests registered for dataset "
              + datasetId
              + ". Explicit ingestName required.");
    }
    return matches.get(0);
  }

  private RowResult decodeDataResult(ByteBuffer ipcBuffer) {
    return ArrowIpcRowDecoder.decodeToRowResult(ipcBuffer, tabularManager.decodeAllocator());
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.manager;

import java.util.List;

final class RowManagerImplSql {
  private RowManagerImplSql() {}

  static String buildCreateActiveTableSql(String tableName, List<RowManagerImpl.AppendColumn> columns) {
    StringBuilder sql = new StringBuilder("create table if not exists ");
    sql.append(quoteIdentifier(tableName)).append(" (");
    for (int index = 0; index < columns.size(); index++) {
      if (index > 0) {
        sql.append(", ");
      }
      RowManagerImpl.AppendColumn column = columns.get(index);
      sql.append(quoteIdentifier(column.field().getName())).append(" ").append(column.duckdbType());
    }
    sql.append(")");
    return sql.toString();
  }

  static String buildCreateActiveTempTableSql(
      String tempTableName, List<RowManagerImpl.AppendColumn> columns) {
    StringBuilder sql = new StringBuilder("create temp table ");
    sql.append(quoteIdentifier(tempTableName)).append(" (");
    for (int index = 0; index < columns.size(); index++) {
      if (index > 0) {
        sql.append(", ");
      }
      RowManagerImpl.AppendColumn column = columns.get(index);
      sql.append(quoteIdentifier(column.field().getName())).append(" ").append(column.duckdbType());
    }
    if (!columns.isEmpty()) {
      sql.append(", ");
    }
    sql.append(quoteIdentifier("__fabric_seq")).append(" BIGINT)");
    return sql.toString();
  }

  static String buildInsertActiveTempSql(String tempTableName, List<RowManagerImpl.AppendColumn> columns) {
    StringBuilder sql = new StringBuilder("insert into ");
    sql.append(quoteIdentifier(tempTableName)).append(" (");
    for (int index = 0; index < columns.size(); index++) {
      if (index > 0) {
        sql.append(", ");
      }
      sql.append(quoteIdentifier(columns.get(index).field().getName()));
    }
    if (!columns.isEmpty()) {
      sql.append(", ");
    }
    sql.append(quoteIdentifier("__fabric_seq")).append(") values (");
    for (int index = 0; index < columns.size(); index++) {
      if (index > 0) {
        sql.append(", ");
      }
      sql.append("?");
    }
    if (!columns.isEmpty()) {
      sql.append(", ");
    }
    sql.append("?)");
    return sql.toString();
  }

  static String buildDuckDbActiveMergeSql(
      String tableName,
      String tempTableName,
      List<RowManagerImpl.AppendColumn> columns,
      List<String> primaryKey,
      boolean hasDeleteMarkColumn,
      boolean hasSequenceColumn,
      String activeDeleteMarkColumn) {
    String columnList =
        columns.stream()
            .map(column -> quoteIdentifier(column.field().getName()))
            .reduce((left, right) -> left + ", " + right)
            .orElseThrow(() -> new IllegalStateException("DUCKDB_ACTIVE merge columns are required"));
    String partitionBy =
        primaryKey.stream()
            .map(RowManagerImplSql::quoteIdentifier)
            .reduce((left, right) -> left + ", " + right)
            .orElseThrow();
    String orderByExpression =
        hasSequenceColumn
            ? quoteIdentifier("__fabric_seq") + " desc"
            : primaryKey.stream()
                .map(RowManagerImplSql::quoteIdentifier)
                .reduce((left, right) -> left + ", " + right)
                .orElse("1");
    String ranked =
        "select "
            + columnList
            + ", row_number() over (partition by "
            + partitionBy
            + " order by "
            + orderByExpression
            + ") as "
            + quoteIdentifier("__fabric_rn")
            + " from "
            + quoteIdentifier(tempTableName);
    String source =
        "select "
            + columnList
            + " from ("
            + ranked
            + ") where "
            + quoteIdentifier("__fabric_rn")
            + " = 1";
    String onClause =
        primaryKey.stream()
            .map(key -> "target." + quoteIdentifier(key) + " = source." + quoteIdentifier(key))
            .reduce((left, right) -> left + " and " + right)
            .orElseThrow();
    String updateSet =
        columns.stream()
            .map(
                column ->
                    quoteIdentifier(column.field().getName())
                        + " = source."
                        + quoteIdentifier(column.field().getName()))
            .reduce((left, right) -> left + ", " + right)
            .orElse("");
    if (hasDeleteMarkColumn) {
      if (updateSet.isEmpty()) {
        updateSet = quoteIdentifier(activeDeleteMarkColumn) + " = false";
      } else {
        updateSet = updateSet + ", " + quoteIdentifier(activeDeleteMarkColumn) + " = false";
      }
    }
    String insertColumns = columnList;
    String insertValues =
        columns.stream()
            .map(column -> "source." + quoteIdentifier(column.field().getName()))
            .reduce((left, right) -> left + ", " + right)
            .orElseThrow();
    if (hasDeleteMarkColumn) {
      insertColumns = insertColumns + ", " + quoteIdentifier(activeDeleteMarkColumn);
      insertValues = insertValues + ", false";
    }
    return "merge into "
        + quoteIdentifier(tableName)
        + " as target using ("
        + source
        + ") as source on "
        + onClause
        + " when matched then update set "
        + updateSet
        + " when not matched then insert ("
        + insertColumns
        + ") values ("
        + insertValues
        + ")";
  }

  static String buildDuckDbActiveDeleteSql(
      String tableName, String tempTableName, List<String> primaryKey) {
    String pkColumns =
        primaryKey.stream()
            .map(RowManagerImplSql::quoteIdentifier)
            .reduce((left, right) -> left + ", " + right)
            .orElseThrow();
    String onClause =
        primaryKey.stream()
            .map(key -> "target." + quoteIdentifier(key) + " = source." + quoteIdentifier(key))
            .reduce((left, right) -> left + " and " + right)
            .orElseThrow();
    return "delete from "
        + quoteIdentifier(tableName)
        + " as target using (select distinct "
        + pkColumns
        + " from "
        + quoteIdentifier(tempTableName)
        + ") as source where "
        + onClause;
  }

  static String buildDuckDbActiveMarkDeletedSql(
      String tableName,
      String tempTableName,
      List<String> primaryKey,
      String activeDeleteMarkColumn) {
    String pkColumns =
        primaryKey.stream()
            .map(RowManagerImplSql::quoteIdentifier)
            .reduce((left, right) -> left + ", " + right)
            .orElseThrow();
    String onClause =
        primaryKey.stream()
            .map(key -> "target." + quoteIdentifier(key) + " = source." + quoteIdentifier(key))
            .reduce((left, right) -> left + " and " + right)
            .orElseThrow();
    return "update "
        + quoteIdentifier(tableName)
        + " as target set "
        + quoteIdentifier(activeDeleteMarkColumn)
        + " = true from (select distinct "
        + pkColumns
        + " from "
        + quoteIdentifier(tempTableName)
        + ") as source where "
        + onClause;
  }

  private static String quoteIdentifier(String identifier) {
    return "\"" + identifier.replace("\"", "\"\"") + "\"";
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.manager;

import java.io.ByteArrayInputStream;
import java.io.IOException;
import java.nio.file.Path;
import java.util.List;
import org.apache.arrow.vector.VectorSchemaRoot;
import org.apache.arrow.vector.ipc.ArrowStreamReader;
import org.apache.arrow.vector.types.pojo.Field;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.duckdb.DuckdbSession;

final class RowManagerImplWrite {
  private RowManagerImplWrite() {}

  static void appendArrowIpcToParquetLocal(
      RowManagerImpl self,
      String canonicalDatasetId,
      Path datasetRoot,
      RowManagerImpl.AppendPartitionConfig partitionConfig,
      byte[] arrowIpcStreamBytes) {
    try {
      java.nio.file.Files.createDirectories(datasetRoot);
    } catch (IOException ex) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "Failed to create dataset PARQUET root directory: " + datasetRoot, ex);
    }

    try (ArrowStreamReader reader =
            new ArrowStreamReader(new ByteArrayInputStream(arrowIpcStreamBytes), self.ipcAllocatorInternal());
        DuckdbSession session = self.engineInternal().openSession()) {
      VectorSchemaRoot root = reader.getVectorSchemaRoot();
      List<Field> fields = root.getSchema().getFields();
      if (fields.isEmpty()) {
        throw new IllegalStateException(
            "Arrow IPC stream schema is empty for dataset " + canonicalDatasetId);
      }
      RowManagerImpl.AppendSchema appendSchema =
          RowManagerImpl.buildAppendSchema(fields, partitionConfig.partitionValueField(), canonicalDatasetId);

      String tempTableName = self.nextTempTableName("append_");
      boolean tempTableCreated = false;
      RuntimeException writeFailure = null;
      try {
        session.exec(RowManagerImpl.buildCreateTempTableSql(tempTableName, appendSchema.columns()));
        tempTableCreated = true;

        long insertedRows =
            self.insertArrowBatches(
                session, tempTableName, root, reader, appendSchema, partitionConfig, canonicalDatasetId);
        if (insertedRows <= 0) {
          return;
        }

        if (appendSchema.partitionValueColumn() == null) {
          Path partitionDirectory =
              RowManagerImpl.resolvePartitionDirectory(
                  datasetRoot, partitionConfig.partitionKey(), partitionConfig.ingestDateValue());
          Path targetFile =
              RowManagerImpl.normalizeWriteTargetPath(partitionDirectory.resolve(self.nextDatasetFilename()));
          session.exec(RowManagerImpl.buildCopySql(tempTableName, null, targetFile));
          return;
        }

        for (RowManagerImpl.PartitionKey partitionKey : appendSchema.partitionKeyOrder().keySet()) {
          Path partitionDirectory =
              RowManagerImpl.resolvePartitionDirectory(
                  datasetRoot, partitionConfig.partitionKey(), partitionKey.partitionPathValue());
          Path targetFile =
              RowManagerImpl.normalizeWriteTargetPath(partitionDirectory.resolve(self.nextDatasetFilename()));
          String whereClause =
              RowManagerImpl.buildPartitionWhereClause(
                  appendSchema.partitionValueColumn(), partitionKey.partitionSourceValue());
          session.exec(RowManagerImpl.buildCopySql(tempTableName, whereClause, targetFile));
        }
      } catch (RuntimeException ex) {
        writeFailure = ex;
        throw ex;
      } finally {
        if (tempTableCreated) {
          try {
            session.exec(RowManagerImpl.buildDropTempTableSql(tempTableName));
          } catch (RuntimeException cleanupEx) {
            if (writeFailure != null) {
              writeFailure.addSuppressed(cleanupEx);
            } else {
              throw new IllegalStateException(
                  "Failed to cleanup DuckDB temp table: " + tempTableName, cleanupEx);
            }
          }
        }
      }
    } catch (IllegalStateException ex) {
      throw ex;
    } catch (RuntimeException | IOException ex) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "Arrow IPC append failed for dataset " + canonicalDatasetId + ": " + ex.getMessage(), ex);
    }
  }

  static void appendArrowIpcToParquetS3(
      RowManagerImpl self,
      String canonicalDatasetId,
      String datasetRootUri,
      String s3ConnectionName,
      RowManagerImpl.AppendPartitionConfig partitionConfig,
      byte[] arrowIpcStreamBytes) {
    String normalizedRoot = RowManagerImpl.normalizeS3Uri(datasetRootUri);
    try (ArrowStreamReader reader =
            new ArrowStreamReader(new ByteArrayInputStream(arrowIpcStreamBytes), self.ipcAllocatorInternal());
        DuckdbSession session = self.engineInternal().openSession()) {
      self.ensureS3Configured(session, s3ConnectionName, canonicalDatasetId);
      VectorSchemaRoot root = reader.getVectorSchemaRoot();
      List<Field> fields = root.getSchema().getFields();
      if (fields.isEmpty()) {
        throw new IllegalStateException(
            "Arrow IPC stream schema is empty for dataset " + canonicalDatasetId);
      }
      RowManagerImpl.AppendSchema appendSchema =
          RowManagerImpl.buildAppendSchema(fields, partitionConfig.partitionValueField(), canonicalDatasetId);

      String tempTableName = self.nextTempTableName("append_");
      boolean tempTableCreated = false;
      RuntimeException writeFailure = null;
      try {
        session.exec(RowManagerImpl.buildCreateTempTableSql(tempTableName, appendSchema.columns()));
        tempTableCreated = true;

        long insertedRows =
            self.insertArrowBatches(
                session, tempTableName, root, reader, appendSchema, partitionConfig, canonicalDatasetId);
        if (insertedRows <= 0) {
          return;
        }

        if (appendSchema.partitionValueColumn() == null) {
          String partitionDirectory =
              RowManagerImpl.resolveS3PartitionDirectory(
                  normalizedRoot, partitionConfig.partitionKey(), partitionConfig.ingestDateValue());
          String targetFile = RowManagerImpl.appendUriPath(partitionDirectory, self.nextDatasetFilename());
          session.exec(RowManagerImpl.buildCopySql(tempTableName, null, targetFile));
          return;
        }

        for (RowManagerImpl.PartitionKey partitionKey : appendSchema.partitionKeyOrder().keySet()) {
          String partitionDirectory =
              RowManagerImpl.resolveS3PartitionDirectory(
                  normalizedRoot, partitionConfig.partitionKey(), partitionKey.partitionPathValue());
          String targetFile = RowManagerImpl.appendUriPath(partitionDirectory, self.nextDatasetFilename());
          String whereClause =
              RowManagerImpl.buildPartitionWhereClause(
                  appendSchema.partitionValueColumn(), partitionKey.partitionSourceValue());
          session.exec(RowManagerImpl.buildCopySql(tempTableName, whereClause, targetFile));
        }
      } catch (RuntimeException ex) {
        writeFailure = ex;
        throw ex;
      } finally {
        if (tempTableCreated) {
          try {
            session.exec(RowManagerImpl.buildDropTempTableSql(tempTableName));
          } catch (RuntimeException cleanupEx) {
            if (writeFailure != null) {
              writeFailure.addSuppressed(cleanupEx);
            } else {
              throw new IllegalStateException(
                  "Failed to cleanup DuckDB temp table: " + tempTableName, cleanupEx);
            }
          }
        }
      }
    } catch (IllegalStateException ex) {
      throw ex;
    } catch (RuntimeException | IOException ex) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "Arrow IPC append failed for dataset " + canonicalDatasetId + ": " + ex.getMessage(), ex);
    }
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.manager;

import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.CloseSupport;
import java.nio.file.Path;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.Fabric;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.cache.DiscoveryCache;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.checkpoints.CheckpointStore;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.DataOptions;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.IngestManager;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.ParquetManager;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.RowManager;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.DataManager;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.TabularManager;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.ViewManager;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.views.ViewManagerImpl;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.common.ServiceInstanceResolver;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class ServiceDataManagerImpl implements DataManager, AutoCloseable {
  private final Object lifecycleLock = new Object();
  private final DiscoveryCache discoveryCache;
  private final String group;
  private final String appName;
  private final String instance;
  private final String env;
  private final String region;
  private final String site;
  private final DataOptions.ServiceOptions serviceOptions;
  private final String kerberosPrincipal;
  private final Path kerberosKeytab;
  private final ServiceInstanceResolver serviceInstanceResolver;
  private final Fabric.Session session;
  private final CheckpointStore checkpointStore;

  private volatile RowManager rowManager;
  private volatile IngestManager ingestManager;
  private volatile TabularManager tabularManager;
  private volatile ViewManager viewManager;
  private volatile ParquetManager parquetManager;

  public ServiceDataManagerImpl(
      DiscoveryCache discoveryCache,
      String group,
      String appName,
      String instance,
      String env,
      String region,
      String site,
      DataOptions.ServiceOptions serviceOptions,
      String kerberosPrincipal,
      Path kerberosKeytab,
      ServiceInstanceResolver serviceInstanceResolver,
      Fabric.Session session,
      CheckpointStore checkpointStore) {
    this.discoveryCache = Objects.requireNonNull(discoveryCache, "discoveryCache");
    this.group = Strings.requireNonBlank(group, "group");
    this.appName = Strings.trimToNull(appName);
    this.instance = Strings.trimToNull(instance);
    this.env = Strings.trimToNull(env);
    this.region = Strings.trimToNull(region);
    this.site = Strings.trimToNull(site);
    this.serviceOptions = Objects.requireNonNull(serviceOptions, "serviceOptions");
    this.kerberosPrincipal = Strings.trimToNull(kerberosPrincipal);
    this.kerberosKeytab = kerberosKeytab;
    this.serviceInstanceResolver =
        Objects.requireNonNull(serviceInstanceResolver, "serviceInstanceResolver");
    this.session = Objects.requireNonNull(session, "session");
    this.checkpointStore = Objects.requireNonNull(checkpointStore, "checkpointStore");
    initialize();
  }

  @Override
  public RowManager rows() {
    return rowManager;
  }

  @Override
  public IngestManager ingest() {
    return ingestManager;
  }

  @Override
  public TabularManager tabular() {
    return tabularManager;
  }

  @Override
  public ViewManager views() {
    return viewManager;
  }

  @Override
  public ParquetManager parquet() {
    return parquetManager;
  }

  @Override
  public void close() {
    synchronized (lifecycleLock) {
      CloseSupport.closeQuietly(viewManager instanceof AutoCloseable closeable ? closeable : null);
      viewManager = null;
      CloseSupport.closeQuietly(ingestManager instanceof AutoCloseable closeable ? closeable : null);
      ingestManager = null;
      CloseSupport.closeQuietly(tabularManager instanceof AutoCloseable closeable ? closeable : null);
      tabularManager = null;
      CloseSupport.closeQuietly(rowManager);
      rowManager = null;
      parquetManager = null;
    }
  }

  private void initialize() {
    synchronized (lifecycleLock) {
      RemoteTabularManager remoteTabular =
          new RemoteTabularManager(
              session,
              discoveryCache,
              group,
              appName,
              instance,
              env,
              region,
              site,
              serviceOptions,
              kerberosPrincipal,
              kerberosKeytab,
              serviceInstanceResolver);
      RemoteRowManager remoteRow =
          new RemoteRowManager(
              session,
              remoteTabular,
              discoveryCache,
              group,
              appName,
              instance,
              env,
              region,
              site,
              serviceOptions,
              kerberosPrincipal,
              kerberosKeytab,
              serviceInstanceResolver);
      this.rowManager = remoteRow;
      this.ingestManager =
          new IngestManagerImpl(remoteRow, discoveryCache, group, session, null, checkpointStore);
      this.tabularManager = remoteTabular;
      this.viewManager =
          new ViewManagerImpl(remoteRow, discoveryCache, group, session, checkpointStore);
      this.parquetManager = ingestManager.parquet();
    }
  }

}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.manager;

import java.io.IOException;
import java.nio.ByteBuffer;
import java.nio.charset.StandardCharsets;
import java.sql.Date;
import java.sql.ResultSet;
import java.sql.ResultSetMetaData;
import java.sql.SQLException;
import java.sql.Timestamp;
import java.sql.Types;
import java.time.Instant;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Collection;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;

import java.util.concurrent.atomic.AtomicBoolean;
import org.apache.arrow.memory.BufferAllocator;
import org.apache.arrow.memory.RootAllocator;
import org.apache.arrow.vector.BigIntVector;
import org.apache.arrow.vector.DateDayVector;
import org.apache.arrow.vector.FieldVector;
import org.apache.arrow.vector.Float8Vector;
import org.apache.arrow.vector.IntVector;

import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.DataQuery;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.TabularManager;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class TabularManagerImpl implements TabularManager, AutoCloseable {
  private static final long MAX_ALLOCATOR_BYTES = 64L * 1024L * 1024L;
  private static final int INITIAL_VECTOR_CAPACITY = 256;

  private final RowManagerImpl rowManager;
  private final DuckdbCatalog catalog;
  private final RootAllocator ipcDecodeAllocator = new RootAllocator(MAX_ALLOCATOR_BYTES);
  private final AtomicBoolean closed = new AtomicBoolean(false);

  public TabularManagerImpl(RowManagerImpl rowManager) {
    this(rowManager, null);
  }

  public TabularManagerImpl(RowManagerImpl rowManager, DuckdbCatalog catalog) {
    this.rowManager = Objects.requireNonNull(rowManager, "rowManager");
    this.catalog = catalog;
  }

  @Override
  public byte[] queryIpc(DataQuery query) {
    return Bytes.toByteArray(queryIpcBuffer(query));
  }

  @Override
  public ByteBuffer queryIpcBuffer(DataQuery query) {
    ByteBuffer buffer = rowManager.queryIpcBuffer(Objects.requireNonNull(query, "query"), catalog);
    assert buffer.isDirect();
    assert buffer.position() == 0;
    return buffer;
  }

  @Override
  public byte[] queryIpc(String sql, int limit) {
    return Bytes.toByteArray(queryIpcBuffer(sql, limit));
  }

  @Override
  public ByteBuffer queryIpcBuffer(String sql, int limit) {
    DuckdbCatalog currentCatalog = catalog;
    if (currentCatalog == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("DuckDB catalog is not initialized");
    }
    String plannedSql = Strings.requireNonBlank(sql, "sql");
    Integer resolvedLimit = null;
    if (limit > 0) {
      resolvedLimit = limit;
    } else if (limit == 0) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("limit must be > 0");
    }
    ByteBuffer buffer = rowManager.queryIpcSqlBuffer(currentCatalog, plannedSql, resolvedLimit);
    assert buffer.isDirect();
    assert buffer.position() == 0;
    return buffer;
  }

  public byte[] queryIpcPublic(String sql, int limit) {
    return Bytes.toByteArray(queryIpcPublicBuffer(sql, limit));
  }

  public ByteBuffer queryIpcPublicBuffer(String sql, int limit) {
    DuckdbCatalog currentCatalog = catalog;
    if (currentCatalog == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("DuckDB catalog is not initialized");
    }
    String plannedSql = Strings.requireNonBlank(sql, "sql");
    Integer resolvedLimit = null;
    if (limit > 0) {
      resolvedLimit = limit;
    } else if (limit == 0) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("limit must be > 0");
    }
    ByteBuffer buffer = rowManager.queryIpcSqlPublicBuffer(currentCatalog, plannedSql, resolvedLimit);
    assert buffer.isDirect();
    assert buffer.position() == 0;
    return buffer;
  }

  public RowManagerImpl rowManager() {
    return rowManager;
  }

  public DuckdbCatalog catalog() {
    return catalog;
  }

  public void installDataset(String datasetId) {
    DuckdbCatalog currentCatalog = catalog;
    if (currentCatalog == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("DuckDB catalog is not initialized");
    }
    currentCatalog.install(Strings.requireNonBlank(datasetId, "datasetId"));
  }

  public void installDatasets(Collection<String> datasetIds) {
    if (datasetIds == null || datasetIds.isEmpty()) {
      return;
    }
    for (String datasetId : datasetIds) {
      String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(datasetId);
      if (normalized != null) {
        installDataset(normalized);
      }
    }
  }

  @Override
  public List<Map<String, Object>> decodeIpcRows(byte[] ipcBytes) {
    if (closed.get()) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Tabular manager is closed");
    }
    return ArrowIpcRowDecoder.decodeToRowMaps(ipcBytes, ipcDecodeAllocator);
  }

  @Override
  public List<Map<String, Object>> decodeIpcRows(ByteBuffer ipcBuffer) {
    if (closed.get()) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Tabular manager is closed");
    }
    return ArrowIpcRowDecoder.decodeToRowMaps(ipcBuffer, ipcDecodeAllocator);
  }

  @Override
  public void close() {
    if (!closed.compareAndSet(false, true)) {
      return;
    }
    ipcDecodeAllocator.close();
  }

  static byte[] toArrowIpcBytes(
      ResultSet resultSet, String datasetId, BufferAllocator allocator) throws SQLException {
    return Bytes.toByteArray(toArrowIpcBuffer(resultSet, datasetId, allocator));
  }

  static ByteBuffer toArrowIpcBuffer(
      ResultSet resultSet, String datasetId, BufferAllocator allocator) throws SQLException {
    Objects.requireNonNull(allocator, "allocator");
    ResultSetMetaData metadata = resultSet.getMetaData();
    int columnCount = metadata.getColumnCount();

    List<Field> fields = new ArrayList<>(columnCount);
    List<Integer> jdbcTypes = new ArrayList<>(columnCount);
    for (int i = 1; i <= columnCount; i++) {
      int jdbcType = metadata.getColumnType(i);
      String columnLabel = metadata.getColumnLabel(i);
      boolean nullable = metadata.isNullable(i) != ResultSetMetaData.columnNoNulls;
      fields.add(new Field(columnLabel, new FieldType(nullable, mapArrowType(jdbcType, metadata.getColumnTypeName(i), columnLabel, datasetId), null, null), null));
      jdbcTypes.add(jdbcType);
    }

    try (VectorSchemaRoot root = VectorSchemaRoot.create(new Schema(fields), allocator);
        Bytes.DirectBufferOutputStream out = Bytes.directOutputStream();
        ArrowStreamWriter writer = new ArrowStreamWriter(root, null, out)) {
      List<FieldVector> vectors = root.getFieldVectors();
      for (FieldVector vector : vectors) {
        vector.setInitialCapacity(INITIAL_VECTOR_CAPACITY);
      }
      root.allocateNew();

      List<ColumnWriter> columnWriters = new ArrayList<>(columnCount);
      for (int i = 0; i < columnCount; i++) {
        columnWriters.add(
            createColumnWriter(
                i + 1, jdbcTypes.get(i), fields.get(i).getName(), vectors.get(i), datasetId));
      }

      int rowIndex = 0;
      while (resultSet.next()) {
        ensureCapacity(vectors, rowIndex);
        for (ColumnWriter columnWriter : columnWriters) {
          columnWriter.write(resultSet, rowIndex);
        }
        rowIndex++;
      }

      for (FieldVector vector : vectors) {
        vector.setValueCount(rowIndex);
      }
      root.setRowCount(rowIndex);

      writer.start();
      writer.writeBatch();
      writer.end();
      ByteBuffer buffer = out.toDirectByteBuffer();
      assert buffer.isDirect();
      assert buffer.position() == 0;
      return buffer;
    } catch (IOException ex) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Failed to serialize Arrow IPC stream", ex);
    }
  }

  private static ArrowType mapArrowType(
      int jdbcType, String jdbcTypeName, String columnLabel, String datasetId) {
    return switch (jdbcType) {
      case Types.CHAR,
          Types.VARCHAR,
          Types.LONGVARCHAR,
          Types.NCHAR,
          Types.NVARCHAR,
          Types.LONGNVARCHAR -> new ArrowType.Utf8();
      case Types.TINYINT, Types.SMALLINT, Types.INTEGER -> new ArrowType.Int(32, true);
      case Types.BIGINT -> new ArrowType.Int(64, true);
      case Types.REAL, Types.FLOAT, Types.DOUBLE ->
          new ArrowType.FloatingPoint(FloatingPointPrecision.DOUBLE);
      case Types.DATE -> new ArrowType.Date(DateUnit.DAY);
      case Types.TIMESTAMP, Types.TIMESTAMP_WITH_TIMEZONE ->
          new ArrowType.Timestamp(TimeUnit.MICROSECOND, null);
      default ->
          throw unsupportedColumnType(columnLabel, jdbcType, jdbcTypeName, datasetId);
    };
  }

  private static ColumnWriter createColumnWriter(
      int jdbcIndex, int jdbcType, String columnLabel, FieldVector vector, String datasetId) {
    return switch (jdbcType) {
      case Types.CHAR,
          Types.VARCHAR,
          Types.LONGVARCHAR,
          Types.NCHAR,
          Types.NVARCHAR,
          Types.LONGNVARCHAR -> {
        VarCharVector valueVector = requireVector(vector, VarCharVector.class, columnLabel);
        yield (resultSet, rowIndex) -> {
          String value = resultSet.getString(jdbcIndex);
          if (value == null) {
            valueVector.setNull(rowIndex);
          } else {
            valueVector.setSafe(rowIndex, value.getBytes(StandardCharsets.UTF_8));
          }
        };
      }
      case Types.TINYINT, Types.SMALLINT, Types.INTEGER -> {
        IntVector valueVector = requireVector(vector, IntVector.class, columnLabel);
        yield (resultSet, rowIndex) -> {
          int value = resultSet.getInt(jdbcIndex);
          if (resultSet.wasNull()) {
            valueVector.setNull(rowIndex);
          } else {
            valueVector.setSafe(rowIndex, value);
          }
        };
      }
      case Types.BIGINT -> {
        BigIntVector valueVector = requireVector(vector, BigIntVector.class, columnLabel);
        yield (resultSet, rowIndex) -> {
          long value = resultSet.getLong(jdbcIndex);
          if (resultSet.wasNull()) {
            valueVector.setNull(rowIndex);
          } else {
            valueVector.setSafe(rowIndex, value);
          }
        };
      }
      case Types.REAL, Types.FLOAT, Types.DOUBLE -> {
        Float8Vector valueVector = requireVector(vector, Float8Vector.class, columnLabel);
        yield (resultSet, rowIndex) -> {
          double value = resultSet.getDouble(jdbcIndex);
          if (resultSet.wasNull()) {
            valueVector.setNull(rowIndex);
          } else {
            valueVector.setSafe(rowIndex, value);
          }
        };
      }
      case Types.DATE -> {
        DateDayVector valueVector = requireVector(vector, DateDayVector.class, columnLabel);
        yield (resultSet, rowIndex) -> {
          Date value = resultSet.getDate(jdbcIndex);
          if (value == null) {
            valueVector.setNull(rowIndex);
          } else {
            valueVector.setSafe(rowIndex, Math.toIntExact(value.toLocalDate().toEpochDay()));
          }
        };
      }
      case Types.TIMESTAMP, Types.TIMESTAMP_WITH_TIMEZONE -> {
        TimeStampMicroVector valueVector =
            requireVector(vector, TimeStampMicroVector.class, columnLabel);
        yield (resultSet, rowIndex) -> {
          Timestamp value = resultSet.getTimestamp(jdbcIndex);
          if (value == null) {
            valueVector.setNull(rowIndex);
          } else {
            valueVector.setSafe(rowIndex, toEpochMicros(value));
          }
        };
      }
      default -> throw unsupportedColumnType(columnLabel, jdbcType, null, datasetId);
    };
  }

  private static <T extends FieldVector> T requireVector(
      FieldVector vector, Class<T> type, String columnLabel) {
    if (!type.isInstance(vector)) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "Arrow vector mismatch for column "
              + columnLabel
              + ": expected "
              + type.getSimpleName()
              + ", got "
              + vector.getClass().getSimpleName());
    }
    return type.cast(vector);
  }

  private static long toEpochMicros(Timestamp timestamp) {
    Instant instant = timestamp.toInstant();
    return Math.addExact(
        Math.multiplyExact(instant.getEpochSecond(), 1_000_000L), instant.getNano() / 1_000L);
  }

  private static void ensureCapacity(List<FieldVector> vectors, int rowIndex) {
    for (FieldVector vector : vectors) {
      while (rowIndex >= vector.getValueCapacity()) {
        vector.reAlloc();
      }
    }
  }

  private static IllegalStateException unsupportedColumnType(
      String columnLabel, int jdbcType, String jdbcTypeName, String datasetId) {
    String resolvedTypeName = jdbcTypeName == null || jdbcTypeName.isBlank() ? "n/a" : jdbcTypeName;
    return new IllegalStateException(
        "Unsupported JDBC type for Arrow IPC column "
            + columnLabel
            + ": jdbcType="
            + jdbcType
            + " typeName="
            + resolvedTypeName
            + " dataset="
            + datasetId);
  }

  @FunctionalInterface
  private interface ColumnWriter {
    void write(ResultSet resultSet, int rowIndex) throws SQLException;
  }
}

FILE: SampleSourceAmps.java

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.schema.sources.amps;

import com.crankuptheamps.client.Message;
import java.nio.charset.StandardCharsets;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Iterator;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.concurrent.CountDownLatch;
import java.util.concurrent.TimeUnit;
import java.util.concurrent.atomic.AtomicBoolean;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.connections.ConnectionManager;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.connectors.amps.AmpsConnection;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionIngestSource;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.schema.client.SchemaSampleOptions;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.schema.PayloadSample;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.schema.SampleSource;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class SampleSourceAmps implements SampleSource {
  private final List<PayloadSample> samples;

  public SampleSourceAmps(
      ConnectionManager connectionManager,
      String ingestId,
      DefinitionIngestSource.AmpsSource amps,
      SchemaSampleOptions options) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(connectionManager, "connectionManager");
    Objects.requireNonNull(amps, "amps");
    Objects.requireNonNull(options, "options");
    String resolvedIngestId = Strings.requireNonBlank(ingestId, "ingestId");
    String connectionName = Strings.requireNonBlank(amps.connectionName(), "amps.connectionName");
    String topic = Strings.requireNonBlank(amps.topic(), "amps.topic");
    this.samples =
        collect(
            connectionManager,
            resolvedIngestId,
            connectionName,
            new AmpsConnection.SubscriptionSpec(
                Boolean.TRUE.equals(amps.sow()), topic, amps.options(), amps.filter()),
            options.maxMessages(),
            options.maxBytes(),
            options.maxMillis());
  }

  @Override
  public Iterator<PayloadSample> iterator() {
    return samples.iterator();
  }

  private static List<PayloadSample> collect(
      ConnectionManager connectionManager,
      String ingestId,
      String connectionName,
      AmpsConnection.SubscriptionSpec subscriptionSpec,
      int maxMessages,
      int maxBytes,
      long maxMillis) {
    List<PayloadSample> collected = new ArrayList<>();
    Object lock = new Object();
    CountDownLatch done = new CountDownLatch(1);
    AtomicBoolean stop = new AtomicBoolean(false);
    Counter counter = new Counter();
    AmpsConnection.Subscription subscription = null;
    try {
      AmpsConnection connection = connectionManager.amps(connectionName);
      subscription =
          connection.subscribe(
              subscriptionSpec,
              (AmpsConnection.SubscriptionListener)
                  message -> {
                    if (message == null || stop.get()) {
                      return;
                    }
                    Message raw = message.raw();
                    if (raw != null
                        && raw.getCommand() == Message.Command.GroupEnd
                        && (subscriptionSpec.sow() || subscriptionSpec.sowOnly())) {
                      if (stop.compareAndSet(false, true)) {
                        done.countDown();
                      }
                      return;
                    }
                    String payload = message.data();
                    if (payload == null) {
                      return;
                    }
                    int payloadBytes = payload.getBytes(StandardCharsets.UTF_8).length;
                    synchronized (lock) {
                      if (stop.get()) {
                        return;
                      }
                      if (counter.messages >= maxMessages || counter.bytes >= maxBytes) {
                        stop.set(true);
                        done.countDown();
                        return;
                      }
                      if (counter.bytes + payloadBytes > maxBytes) {
                        stop.set(true);
                        done.countDown();
                        return;
                      }
                      collected.add(
                          new PayloadSample(
                              Strings.trimToNull(message.topic()),
                              payload,
                              System.currentTimeMillis()));
                      counter.messages++;
                      counter.bytes += payloadBytes;
                      if (counter.messages >= maxMessages || counter.bytes >= maxBytes) {
                        stop.set(true);
                        done.countDown();
                      }
                    }
                  });
      long waitMillis = Math.max(1L, maxMillis);
      done.await(waitMillis, TimeUnit.MILLISECONDS);
      stop.set(true);
      return List.copyOf(collected);
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "Failed to sample AMPS source ingest="
              + ingestId
              + " connection="
              + connectionName
              + " topic="
              + subscriptionSpec.topic(),
          ex);
    } finally {
      if (subscription != null) {
        try {
          subscription.close();
        } catch (Exception ignore) {
        }
      }
    }
  }

  private static final class Counter {
    private int messages;
    private int bytes;
  }
}

FILE: ViewGraphPlanner.java
