package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.views;

import java.util.ArrayDeque;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.Deque;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Set;

public final class ViewGraphPlanner {
  private static final Comparator<String> ORDER =
      String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER.thenComparing(Comparator.naturalOrder());

  public List<String> plan(String rootDatasetId, Map<String, List<String>> viewDependencies) {
    String root = requireDatasetId(rootDatasetId, "rootDatasetId");
    Map<String, List<String>> graph = viewDependencies == null ? Map.of() : viewDependencies;
    if (!graph.containsKey(root)) {
      return List.of(root);
    }
    LinkedHashSet<String> ordered = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    Deque<String> stack = new ArrayDeque<>();
    Set<String> visiting = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    visit(root, graph, ordered, stack, visiting);
    return List.copyOf(ordered);
  }

  private static void visit(
      String current,
      Map<String, List<String>> graph,
      LinkedHashSet<String> ordered,
      Deque<String> stack,
      Set<String> visiting) {
    if (ordered.contains(current)) {
      return;
    }
    if (!visiting.add(current)) {
      throw cycle(current, stack);
    }
    stack.addLast(current);
    List<String> deps = graph.get(current);
    if (deps != null && !deps.isEmpty()) {
      List<String> sorted = new ArrayList<>(deps);
      sorted.sort(ORDER);
      for (String dependency : sorted) {
        String normalized = requireDatasetId(dependency, "dependency");
        if (!graph.containsKey(normalized)) {
          continue;
        }
        visit(normalized, graph, ordered, stack, visiting);
      }
    }
    stack.removeLast();
    visiting.remove(current);
    ordered.add(current);
  }

  private static IllegalStateException cycle(String repeated, Deque<String> stack) {
    List<String> cycle = new ArrayList<>();
    boolean include = false;
    for (String candidate : stack) {
      if (candidate.equals(repeated)) {
        include = true;
      }
      if (include) {
        cycle.add(candidate);
      }
    }
    cycle.add(repeated);
    return new IllegalStateException("View dependency cycle detected: " + String.join(" -> ", cycle));
  }

  private static String requireDatasetId(String value, String field) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(field + " is required");
    }
    return value.trim();
  }
}


FILE: ViewManagerImplRefresh.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.views;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.function.BiFunction;
import java.util.function.Function;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionDataset;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionEnvelope;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.checkpoints.CheckpointKey;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.checkpoints.CheckpointRecord;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.checkpoints.CheckpointStore;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.checkpoints.CheckpointType;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.dataset.DatasetId;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

final class ViewManagerImplRefresh {

  private ViewManagerImplRefresh() {}

  static List<DatasetId> parseDependencies(
      List<String> dependencies,
      String datasetId,
      BiFunction<String, String, DatasetId> dependencyResolver) {
    if (dependencies == null || dependencies.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<DatasetId> parsed = new ArrayList<>();
    for (String dependency : dependencies) {
      String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(dependency);
      if (normalized == null) {
        continue;
      }
      parsed.add(dependencyResolver.apply(normalized, datasetId));
    }
    parsed.sort(
        Comparator.comparing(DatasetId::toString, String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER)
            .thenComparing(DatasetId::toString));
    return List.copyOf(parsed);
  }

  static Map<String, String> buildInputFingerprints(
      List<DatasetId> dependencies, Function<DatasetId, DefinitionDataset> datasetResolver) {
    if (dependencies == null || dependencies.isEmpty()) {
      return Map.of();
    }
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> fingerprints = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    List<String> keys = new ArrayList<>();
    for (DatasetId dependency : dependencies) {
      keys.add(dependency.toString());
    }
    keys.sort(String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER);
    for (String dependencyId : keys) {
      DefinitionDataset dependency = datasetResolver.apply(DatasetId.parse(dependencyId));
      DefinitionEnvelope envelope = dependency.envelope();
      String fingerprint =
          Strings.firstNonBlank(
              envelope == null ? null : Strings.trimToNull(envelope.updatedTimeUtc()),
              envelope == null ? null : Strings.trimToNull(envelope.uuid()),
              "n/a");
      fingerprints.put(dependencyId, fingerprint);
    }
    return Map.copyOf(fingerprints);
  }

  static void writeViewCheckpoint(
      CheckpointStore checkpointStore,
      String group,
      String datasetId,
      String status,
      String refreshEndUtc,
      long durationMs,
      Long rowCount,
      String error) {
    checkpointStore.save(
        CheckpointRecord.of(
            new CheckpointKey(group, CheckpointType.VIEW, datasetId, "refresh"),
            Map.ofEntries(
                Map.entry("status", Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(status), "UNKNOWN")),
                Map.entry(
                    "refreshEndUtc",
                    Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(refreshEndUtc), "n/a")),
                Map.entry("durationMs", Long.toString(Math.max(0L, durationMs))),
                Map.entry("rowCount", rowCount == null ? "n/a" : Long.toString(rowCount)),
                Map.entry("error", Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(error), "none")))));
  }

  static String truncateError(String error, int maxErrorChars) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(error);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return "refresh failed";
    }
    if (normalized.length() <= maxErrorChars) {
      return normalized;
    }
    return normalized.substring(0, maxErrorChars);
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.views.internal;

import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionDataset;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionEnvelope;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionType;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.dataset.DatasetId;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.dataset.DatasetType;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.views.model.ViewModel;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.views.model.ViewQueryModel;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.views.model.ViewRefreshModel;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.views.model.ViewRefreshType;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.views.model.ViewTargetModel;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.views.model.ViewTargetType;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.schemas.SchemaCompatibility;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.schemas.SchemaModel;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.DefinitionModelMapperSupport;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class ViewModelMapper {
  public DefinitionDataset toDefinitionDataset(
      ViewModel model, String sessionGroup, String actor, String schemaName) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(model, "model");
    String group = DefinitionModelMapperSupport.requireNonBlank(sessionGroup, "sessionGroup");
    String namespace =
        DefinitionModelMapperSupport.requireNonBlank(model.namespace(), "model.namespace");
    String viewName = DefinitionModelMapperSupport.requireNonBlank(model.name(), "model.name");
    DatasetId outputDataset = resolveOutputDatasetId(group, namespace, viewName, model.outputDatasetId());

    DefinitionDataset.Binding binding = toBinding(outputDataset, Objects.requireNonNull(model.target(), "model.target"));
    DefinitionDataset.View view =
        new DefinitionDataset.View(
            Objects.requireNonNull(model.query(), "model.query").sql(),
            model.dependencies(),
            toRefresh(model.refresh()),
            toTarget(model.target()),
            Strings.requireNonBlank(schemaName, "schemaName"),
            (model.schemaCompatibility() == null ? SchemaCompatibility.BACKWARDS : model.schemaCompatibility())
                .name()
                .toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT),
            null);
    DefinitionEnvelope envelope =
        DefinitionModelMapperSupport.envelopeNow(
            group,
            DefinitionType.DATASET,
            DefinitionModelMapperSupport.buildScopedName(
                outputDataset.namespace(),
                outputDataset.name(),
                "dataset.namespace",
                "dataset.name"),
            Strings.firstNonBlank(
                Strings.trimToNull(model.uuid()),
                DefinitionModelMapperSupport.buildDefinitionId(
                    "view",
                    group,
                    DefinitionModelMapperSupport.buildScopedName(
                        outputDataset.namespace(),
                        outputDataset.name(),
                        "dataset.namespace",
                        "dataset.name"))),
            model.enabled(),
            model.lifecycleStatus(),
            actor);
    return new DefinitionDataset(
        envelope,
        bindingType(model.target().type()),
        outputDataset.namespace(),
        binding,
        view);
  }

  public ViewModel fromDefinitionDataset(DefinitionDataset dataset, SchemaModel schema) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(dataset, "dataset");
    Objects.requireNonNull(dataset.view(), "dataset.view");
    Objects.requireNonNull(schema, "schema");
    DefinitionEnvelope envelope = Objects.requireNonNull(dataset.envelope(), "dataset.envelope");
    String namespace = Strings.requireNonBlank(dataset.namespace(), "dataset.namespace");
    String baseName = requireDatasetBaseName(envelope.name(), namespace);
    String datasetId = DatasetId.of(envelope.group(), namespace, baseName).toString();
    return ViewModel.builder()
        .withName(baseName)
        .withNamespace(namespace)
        .withUuid(envelope.uuid())
        .withEnabled(!Boolean.FALSE.equals(envelope.enabled()))
        .withLifecycleStatus(envelope.lifecycleStatus())
        .withOutputDatasetId(datasetId)
        .withQuery(ViewQueryModel.builder().withSql(dataset.view().querySql()).build())
        .withDependencies(dataset.view().dependencies())
        .withSchema(schema)
        .withSchemaCompatibility(parseSchemaCompatibility(dataset.view().schemaCompatibility()))
        .withTarget(fromTarget(dataset))
        .withRefresh(fromRefresh(dataset.view().refresh()))
        .build();
  }

  public String deterministicSchemaName(String namespace, String viewName) {
    String resolvedNamespace =
        DefinitionModelMapperSupport.requireNonBlank(namespace, "namespace");
    String resolvedName = DefinitionModelMapperSupport.requireNonBlank(viewName, "viewName");
    return "view:" + resolvedNamespace + "/" + resolvedName;
  }

  public String deterministicOutputDatasetId(String sessionGroup, String namespace, String viewName) {
    return DatasetId.of(
            DefinitionModelMapperSupport.requireNonBlank(sessionGroup, "sessionGroup"),
            DefinitionModelMapperSupport.requireNonBlank(namespace, "namespace"),
            DefinitionModelMapperSupport.requireNonBlank(viewName, "viewName"))
        .toString();
  }

  private static DefinitionDataset.Binding toBinding(DatasetId outputDataset, ViewTargetModel target) {
    ViewTargetType type = target.type() == null ? ViewTargetType.DUCKDB_TABLE : target.type();
    return switch (type) {
      case DUCKDB_TABLE, DUCKDB_TABLE_AND_PARQUET ->
          new DefinitionDataset.Binding(
              new DefinitionDataset.DuckdbBinding(
                  target.duckdbTableName(),
                  type.name(),
                  List.of(),
                  null,
                  null,
                  null,
                  null,
                  null),
              null,
              null);
      case PARQUET_SNAPSHOT ->
          new DefinitionDataset.Binding(
              null,
              new DefinitionDataset.ParquetBinding(
                  Strings.requireNonBlank(target.parquetPath(), "view.target.parquetPath"),
                  null,
                  null,
                  null,
                  null,
                  null,
                  null),
              null);
    };
  }

  private static DefinitionDataset.Target toTarget(ViewTargetModel target) {
    return new DefinitionDataset.Target(
        Strings.requireNonBlank(target.duckdbTableName(), "view.target.duckdbTableName"),
        Strings.trimToNull(target.parquetPath()),
        (target.type() == null ? ViewTargetType.DUCKDB_TABLE : target.type()).name());
  }

  private static DefinitionDataset.Refresh toRefresh(ViewRefreshModel refresh) {
    ViewRefreshModel resolved = refresh == null ? ViewRefreshModel.builder().build() : refresh;
    ViewRefreshType type = resolved.type() == null ? ViewRefreshType.MANUAL : resolved.type();
    Long interval = type == ViewRefreshType.PERIODIC ? resolved.intervalMillis() : null;
    Boolean runOnStart = type == ViewRefreshType.PERIODIC ? resolved.runOnStart() : Boolean.FALSE;
    return new DefinitionDataset.Refresh(type.name(), interval, runOnStart);
  }

  private static ViewTargetModel fromTarget(DefinitionDataset dataset) {
    DefinitionDataset.Target target = dataset.view().target();
    if (target != null) {
      return ViewTargetModel.builder()
          .withType(parseTargetType(target.targetType()))
          .withDuckdbTableName(target.duckdbTableName())
          .withParquetPath(target.parquetPath())
          .build();
    }
    DefinitionDataset.Binding binding = dataset.binding();
    if (binding != null && binding.duckdb() != null) {
      return ViewTargetModel.builder()
          .withType(ViewTargetType.DUCKDB_TABLE)
          .withDuckdbTableName(binding.duckdb().relationName())
          .build();
    }
    if (binding != null && binding.parquet() != null) {
      return ViewTargetModel.builder()
          .withType(ViewTargetType.PARQUET_SNAPSHOT)
          .withDuckdbTableName(requireDatasetBaseName(dataset.envelope().name(), dataset.namespace()))
          .withParquetPath(binding.parquet().uri())
          .build();
    }
    throw new IllegalArgumentException("View dataset is missing target information: " + dataset);
  }

  private static ViewRefreshModel fromRefresh(DefinitionDataset.Refresh refresh) {
    DefinitionDataset.Refresh resolved =
        refresh == null
            ? new DefinitionDataset.Refresh(ViewRefreshType.MANUAL.name(), null, Boolean.FALSE)
            : refresh;
    return ViewRefreshModel.builder()
        .withType(parseRefreshType(resolved.type()))
        .withIntervalMillis(resolved.intervalMillis())
        .withRunOnStart(Boolean.TRUE.equals(resolved.runOnStart()))
        .build();
  }

  private static DatasetType bindingType(ViewTargetType type) {
    ViewTargetType resolved = type == null ? ViewTargetType.DUCKDB_TABLE : type;
    return switch (resolved) {
      case PARQUET_SNAPSHOT -> DatasetType.PARQUET;
      case DUCKDB_TABLE, DUCKDB_TABLE_AND_PARQUET -> DatasetType.DUCKDB;
    };
  }

  private static ViewTargetType parseTargetType(String token) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(token);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return ViewTargetType.DUCKDB_TABLE;
    }
    try {
      return ViewTargetType.valueOf(normalized.toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT));
    } catch (IllegalArgumentException ex) {
      return ViewTargetType.DUCKDB_TABLE;
    }
  }

  private static ViewRefreshType parseRefreshType(String token) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(token);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return ViewRefreshType.MANUAL;
    }
    try {
      return ViewRefreshType.valueOf(normalized.toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT));
    } catch (IllegalArgumentException ex) {
      return ViewRefreshType.MANUAL;
    }
  }

  private static SchemaCompatibility parseSchemaCompatibility(String token) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(token);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return SchemaCompatibility.BACKWARDS;
    }
    try {
      return SchemaCompatibility.valueOf(normalized.toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT));
    } catch (IllegalArgumentException ex) {
      return SchemaCompatibility.BACKWARDS;
    }
  }

  private static DatasetId resolveOutputDatasetId(
      String sessionGroup, String namespace, String viewName, String configuredOutputDatasetId) {
    String configured = Strings.trimToNull(configuredOutputDatasetId);
    if (configured == null) {
      return DatasetId.of(sessionGroup, namespace, viewName);
    }
    DatasetId parsed = DatasetId.parse(configured);
    if (!sessionGroup.equals(parsed.group())) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(
          "view.outputDatasetId group must match session group: expected="
              + sessionGroup
              + " actual="
              + parsed.group());
    }
    if (!namespace.equals(parsed.namespace()) || !viewName.equals(parsed.name())) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(
          "view.outputDatasetId must match view namespace/name: expected="
              + namespace
              + "/"
              + viewName
              + " actual="
              + parsed.namespace()
              + "/"
              + parsed.name());
    }
    return parsed;
  }

  private static String requireDatasetBaseName(String envelopeName, String namespace) {
    String prefix = namespace + "/";
    if (envelopeName == null || !envelopeName.startsWith(prefix) || envelopeName.length() <= prefix.length()) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(
          "Dataset definition invalid envelope.name. Expected namespace/baseName with namespace='"
              + namespace
              + "' and envelope.name='"
              + envelopeName
              + "'");
    }
    String base = envelopeName.substring(prefix.length());
    if (base.indexOf('/') >= 0) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(
          "Dataset definition invalid envelope.name. Expected namespace/baseName with namespace='"
              + namespace
              + "' and envelope.name='"
              + envelopeName
              + "'");
    }
    return base;
  }

}

FILE: SchemaCompatibilityResult.java

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.schemas.manager;

import java.util.List;
import java.util.TreeSet;

public record SchemaCompatibilityResult(
    boolean compatible,
    List<String> addedFields,
    List<String> removedFields,
    List<String> madeNullable,
    List<String> madeNonNullable,
    List<String> widenedTypes,
    List<String> narrowedTypes,
    List<String> changedTypesOther) {

  public SchemaCompatibilityResult {
    addedFields = sorted(addedFields);
    removedFields = sorted(removedFields);
    madeNullable = sorted(madeNullable);
    madeNonNullable = sorted(madeNonNullable);
    widenedTypes = sorted(widenedTypes);
    narrowedTypes = sorted(narrowedTypes);
    changedTypesOther = sorted(changedTypesOther);
  }

  private static List<String> sorted(List<String> values) {
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    TreeSet<String> sorted = new TreeSet<>();
    for (String value : values) {
      if (value != null) {
        sorted.add(value);
      }
    }
    return List.copyOf(sorted);
  }
}


FILE: SchemaCompatibilityRules.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.schemas.manager;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.TreeSet;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.schemas.SchemaCompatibility;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class SchemaCompatibilityRules {
  private SchemaCompatibilityRules() {}

  public static void requireCompatible(
      String contextLabel,
      SchemaCompatibility mode,
      TabularSchemaView previous,
      TabularSchemaView next) {
    String context = Strings.requireNonBlank(contextLabel, "contextLabel");
    SchemaCompatibility resolvedMode = mode == null ? SchemaCompatibility.BACKWARDS : mode;
    Objects.requireNonNull(previous, "previous");
    Objects.requireNonNull(next, "next");
    if (resolvedMode == SchemaCompatibility.NONE) {
      return;
    }

    Map<String, TabularField> previousByName = previous.fieldsByName();
    Map<String, TabularField> nextByName = next.fieldsByName();
    SchemaCompatibilityResult diff = diff(previousByName, nextByName);
    List<String> reasons = violations(resolvedMode, diff, nextByName);
    if (!reasons.isEmpty()) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(
          "Schema compatibility violation context="
              + context
              + " mode="
              + resolvedMode
              + " diff="
              + diffSummary(diff)
              + " reasons="
              + reasons);
    }
  }

  private static SchemaCompatibilityResult diff(
      Map<String, TabularField> previousByName,
      Map<String, TabularField> nextByName) {
    TreeSet<String> addedFields = new TreeSet<>();
    TreeSet<String> removedFields = new TreeSet<>();
    TreeSet<String> madeNullable = new TreeSet<>();
    TreeSet<String> madeNonNullable = new TreeSet<>();
    TreeSet<String> widenedTypes = new TreeSet<>();
    TreeSet<String> narrowedTypes = new TreeSet<>();
    TreeSet<String> changedTypesOther = new TreeSet<>();

    for (Map.Entry<String, TabularField> previousEntry : previousByName.entrySet()) {
      String fieldName = previousEntry.getKey();
      TabularField previousField = previousEntry.getValue();
      TabularField nextField = nextByName.get(fieldName);
      if (nextField == null) {
        removedFields.add(fieldName);
        continue;
      }
      if (previousField.nullable() && !nextField.nullable()) {
        madeNonNullable.add(fieldName);
      }
      if (!previousField.nullable() && nextField.nullable()) {
        madeNullable.add(fieldName);
      }
      if (previousField.type() != nextField.type()) {
        String typeChange = fieldName + ":" + previousField.type() + "->" + nextField.type();
        if (isSafeWiden(previousField.type(), nextField.type())) {
          widenedTypes.add(typeChange);
        } else if (isSafeWiden(nextField.type(), previousField.type())) {
          narrowedTypes.add(typeChange);
        } else {
          changedTypesOther.add(typeChange);
        }
      }
    }
    for (String fieldName : nextByName.keySet()) {
      if (!previousByName.containsKey(fieldName)) {
        addedFields.add(fieldName);
      }
    }
    return new SchemaCompatibilityResult(
        true,
        List.copyOf(addedFields),
        List.copyOf(removedFields),
        List.copyOf(madeNullable),
        List.copyOf(madeNonNullable),
        List.copyOf(widenedTypes),
        List.copyOf(narrowedTypes),
        List.copyOf(changedTypesOther));
  }

  private static List<String> violations(
      SchemaCompatibility mode,
      SchemaCompatibilityResult diff,
      Map<String, TabularField> nextByName) {
    return switch (mode) {
      case BACKWARDS -> backwardsViolations(diff, nextByName);
      case FORWARD -> forwardViolations(diff, nextByName);
      case FULL -> fullViolations(diff, nextByName);
      case NONE -> List.of();
    };
  }

  private static List<String> backwardsViolations(
      SchemaCompatibilityResult diff, Map<String, TabularField> nextByName) {
    List<String> reasons = new ArrayList<>();
    addNonNullableAdditionReason(reasons, diff.addedFields(), nextByName);
    addReason(reasons, "removedFields", diff.removedFields());
    addReason(reasons, "nullableToNonNullable", diff.madeNonNullable());
    addReason(reasons, "narrowedTypes", diff.narrowedTypes());
    addReason(reasons, "changedTypes", diff.changedTypesOther());
    return List.copyOf(reasons);
  }

  private static List<String> forwardViolations(
      SchemaCompatibilityResult diff, Map<String, TabularField> nextByName) {
    List<String> reasons = new ArrayList<>();
    addNonNullableAdditionReason(reasons, diff.addedFields(), nextByName);
    addReason(reasons, "nullableToNonNullable", diff.madeNonNullable());
    TreeSet<String> changedTypes = new TreeSet<>();
    changedTypes.addAll(diff.widenedTypes());
    changedTypes.addAll(diff.narrowedTypes());
    changedTypes.addAll(diff.changedTypesOther());
    addReason(reasons, "changedTypes", List.copyOf(changedTypes));
    return List.copyOf(reasons);
  }

  private static List<String> fullViolations(
      SchemaCompatibilityResult diff, Map<String, TabularField> nextByName) {
    LinkedHashSet<String> merged = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    merged.addAll(backwardsViolations(diff, nextByName));
    merged.addAll(forwardViolations(diff, nextByName));
    return List.copyOf(merged);
  }

  private static void addNonNullableAdditionReason(
      List<String> reasons, List<String> addedFields, Map<String, TabularField> nextByName) {
    if (addedFields == null || addedFields.isEmpty()) {
      return;
    }
    TreeSet<String> nonNullableAdded = new TreeSet<>();
    for (String fieldName : addedFields) {
      TabularField field = nextByName.get(fieldName);
      if (field != null && !field.nullable()) {
        nonNullableAdded.add(fieldName);
      }
    }
    if (!nonNullableAdded.isEmpty()) {
      reasons.add("addedNonNullable=" + List.copyOf(nonNullableAdded));
    }
  }

  private static void addReason(List<String> reasons, String token, List<String> values) {
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      return;
    }
    TreeSet<String> sorted = new TreeSet<>();
    for (String value : values) {
      if (value != null) {
        sorted.add(value);
      }
    }
    if (!sorted.isEmpty()) {
      reasons.add(token + "=" + List.copyOf(sorted));
    }
  }

  private static boolean isSafeWiden(SchemaPrimitiveType previous, SchemaPrimitiveType next) {
    if (previous == null || next == null || previous == next) {
      return false;
    }
    return switch (previous) {
      case INT32 -> next == SchemaPrimitiveType.INT64 || next == SchemaPrimitiveType.FLOAT64;
      case INT64 -> next == SchemaPrimitiveType.FLOAT64;
      case DATE -> next == SchemaPrimitiveType.TIMESTAMP;
      default -> false;
    };
  }

  private static String diffSummary(SchemaCompatibilityResult diff) {
    return "{addedFields="
        + diff.addedFields()
        + ", removedFields="
        + diff.removedFields()
        + ", typeChanges={widened="
        + diff.widenedTypes()
        + ", narrowed="
        + diff.narrowedTypes()
        + ", changed="
        + diff.changedTypesOther()
        + "}, nullabilityChanges={madeNullable="
        + diff.madeNullable()
        + ", madeNonNullable="
        + diff.madeNonNullable()
        + "}}";
  }
}


FILE: SchemaManagerImplDefinition.java

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.schemas.manager;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.regex.Pattern;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.cache.DiscoveryCache;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionSchema;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.schemas.SchemaModel;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

final class SchemaManagerImplDefinition {

  private SchemaManagerImplDefinition() {}

  static List<SchemaModel> mapSchemas(List<DefinitionSchema> definitions) {
    if (definitions == null || definitions.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<SchemaModel> models = new ArrayList<>();
    for (DefinitionSchema definition : definitions) {
      SchemaModel model = SchemaModelMapper.fromDefinition(definition);
      if (model != null) {
        models.add(model);
      }
    }
    return List.copyOf(models);
  }

  static List<SchemaModel> sortSchemas(List<SchemaModel> schemas, Comparator<SchemaModel> schemaOrder) {
    if (schemas == null || schemas.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<SchemaModel> sorted = new ArrayList<>();
    for (SchemaModel schema : schemas) {
      if (schema != null) {
        sorted.add(schema);
      }
    }
    sorted.sort(schemaOrder);
    return List.copyOf(sorted);
  }

  static String schemaName(SchemaModel schema) {
    return Strings.firstNonBlank(schema == null ? null : schema.getName(), "");
  }

  static String schemaTypeName(SchemaModel schema) {
    return schema == null || schema.getType() == null ? "" : schema.getType().name();
  }

  static List<SchemaModel> filterCanonicalSchemas(
      List<SchemaModel> schemas, Pattern versionSuffixPattern) {
    if (schemas == null || schemas.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<SchemaModel> canonical = new ArrayList<>();
    for (SchemaModel schema : schemas) {
      if (schema == null || isVersionedSchemaName(schema.getName(), versionSuffixPattern)) {
        continue;
      }
      canonical.add(schema);
    }
    return List.copyOf(canonical);
  }

  static String nextVersionedSchemaName(
      DiscoveryCache cache, String group, String canonicalName, String versionSeparator) {
    int max = 0;
    String prefix = canonicalName + versionSeparator;
    for (DefinitionSchema candidate : cache.listSchemas(group)) {
      if (candidate == null || candidate.envelope() == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String candidateName = Strings.trimToNull(candidate.envelope().name());
      if (candidateName == null || !candidateName.startsWith(prefix)) {
        continue;
      }
      Integer version = parseVersionSuffix(candidateName, canonicalName, versionSeparator);
      if (version != null && version > max) {
        max = version;
      }
    }
    return canonicalName + versionSeparator + String.format(Locale.ROOT, "%04d", max + 1);
  }

  static boolean matchesVersionFamily(
      String canonicalName, String candidateName, String versionSeparator) {
    if (canonicalName == null || candidateName == null) {
      return false;
    }
    if (canonicalName.equals(candidateName)) {
      return true;
    }
    return parseVersionSuffix(candidateName, canonicalName, versionSeparator) != null;
  }

  static int normalizedVersionNum(Integer versionNum) {
    return versionNum == null || versionNum <= 0 ? 1 : versionNum;
  }

  static String versionName(int versionNum) {
    return "v" + String.format(Locale.ROOT, "%04d", Math.max(1, versionNum));
  }

  static Integer parseVersionToken(String token, String versionSeparator) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(token);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return null;
    }
    if (normalized.startsWith(versionSeparator)) {
      normalized = normalized.substring(versionSeparator.length());
    } else if (normalized.startsWith("v") || normalized.startsWith("V")) {
      normalized = normalized.substring(1);
    }
    if (normalized.isEmpty()) {
      return null;
    }
    for (int index = 0; index < normalized.length(); index++) {
      if (!Character.isDigit(normalized.charAt(index))) {
        return null;
      }
    }
    try {
      return Integer.parseInt(normalized);
    } catch (NumberFormatException ex) {
      return null;
    }
  }

  static Integer parseVersionSuffix(String value, String canonicalName, String versionSeparator) {
    String token = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (token == null || canonicalName == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String prefix = canonicalName + versionSeparator;
    if (!token.startsWith(prefix) || token.length() != prefix.length() + 4) {
      return null;
    }
    String suffix = token.substring(prefix.length());
    for (int i = 0; i < suffix.length(); i++) {
      if (!Character.isDigit(suffix.charAt(i))) {
        return null;
      }
    }
    return Integer.parseInt(suffix);
  }

  static boolean isVersionedSchemaName(String name, Pattern versionSuffixPattern) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(name);
    return normalized != null && versionSuffixPattern.matcher(normalized).matches();
  }
}


FILE: SchemaModelMapper.java

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.schemas.manager;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonNode;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.SerializationFeature;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.node.ArrayNode;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.node.ObjectNode;
import java.nio.charset.StandardCharsets;
import java.security.MessageDigest;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.codec.DiscoveryCodec;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionEnvelope;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionSchema;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionType;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.schemas.SchemaCompatibility;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.schemas.SchemaModel;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.schemas.SchemaType;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.DefinitionModelMapperSupport;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class SchemaModelMapper {
  private static final String ARTIFACT_TYPE = "DESCRIPTOR";
  private static final String STATUS_ACTIVE = "ACTIVE";
  private static final String SCHEMA_FORMAT_TABULAR = "FLOW_TABULAR_V1";
  private static final String SCHEMA_FORMAT_TRANSPORT = "FLOW_TRANSPORT_V1";
  private static final String SCHEMA_FORMAT_MAPPING = "FLOW_MAPPING_V1";
  private static final String SCHEMA_FORMAT_METASET = "FLOW_METASET_V1";
  private static final ObjectMapper CANONICAL_MAPPER =
      DiscoveryCodec.mapper().copy().configure(SerializationFeature.ORDER_MAP_ENTRIES_BY_KEYS, true);

  private SchemaModelMapper() {}

  public static DefinitionSchema toDefinition(
      SchemaModel model,
      String nowIso,
      String systemUser) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(model, "model");
    String now = DefinitionModelMapperSupport.requireNonBlank(nowIso, "nowIso");
    String actor = DefinitionModelMapperSupport.requireNonBlank(systemUser, "systemUser");
    String canonicalSchemaJson = canonicalSchemaJson(model.getFields());
    String normalizedGroup =
        DefinitionModelMapperSupport.requireNonBlank(model.getGroup(), "model.group");
    String normalizedName =
        DefinitionModelMapperSupport.requireNonBlank(model.getName(), "model.name");
    String lifecycleStatus =
        DefinitionModelMapperSupport.requireNonBlank(
            model.getLifecycleStatus(), "model.lifecycleStatus");
    boolean enabled = !Boolean.FALSE.equals(model.getEnabled());
    SchemaType schemaType = Objects.requireNonNull(model.getType(), "model.type");

    return new DefinitionSchema(
        DefinitionModelMapperSupport.envelopeAt(
            normalizedGroup,
            DefinitionType.SCHEMA,
            normalizedName,
            DefinitionModelMapperSupport.buildDefinitionId(
                "schema", normalizedGroup, normalizedName),
            enabled,
            lifecycleStatus,
            actor,
            now),
        model.getVersionName(),
        model.getVersionNum(),
        ARTIFACT_TYPE,
        Strings.firstNonBlank(model.getSchemaFormat(), schemaFormat(schemaType)),
        canonicalSchemaJson,
        STATUS_ACTIVE,
        toDefinitionCompatibility(model.getCompatibility()),
        List.of(),
        List.of(),
        sha256Hex(canonicalSchemaJson),
        now,
        null,
        toDefinitionType(schemaType),
        null,
        null,
        null);
  }

  public static SchemaModel fromDefinition(DefinitionSchema def) {
    if (def == null) {
      return null;
    }
    DefinitionEnvelope envelope = def.envelope();
    List<SchemaModel.Field> fields = fieldsFromSchemaJson(def.schema());
    return SchemaModel.builder()
        .withGroup(envelope == null ? null : envelope.group())
        .withName(envelope == null ? null : envelope.name())
        .withType(fromDefinitionType(def.schemaType(), def.format()))
        .withFields(fields)
        .withSchemaFormat(def.format())
        .withHash(def.hash())
        .withVersionNum(def.versionNum())
        .withVersionName(def.versionSemantic())
        .withCompatibility(fromDefinitionCompatibility(def.compatibility()))
        .withEnabled(envelope == null ? null : envelope.enabled())
        .withLifecycleStatus(envelope == null ? null : envelope.lifecycleStatus())
        .build();
  }

  public static DefinitionSchema toVersionedDefinition(
      DefinitionSchema canonical, String versionedName) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(canonical, "canonical");
    DefinitionEnvelope envelope = canonical.envelope();
    String group = Strings.requireNonBlank(envelope == null ? null : envelope.group(), "group");
    String sourceName = Strings.requireNonBlank(envelope == null ? null : envelope.name(), "schemaName");
    String resolvedVersionedName = Strings.requireNonBlank(versionedName, "versionedName");
    String uuid = "schema:" + group + "/" + sourceName + "->" + resolvedVersionedName;
    DefinitionEnvelope versionedEnvelope =
        new DefinitionEnvelope(
            group,
            DefinitionType.SCHEMA,
            resolvedVersionedName,
            uuid,
            envelope.enabled(),
            envelope.lifecycleStatus(),
            envelope.createdTimeUtc(),
            envelope.createdBy(),
            envelope.updatedTimeUtc(),
            envelope.updatedBy());
    return new DefinitionSchema(
        versionedEnvelope,
        canonical.versionSemantic(),
        canonical.versionNum(),
        canonical.artifactType(),
        canonical.format(),
        canonical.schema(),
        canonical.status(),
        canonical.compatibility(),
        canonical.refs(),
        canonical.tags(),
        canonical.hash(),
        canonical.createdTimeUtc(),
        canonical.schemaUsage(),
        canonical.schemaType(),
        canonical.doc(),
        canonical.usageGroup(),
        canonical.semantic());
  }

  public static DefinitionSchema.SchemaType toDefinitionType(SchemaType type) {
    SchemaType normalized = Objects.requireNonNull(type, "schemaType");
    return switch (normalized) {
      case TABULAR -> DefinitionSchema.SchemaType.TABULAR;
      case TRANSPORT -> DefinitionSchema.SchemaType.TRANSPORT;
      case MAPPING -> DefinitionSchema.SchemaType.MAPPING;
      case METASET -> DefinitionSchema.SchemaType.CONFIG;
    };
  }

  private static SchemaType fromDefinitionType(DefinitionSchema.SchemaType type, String format) {
    if (type != null) {
      return switch (type) {
        case TABULAR -> SchemaType.TABULAR;
        case TRANSPORT -> SchemaType.TRANSPORT;
        case MAPPING -> SchemaType.MAPPING;
        case CONFIG -> SchemaType.METASET;
        case UNKNOWN -> throw new IllegalArgumentException("Unsupported schema type UNKNOWN");
      };
    }
    String normalizedFormat = Strings.trimToNull(format);
    if (normalizedFormat == null) {
      return SchemaType.TABULAR;
    }
    return switch (normalizedFormat.toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT)) {
      case SCHEMA_FORMAT_TRANSPORT -> SchemaType.TRANSPORT;
      case SCHEMA_FORMAT_MAPPING -> SchemaType.MAPPING;
      case SCHEMA_FORMAT_METASET -> SchemaType.METASET;
      default -> SchemaType.TABULAR;
    };
  }

  private static String canonicalSchemaJson(List<SchemaModel.Field> fields) {
    if (fields == null || fields.isEmpty()) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("schema requires at least one field");
    }
    ObjectNode root = CANONICAL_MAPPER.createObjectNode();
    ArrayNode fieldNodes = root.putArray("fields");
    for (SchemaModel.Field field : fields) {
      if (field == null) {
        continue;
      }
      ObjectNode node = fieldNodes.addObject();
      node.put("name", field.getName());
      node.put("type", field.getType().token());
      node.put("nullable", field.isNullable());
      if (Strings.isNotBlank(field.getDescription())) {
        node.put("description", field.getDescription());
      }
    }
    try {
      return CANONICAL_MAPPER.writeValueAsString(root);
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Failed to render schema JSON", ex);
    }
  }

  private static List<SchemaModel.Field> fieldsFromSchemaJson(String schemaJson) {
    String payload = Strings.requireNonBlank(schemaJson, "schema.schema");
    try {
      JsonNode root = CANONICAL_MAPPER.readTree(payload);
      JsonNode fieldsNode = root.path("fields");
      if (!fieldsNode.isArray()) {
        fieldsNode = root.path("columns");
      }
      if (!fieldsNode.isArray() || fieldsNode.isEmpty()) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("schema JSON must contain fields");
      }
      List<SchemaModel.Field> fields = new ArrayList<>();
      for (JsonNode fieldNode : fieldsNode) {
        String name = Strings.trimToNull(fieldNode.path("name").asText(null));
        if (name == null) {
          throw new IllegalArgumentException("schema JSON field name is required");
        }
        String typeToken = Strings.trimToNull(fieldNode.path("type").asText(null));
        if (typeToken == null) {
          throw new IllegalArgumentException("schema JSON field type is required for " + name);
        }
        fields.add(
            SchemaModel.Field.builder()
                .withName(name)
                .withType(SchemaModel.FieldType.fromToken(typeToken))
                .withNullable(fieldNode.path("nullable").asBoolean(true))
                .withDescription(Strings.trimToNull(fieldNode.path("description").asText(null)))
                .build());
      }
      return List.copyOf(fields);
    } catch (RuntimeException ex) {
      throw ex;
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("schema JSON must be valid JSON", ex);
    }
  }

  private static String sha256Hex(String value) {
    try {
      MessageDigest digest = MessageDigest.getInstance("SHA-256");
      byte[] hash = digest.digest((value == null ? "" : value).getBytes(StandardCharsets.UTF_8));
      StringBuilder builder = new StringBuilder(hash.length * 2);
      for (byte b : hash) {
        builder.append(String.format(Locale.ROOT, "%02x", b & 0xff));
      }
      return builder.toString();
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Failed to compute schema hash", ex);
    }
  }

  private static String schemaFormat(SchemaType schemaType) {
    return switch (schemaType) {
      case TABULAR -> SCHEMA_FORMAT_TABULAR;
      case TRANSPORT -> SCHEMA_FORMAT_TRANSPORT;
      case MAPPING -> SCHEMA_FORMAT_MAPPING;
      case METASET -> SCHEMA_FORMAT_METASET;
    };
  }

  private static DefinitionSchema.Compatibility toDefinitionCompatibility(SchemaCompatibility value) {
    SchemaCompatibility normalized = value == null ? SchemaCompatibility.BACKWARDS : value;
    return switch (normalized) {
      case BACKWARDS -> DefinitionSchema.Compatibility.BACKWARDS;
      case FORWARD -> DefinitionSchema.Compatibility.FORWARD;
      case FULL -> DefinitionSchema.Compatibility.FULL;
      case NONE -> DefinitionSchema.Compatibility.NONE;
    };
  }

  private static SchemaCompatibility fromDefinitionCompatibility(DefinitionSchema.Compatibility value) {
    if (value == null) {
      return SchemaCompatibility.BACKWARDS;
    }
    return switch (value) {
      case BACKWARDS -> SchemaCompatibility.BACKWARDS;
      case FORWARD -> SchemaCompatibility.FORWARD;
      case FULL -> SchemaCompatibility.FULL;
      case NONE -> SchemaCompatibility.NONE;
      case UNKNOWN ->
          throw new IllegalArgumentException("Unsupported schema compatibility UNKNOWN");
    };
  }
}

FILE: SchemaViews.java

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.schemas.manager;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.schemas.SchemaModel;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class SchemaViews {
  private SchemaViews() {}

  public static TabularSchemaView fromSchemaModel(SchemaModel model) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(model, "model");
    List<TabularField> fields = new ArrayList<>();
    for (SchemaModel.Field field : model.getFields()) {
      if (field == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String name = Strings.requireNonBlank(field.getName(), "field.name");
      fields.add(new TabularField(name, fromSchemaType(field.getType()), field.isNullable()));
    }
    return new TabularSchemaView(validate(fields));
  }

  private static List<TabularField> validate(List<TabularField> fields) {
    if (fields == null || fields.isEmpty()) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("schema requires at least one field");
    }
    LinkedHashSet<String> names = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    for (TabularField field : fields) {
      if (field == null) {
        continue;
      }
      if (!names.add(field.name())) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("Duplicate field name: " + field.name());
      }
    }
    return List.copyOf(fields);
  }

  private static SchemaPrimitiveType fromSchemaType(SchemaModel.FieldType value) {
    SchemaModel.FieldType type = Objects.requireNonNull(value, "field.type");
    return switch (type) {
      case BOOL -> SchemaPrimitiveType.BOOL;
      case INT32 -> SchemaPrimitiveType.INT32;
      case INT64 -> SchemaPrimitiveType.INT64;
      case FLOAT64 -> SchemaPrimitiveType.FLOAT64;
      case STRING -> SchemaPrimitiveType.STRING;
      case DATE -> SchemaPrimitiveType.DATE;
      case TIMESTAMP -> SchemaPrimitiveType.TIMESTAMP;
      case BINARY -> SchemaPrimitiveType.BINARY;
    };
  }

}

FILE: TabularSchemaView.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.schemas.manager;

import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;

public record TabularSchemaView(List<TabularField> fields) {
  public TabularSchemaView {
    fields = fields == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(fields);
  }

  public Map<String, TabularField> fieldsByName() {
    Map<String, TabularField> byName = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (TabularField field : fields) {
      if (field == null || field.name() == null) {
        continue;
      }
      if (byName.putIfAbsent(field.name(), field) != null) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("Duplicate field name: " + field.name());
      }
    }
    return Map.copyOf(byName);
  }
}

FILE: HashCallerAppRoutingStrategy.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.common.routing;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.List;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.status.service.ServiceHbCache;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.common.ServiceAdvertise;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

public final class HashCallerAppRoutingStrategy implements ServiceRoutingStrategy {
  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(HashCallerAppRoutingStrategy.class);
  private static final Comparator<ServiceHbCache.Target> TARGET_ORDER =
      Comparator.comparing(PickFirstRoutingStrategy::targetKey);
  private final RoundRobinRoutingStrategy roundRobinFallback = new RoundRobinRoutingStrategy();

  @Override
  public ServiceHbCache.Target select(
      List<ServiceHbCache.Target> targets,
      String serviceId,
      ServiceRoutingContext context,
      ServiceRoutingState state) {
    String callerAppSubject = context == null ? null : Strings.trimToNull(context.callerAppSubject());
    if (callerAppSubject == null) {
      ServiceHbCache.Target fallback = roundRobinFallback.select(targets, serviceId, context, state);
      if (LOGGER.isDebugEnabled()) {
        LOGGER.debug(
            "[ServiceRouting][HASH_CALLER_APP][fallback] serviceId={} reason=missing-caller-app fallbackInstance={}",
            serviceId,
            fallback.instanceId);
      }
      return fallback;
    }
    List<ServiceHbCache.Target> ordered = orderedTargets(targets);
    int start = Math.floorMod(callerAppSubject.hashCode(), ordered.size());
    for (int i = 0; i < ordered.size(); i++) {
      int index = Math.floorMod(start + i, ordered.size());
      ServiceHbCache.Target candidate = ordered.get(index);
      if (isUsable(candidate)) {
        if (LOGGER.isDebugEnabled()) {
          LOGGER.debug(
              "[ServiceRouting][HASH_CALLER_APP] serviceId={} callerApp={} selectedIndex={} fallbackStep={} instance={}",
              serviceId,
              callerAppSubject,
              index,
              i,
              candidate.instanceId);
        }
        return candidate;
      }
    }
    return ordered.get(start);
  }

  private static List<ServiceHbCache.Target> orderedTargets(List<ServiceHbCache.Target> targets) {
    List<ServiceHbCache.Target> ordered = new ArrayList<>(targets);
    ordered.sort(TARGET_ORDER);
    return ordered;
  }

  private static boolean isUsable(ServiceHbCache.Target target) {
    if (target == null || target.port <= 0) {
      return false;
    }
    try {
      ServiceAdvertise.requireRoutableHost(target.host, "grpc target host");
      return true;
    } catch (RuntimeException ex) {
      return false;
    }
  }
}

FILE: PickFirstRoutingStrategy.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.common.routing;

import java.util.List;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.status.service.ServiceHbCache;

public final class PickFirstRoutingStrategy implements ServiceRoutingStrategy {
  @Override
  public ServiceHbCache.Target select(
      List<ServiceHbCache.Target> targets,
      String serviceId,
      ServiceRoutingContext context,
      ServiceRoutingState state) {
    ServiceRoutingState resolved = state == null ? new ServiceRoutingState() : state;
    String stickyKey = resolved.stickyTargetKey();
    if (stickyKey != null) {
      for (ServiceHbCache.Target candidate : targets) {
        if (stickyKey.equals(targetKey(candidate))) {
          return candidate;
        }
      }
    }
    int index = resolved.nextPickFirstIndex(targets.size());
    ServiceHbCache.Target selected = targets.get(index);
    resolved.stickyTargetKey(targetKey(selected));
    return selected;
  }

  static String targetKey(ServiceHbCache.Target target) {
    if (target == null) {
      return "";
    }
    String instanceId = target.instanceId == null ? "" : target.instanceId;
    String host = target.host == null ? "" : target.host;
    String authority = target.authorityOverride == null ? "" : target.authorityOverride;
    return instanceId + "|" + host + ":" + target.port + "|" + target.tls + "|" + authority;
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.common.routing;

import java.util.List;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.status.service.ServiceHbCache;

public final class RoundRobinRoutingStrategy implements ServiceRoutingStrategy {
  @Override
  public ServiceHbCache.Target select(
      List<ServiceHbCache.Target> targets,
      String serviceId,
      ServiceRoutingContext context,
      ServiceRoutingState state) {
    ServiceRoutingState resolved = state == null ? new ServiceRoutingState() : state;
    int index = resolved.nextRoundRobinIndex(targets.size());
    return targets.get(index);
  }
}

FILE: ServiceRoutingMode.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.common.routing;

import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionService;

public enum ServiceRoutingMode {
  ROUND_ROBIN,
  PICK_FIRST,
  HASH_SUBJECT,
  HASH_CALLER_APP,
  HASH_KEY;

  public static ServiceRoutingMode requireSupported(
      DefinitionService.RoutingMode rawMode, String serviceId, String fieldPath, String usage) {
    if (rawMode == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(
          "Invalid routing configuration for serviceId="
              + serviceId
              + ": missing field "
              + fieldPath
              + " (required for "
              + usage
              + ")");
    }
    return switch (rawMode) {
      case ROUND_ROBIN -> ROUND_ROBIN;
      case PICK_FIRST -> PICK_FIRST;
      case HASH_SUBJECT -> HASH_SUBJECT;
      case HASH_CALLER_APP -> HASH_CALLER_APP;
      case HASH_KEY -> HASH_KEY;
      case UNKNOWN ->
          throw new IllegalArgumentException(
              "Invalid routing configuration for serviceId="
                  + serviceId
                  + ": unsupported value UNKNOWN for "
                  + fieldPath
                  + " (required for "
                  + usage
                  + ")");
    };
  }
}


FILE: ServiceRoutingState.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.common.routing;

import java.util.concurrent.atomic.AtomicInteger;

public final class ServiceRoutingState {
  private final AtomicInteger roundRobinCounter = new AtomicInteger(-1);
  private final AtomicInteger pickFirstCounter = new AtomicInteger(seed());
  private volatile String stickyTargetKey;

  public int nextRoundRobinIndex(int size) {
    if (size <= 0) {
      return -1;
    }
    return Math.floorMod(roundRobinCounter.incrementAndGet(), size);
  }

  public int nextPickFirstIndex(int size) {
    if (size <= 0) {
      return -1;
    }
    return Math.floorMod(pickFirstCounter.getAndIncrement(), size);
  }

  public String stickyTargetKey() {
    return stickyTargetKey;
  }

  public void stickyTargetKey(String value) {
    stickyTargetKey = value;
  }

  private static int seed() {
    return (int) (System.nanoTime() & Integer.MAX_VALUE);
  }
}


FILE: ServiceRoutingStrategies.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.common.routing;

import java.util.EnumMap;
import java.util.Map;

public final class ServiceRoutingStrategies {
  private static final Map<ServiceRoutingMode, ServiceRoutingStrategy> STRATEGIES =
      buildStrategies();

  private ServiceRoutingStrategies() {}

  public static ServiceRoutingStrategy strategyFor(ServiceRoutingMode mode) {
    ServiceRoutingMode resolved = mode == null ? ServiceRoutingMode.ROUND_ROBIN : mode;
    ServiceRoutingStrategy strategy = STRATEGIES.get(resolved);
    if (strategy == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("No routing strategy registered for mode " + resolved);
    }
    return strategy;
  }

  private static Map<ServiceRoutingMode, ServiceRoutingStrategy> buildStrategies() {
    EnumMap<ServiceRoutingMode, ServiceRoutingStrategy> strategies =
        new EnumMap<>(ServiceRoutingMode.class);
    strategies.put(ServiceRoutingMode.ROUND_ROBIN, new RoundRobinRoutingStrategy());
    strategies.put(ServiceRoutingMode.PICK_FIRST, new PickFirstRoutingStrategy());
    strategies.put(ServiceRoutingMode.HASH_SUBJECT, new HashSubjectRoutingStrategy());
    strategies.put(ServiceRoutingMode.HASH_CALLER_APP, new HashCallerAppRoutingStrategy());
    strategies.put(ServiceRoutingMode.HASH_KEY, new HashKeyRoutingStrategy());
    return Map.copyOf(strategies);
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.flight;

import io.grpc.ManagedChannel;
import java.io.File;
import java.nio.file.Path;
import java.util.List;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.kerberos.KerberosSpn;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.ServiceRunOptions;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.grpc.GrpcClientRuntime;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class FlightClientChannelSupport {
  private FlightClientChannelSupport() {}

  public static ManagedChannel createChannel(
      String host,
      int port,
      boolean tlsEnabled,
      boolean kerberosEnabled,
      String kerberosSpn,
      ServiceRunOptions options,
      String sessionKerberosPrincipal,
      Path sessionKerberosKeytab)
      throws Exception {
    ServiceRunOptions resolvedOptions = options == null ? ServiceRunOptions.defaults() : options;
    GrpcClientRuntime.Config cfg = new GrpcClientRuntime.Config();
    cfg.host = Strings.requireNonBlank(host, "arrow target host");
    cfg.port = port;
    cfg.tlsEnabled = tlsEnabled;
    cfg.trustCertPem =
        toFile(
            resolvedOptions.tlsTrustCert() == null
                ? resolvedOptions.clientTrustCert()
                : resolvedOptions.tlsTrustCert());
    cfg.kerberosEnabled = kerberosEnabled;
    cfg.kerberosRequireTls = true;
    cfg.kerberosSpn = Strings.trimToNull(kerberosSpn);
    cfg.kerberosPrincipal = Strings.trimToNull(sessionKerberosPrincipal);
    cfg.kerberosKeytab = sessionKerberosKeytab == null ? null : sessionKerberosKeytab.toFile();
    cfg.kerberosRealm = KerberosSpn.extractRealm(cfg.kerberosPrincipal);
    return GrpcClientRuntime.createChannel(cfg, List.of());
  }

  private static File toFile(Path path) {
    return path == null ? null : path.toFile();
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.flight;

import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.dataset.DatasetId;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class FlightDatasetStreamTicket {
  public enum Start {
    BEGINNING,
    LATEST,
    RESUME,
    FROM_SEQUENCE
  }

  private static final int DEFAULT_BATCH_MAX_ROWS = 256;
  private static final int DEFAULT_FLUSH_MILLIS = 250;

  private final DatasetId datasetId;
  private final Start start;
  private final long fromSequence;
  private final int batchMaxRows;
  private final int flushMillis;
  private final String subscriptionId;
  private final String filterSql;
  private final String accessMode;

  private FlightDatasetStreamTicket(Builder builder) {
    this.datasetId = builder.datasetId;
    this.start = builder.start;
    this.fromSequence = builder.fromSequence;
    this.batchMaxRows = builder.batchMaxRows;
    this.flushMillis = builder.flushMillis;
    this.subscriptionId = builder.subscriptionId;
    this.filterSql = builder.filterSql;
    this.accessMode = builder.accessMode;
  }

  public static Builder builder() {
    return new Builder();
  }

  public DatasetId datasetId() {
    return datasetId;
  }

  public Start start() {
    return start;
  }

  public long fromSequence() {
    return fromSequence;
  }

  public int batchMaxRows() {
    return batchMaxRows;
  }

  public int flushMillis() {
    return flushMillis;
  }

  public String subscriptionId() {
    return subscriptionId;
  }

  public String filterSql() {
    return filterSql;
  }

  public String accessMode() {
    return accessMode;
  }

  public static final class Builder {
    private DatasetId datasetId;
    private Start start = Start.LATEST;
    private long fromSequence = 0L;
    private int batchMaxRows = DEFAULT_BATCH_MAX_ROWS;
    private int flushMillis = DEFAULT_FLUSH_MILLIS;
    private String subscriptionId;
    private String filterSql;
    private String accessMode;

    private Builder() {}

    public Builder withDatasetId(DatasetId value) {
      this.datasetId = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withStart(Start value) {
      this.start = value == null ? Start.LATEST : value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withFromSequence(long value) {
      this.fromSequence = value;
      this.start = Start.FROM_SEQUENCE;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withBatchMaxRows(int value) {
      this.batchMaxRows = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withFlushMillis(int value) {
      this.flushMillis = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withSubscriptionId(String value) {
      String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      this.subscriptionId = normalized;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withFilterSql(String value) {
      this.filterSql = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withAccessMode(String value) {
      String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      if (normalized == null) {
        this.accessMode = null;
      } else if ("PUBLIC".equalsIgnoreCase(normalized)) {
        this.accessMode = "PUBLIC";
      } else if ("PRIVATE".equalsIgnoreCase(normalized)) {
        this.accessMode = "PRIVATE";
      } else {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("accessMode must be PUBLIC or PRIVATE");
      }
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withPublic(boolean value) {
      return withAccessMode(value ? "PUBLIC" : "PRIVATE");
    }

    public FlightDatasetStreamTicket build() {
      if (datasetId == null) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("datasetId is required");
      }
      if (start == Start.FROM_SEQUENCE && fromSequence < 0L) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("fromSequence must be >= 0");
      }
      if (batchMaxRows <= 0) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("batchMaxRows must be > 0");
      }
      if (flushMillis <= 0) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("flushMillis must be > 0");
      }
      String normalizedSubscription = Strings.trimToNull(subscriptionId);
      this.subscriptionId =
          normalizedSubscription == null
              ? deterministicSubscriptionId(datasetId)
              : normalizedSubscription;
      return new FlightDatasetStreamTicket(this);
    }

    private static String deterministicSubscriptionId(DatasetId datasetId) {
      String token = datasetId.toString().replace(':', '_').replace('/', '_');
      return "stream_" + token;
    }
  }
}


FILE: FlightDatasetStreamTicketCodec.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.flight;

import java.nio.charset.StandardCharsets;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.Map;
import org.apache.arrow.flight.Ticket;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.dataset.DatasetId;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class FlightDatasetStreamTicketCodec {
  private static final String PREFIX = "fabric.stream.v1;";
  private static final String KEY_DATASET_ID = "datasetId";
  private static final String KEY_START = "start";
  private static final String KEY_BATCH_MAX_ROWS = "batchMaxRows";
  private static final String KEY_FLUSH_MILLIS = "flushMillis";
  private static final String KEY_SUBSCRIPTION_ID = "subscriptionId";
  private static final String KEY_FILTER_SQL = "filterSql";
  private static final String KEY_ACCESS_MODE = "accessMode";

  private FlightDatasetStreamTicketCodec() {}

  public static Ticket encode(FlightDatasetStreamTicket ticket) {
    FlightDatasetStreamTicket resolved = ticket == null ? null : ticket;
    if (resolved == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("ticket is required");
    }
    StringBuilder builder = new StringBuilder(PREFIX.length() + 128);
    builder.append(PREFIX);
    builder.append(KEY_DATASET_ID).append('=').append(resolved.datasetId());
    builder.append(';');
    builder.append(KEY_START).append('=').append(encodeStart(resolved));
    builder.append(';');
    builder.append(KEY_BATCH_MAX_ROWS).append('=').append(resolved.batchMaxRows());
    builder.append(';');
    builder.append(KEY_FLUSH_MILLIS).append('=').append(resolved.flushMillis());
    builder
        .append(';')
        .append(KEY_SUBSCRIPTION_ID)
        .append('=')
        .append(resolved.subscriptionId());
    String filterSql = Strings.trimToNull(resolved.filterSql());
    if (filterSql != null) {
      builder.append(';').append(KEY_FILTER_SQL).append('=').append(filterSql);
    }
    String accessMode = Strings.trimToNull(resolved.accessMode());
    if (accessMode != null) {
      builder.append(';').append(KEY_ACCESS_MODE).append('=').append(accessMode);
    }
    return new Ticket(builder.toString().getBytes(StandardCharsets.UTF_8));
  }

  public static boolean isStreamTicket(Ticket ticket) {
    if (ticket == null || ticket.getBytes() == null || ticket.getBytes().length == 0) {
      return false;
    }
    byte[] bytes = ticket.getBytes();
    byte[] prefix = PREFIX.getBytes(StandardCharsets.UTF_8);
    if (bytes.length < prefix.length) {
      return false;
    }
    for (int i = 0; i < prefix.length; i++) {
      if (bytes[i] != prefix[i]) {
        return false;
      }
    }
    return true;
  }

  public static FlightDatasetStreamTicket decode(Ticket ticket) {
    if (!isStreamTicket(ticket)) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Ticket is not a stream ticket");
    }
    String payload = new String(ticket.getBytes(), StandardCharsets.UTF_8);
    String body = payload.substring(PREFIX.length());
    Map<String, String> kv = parseBody(body);

    String datasetIdRaw = kv.get(KEY_DATASET_ID);
    if (Strings.trimToNull(datasetIdRaw) == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("stream ticket datasetId is required");
    }
    DatasetId datasetId = DatasetId.parse(datasetIdRaw);

    String startRaw = Strings.trimToNull(kv.get(KEY_START));
    FlightDatasetStreamTicket.Builder builder =
        FlightDatasetStreamTicket.builder().withDatasetId(datasetId);
    if (startRaw != null) {
      if ("beginning".equalsIgnoreCase(startRaw)) {
        builder.withStart(FlightDatasetStreamTicket.Start.BEGINNING);
      } else if ("latest".equalsIgnoreCase(startRaw)) {
        builder.withStart(FlightDatasetStreamTicket.Start.LATEST);
      } else if ("resume".equalsIgnoreCase(startRaw)) {
        builder.withStart(FlightDatasetStreamTicket.Start.RESUME);
      } else {
        long seq;
        try {
          seq = Long.parseLong(startRaw);
        } catch (NumberFormatException ex) {
          throw new IllegalArgumentException(
              "stream ticket start must be 'beginning', 'latest', 'resume', or >= 0 sequence", ex);
        }
        if (seq < 0L) {
          throw new IllegalArgumentException("stream ticket sequence start must be >= 0");
        }
        builder.withFromSequence(seq);
      }
    }

    String batchMaxRowsRaw = Strings.trimToNull(kv.get(KEY_BATCH_MAX_ROWS));
    if (batchMaxRowsRaw != null) {
      builder.withBatchMaxRows(parsePositiveInt(batchMaxRowsRaw, KEY_BATCH_MAX_ROWS));
    }
    String flushMillisRaw = Strings.trimToNull(kv.get(KEY_FLUSH_MILLIS));
    if (flushMillisRaw != null) {
      builder.withFlushMillis(parsePositiveInt(flushMillisRaw, KEY_FLUSH_MILLIS));
    }
    builder.withSubscriptionId(kv.get(KEY_SUBSCRIPTION_ID));
    builder.withFilterSql(kv.get(KEY_FILTER_SQL));
    builder.withAccessMode(kv.get(KEY_ACCESS_MODE));
    return builder.build();
  }

  private static String encodeStart(FlightDatasetStreamTicket ticket) {
    if (ticket.start() == FlightDatasetStreamTicket.Start.BEGINNING) {
      return "beginning";
    }
    if (ticket.start() == FlightDatasetStreamTicket.Start.FROM_SEQUENCE) {
      return Long.toString(ticket.fromSequence());
    }
    if (ticket.start() == FlightDatasetStreamTicket.Start.RESUME) {
      return "resume";
    }
    return "latest";
  }

  private static int parsePositiveInt(String value, String label) {
    try {
      int parsed = Integer.parseInt(value);
      if (parsed <= 0) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException(label + " must be > 0");
      }
      return parsed;
    } catch (NumberFormatException ex) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(label + " must be a positive integer", ex);
    }
  }

  private static Map<String, String> parseBody(String body) {
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> kv = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    if (Strings.trimToNull(body) == null) {
      return kv;
    }
    String[] fields = body.split(";");
    for (String field : fields) {
      String trimmed = Strings.trimToNull(field);
      if (trimmed == null) {
        continue;
      }
      int delimiter = trimmed.indexOf('=');
      if (delimiter <= 0 || delimiter >= trimmed.length() - 1) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("Malformed stream ticket field: " + trimmed);
      }
      String key = Strings.trimToNull(trimmed.substring(0, delimiter));
      String value = Strings.trimToNull(trimmed.substring(delimiter + 1));
      if (key == null || value == null) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("Malformed stream ticket field: " + trimmed);
      }
      if (!isKnownField(key)) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("Unknown stream ticket field: " + key);
      }
      if (kv.putIfAbsent(key, value) != null) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("Duplicate stream ticket field: " + key);
      }
    }
    return Map.copyOf(kv);
  }

  private static boolean isKnownField(String key) {
    return KEY_DATASET_ID.equals(key)
        || KEY_START.equals(key)
        || KEY_BATCH_MAX_ROWS.equals(key)
        || KEY_FLUSH_MILLIS.equals(key)
        || KEY_SUBSCRIPTION_ID.equals(key)
        || KEY_FILTER_SQL.equals(key)
        || KEY_ACCESS_MODE.equals(key);
  }
}


FILE: FlightSqlRequestHeadersMiddleware.java

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.flight;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import org.apache.arrow.flight.CallHeaders;
import org.apache.arrow.flight.CallInfo;
import org.apache.arrow.flight.CallStatus;
import org.apache.arrow.flight.FlightServerMiddleware;
import org.apache.arrow.flight.RequestContext;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.headers.FabricRequestHeaders;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

public final class FlightSqlRequestHeadersMiddleware implements FlightServerMiddleware {
  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(FlightSqlRequestHeadersMiddleware.class);

  public static final FlightServerMiddleware.Key<FlightSqlRequestHeadersMiddleware> KEY =
      FlightServerMiddleware.Key.of("fabric-flight-sql-headers");

  public static final String HEADER_DATASET_ID = "x-fabric-dataset-id";

  private final FabricRequestHeaders requestHeaders;
  private final String datasetId;
  private final Map<String, String> headerSnapshot;
  private final String callSummary;

  private FlightSqlRequestHeadersMiddleware(
      FabricRequestHeaders requestHeaders,
      String datasetId,
      Map<String, String> headerSnapshot,
      String callSummary) {
    this.requestHeaders = requestHeaders;
    this.datasetId = datasetId;
    this.headerSnapshot = headerSnapshot == null ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(headerSnapshot);
    this.callSummary = Strings.trimToNull(callSummary);
  }

  public static FlightServerMiddleware.Factory<FlightSqlRequestHeadersMiddleware> factory() {
    return new FlightServerMiddleware.Factory<>() {
      @Override
      public FlightSqlRequestHeadersMiddleware onCallStarted(
          CallInfo callInfo, CallHeaders incomingHeaders, RequestContext requestContext) {
        try {
          FabricRequestHeaders requestHeaders = FabricRequestHeaders.fromFlight(incomingHeaders, null);
          String datasetId =
              incomingHeaders == null
                  ? null
                  : Strings.trimToNull(incomingHeaders.get(HEADER_DATASET_ID));
          Map<String, String> snapshot = snapshotHeaders(incomingHeaders);
          String callSummary = callSummary(callInfo);
          LOGGER.info("[Flight][Inbound] call={} requestId={} traceId={} callerApp={} oboUser={} datasetId={} headers={}", Strings.firstNonBlank(callSummary, "<unknown>"), requestHeaders.requestMetadata().requestId(), Strings.firstNonBlank(requestHeaders.requestMetadata().traceId(), "<none>"), Strings.firstNonBlank(requestHeaders.callerApp().asSubject(), "<none>"), Strings.firstNonBlank(requestHeaders.oboUser(), "<none>"), Strings.firstNonBlank(datasetId, "<none>"), snapshot);
          return new FlightSqlRequestHeadersMiddleware(
              requestHeaders, datasetId, snapshot, callSummary);
        } catch (FabricRequestHeaders.ParseException ex) {
          throw CallStatus.UNAUTHENTICATED
              .withDescription(ex.getMessage())
              .withCause(ex)
              .toRuntimeException();
        }
      }
    };
  }

  public FabricRequestHeaders requestHeaders() {
    return requestHeaders;
  }

  public String datasetId() {
    return datasetId;
  }

  public Map<String, String> headerSnapshot() {
    return headerSnapshot;
  }

  public String callSummary() {
    return callSummary;
  }

  @Override
  public void onBeforeSendingHeaders(CallHeaders outgoingHeaders) {}

  @Override
  public void onCallCompleted(CallStatus status) {}

  @Override
  public void onCallErrored(Throwable throwable) {}

  private static String callSummary(CallInfo callInfo) {
    if (callInfo == null) {
      return null;
    }
    try {
      String method = Strings.trimToNull(callInfo.method() == null ? null : callInfo.method().toString());
      if (method != null) {
        return method;
      }
    } catch (RuntimeException ignore) {
    }
    return Strings.trimToNull(String.valueOf(callInfo));
  }

  private static Map<String, String> snapshotHeaders(CallHeaders headers) {
    if (headers == null) {
      return Map.of();
    }
    List<String> keys = new ArrayList<>();
    headers.keys().forEach(keys::add);
    keys.sort(String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER);
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> snapshot = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (String key : keys) {
      String normalizedKey = Strings.trimToNull(key);
      if (normalizedKey == null || snapshot.containsKey(normalizedKey.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT))) {
        continue;
      }
      String value = Strings.trimToNull(headers.get(key));
      snapshot.put(normalizedKey.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT), redactIfSensitive(normalizedKey, value));
    }
    return Map.copyOf(snapshot);
  }

  private static String redactIfSensitive(String key, String value) {
    String normalizedValue = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalizedValue == null) {
      return "<empty>";
    }
    String normalizedKey = Strings.trimToNull(key);
    String token = normalizedKey == null ? "" : normalizedKey.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
    if (token.contains("authorization")
        || token.contains("token")
        || token.contains("cookie")
        || token.contains("set-cookie")) {
      return "<redacted>";
    }
    if (normalizedValue.length() > 256) {
      return normalizedValue.substring(0, 256) + "...";
    }
    return normalizedValue;
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.flight;

import org.apache.arrow.flight.CallStatus;
import org.apache.arrow.flight.FlightProducer;
import org.apache.arrow.flight.sql.impl.FlightSql;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.dataset.DatasetId;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.identity.RequestIdentityResolver;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.flight.kerberos.FlightKerberosServerMiddlewareFactory;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

final class FlightSqlServiceProducerHeaders {

  private FlightSqlServiceProducerHeaders() {}

  static String requireSql(FlightSql.CommandStatementQuery command) {
    String sql = command == null ? null : Strings.trimToNull(command.getQuery());
    if (sql == null) {
      throw CallStatus.INVALID_ARGUMENT
          .withDescription("Flight SQL statement query is required")
          .toRuntimeException();
    }
    return sql;
  }

  static DatasetId resolveDatasetId(FlightProducer.CallContext context) {
    FlightSqlRequestHeadersMiddleware headers =
        context == null ? null : context.getMiddleware(FlightSqlRequestHeadersMiddleware.KEY);
    String raw = headers == null ? null : Strings.trimToNull(headers.datasetId());
    if (raw == null) {
      return null;
    }
    try {
      return DatasetId.parse(raw);
    } catch (IllegalArgumentException ex) {
      throw CallStatus.INVALID_ARGUMENT
          .withDescription(ex.getMessage())
          .withCause(ex)
          .toRuntimeException();
    }
  }

  static String safeSubject(String subject) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(subject);
    return normalized == null ? "<unknown>" : normalized;
  }

  static String safeCaller(String callerAppSubject) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(callerAppSubject);
    return normalized == null ? "<none>" : normalized;
  }

  static String kerberosPrincipal(FlightProducer.CallContext context) {
    if (context == null) {
      return null;
    }
    FlightKerberosServerMiddlewareFactory.ServerMiddleware middleware =
        context.getMiddleware(FlightKerberosServerMiddlewareFactory.KEY);
    return middleware == null ? null : Strings.trimToNull(middleware.principal());
  }

  static RuntimeException toFlightRuntime(RequestIdentityResolver.ResolutionException ex) {
    if (ex.code() == RequestIdentityResolver.Code.PERMISSION_DENIED) {
      return CallStatus.UNAUTHORIZED
          .withDescription(ex.getMessage())
          .withCause(ex)
          .toRuntimeException();
    }
    return CallStatus.UNAUTHENTICATED
        .withDescription(ex.getMessage())
        .withCause(ex)
        .toRuntimeException();
  }
}
