package org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.flight;

import java.io.File;
import java.io.IOException;
import java.net.BindException;
import java.net.ServerSocket;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.concurrent.TimeUnit;
import org.apache.arrow.flight.FlightProducer;
import org.apache.arrow.flight.FlightServer;
import org.apache.arrow.flight.FlightServerMiddleware;
import org.apache.arrow.flight.Location;
import org.apache.arrow.memory.RootAllocator;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.kerberos.KerberosClient;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.kerberos.KerberosConfig;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.kerberos.KerberosKrb5Source;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.kerberos.KerberosSpn;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.common.ServiceAdvertise;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.flight.kerberos.FlightKerberosServerMiddlewareFactory;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Exceptions;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

public final class FlightSqlServiceRuntime implements AutoCloseable {
  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(FlightSqlServiceRuntime.class);
  private final Config cfg;
  private final FlightProducer producer;
  private FlightServer server;
  private RootAllocator allocator;
  private KerberosClient ownedKerberosContext;
  private int boundPort;

  private FlightSqlServiceRuntime(Config cfg, FlightProducer producer) {
    this.cfg = Objects.requireNonNull(cfg, "cfg");
    this.producer = Objects.requireNonNull(producer, "producer");
  }

  public static FlightSqlServiceRuntime start(Config cfg, FlightProducer producer) throws Exception {
    FlightSqlServiceRuntime runtime = new FlightSqlServiceRuntime(cfg, producer);
    runtime.start();
    return runtime;
  }

  public int port() {
    return server == null ? boundPort : server.getPort();
  }

  public void blockUntilShutdown() throws InterruptedException {
    if (server != null) {
      server.awaitTermination();
    }
  }

  @Override
  public synchronized void close() {
    if (server != null) {
      try {
        server.shutdown();
        server.awaitTermination(3, TimeUnit.SECONDS);
      } catch (Exception ex) {
        if (ex instanceof InterruptedException) {
          Thread.currentThread().interrupt();
        }
      } finally {
        server = null;
      }
    }
    closeOwnedKerberos();
    if (allocator != null) {
      try {
        allocator.close();
      } catch (Exception ignore) {
      } finally {
        allocator = null;
      }
    }
    if (producer instanceof AutoCloseable closeable) {
      try {
        closeable.close();
      } catch (Exception ignore) {
      }
    }
  }

  @SuppressWarnings({"rawtypes", "unchecked"})
  private synchronized void start() throws Exception {
    cfg.validate();
    allocator = new RootAllocator(Long.MAX_VALUE);
    String bindHost = resolveBindHost(cfg.bindHost);
    String advertiseHost = resolveAdvertiseHost(cfg.advertiseHost, bindHost);

    int maxAttempts = cfg.portFailback ? Math.max(1, cfg.portFailbackAttempts) : 1;
    int currentPort = cfg.bindPort;
    int attempt = 0;
    Exception lastFailure = null;
    while (attempt < maxAttempts) {
      attempt++;
      FlightServer.Builder builder =
          FlightServer.builder(
              allocator,
              cfg.tlsEnabled
                  ? Location.forGrpcTls(bindHost, currentPort)
                  : Location.forGrpcInsecure(bindHost, currentPort),
              producer);
      if (cfg.tlsEnabled) {
        builder.useTls(cfg.certChainPem, cfg.privateKeyPem);
      }
      if (cfg.kerberosEnabled) {
        ownedKerberosContext = startKerberos(cfg);
        String realm = KerberosSpn.resolveRealm(cfg.kerberosRealm, ownedKerberosContext.getSubject());
        String baseSpn = KerberosSpn.resolveSpn(cfg.kerberosSpn, advertiseHost);
        String normalizedSpn = KerberosSpn.normalizeSpnWithRealm(baseSpn, realm);
        String acceptorPrincipal =
            resolveAcceptorPrincipal(cfg.kerberosPrincipal, normalizedSpn, realm);
        LOGGER.info("[Flight][Kerberos] enabled=true principal={} keytab={} advertiseHost={} derivedSpn={}", cfg.kerberosPrincipal, cfg.kerberosKeytab, advertiseHost, normalizedSpn);
        builder.middleware(
            FlightKerberosServerMiddlewareFactory.KEY,
            FlightKerberosServerMiddlewareFactory.login(
                acceptorPrincipal,
                ownedKerberosContext.getResolvedKeytabPath(),
                ownedKerberosContext.getResolvedKrb5Path()));
      }
      for (Map.Entry<
              FlightServerMiddleware.Key<?>,
              FlightServerMiddleware.Factory<? extends FlightServerMiddleware>>
          entry : cfg.middlewares.entrySet()) {
        if (entry.getKey() != null && entry.getValue() != null) {
          builder.middleware((FlightServerMiddleware.Key) entry.getKey(), entry.getValue());
        }
      }
      try {
        server = builder.build().start();
        boundPort = server.getPort();
        return;
      } catch (IOException ex) {
        closeOwnedKerberos();
        lastFailure = ex;
        if (cfg.portFailback && attempt < maxAttempts && isBindException(ex)) {
          currentPort = selectRandomPort();
          continue;
        }
        throw ex;
      }
    }
    if (lastFailure != null) {
      throw lastFailure;
    }
    throw new IllegalStateException("Unable to start Arrow Flight SQL service runtime");
  }

  private static KerberosClient startKerberos(Config cfg) {
    KerberosConfig kerberosConfig =
        new KerberosConfig(
            KerberosConfig.DEFAULT_CONTEXT_NAME,
            true,
            cfg.kerberosPrincipal,
            cfg.kerberosKeytab.toPath(),
            null,
            KerberosKrb5Source.DEFAULT,
            cfg.kerberosRealm,
            false,
            true);
    return new KerberosClient(kerberosConfig).start();
  }

  private void closeOwnedKerberos() {
    KerberosClient context = ownedKerberosContext;
    ownedKerberosContext = null;
    if (context == null) {
      return;
    }
    try {
      context.close();
    } catch (Exception ignore) {
    }
  }

  private static boolean isBindException(Throwable error) {
    return Exceptions.hasCause(error, BindException.class);
  }

  private static int selectRandomPort() throws IOException {
    try (ServerSocket socket = new ServerSocket(0)) {
      socket.setReuseAddress(true);
      return socket.getLocalPort();
    }
  }

  private static String resolveBindHost(String bindHost) {
    String resolved = Strings.trimToNull(bindHost);
    return resolved == null ? "0.0.0.0" : resolved;
  }

  private static String resolveAdvertiseHost(String advertiseHost, String bindHost) {
    String resolved = ServiceAdvertise.resolveAdvertiseHost(advertiseHost, bindHost);
    return ServiceAdvertise.requireRoutableHost(resolved, "arrow advertise host");
  }

  private static String resolveAcceptorPrincipal(
      String configuredPrincipal, String normalizedSpn, String realm) {
    String principal = Strings.trimToNull(configuredPrincipal);
    if (principal != null && isHttpServicePrincipal(principal)) {
      return KerberosSpn.normalizeSpnWithRealm(principal, realm);
    }
    return Strings.trimToNull(normalizedSpn);
  }

  private static boolean isHttpServicePrincipal(String principal) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(principal);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return false;
    }
    String withoutRealm = KerberosSpn.stripRealm(normalized);
    return withoutRealm != null && withoutRealm.regionMatches(true, 0, "HTTP/", 0, 5);
  }

  public static final class Config {
    public String bindHost;
    public int bindPort;
    public String advertiseHost;
    public Integer advertisePort;
    public boolean portFailback;
    public int portFailbackAttempts = 5;
    public boolean tlsEnabled;
    public File certChainPem;
    public File privateKeyPem;
    public boolean kerberosEnabled;
    public String kerberosSpn;
    public String kerberosPrincipal;
    public File kerberosKeytab;
    public String kerberosRealm;
    public Map<FlightServerMiddleware.Key<?>, FlightServerMiddleware.Factory<? extends FlightServerMiddleware>>
        middlewares = Map.of();

    public void validate() {
      if (bindPort <= 0) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("arrow bind port must be > 0");
      }
      if (tlsEnabled) {
        if (certChainPem == null || privateKeyPem == null) {
          throw new IllegalArgumentException(
              "TLS enabled but certChainPem/privateKeyPem are not configured");
        }
        if (!certChainPem.isFile()) {
          throw new IllegalArgumentException(
              "TLS certificate chain does not exist: " + certChainPem.getAbsolutePath());
        }
        if (!privateKeyPem.isFile()) {
          throw new IllegalArgumentException(
              "TLS private key does not exist: " + privateKeyPem.getAbsolutePath());
        }
      }
      if (kerberosEnabled) {
        kerberosPrincipal = Strings.trimToNull(kerberosPrincipal);
        if (kerberosPrincipal == null) {
          throw new IllegalArgumentException(
              "Kerberos principal is required when arrow.kerberos.enabled=true");
        }
        if (kerberosKeytab == null) {
          throw new IllegalArgumentException(
              "Kerberos keytab is required when arrow.kerberos.enabled=true");
        }
        if (!kerberosKeytab.isFile()) {
          throw new IllegalArgumentException(
              "Kerberos keytab does not exist: " + kerberosKeytab.getAbsolutePath());
        }
        kerberosSpn = Strings.trimToNull(kerberosSpn);
        kerberosRealm = Strings.trimToNull(kerberosRealm);
      }
      middlewares = middlewares == null ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(new LinkedHashMap<>(middlewares));
    }

  }
}


FILE: StreamFilterSqlValidator.java

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.flight;

import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Set;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class StreamFilterSqlValidator {
  private static final int MAX_FILTER_LENGTH = 1024;
  private static final Set<String> FORBIDDEN_KEYWORDS =
      Set.of(
          "select",
          "from",
          "join",
          "with",
          "union",
          "intersect",
          "except",
          "update",
          "insert",
          "delete",
          "drop",
          "create",
          "alter",
          "attach",
          "detach");

  private StreamFilterSqlValidator() {}

  public static String validate(String filterSql) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(filterSql);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return null;
    }
    if (normalized.length() > MAX_FILTER_LENGTH) {
      throw invalid("filterSql exceeds max length " + MAX_FILTER_LENGTH);
    }
    if (normalized.contains(";")) {
      throw invalid("filterSql must not contain ';'");
    }
    if (normalized.contains("--") || normalized.contains("/*") || normalized.contains("*/")) {
      throw invalid("filterSql must not contain SQL comments");
    }
    int depth = 0;
    StringBuilder token = new StringBuilder();
    for (int i = 0; i < normalized.length(); i++) {
      char c = normalized.charAt(i);
      if (c == '\'') {
        i = scanStringLiteral(normalized, i);
        token.setLength(0);
        continue;
      }
      if (Character.isISOControl(c) && !Character.isWhitespace(c)) {
        throw invalid("filterSql contains unsupported control character at offset " + i);
      }
      if (c == '(') {
        depth++;
        token.setLength(0);
        continue;
      }
      if (c == ')') {
        depth--;
        if (depth < 0) {
          throw invalid("filterSql has unbalanced parentheses");
        }
        token.setLength(0);
        continue;
      }
      if (isIdentifierPart(c)) {
        token.append(c);
        continue;
      }
      if (!token.isEmpty()) {
        rejectForbiddenKeyword(token.toString(), i - token.length());
        token.setLength(0);
      }
    }
    if (!token.isEmpty()) {
      rejectForbiddenKeyword(token.toString(), normalized.length() - token.length());
    }
    if (depth != 0) {
      throw invalid("filterSql has unbalanced parentheses");
    }
    return normalized;
  }

  private static int scanStringLiteral(String sql, int start) {
    int index = start + 1;
    while (index < sql.length()) {
      char c = sql.charAt(index);
      if (c == '\'') {
        if (index + 1 < sql.length() && sql.charAt(index + 1) == '\'') {
          index += 2;
          continue;
        }
        return index;
      }
      index++;
    }
    throw invalid("filterSql has unterminated string literal");
  }

  private static boolean isIdentifierPart(char c) {
    return Character.isLetterOrDigit(c) || c == '_' || c == '$';
  }

  private static void rejectForbiddenKeyword(String token, int offset) {
    String lower = token.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
    if (FORBIDDEN_KEYWORDS.contains(lower)) {
      throw invalid("filterSql contains forbidden keyword '" + lower + "' at offset " + offset);
    }
  }

  private static IllegalArgumentException invalid(String message) {
    return new IllegalArgumentException("Invalid stream filterSql: " + message);
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.flight.streaming;

import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.nio.ByteBuffer;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.TabularManager;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.dataset.DatasetId;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.manager.DuckdbActiveChangeLog;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.manager.TabularManagerImpl;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.identity.RequestIdentityResolver;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

final class ArrowBatchPublisher {
  private final TabularManager tabularManager;
  private final TabularManagerImpl localTabularManager;

  ArrowBatchPublisher(TabularManager tabularManager) {
    this.tabularManager = Objects.requireNonNull(tabularManager, "tabularManager");
    this.localTabularManager =
        tabularManager instanceof TabularManagerImpl local ? local : null;
  }

  ByteBuffer querySchemaIpc(StreamSubscriptionContext context) {
    String sql = "select * from " + sqlToken(context.datasetId()) + " limit 1";
    return queryIpc(context, sql);
  }

  ByteBuffer buildBatchIpc(
      StreamSubscriptionContext context, List<String> primaryKeyColumns, List<String> keys) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(context, "context");
    if (keys == null || keys.isEmpty()) {
      return null;
    }
    String sql = buildBatchSql(context.datasetId(), primaryKeyColumns, keys, context.filterSql());
    return queryIpc(context, sql);
  }

  private ByteBuffer queryIpc(StreamSubscriptionContext context, String sql) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(context, "context");
    String plannedSql = Strings.requireNonBlank(sql, "sql");
    if (context.isPublic()) {
      if (localTabularManager == null) {
        throw new IllegalStateException("PUBLIC dataset streaming requires DIRECT tabular manager");
      }
      return localTabularManager.queryIpcPublicBuffer(plannedSql, -1);
    }
    return RequestIdentityResolver.callAsRequestIdentity(
        context.requestIdentity(), () -> tabularManager.queryIpcBuffer(plannedSql));
  }

  static String buildBatchSql(
      DatasetId datasetId, List<String> primaryKeyColumns, List<String> keys, String filterSql) {
    if (keys == null || keys.isEmpty()) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("keys are required");
    }
    List<String> uniqueKeys = List.copyOf(new LinkedHashSet<>(keys));
    String inList =
        uniqueKeys.stream()
            .map(DuckdbActiveChangeLog::quoteSqlString)
            .reduce((left, right) -> left + ", " + right)
            .orElseThrow();
    String pkExpr = DuckdbActiveChangeLog.primaryKeyTextExpression(primaryKeyColumns, null);
    StringBuilder sql =
        new StringBuilder("select * from ")
            .append(sqlToken(datasetId))
            .append(" where ")
            .append(pkExpr)
            .append(" in (")
            .append(inList)
            .append(")");
    String normalizedFilter = Strings.trimToNull(filterSql);
    if (normalizedFilter != null) {
      sql.append(" and (").append(normalizedFilter).append(")");
    }
    return sql.toString();
  }

  static String sqlToken(DatasetId datasetId) {
    return quoteIdentifier(datasetId.group())
        + "."
        + quoteIdentifier(datasetId.namespace())
        + "."
        + quoteIdentifier(datasetId.name());
  }

  static String quoteIdentifier(String identifier) {
    return "\"" + identifier.replace("\"", "\"\"") + "\"";
  }
}


FILE: DatasetStreamHubRegistry.java

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.flight.streaming;

import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.concurrent.ConcurrentHashMap;
import java.util.concurrent.ConcurrentMap;
import java.util.function.Supplier;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.dataset.DatasetId;

public final class DatasetStreamHubRegistry {
  private final ConcurrentMap<DatasetId, DatasetStreamHub> hubs = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();

  public DatasetStreamHub getOrCreate(DatasetId datasetId, Supplier<DatasetStreamHub> hubFactory) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(datasetId, "datasetId");
    Objects.requireNonNull(hubFactory, "hubFactory");
    return hubs.computeIfAbsent(datasetId, ignored -> hubFactory.get());
  }

  public void evict(DatasetId datasetId, DatasetStreamHub hub) {
    if (datasetId == null || hub == null) {
      return;
    }
    hubs.remove(datasetId, hub);
  }

  public void closeAll() {
    for (DatasetStreamHub hub : List.copyOf(hubs.values())) {
      if (hub != null) {
        hub.close();
      }
    }
    hubs.clear();
  }

  int size() {
    return hubs.size();
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.flight.streaming;

import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.dataset.DatasetId;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.headers.FabricRequestHeaders;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.identity.RequestIdentity;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.flight.FlightDatasetStreamTicket;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public record StreamSubscriptionContext(
    DatasetId datasetId,
    String accessMode,
    String effectiveUserSubject,
    String callerAppSubject,
    FabricRequestHeaders.RequestMetadata requestMetadata,
    String subscriptionId,
    FlightDatasetStreamTicket.Start startMode,
    long startingSeq,
    int batchMaxRows,
    int flushMillis,
    String filterSql,
    RequestIdentity requestIdentity) {

  public StreamSubscriptionContext {
    if (datasetId == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("datasetId is required");
    }
    String normalizedAccessMode = Strings.trimToNull(accessMode);
    if (normalizedAccessMode == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("accessMode is required");
    }
    if ("PUBLIC".equalsIgnoreCase(normalizedAccessMode)) {
      accessMode = "PUBLIC";
    } else if ("PRIVATE".equalsIgnoreCase(normalizedAccessMode)) {
      accessMode = "PRIVATE";
    } else {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("accessMode must be PUBLIC or PRIVATE");
    }
    if ("PRIVATE".equals(accessMode) && Strings.trimToNull(effectiveUserSubject) == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("effectiveUserSubject is required for PRIVATE subscriptions");
    }
    effectiveUserSubject = Strings.trimToNull(effectiveUserSubject);
    callerAppSubject = Strings.trimToNull(callerAppSubject);
    if (requestMetadata == null) {
      requestMetadata = new FabricRequestHeaders.RequestMetadata(null, null, null, null, null);
    }
    subscriptionId = Strings.requireNonBlank(subscriptionId, "subscriptionId");
    startMode = startMode == null ? FlightDatasetStreamTicket.Start.LATEST : startMode;
    if (startingSeq < 0L) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("startingSeq must be >= 0");
    }
    if (batchMaxRows <= 0) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("batchMaxRows must be > 0");
    }
    if (flushMillis <= 0) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("flushMillis must be > 0");
    }
    filterSql = Strings.trimToNull(filterSql);
  }

  public boolean isPublic() {
    return "PUBLIC".equals(accessMode);
  }
}

FILE: GrpcKerberosAcceptor.java

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.grpc;

import java.nio.file.Files;
import java.nio.file.Path;
import java.security.PrivilegedActionException;
import java.security.PrivilegedExceptionAction;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import javax.security.auth.Subject;
import javax.security.auth.login.AppConfigurationEntry;
import javax.security.auth.login.Configuration;
import javax.security.auth.login.LoginContext;
import javax.security.auth.login.LoginException;
import org.ietf.jgss.GSSContext;
import org.ietf.jgss.GSSCredential;
import org.ietf.jgss.GSSManager;
import org.ietf.jgss.GSSName;
import org.ietf.jgss.Oid;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class GrpcKerberosAcceptor {
  private static final String KRB5_LOGIN_MODULE = "com.sun.security.auth.module.Krb5LoginModule";
  private static final String LOGIN_CONTEXT_NAME = "Krb5";
  private static final Oid SPNEGO_OID = oid("1.3.6.1.5.5.2");
  private static final String JVM_KRB5_CONF = "java.security.krb5.conf";
  private static final String JVM_KRB5_CONFIG = "sun.security.krb5.config";

  private final Subject acceptorSubject;
  private final GSSCredential acceptorCredential;

  private GrpcKerberosAcceptor(Subject acceptorSubject, GSSCredential acceptorCredential) {
    this.acceptorSubject = acceptorSubject;
    this.acceptorCredential = acceptorCredential;
  }

  public static GrpcKerberosAcceptor login(
      String acceptorPrincipal, Path keytabPath, Path krb5ConfPath) {
    String principal = require(acceptorPrincipal, "acceptorPrincipal");
    Path keytab = requireReadableFile(keytabPath, "keytabPath");
    Path krb5 = requireReadableFile(krb5ConfPath, "krb5ConfPath");
    ensureJvmKrb5Configured(krb5);
    try {
      Subject subject = loginAcceptorSubject(principal, keytab);
      GSSCredential credential = initializeAcceptorCredential(subject, principal);
      return new GrpcKerberosAcceptor(subject, credential);
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Failed to initialize gRPC Kerberos acceptor", ex);
    }
  }

  @SuppressWarnings("removal")
  public AcceptResult accept(byte[] incomingToken) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(incomingToken, "incomingToken");
    if (incomingToken.length == 0) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("incomingToken is required");
    }
    try {
      return Subject.doAs(
          acceptorSubject,
          (PrivilegedExceptionAction<AcceptResult>) () -> acceptInSubject(incomingToken));
    } catch (PrivilegedActionException ex) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Failed to accept SPNEGO token", ex.getException());
    }
  }

  private static Subject loginAcceptorSubject(String acceptorPrincipal, Path keytabPath)
      throws LoginException {
    Configuration config = new AcceptorLoginConfiguration(acceptorPrincipal, keytabPath);
    LoginContext loginContext = new LoginContext(LOGIN_CONTEXT_NAME, null, null, config);
    loginContext.login();
    Subject subject = Objects.requireNonNull(loginContext.getSubject(), "acceptorSubject");
    if (!subject.isReadOnly()) {
      subject.setReadOnly();
    }
    return subject;
  }

  @SuppressWarnings("removal")
  private static GSSCredential initializeAcceptorCredential(Subject subject, String acceptorPrincipal)
      throws Exception {
    try {
      return Subject.doAs(
          subject,
          (PrivilegedExceptionAction<GSSCredential>)
              () -> {
                GSSManager manager = GSSManager.getInstance();
                GSSName acceptorName = manager.createName(acceptorPrincipal, GSSName.NT_USER_NAME);
                return manager.createCredential(
                    acceptorName,
                    GSSCredential.DEFAULT_LIFETIME,
                    SPNEGO_OID,
                    GSSCredential.ACCEPT_ONLY);
              });
    } catch (PrivilegedActionException ex) {
      throw ex.getException();
    }
  }

  private AcceptResult acceptInSubject(byte[] incomingToken) throws Exception {
    GSSContext context = GSSManager.getInstance().createContext(acceptorCredential);
    try {
      byte[] response = context.acceptSecContext(incomingToken, 0, incomingToken.length);
      boolean established = context.isEstablished();
      String sourcePrincipal = context.getSrcName() == null ? null : context.getSrcName().toString();
      return new AcceptResult(sourcePrincipal, established, response);
    } finally {
      context.dispose();
    }
  }

  private static Path requireReadableFile(Path value, String label) {
    if (value == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(label + " is required");
    }
    Path normalized = value.toAbsolutePath().normalize();
    if (!Files.isRegularFile(normalized) || !Files.isReadable(normalized)) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(label + " is missing/unreadable: " + normalized);
    }
    return normalized;
  }

  private static String require(String value, String label) {
    String trimmed = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (trimmed == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(label + " is required");
    }
    return trimmed;
  }

  private static Oid oid(String value) {
    try {
      return new Oid(value);
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Invalid OID: " + value, ex);
    }
  }

  private static void ensureJvmKrb5Configured(Path expectedKrb5Path) {
    String configured = Strings.trimToNull(System.getProperty(JVM_KRB5_CONF));
    if (configured == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "JVM Kerberos config is not initialized: expected " + expectedKrb5Path);
    }
    Path configuredPath = Path.of(configured).toAbsolutePath().normalize();
    Path expectedPath = expectedKrb5Path.toAbsolutePath().normalize();
    if (!configuredPath.equals(expectedPath)) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "JVM Kerberos config mismatch: configured=" + configuredPath + " expected=" + expectedPath);
    }
    String configuredAlias = Strings.trimToNull(System.getProperty(JVM_KRB5_CONFIG));
    if (configuredAlias != null) {
      Path configuredAliasPath = Path.of(configuredAlias).toAbsolutePath().normalize();
      if (!configuredAliasPath.equals(expectedPath)) {
        throw new IllegalStateException(
            "JVM Kerberos alias config mismatch: configured="
                + configuredAliasPath
                + " expected="
                + expectedPath);
      }
    }
  }

  public record AcceptResult(String sourcePrincipal, boolean established, byte[] responseToken) {
    public AcceptResult {
      responseToken = responseToken == null ? null : responseToken.clone();
    }

    @Override
    public byte[] responseToken() {
      return responseToken == null ? null : responseToken.clone();
    }
  }

  private static final class AcceptorLoginConfiguration extends Configuration {
    private final AppConfigurationEntry[] entries;

    private AcceptorLoginConfiguration(String principal, Path keytabPath) {
      this.entries =
          new AppConfigurationEntry[] {
            new AppConfigurationEntry(
                KRB5_LOGIN_MODULE,
                AppConfigurationEntry.LoginModuleControlFlag.REQUIRED,
                options(principal, keytabPath))
          };
    }

    @Override
    public AppConfigurationEntry[] getAppConfigurationEntry(String name) {
      return entries;
    }

    private static Map<String, String> options(String principal, Path keytabPath) {
      Map<String, String> options = new LinkedHashMap<>();
      options.put("useKeyTab", "true");
      options.put("keyTab", keytabPath.toAbsolutePath().toString());
      options.put("principal", principal);
      options.put("storeKey", "true");
      options.put("doNotPrompt", "true");
      options.put("isInitiator", "false");
      options.put("useTicketCache", "false");
      options.put("refreshKrb5Config", "true");
      return options;
    }
  }
}


FILE: GrpcKerberosClientInterceptor.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.grpc;

import io.grpc.CallOptions;
import io.grpc.Channel;
import io.grpc.ClientCall;
import io.grpc.ClientInterceptor;
import io.grpc.ForwardingClientCall.SimpleForwardingClientCall;
import io.grpc.Metadata;
import io.grpc.MethodDescriptor;
import io.grpc.Status;
import java.util.Base64;
import java.util.Objects;
import javax.security.auth.Subject;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.kerberos.KerberosClient;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.kerberos.KerberosSpn;

final class GrpcKerberosClientInterceptor implements ClientInterceptor {
  private static final Metadata.Key<String> AUTHORIZATION =
      Metadata.Key.of("authorization", Metadata.ASCII_STRING_MARSHALLER);

  private final KerberosClient kerberosContext;
  private final String spn;
  private final boolean useDelegatedSubjectIfPresent;

  GrpcKerberosClientInterceptor(
      KerberosClient kerberosContext, String spn, boolean useDelegatedSubjectIfPresent) {
    this.kerberosContext = Objects.requireNonNull(kerberosContext, "kerberosContext");
    this.spn = requireTrimmed(spn, "spn");
    KerberosSpn.validateHttpSpn(this.spn);
    this.useDelegatedSubjectIfPresent = useDelegatedSubjectIfPresent;
  }

  @Override
  public <ReqT, RespT> ClientCall<ReqT, RespT> interceptCall(
      MethodDescriptor<ReqT, RespT> method, CallOptions callOptions, Channel next) {
    ClientCall<ReqT, RespT> delegate = next.newCall(method, callOptions);
    return new SimpleForwardingClientCall<>(delegate) {
      @Override
      public void start(Listener<RespT> responseListener, Metadata headers) {
        Metadata effectiveHeaders = headers == null ? new Metadata() : headers;
        try {
          Subject subject = kerberosContext.getSubject();
          if (useDelegatedSubjectIfPresent) {
            Subject delegated = GrpcKerberosContextKeys.DELEGATED_SUBJECT.get();
            if (delegated != null) {
              subject = delegated;
            }
          }
          byte[] token = kerberosContext.mintSpnegoTokenAsSubject(spn, subject);
          effectiveHeaders.removeAll(AUTHORIZATION);
          effectiveHeaders.put(AUTHORIZATION, "Negotiate " + Base64.getEncoder().encodeToString(token));
          super.start(responseListener, effectiveHeaders);
        } catch (Exception ex) {
          responseListener.onClose(
              Status.UNAUTHENTICATED
                  .withDescription("Kerberos SPNEGO init failed")
                  .withCause(ex),
              new Metadata());
        }
      }
    };
  }

  private static String requireTrimmed(String value, String label) {
    if (value == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(label + " is required");
    }
    String trimmed = value.trim();
    if (trimmed.isEmpty()) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(label + " is required");
    }
    return trimmed;
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.grpc;

import io.grpc.Context;
import javax.security.auth.Subject;

public final class GrpcKerberosContextKeys {
  static final Context.Key<String> AUTHENTICATED_PRINCIPAL =
      Context.key("fabric.grpc.kerberos.authenticatedPrincipal");
  static final Context.Key<Subject> DELEGATED_SUBJECT =
      Context.key("fabric.grpc.kerberos.delegatedSubject");

  public static String authenticatedPrincipal() {
    return AUTHENTICATED_PRINCIPAL.get();
  }

  private GrpcKerberosContextKeys() {}
}


FILE: GrpcKerberosServerInterceptor.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.grpc;

import io.grpc.Context;
import io.grpc.Contexts;
import io.grpc.Metadata;
import io.grpc.ServerCall;
import io.grpc.ServerCallHandler;
import io.grpc.ServerInterceptor;
import io.grpc.Status;
import java.util.Base64;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Objects;

final class GrpcKerberosServerInterceptor implements ServerInterceptor {
  private static final String NEGOTIATE_PREFIX = "Negotiate ";
  private static final Metadata.Key<String> AUTHORIZATION =
      Metadata.Key.of("authorization", Metadata.ASCII_STRING_MARSHALLER);

  private final GrpcKerberosAcceptor acceptor;

  GrpcKerberosServerInterceptor(GrpcKerberosAcceptor acceptor) {
    this.acceptor = Objects.requireNonNull(acceptor, "acceptor");
  }

  @Override
  public <ReqT, RespT> ServerCall.Listener<ReqT> interceptCall(
      ServerCall<ReqT, RespT> call, Metadata headers, ServerCallHandler<ReqT, RespT> next) {
    String authorization = extractAuthorization(headers);
    if (authorization == null) {
      call.close(
          Status.UNAUTHENTICATED.withDescription("Missing Kerberos Negotiate token"),
          new Metadata());
      return new ServerCall.Listener<>() {};
    }

    try {
      byte[] token = decodeNegotiateToken(authorization);
      GrpcKerberosAcceptor.AcceptResult result = acceptor.accept(token);
      if (result == null || !result.established()) {
        call.close(
            Status.UNAUTHENTICATED.withDescription("SPNEGO accept did not establish context"),
            new Metadata());
        return new ServerCall.Listener<>() {};
      }
      String principal = trimToNull(result.sourcePrincipal());
      if (principal == null) {
        call.close(
            Status.UNAUTHENTICATED.withDescription("Kerberos principal not available"),
            new Metadata());
        return new ServerCall.Listener<>() {};
      }
      Context context =
          Context.current().withValue(GrpcKerberosContextKeys.AUTHENTICATED_PRINCIPAL, principal);
      return Contexts.interceptCall(context, call, headers, next);
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      call.close(
          Status.UNAUTHENTICATED.withDescription("Kerberos authentication failed").withCause(ex),
          new Metadata());
      return new ServerCall.Listener<>() {};
    }
  }

  private static String extractAuthorization(Metadata headers) {
    if (headers == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String direct = trimToNull(headers.get(AUTHORIZATION));
    if (direct != null) {
      return direct;
    }
    for (String key : headers.keys()) {
      if (key != null && "authorization".equalsIgnoreCase(key)) {
        Metadata.Key<String> resolved = Metadata.Key.of(key, Metadata.ASCII_STRING_MARSHALLER);
        String value = trimToNull(headers.get(resolved));
        if (value != null) {
          return value;
        }
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  private static byte[] decodeNegotiateToken(String authorizationHeader) {
    String value = authorizationHeader == null ? "" : authorizationHeader.trim();
    if (!startsWithIgnoreCase(value, NEGOTIATE_PREFIX)) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Unsupported authorization scheme; expected Negotiate");
    }
    String tokenPart = value.substring(NEGOTIATE_PREFIX.length()).trim();
    if (tokenPart.isEmpty()) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Negotiate token is empty");
    }
    return Base64.getDecoder().decode(tokenPart);
  }

  private static boolean startsWithIgnoreCase(String value, String prefix) {
    if (value.length() < prefix.length()) {
      return false;
    }
    return value.substring(0, prefix.length()).toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT)
        .equals(prefix.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT));
  }

  private static String trimToNull(String value) {
    if (value == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String trimmed = value.trim();
    return trimmed.isEmpty() ? null : trimmed;
  }
}


FILE: GrpcServiceRuntime.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.grpc;

import io.grpc.BindableService;
import io.grpc.Server;
import io.grpc.ServerInterceptor;
import io.grpc.netty.shaded.io.grpc.netty.GrpcSslContexts;
import io.grpc.netty.shaded.io.grpc.netty.NettyServerBuilder;
import io.grpc.netty.shaded.io.netty.handler.ssl.SslContext;
import io.grpc.netty.shaded.io.netty.handler.ssl.SslContextBuilder;
import java.io.File;
import java.io.IOException;
import java.net.BindException;
import java.net.InetSocketAddress;
import java.net.ServerSocket;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.concurrent.TimeUnit;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.kerberos.KerberosClient;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.kerberos.KerberosConfig;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.kerberos.KerberosKrb5Source;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.kerberos.KerberosSpn;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.common.ServiceAdvertise;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Exceptions;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class GrpcServiceRuntime implements AutoCloseable {
  private final Config cfg;
  private final BindableService service;
  private final List<ServerInterceptor> interceptors;
  private Server server;
  private KerberosClient ownedKerberosContext;
  private int boundPort;

  private GrpcServiceRuntime(
      Config cfg, BindableService service, List<ServerInterceptor> interceptors) {
    this.cfg = Objects.requireNonNull(cfg, "cfg");
    this.service = Objects.requireNonNull(service, "service");
    this.interceptors = interceptors == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(interceptors);
  }

  public static GrpcServiceRuntime start(
      Config cfg, BindableService service, List<ServerInterceptor> interceptors) throws Exception {
    GrpcServiceRuntime runtime = new GrpcServiceRuntime(cfg, service, interceptors);
    runtime.start();
    return runtime;
  }

  public int port() {
    return server == null ? boundPort : server.getPort();
  }

  public void blockUntilShutdown() throws InterruptedException {
    if (server != null) {
      server.awaitTermination();
    }
  }

  @Override
  public synchronized void close() {
    if (server != null) {
      try {
        server.shutdownNow();
        server.awaitTermination(3, TimeUnit.SECONDS);
      } catch (InterruptedException ex) {
        Thread.currentThread().interrupt();
      } finally {
        server = null;
      }
    }
    if (ownedKerberosContext != null) {
      try {
        ownedKerberosContext.close();
      } catch (Exception ignore) {
      } finally {
        ownedKerberosContext = null;
      }
    }
  }

  private synchronized void start() throws Exception {
    cfg.validate();
    String bindHost = resolveBindHost(cfg.bindHost);
    String advertiseHost = resolveAdvertiseHost(cfg.advertiseHost, bindHost);
    int advertisePort = resolveAdvertisePort(cfg.advertisePort, cfg.bindPort);

    int maxAttempts = cfg.portFailback ? Math.max(1, cfg.portFailbackAttempts) : 1;
    int attempt = 0;
    int currentPort = cfg.bindPort;
    Exception lastFailure = null;
    while (attempt < maxAttempts) {
      attempt++;
      NettyServerBuilder builder =
          NettyServerBuilder.forAddress(new InetSocketAddress(bindHost, currentPort)).addService(service);
      for (ServerInterceptor interceptor : interceptors) {
        if (interceptor != null) {
          builder.intercept(interceptor);
        }
      }

      if (cfg.tlsEnabled) {
        SslContextBuilder sslBuilder = GrpcSslContexts.forServer(cfg.certChainPem, cfg.privateKeyPem);
        SslContext context = sslBuilder.build();
        builder.sslContext(context);
      }

      if (cfg.kerberosEnabled) {
        ownedKerberosContext = startKerberos(cfg);
        String realm = KerberosSpn.resolveRealm(cfg.kerberosRealm, ownedKerberosContext.getSubject());
        String baseSpn = KerberosSpn.resolveSpn(cfg.kerberosSpn, advertiseHost);
        String normalizedSpn = KerberosSpn.normalizeSpnWithRealm(baseSpn, realm);
        String acceptorPrincipal =
            resolveAcceptorPrincipal(cfg.kerberosPrincipal, normalizedSpn, realm);
        GrpcKerberosAcceptor acceptor =
            GrpcKerberosAcceptor.login(
                acceptorPrincipal,
                ownedKerberosContext.getResolvedKeytabPath(),
                ownedKerberosContext.getResolvedKrb5Path());
        builder.intercept(new GrpcKerberosServerInterceptor(acceptor));
      }

      try {
        server = builder.build().start();
        boundPort = server.getPort();
        if (cfg.advertisePort == null || cfg.advertisePort <= 0) {
          advertisePort = boundPort;
        }
        return;
      } catch (IOException ex) {
        closeOwnedKerberos();
        lastFailure = ex;
        if (cfg.portFailback && attempt < maxAttempts && isBindException(ex)) {
          currentPort = selectRandomPort();
          continue;
        }
        throw ex;
      }
    }
    if (lastFailure != null) {
      throw lastFailure;
    }
    throw new IllegalStateException("Unable to start gRPC service runtime");
  }

  private static KerberosClient startKerberos(Config cfg) {
    KerberosConfig kerberosConfig =
        new KerberosConfig(
            KerberosConfig.DEFAULT_CONTEXT_NAME,
            true,
            cfg.kerberosPrincipal,
            cfg.kerberosKeytab.toPath(),
            null,
            KerberosKrb5Source.DEFAULT,
            cfg.kerberosRealm,
            false,
            true);
    return new KerberosClient(kerberosConfig).start();
  }

  private void closeOwnedKerberos() {
    KerberosClient context = ownedKerberosContext;
    ownedKerberosContext = null;
    if (context == null) {
      return;
    }
    try {
      context.close();
    } catch (Exception ignore) {
    }
  }

  private static boolean isBindException(Throwable error) {
    return Exceptions.hasCause(error, BindException.class);
  }

  private static int selectRandomPort() throws IOException {
    try (ServerSocket socket = new ServerSocket(0)) {
      socket.setReuseAddress(true);
      return socket.getLocalPort();
    }
  }

  private static String resolveBindHost(String bindHost) {
    String resolved = Strings.trimToNull(bindHost);
    return resolved == null ? "0.0.0.0" : resolved;
  }

  private static String resolveAdvertiseHost(String advertiseHost, String bindHost) {
    String resolved = ServiceAdvertise.resolveAdvertiseHost(advertiseHost, bindHost);
    return ServiceAdvertise.requireRoutableHost(resolved, "grpc advertise host");
  }

  private static int resolveAdvertisePort(Integer advertisePort, int bindPort) {
    Integer resolved = ServiceAdvertise.resolveAdvertisePort(advertisePort, bindPort);
    if (resolved == null || resolved <= 0) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("grpc advertise port is required");
    }
    return resolved;
  }

  private static String resolveAcceptorPrincipal(
      String configuredPrincipal, String normalizedSpn, String realm) {
    String principal = Strings.trimToNull(configuredPrincipal);
    if (principal != null && isHttpServicePrincipal(principal)) {
      return KerberosSpn.normalizeSpnWithRealm(principal, realm);
    }
    return Strings.trimToNull(normalizedSpn);
  }

  private static boolean isHttpServicePrincipal(String principal) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(principal);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return false;
    }
    String withoutRealm = KerberosSpn.stripRealm(normalized);
    return withoutRealm != null && withoutRealm.regionMatches(true, 0, "HTTP/", 0, 5);
  }

  public static final class Config {
    public String bindHost;
    public int bindPort;
    public String advertiseHost;
    public Integer advertisePort;
    public boolean portFailback;
    public int portFailbackAttempts = 5;
    public boolean tlsEnabled;
    public File certChainPem;
    public File privateKeyPem;
    public boolean kerberosEnabled;
    public String kerberosSpn;
    public String kerberosPrincipal;
    public File kerberosKeytab;
    public String kerberosRealm;

    public void validate() {
      if (bindPort <= 0) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("grpc bind port must be > 0");
      }
      if (tlsEnabled) {
        if (certChainPem == null || privateKeyPem == null) {
          throw new IllegalArgumentException(
              "TLS enabled but certChainPem/privateKeyPem are not configured");
        }
        if (!certChainPem.isFile()) {
          throw new IllegalArgumentException(
              "TLS certificate chain does not exist: " + certChainPem.getAbsolutePath());
        }
        if (!privateKeyPem.isFile()) {
          throw new IllegalArgumentException(
              "TLS private key does not exist: " + privateKeyPem.getAbsolutePath());
        }
      }
      if (kerberosEnabled) {
        kerberosPrincipal = Strings.trimToNull(kerberosPrincipal);
        if (kerberosPrincipal == null) {
          throw new IllegalArgumentException(
              "Kerberos principal is required when grpc.kerberos.enabled=true");
        }
        if (kerberosKeytab == null) {
          throw new IllegalArgumentException(
              "Kerberos keytab is required when grpc.kerberos.enabled=true");
        }
        if (!kerberosKeytab.isFile()) {
          throw new IllegalArgumentException(
              "Kerberos keytab does not exist: " + kerberosKeytab.getAbsolutePath());
        }
        kerberosSpn = Strings.trimToNull(kerberosSpn);
        kerberosRealm = Strings.trimToNull(kerberosRealm);
      }
    }
  }
}

FILE: Bytes.java

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.util;

import java.io.IOException;
import java.io.InputStream;
import java.io.OutputStream;
import java.nio.ByteBuffer;
import java.util.Objects;

public final class Bytes {
  private static final int DEFAULT_DIRECT_OUTPUT_CAPACITY = 8 * 1024;
  private static final int MAX_DIRECT_OUTPUT_CAPACITY = Integer.MAX_VALUE - 8;

  private Bytes() {}

  public static ByteBuffer toDirectBuffer(byte[] bytes) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(bytes, "bytes");
    ByteBuffer direct = ByteBuffer.allocateDirect(bytes.length);
    direct.put(bytes);
    direct.flip();
    assert direct.isDirect();
    assert direct.position() == 0;
    assert direct.limit() == bytes.length;
    return direct;
  }

  public static ByteBuffer toDirectBuffer(ByteBuffer source) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(source, "source");
    ByteBuffer copy = source.asReadOnlyBuffer();
    int expectedLimit = copy.remaining();
    ByteBuffer direct = ByteBuffer.allocateDirect(copy.remaining());
    direct.put(copy);
    direct.flip();
    assert direct.isDirect();
    assert direct.position() == 0;
    assert direct.limit() == expectedLimit;
    return direct;
  }

  public static byte[] toByteArray(ByteBuffer buffer) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(buffer, "buffer");
    ByteBuffer copy = buffer.asReadOnlyBuffer();
    byte[] bytes = new byte[copy.remaining()];
    copy.get(bytes);
    return bytes;
  }

  public static InputStream asInputStream(ByteBuffer buffer) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(buffer, "buffer");
    return new ByteBufferInputStream(buffer.asReadOnlyBuffer());
  }

  public static DirectBufferOutputStream directOutputStream() {
    return new DirectBufferOutputStream(DEFAULT_DIRECT_OUTPUT_CAPACITY);
  }

  public static DirectBufferOutputStream directOutputStream(int initialCapacity) {
    return new DirectBufferOutputStream(initialCapacity);
  }

  public static final class DirectBufferOutputStream extends OutputStream {
    private ByteBuffer buffer;

    private DirectBufferOutputStream(int initialCapacity) {
      if (initialCapacity <= 0) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("initialCapacity must be > 0");
      }
      this.buffer = ByteBuffer.allocateDirect(initialCapacity);
    }

    @Override
    public void write(int value) throws IOException {
      ensureRemaining(1);
      buffer.put((byte) value);
    }

    @Override
    public void write(byte[] bytes, int offset, int length) throws IOException {
      Objects.requireNonNull(bytes, "bytes");
      if (offset < 0 || length < 0 || length > bytes.length - offset) {
        throw new IndexOutOfBoundsException(
            "offset=" + offset + ", length=" + length + ", arrayLength=" + bytes.length);
      }
      if (length == 0) {
        return;
      }
      ensureRemaining(length);
      buffer.put(bytes, offset, length);
    }

    public ByteBuffer toDirectByteBuffer() {
      int expectedSize = buffer.position();
      ByteBuffer view = buffer.asReadOnlyBuffer();
      view.flip();
      assert view.isDirect();
      assert view.position() == 0;
      assert view.limit() == expectedSize;
      return view;
    }

    public int size() {
      return buffer.position();
    }

    private void ensureRemaining(int additionalBytes) throws IOException {
      if (additionalBytes <= buffer.remaining()) {
        return;
      }
      int required;
      try {
        required = Math.addExact(buffer.position(), additionalBytes);
      } catch (ArithmeticException ex) {
        throw new IOException("Direct IPC buffer size overflow", ex);
      }
      int expanded = buffer.capacity();
      while (expanded < required) {
        if (expanded >= MAX_DIRECT_OUTPUT_CAPACITY) {
          throw new IOException("Direct IPC buffer exceeded max capacity");
        }
        expanded = Math.min(MAX_DIRECT_OUTPUT_CAPACITY, Math.max(expanded << 1, required));
      }
      ByteBuffer next = ByteBuffer.allocateDirect(expanded);
      buffer.flip();
      next.put(buffer);
      buffer = next;
    }
  }

  private static final class ByteBufferInputStream extends InputStream {
    private final ByteBuffer buffer;

    private ByteBufferInputStream(ByteBuffer buffer) {
      this.buffer = Objects.requireNonNull(buffer, "buffer");
    }

    @Override
    public int read() {
      if (!buffer.hasRemaining()) {
        return -1;
      }
      return buffer.get() & 0xFF;
    }

    @Override
    public int read(byte[] b, int off, int len) {
      Objects.requireNonNull(b, "b");
      if (off < 0 || len < 0 || len > b.length - off) {
        throw new IndexOutOfBoundsException(
            "off=" + off + ", len=" + len + ", arrayLength=" + b.length);
      }
      if (len == 0) {
        return 0;
      }
      if (!buffer.hasRemaining()) {
        return -1;
      }
      int read = Math.min(len, buffer.remaining());
      buffer.get(b, off, read);
      return read;
    }

    @Override
    public long skip(long n) {
      if (n <= 0) {
        return 0L;
      }
      int skipped = (int) Math.min(n, buffer.remaining());
      buffer.position(buffer.position() + skipped);
      return skipped;
    }

    @Override
    public int available() {
      return buffer.remaining();
    }
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.util;

import java.time.Instant;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionEnvelope;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionType;

public final class DefinitionModelMapperSupport {
  public static final String DEFAULT_LIFECYCLE_STATUS = "ACTIVE";
  public static final String DEFAULT_ACTOR = "fabric-lite";

  private DefinitionModelMapperSupport() {}

  public static String requireNonBlank(String value, String fieldName) {
    return Strings.requireNonBlank(value, fieldName);
  }

  public static String normalizeLifecycleStatus(String lifecycleStatus) {
    return Strings.firstNonBlank(lifecycleStatus, DEFAULT_LIFECYCLE_STATUS);
  }

  public static String normalizeActor(String actor) {
    return Strings.firstNonBlank(actor, DEFAULT_ACTOR);
  }

  public static String buildDefinitionId(String kind, String group, String name) {
    return requireNonBlank(kind, "kind")
        + ":"
        + requireNonBlank(group, "group")
        + "/"
        + requireNonBlank(name, "name");
  }

  public static String buildScopedName(
      String namespace, String name, String namespaceFieldName, String nameFieldName) {
    return requireNonBlank(namespace, namespaceFieldName)
        + "/"
        + requireNonBlank(name, nameFieldName);
  }

  public static DefinitionEnvelope envelopeNow(
      String group,
      DefinitionType type,
      String name,
      String uuid,
      boolean enabled,
      String lifecycleStatus,
      String actor) {
    return envelopeAt(
        group,
        type,
        name,
        uuid,
        enabled,
        lifecycleStatus,
        actor,
        Instant.now().toString());
  }

  public static DefinitionEnvelope envelopeAt(
      String group,
      DefinitionType type,
      String name,
      String uuid,
      boolean enabled,
      String lifecycleStatus,
      String actor,
      String timestampIso) {
    String now = requireNonBlank(timestampIso, "timestampIso");
    String resolvedActor = normalizeActor(actor);
    return new DefinitionEnvelope(
        requireNonBlank(group, "group"),
        type,
        requireNonBlank(name, "name"),
        requireNonBlank(uuid, "uuid"),
        enabled,
        normalizeLifecycleStatus(lifecycleStatus),
        now,
        resolvedActor,
        now,
        resolvedActor);
  }
}


FILE: Exceptions.java

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.util;

public final class Exceptions {

  private Exceptions() {}

  public static Throwable rootCause(Throwable error) {
    Throwable cursor = error;
    while (cursor != null && cursor.getCause() != null && cursor.getCause() != cursor) {
      cursor = cursor.getCause();
    }
    return cursor;
  }

  public static boolean hasCause(Throwable error, Class<? extends Throwable> type) {
    if (type == null) {
      return false;
    }
    Throwable cursor = error;
    while (cursor != null) {
      if (type.isInstance(cursor)) {
        return true;
      }
      Throwable next = cursor.getCause();
      if (next == cursor) {
        break;
      }
      cursor = next;
    }
    return false;
  }

  public static String rootMessageNullable(Throwable error) {
    Throwable root = rootCause(error);
    return root == null ? null : Strings.trimToNull(root.getMessage());
  }

  public static String rootMessage(Throwable error) {
    Throwable root = rootCause(error);
    if (root == null) {
      return "unknown error";
    }
    String message = Strings.trimToNull(root.getMessage());
    return message == null ? root.getClass().getSimpleName() : message;
  }

  public static String normalizeMessage(Throwable error) {
    if (error == null) {
      return "unknown failure";
    }
    String message = error.getMessage();
    if (message == null || message.isBlank()) {
      return error.getClass().getSimpleName();
    }
    return message;
  }
}


FILE: IdentityParsingSupport.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.util;

public final class IdentityParsingSupport {
  private IdentityParsingSupport() {}

  public static String requireGroup(String group) {
    return requireGroup(group, "session.group");
  }

  public static String requireGroup(String group, String fieldName) {
    return Strings.requireNonBlank(group, fieldName);
  }

  public static String requireNamespace(String namespace, String fieldName) {
    return Strings.requireNonBlank(namespace, fieldName);
  }

  public static String requireName(String name, String fieldName) {
    return Strings.requireNonBlank(name, fieldName);
  }

  public static <T> T requireNonNullRuntime(T value, String message) {
    if (value == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(message);
    }
    return value;
  }

  public static ScopedName parseScopedName(
      String scopedName, String namespaceFieldName, String nameFieldName) {
    String normalized = Strings.requireNonBlank(scopedName, "scopedName");
    int slash = normalized.indexOf('/');
    if (slash < 0) {
      return new ScopedName(null, requireName(normalized, nameFieldName));
    }
    String namespace = requireNamespace(normalized.substring(0, slash), namespaceFieldName);
    String name = requireName(normalized.substring(slash + 1), nameFieldName);
    return new ScopedName(namespace, name);
  }

  public record ScopedName(String namespace, String name) {}
}


FILE: Io.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.util;

import java.io.IOException;
import java.io.InputStream;
import java.nio.file.Files;
import java.nio.file.Path;
import java.nio.file.StandardOpenOption;

public final class Io {

  private Io() {}

  public static Path writeTempFile(String prefix, String suffix, byte[] data) throws IOException {
    if (data == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("data is required");
    }
    Path temp = Files.createTempFile(prefix, suffix);
    Files.write(temp, data, StandardOpenOption.TRUNCATE_EXISTING);
    temp.toFile().deleteOnExit();
    return temp.toAbsolutePath().normalize();
  }

  public static byte[] readClasspathBytes(String resourcePath, Class<?> anchor) throws IOException {
    if (anchor == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("anchor is required");
    }
    String normalized = normalizeResourcePath(resourcePath);
    ClassLoader tccl = Thread.currentThread().getContextClassLoader();
    InputStream in = tccl == null ? null : tccl.getResourceAsStream(normalized);
    if (in == null) {
      ClassLoader anchorLoader = anchor.getClassLoader();
      in = anchorLoader == null ? ClassLoader.getSystemResourceAsStream(normalized) : anchorLoader.getResourceAsStream(normalized);
    }
    if (in == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Classpath resource not found: " + resourcePath);
    }
    try (InputStream stream = in) {
      return stream.readAllBytes();
    }
  }

  public static void deleteIfExists(Path path) {
    if (path == null) {
      return;
    }
    try {
      Files.deleteIfExists(path);
    } catch (IOException ignore) {
    }
  }

  private static String normalizeResourcePath(String resourcePath) {
    String path = Strings.trimToNull(resourcePath);
    if (path == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("resourcePath is required");
    }
    return path.startsWith("/") ? path.substring(1) : path;
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.util;

/** Shared namespace utilities for normalization. */
public final class Namespaces {

  public static final String DEFAULT_NAMESPACE = "default";

  private Namespaces() {}

  public static String resolveNamespace(String namespace) {
    return Strings.requireNonBlank(namespace, "namespace");
  }

  public static String normalizeNamespace(String namespace) {
    return Strings.trimToNull(namespace);
  }
}


FILE: Strings.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.util;

import java.util.Collection;
import java.util.Map;

public final class Strings {

  private Strings() {
    // utility
  }

  /**
   * Returns {@code true} when the value is {@code null} or contains only whitespace.
   */
  public static boolean isBlank(String value) {
    return value == null || value.isBlank();
  }

  /**
   * Returns {@code true} when the value is not {@code null} and has non-whitespace content.
   */
  public static boolean isNotBlank(String value) {
    return !isBlank(value);
  }

  /**
   * Returns {@code true} when the value is {@code null} or empty (no trim).
   */
  public static boolean isEmpty(String value) {
    return value == null || value.isEmpty();
  }

  /**
   * Returns {@code true} when the value is not {@code null} and not empty (no trim).
   */
  public static boolean isNotEmpty(String value) {
    return !isEmpty(value);
  }

  /**
   * Returns {@code true} when the collection is {@code null} or empty.
   */
  public static boolean isEmpty(Collection<?> value) {
    return value == null || value.isEmpty();
  }

  /**
   * Returns {@code true} when the collection is not {@code null} and not empty.
   */
  public static boolean isNotEmpty(Collection<?> value) {
    return value != null && !value.isEmpty();
  }

  /**
   * Returns {@code true} when the map is {@code null} or empty.
   */
  public static boolean isEmpty(Map<?, ?> value) {
    return value == null || value.isEmpty();
  }

  /**
   * Returns {@code true} when the map is not {@code null} and not empty.
   */
  public static boolean isNotEmpty(Map<?, ?> value) {
    return value != null && !value.isEmpty();
  }

  /**
   * Returns {@code true} when the array is {@code null} or empty.
   */
  public static boolean isEmpty(Object[] value) {
    return value == null || value.length == 0;
  }

  /**
   * Returns {@code true} when the array is not {@code null} and not empty.
   */
  public static boolean isNotEmpty(Object[] value) {
    return value != null && value.length > 0;
  }

  /**
   * Trims the value, returning {@code null} when the input is {@code null} or blank after trim.
   */
  public static String trimToNull(String value) {
    if (value == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String trimmed = value.trim();
    return trimmed.isEmpty() ? null : trimmed;
  }

  /**
   * Trims the value, returning an empty string when the input is {@code null}.
   */
  public static String trimToEmpty(String value) {
    return value == null ? "" : value.trim();
  }

  /**
   * Returns an empty string when the input is {@code null}.
   */
  public static String nullToEmpty(String value) {
    return value == null ? "" : value;
  }

  /**
   * Returns {@code null} when the input is an empty string; leaves whitespace unchanged.
   */
  public static String emptyToNull(String value) {
    if (value == null) {
      return null;
    }
    return value.isEmpty() ? null : value;
  }

  /**
   * Returns {@code null} when the input is {@code null} or blank; leaves non-blank values unchanged.
   */
  public static String blankToNull(String value) {
    return isBlank(value) ? null : value;
  }

  /**
   * Returns a normalized string with trimmed edges and single spaces between tokens.
   * Returns {@code null} when the input is {@code null}.
   */
  public static String normalizeSpace(String value) {
    if (value == null) {
      return null;
    }
    return value.trim().replaceAll("\\s+", " ");
  }

  /**
   * Returns the trimmed value or throws {@link IllegalArgumentException} when blank.
   */
  public static String requireNonBlank(String value, String name) {
    if (isBlank(value)) {
      String label = name == null ? "value" : name;
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(label + " is required");
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

  /**
   * Returns the value or throws {@link IllegalArgumentException} when null or empty.
   */
  public static String requireNonEmpty(String value, String name) {
    if (isEmpty(value)) {
      String label = name == null ? "value" : name;
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(label + " is required");
    }
    return value;
  }

  /**
   * Null-safe equality check.
   */
  public static boolean equals(String left, String right) {
    if (left == null) {
      return right == null;
    }
    return left.equals(right);
  }

  /**
   * Null-safe case-insensitive equality check.
   */
  public static boolean equalsIgnoreCase(String left, String right) {
    if (left == null) {
      return right == null;
    }
    return right != null && left.equalsIgnoreCase(right);
  }

  /**
   * Returns the first non-blank value (after trimming) or {@code null} if none.
   */
  public static String firstNonBlank(String... values) {
    if (values == null) {
      return null;
    }
    for (String value : values) {
      String trimmed = trimToNull(value);
      if (trimmed != null) {
        return trimmed;
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  /**
   * Returns the first non-null value or {@code null} if none.
   */
  public static String firstNonNull(String... values) {
    if (values == null) {
      return null;
    }
    for (String value : values) {
      if (value != null) {
        return value;
      }
    }
    return null;
  }
}
